Viṣṇudharma nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya maṅg naraṃ caiva narottamam maṅg devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva maṅg tato jayam udīrayet maṅg dvaipāyanauṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtam aprameyaṃ maṅg puṇyaṃ pavitram atha pāpaharaṃ śubhaṃ ca maṅg yo bhārataṃ samadhigacchati vācyamānaṃ maṅg kiṃ tasya puṣkarajalair abhiṣecanena maṅg namo vyāsāya gurave maṅglt sarvajñāya maharṣaye maṅglt pārāśaryāya śāntāya maṅglt namo nārāyaṇāya te maṅglt kṛtābhiṣekaṃ tanayam rājñaḥ pārīkṣitasya ha draṣṭum abhyāyayuḥ prītyā śaunakādyā maharṣayaḥ tān āgatān sa rājarṣiḥ pādyārghyādibhir arcitān sukhopaviṣṭān viśrāntān kṛtasaṃpraśnasatkathān tatkathābhiḥ kṛtāhlādaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ śatānīko atha papraccha nārāyaṇakathāṃ parām yam āśritya jagannātham mama pūrvapitāmahāḥ vipakṣāpahṛtaṃ rājyam avāpuḥ puruṣottamāḥ drauṇibrahmāstranirdagdho mama yena pitāmahaḥ parīkṣit prāṇasaṃyogaṃ devadevena lambhitaḥ tasya devasya māhātmyaṃ devarṣisiddhamanujaiḥ śrutaṃ subahuśo mayā stutasyāśeṣajanmanaḥ kaḥ stotum īśas tam ajaṃ yasyaitat sacarācaram avyayasyāprameyasya brahmāṇḍam udare śayam rudraḥ krodhodbhavo yasya prasādāc ca pitāmahaḥ tasya devasya kaḥ śaktaḥ pravaktuṃ vā vibhūtayaḥ so aham icchāmi devasya tasya sarvātmanaḥ prabhoḥ śrotum ārādhanaṃ yena nistareyaṃ bhavārṇavam kenopāyena mantrair vā rahasyaiḥ paricaryayā dānair vratopavāsair vā japyair homair athāpi vā ārādhitaḥ samastānāṃ kleśānāṃ hānido hariḥ śakyaḥ samārādhayituṃ tan naḥ śaṃsata sattamāḥ vidyānām api sā vidyā śrutānām api tac chrutam rahasyānāṃ rahasyaṃ tad yena viṣṇuḥ prasīdati mantrāṇāṃ paramo mantro vratānāṃ tan mahāvratam upoṣitaṃ hi tac chreṣṭhaṃ yena tuṣyati keśavaḥ sā jihvā yā hariṃ stauti tac cittaṃ yat tadarpaṇam tāv eva kevalau ślāghyau yau tatpūjākarau karau sujanma deham atyantaṃ tad evāśeṣajanmasu yad eva pulakodbhāsi viṣṇor nāmābhikīrtanāt sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sā cāndhajaḍamūkatā yan muhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate nūnaṃ tat kaṇṭhaśālūkam athavā pratijihvikā rogo vānyo na sā jihvā yā na vakti harer guṇān santy anekā bilās tadvac śrotram apy alpamedhasām dattvāvadhānaṃ yac chabde vinaiva harisaṃstutim dharmārthakāmasaṃprāptau puruṣāṇāṃ viceṣṭitam janmany aviphalā saikā yā govindāśrayā kriyā durgasaṃsārakāntāram apāram abhidhāvatām ekaḥ kṛṣṇanamaskāro muktitīrasya deśikaḥ sarvaratnamayo meruḥ sarvāścaryamayaṃ nabhaḥ sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvadevamayo hariḥ evam ādiguṇo bhogaḥ kṛṣṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ śruto me bahuśo siddhaiḥ gīyamānas tathāparaiḥ so aham icchāmi taṃ devaṃ sarvalokaparāyaṇam nārāyaṇam aśeṣasya jagato hṛdy avasthitam ārādhayitum īśānam anantam amitaujasam śaṃkaraṃ jagataḥ prāṇaṃ smṛtamātrāghahāriṇam tan mamādya muniśreṣṭhāḥ prasādayitum icchataḥ upadeśapradānena prasādaṃ kartum arhata tasyaitad vacanaṃ śrutvā bhaktim udvahato hareḥ paritoṣaṃ paraṃ jagmur munayaḥ sarva eva te sarve ca te muniśreṣṭhā bhṛguśreṣṭhaṃ ca śaunakam yathārthaṃ bhagavaṃs tasmai kathyatām ity acodayan sarvajñānanidhiḥ sphītas tvam atra bhṛgunandana trailokyasarvasaṃdeha- tamodīpas tapodhana evam ukto munivaraiḥ prītyā tasya ca bhūpateḥ bhaktyā ca devadevasya pravaṇīkṛtamānasaḥ kṛtvottarīyaparyaṅkaṃ śithilaṃ bhagavān atha pratyuvāca mahābhāgaḥ śaunakas taṃ mahīpatim yat pṛcchasi mahīpāla kṛṣṇasyārādhanaṃ prati vratopavāsajapyādi tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu anādimat paraṃ brahma sarvaheyavivarjitam vyāpi yat sarvabhūteṣu sthitaṃ sadasataḥ param pradhānapuṃsor ajayor yataḥ kṣobhaḥ pravartate nityayor vyāpinoś caiva jagadādau mahātmanoḥ tatkṣobhakatvād brahmāṇḍa- sṛṣṭihetur nirañjanaḥ ahetur api sarvātmanaḥ jāyate parameśvaraḥ pradhānapuruṣatvaṃ ca tathaiveśvaralīlayā samupaiti tataś caiva brahmatvaṃ chandataḥ prabhuḥ tataḥ sthitau pālayitā viṣṇutvaṃ jagataḥ kṣaye rudratvaṃ ca jagannāthaḥ svecchayā kurute avyayaḥ tad ekam akṣaraṃ dhāma paraṃ sadasator mahat bhedābhedasvarūpasthaṃ praṇipatya paraṃ padam pravakṣyāmi yathā pūrvaṃ matpitrā kathitaṃ mama tasyāpi kila tatpitrā tasmai cāha kilośanāḥ tenāpi bhṛgum ārādhya prāptam ārādhanaṃ hareḥ sakāśād brahmaṇaḥ prāptaṃ bhṛguṇāpi mahātmanā marīcimiśraiś ca purā param etan maharṣibhiḥ prāptaṃ sakāśād devasya brahmaṇo vyaktajanmanaḥ yogaṃ brahmā paraṃ prāha maharṣīṇāṃ yadā prabhuḥ samastavṛttisaṃrodhāt kaivalyapratipādakam tadā jagatpatir brahmā praṇipatya maharṣibhiḥ sarvaiḥ kilokto bhagavān ātmayoniḥ prajāhitam yo yogo bhavatā prokto manovṛttinirodhajaḥ prāptuṃ śakyaḥ sa tv anekaiḥ janmabhir jagataḥ pate viṣayā durjayā nṝṇām indriyākarṣaṇāḥ prabho vṛttayaś cetasaś cāpi capalā cātidurdharāḥ rāgādayaḥ kathaṃ jetuṃ śakyā varṣaśatair api na yogayogyaṃ hi mano bhavaty ebhir anirjitaiḥ alpāyuṣaś ca puruṣā brahman kṛtayuge apy amī tretāyāṃ dvāpare caiva kimu prāpte kalau yuge bhagavaṃs tvam upāyajñaḥ prasanno vaktum arhasi anāyāsena yenemam uttarema bhavārṇavam duḥkhāmbumagnāḥ puruṣāḥ prāpya brahma mahāplavam uttareyur bhavāmbhodhiṃ tathā tvam anucintaya evam uktas tadā brahmā kriyāyogaṃ mahātmanām teṣām ṛṣīṇām ācaṣṭa narāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ārādhayata viśveśam nārāyaṇam atandritāḥ bāhyālambanasāpekṣās tam ajaṃ jagataḥ patim ijyāpūjānamaskāra- śuśrūṣābhir aharniśam vratopavāsair vividhair brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ tais taiś cābhimataiḥ kāmair ye ca cetasi tuṣṭidāḥ aparicchedyamāhātmyam ārādhayata keśavam tanniṣṭhās tadgatadhiyas tatkarmāṇas tadāśrayāḥ taddṛṣṭayas tanmanasaḥ sarvasmin sa iti sthitaḥ samastāny atha karmāṇi tatra sarvātmanātmani saṃnyasyadhvaṃ sa vaḥ kartā samastāvaraṇakṣayam etat tad akṣaraṃ brahma pradhānapuruṣāv ubhau yato yasmin yathā cobhau sarvavyāpiny avasthitau paraḥ parāṇāṃ paramaḥ sa ekaḥ puruṣottamaḥ yasyābhinnam idaṃ sarvam yac ceṅgaṃ yac ca neṅgati tam ārādhya jagannāthaṃ mokṣakāraṇam avyaktam acintyam aparigraham kriyāyogena mucyate iti te brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā rahasyam ṛṣisattamāḥ narāṇām upakārāya yogaśāstrāṇi cakrire kriyāyogaparāṇīha muktikāryāṇy anekaśaḥ ārādhyate jagannātho yadanuṣṭhānatatparaiḥ paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ tāni te nṛpaśārdūla sarvapāpaharāṇy aham vakṣyāmi śrūyatām anyad rahasyam idam uttamam saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ viṣayākrāntacetasām uttāram icchatāṃ tasmād bhṛśaṃ yan nāntarair api viṣṇupotaṃ vinā nānyat kiṃcid asti parāyaṇam uttiṣṭhaṃś cintaya hariṃ vrajaṃś cintaya keśavam bhuñjaṃś cintaya govindam svapaṃś cintaya mādhavam evam ekāgracittas tvaṃ saṃśrito madhusūdanam janmamṛtyujarāgrāhaṃ saṃsārāmbhas tariṣyasi anantam īḍyaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ jagadvidhātāram ajaṃ janitryam samāśritā ye harim īśitāraṃ teṣāṃ bhavo nāsti hi muktibhājām śrūyatāṃ kuruśārdūla saṃvādo ayam anuttamaḥ ambarīṣasya rājarṣeḥ saha devena cakriṇā ambarīṣo mahīpālaḥ pālayann eva medinīm udvigna eva dvandvāntam abhīpsuḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ devadevāt sa govindād abhīpsur dvandvasaṃkṣayam tapas tepe nirāhāro gṛṇan brahma sanātanam tasya kālena mahatā bhaktim udvahataḥ parām tutoṣa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvalokapatiḥ prabhuḥ sa rūpam aindram āsthāya tam uvāca mahīpatim meghagambhīranirghoṣo vāraṇendragatis tadā rājarṣe vada yat kāryaṃ tava cetasy avasthitam varado aham anuprāpto varaṃ varaya suvrata evam uktas tato rājā vilokya ca puraṃdaraṃ pratyuvācārghyam udyamya svāgataṃ te astv iti prabho nāham ārādhayāmi tvāṃ tava baddho ayam añjaliḥ varārthināṃ tvaṃ varadaḥ prayacchābhimatān varān varārthāya tvayānyaiś ca kriyate nṛpate tapaḥ sa kim arthaṃ tvam asmatto na gṛhṇāsy abhivāṃchitam na varārtham ayaṃ yatnas tvatto devapate mama viṣṇor ārādhanārthāya viddhi māṃ tvaṃ kṛtodyamam ahaṃ hi sarvadevānāṃ trailokyasya tatheśvaraḥ pālayanti mamaivājñām ādityādyāḥ sadā surāḥ ādityā vasavo rudrā nāsatyau marutāṃ gaṇāḥ prajānāṃ patayaḥ sādhyā viśvedevā maharṣayaḥ kurvanty ete mamaivājñāṃ siddhagandharvapannagāḥ matto hi ko anyo varadaḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva vāñchitam tvam indraḥ satyam evaitad devas tribhuvaneśvaraḥ tvayāpi prāptam aiśvaryaṃ yatas taṃ toṣayāmy aham trailokyaṃ tava deveśa vaśe yasya mahātmanaḥ saptodare śayā lokās tam īśaṃ toṣayāmy aham yasya tvam amaraiḥ sarvaiḥ samavetāḥ sureśvara dehaprāpto antarastho vai taṃ namāmi janārdanam nimeṣo brahmaṇo rātrir unmeṣo yasya vāsaraḥ tam īḍyam īśam ajaraṃ praṇato asmi janārdanam yo hartā jagato devaḥ kartā pālāyitā ca yaḥ trayasyāsya ca yo yonis taṃ viṣṇuṃ toṣayāmy aham hiraṇyakaśipuḥ pūrvaṃ hiraṇyākṣaś ca te ripuḥ tavānukampayā yena hatau daityau nato asmi tam balināpahṛtaṃ śakra dattaṃ yena purā tava trailokyarājyaṃ taṃ baddhvā taṃ namāmi janārdanam prasīda śakra gaccha tvam aham apy atra saṃsthitaḥ tapas tapsye jagannāthaṃ draṣṭuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim evam uktas tatas tena śakrarūpī janārdanaḥ punar apy āha taṃ kopāt pārthivaṃ tapasi sthitam yadi madvacanād adya na bhavāṃs tyakṣyate tapaḥ vajraṃ te prahariṣyāmi budhyasvaitad yadīcchasi nāpy alpam aparādhaṃ te karomi tridaśeśvara tathāpi vadhayogyaṃ māṃ manyase cet kṣipāyudham śrūyate kila govinde bhaktim udvahatāṃ nṛṇām saṃsārārṇāvabhītānāṃ tridaśāḥ paripanthinaḥ tāpaso ahaṃ kva niḥsaṅgaḥ kva ca kopas tavedṛśaḥ vijñātam etad govinda- bhaktivighnopapāditam bhavanti bahavo vighnā nare śreyaḥparāyaṇe govindabhaktyabhyadhikaṃ śreyaś cānyan na vidyate sa tvaṃ prahara vā mā vā mayi vajraṃ puraṃdara nāham utsṛjya govindam anyam ārādhayāmi bhoḥ na cāpi vajraṃ vajrī vā tvaṃ ca nānye surāsurāḥ śaktā nihantum īśāne hṛdayasthe janārdane kiṃ ca no bahunoktena nāhaṃ vakṣyāmy ataḥ paraṃ yathepsitaṃ kuruṣva tvaṃ kariṣye aham abhīpsitam evam uktvā surapatiṃ pārthivaḥ sa punas tapaḥ cacāra maunam āsthāya tenātuṣyata keśavaḥ saṃdarśayām āsa tataḥ svaṃ vapuḥ kaiṭabhārdanaḥ caturbhujam udārāṅgaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam kirīṭasragdharaṃ spaṣṭaṃ nīlotpaladalacchavim airāvataś ca garuḍas tatkṣaṇāt samadṛśyata sa ca rājavaro devaṃ pītavāsasam acyutam vilokya bhaktiśirasā sahasaiva mahīṃ yayau pratyuvāca ca bhūpālaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ romāñcitatanuḥ stotram padmanābhaṃ tato astuvat ādideva jayājeya jaya sargādikāraka jayāspaṣṭaprakāśāṇḍa bṛhanmūrte jayākṣara jaya sarvagatācintya jaya janmajarāpaha jaya vyāpiñ jayābheda sarvabhūteṣv avasthita jaya yajñapate nātha havyakavyāśanāvyaya jaya vijñātasiddhānta māyāmohaka keśava lokasthityartham anagha varāha jaya bhūdhara nṛsiṃha jaya devāri- vakṣaḥsthalavidāraṇa devānām aribhītānām ārtināśana vāmana jaya krāntasamastorvī- nabhaḥsvarlokabhāvana jitaṃ te jagatām īśa jitaṃ te sarva sarvada jitaṃ te sarvabhūteśa yogidhyeya namo astu te namo astv avyapadeśyāya namaḥ sūkṣmasvarūpiṇe namas trimūrtaye tubhyaṃ viśvamūrte namo astu te brahmādyaiś cintyate rūpaṃ yat tat sadasataḥ paraṃ viśeṣair aviśeṣyāya tasmai tubhyaṃ namo namaḥ puruṣākhyaṃ tato rūpaṃ nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ ca prakṛteḥ parataḥ sūkṣmaṃ tan namasyāmi te hare avyaktādiviśeṣāntam atisūkṣmatamaṃ mahat prākṛtaṃ tava tad rūpaṃ tasmai deva namāmy aham rūpair nānāvidhair yaś ca tadrūpāntaragocaram līlayā vyavahāras te tasmai devātmane namaḥ prasīda viṣṇo govinda śaṅkhacakragadādhara dharādharāravindākṣa vāsudeva maheśvara itthaṃ stuto jagannāthaḥ proktavān iti keśavaḥ ambarīṣaṃ pṛthivīśaṃ jagat saṃnādayan girā ambarīṣa prasanno asmi bhaktyā stotreṇa cānagha varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dharmajña yat te manasi vartate eṣa eva varaḥ ślāghyo yad dṛṣṭo asi jagatpate tvaddarśanam apuṇyānāṃ svapneṣv api hi durlabham bālyāt prabhṛti yā deva tvayi bhaktir mamācyuta vetti tāṃ bhagavān eva hṛdisthaḥ sarvadehinām tvatprasādān mameśāna rājyam avyāhataṃ bhuvi kośadaṇḍau tathātīva śarīrārogyam uttamam striyo annapānasāmarthyā hāniḥ svalpāpi nāsti me balaṃ nāgasahasrasya dhārayāmy arisūdana saṃtatir nibhṛtā bhṛtyā sānurāgāś ca me janāḥ dharmahāniś ca deveśa na hi me pālane bhuvaḥ yad yad icchāmy ahaṃ tat tat sarvam asti jagatpate etenaivānumānena prasanno bhagavān iti jñātaṃ mayā hi govinde nāprasanne vibhūtayaḥ evaṃ sarvasukhāhlāda- madhyastho api ca keśava punarāvṛttiduḥkhānāṃ trāsād udvignamānasaḥ mayi prasādābhimukhaṃ manas te yadi keśava tan mām agādhe saṃsāre magnam uddhartum arhasi sukhāni tāni naivānte yeṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na tat sukham yad ante duḥkham āgāmi kiṃpākasyaiva bhakṣaṇam sa prasādaṃ kuru guro jagatām tvaṃ janārdana jñānadānena yenemāṃ vāgurān nistaremahi ity uktas tasya govindaḥ kathayām āsa yogavit yogaṃ nirbījam atyanta- duḥkhasaṃyogabheṣajam upadiṣṭe tato yoge praṇipatyācyutaṃ nṛpaḥ punaḥ prāha mahābāhur vinayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ devadeva tvayā yogo yaḥ prokto madhusūdana naiṣa prāpyo mayā nānyair mānavair ajitendriyaiḥ viṣayā durjayāḥ puṃbhir indriyākarṣiṇaḥ sadā indriyāṇāṃ jayaṃ teṣu kaḥ śaktānāṃ kariṣyati ahaṃ mameti cākhyāti durjayaṃ cañcalaṃ manaḥ rāgādayaḥ kathaṃ jetuṃ śakyā janmāntarair api so aham icchāmi deveśa tvatprasādād anirjitaiḥ rāgādibhir amartyatvaṃ prāptuṃ prakṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ yady evaṃ muktikāmas tvaṃ naranātha śṛṇuṣva tat kriyāyogaṃ samastānāṃ kleśānāṃ hānikārakam manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṃ namaskuru mām evaiṣyasi yuktvaivam ātmānaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ madbhāvanā madyajanā madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥ mama pūjāparāś caiva mayi yānti layaṃ narāḥ sarvabhūteṣu māṃ paśya samavasthitam īśvaram kartāsi kena vairatvaṃ evaṃ doṣān prahāsyasi jaṅgamājaṅgame jñāte mayy ātmani tathā tava rāgalobhādināśena bhavitrī kṛtakṛtyatā bhaktyātipravaṇasyāpi cañcalatvān mano yadi mayy anāsādavad bhūpa kuru madrūpiṇīṃ tanum suvarṇarajatādyais tvaṃ śailamṛddārulekhajām pūjāmaharhair vividhaiḥ saṃpūjaya ca pārthiva tasyāṃ cittaṃ samāveśya tyājayānyān vyapāśrayān pūjitā saiva te bhaktyā dhyātā caivopakāriṇī gacchaṃs tiṣṭhan svapan bhuñjaṃs tām evāgre ca pṛṣṭhataḥ upary adhas tathā pārśve cintayāntas tathātmanaḥ snānais tīrthodakair hṛdyaiḥ puṣpagandhānulepanaiḥ vāsobhir bhūṣaṇair bhakṣyair gītavādyair manoharaiḥ yac ca yac ca nṛpeṣṭaṃ te kiṃcid bhojyādi tena tām bhaktinamro naraśreṣṭha prīṇayārcāṃ kṛtāṃ mama rāgeṇākṛṣyate ceto gandharvābhimukhaṃ yadi mayi buddhiṃ samāveśya gāyethā mama tāṃ kathām kathāyāṃ ramate ceto yadi tatbhāvanā mama śrotavyā prītiyuktena avatāreṣu yā kathā evaṃ mayy arpitamanāś cetaso ye vyapāśrayāḥ heyās tān akhilān bhūpa parityakṣyasy abhīr bhava akṣīṇarāgadoṣo api matkriyā paramaḥ param padam āpsyasi mā bhais tvaṃ mayy arpitamanā bhava mayi saṃnyasya sarvaṃ tvam ātmānaṃ yat tavāsti ca madarthaṃ kuru karmāṇi mā ca dharmavyatikramam rājyaṃ kuru naraśreṣṭha nivedya pṛthivīṃ mama tadvyāghātaparā ye ca jahi tān avanīpate etenaivopadeśena vyākhyātam akhilaṃ tava kriyāyogaṃ samāsthāya mayy arpitamanā bhava maddhitāya jagannātha kriyāyogāśritaṃ mama vistareṇedam ākhyāhi prasannas tvaṃ hi duḥkhahā tvām ṛtena hi no vaktuṃ samartho anyo jagadguro guhyam etat pavitraṃ ca tad ācakṣya prasīda me ākhyāsyaty etad akhilaṃ vasiṣṭhas te purohitaḥ matprasādād avikalaṃ sa ca vetsyaty aśeṣataḥ ity uktvāntardadhe devaḥ sarvalokeśvaro hariḥ sa ca rājā vanād bhūyo nijam abhyāgamat puram rājyasthas tu mahīpālaḥ praṇipatya purohitam vasiṣṭhaṃ paripapraccha viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ prati devadevena bhagavann ādiṣṭo asi mahātmanā kriyāyogāśritaṃ sarvaṃ vyākhyāsyati bhavān kila sa tvāṃ pṛcchāmy ahaṃ sarvaṃ kriyāyogena keśavam saṃtoṣayitum īśānaṃ yathā śakṣyāmi tad vada devaprasādād akhilā mamāpi smṛtir āgatā jñānam etad aśeṣaṃ te kathayāmi nibodha tat bhaktimān abhavad daityo hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ nārāyaṇe mahāprajñaḥ sarvalokaparāyaṇe sa papraccha bhṛguśreṣṭhaṃ śukram ātmapurohitam bhagavan nṛsiṃharūpasya viṣṇos tātaṃ jighāṃsataḥ dṛṣṭaṃ dehe mayā sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ bhūrbhuvādikam brahmā prajāpatiś cendro rudraiḥ paśupatiḥ saha vasavo aṣṭau tathādityā dvādaśāhaḥkṣapā mahī diśo nabhas tārakaughaṃ nakṣatragrahasaṃkulam aśvinau marutaḥ sādhyā viśvedevās tatha rṣayaḥ varṣācalās tathā nadyaḥ sapta sapta kulācalāḥ samudrāḥ sapta ṛtavaḥ kāntārāṇi vanāni ca nagaragrāmatarubhiḥ samāvetaṃ ca bhūtalam etac cānyac ca yat kiṃcid devarṣipitṛmānavam satiryagūrdhvapātālaṃ tasya dṛṣṭaṃ tanau mayā so ahaṃ tam ajaraṃ devaṃ duṣṭadaityanivarhaṇam ārādhayitum icchāmi bhagavaṃs tvadanujñayā anugrāhyo asmi yadi te mamāyaṃ bhaktimān iti tan mamopadiśādya tvaṃ mahad ārādhanaṃ hareḥ anugrāhyo asi devasya nūnam avyaktajanmanaḥ ārādhanāya daityendra yat te tatpravaṇaṃ manaḥ yadi devapatiṃ viṣṇum ārādhayitum icchasi bhagavantam anādyantaṃ bhava bhāgavato asura na hy abhāgavatair viṣṇur jñātuṃ stotuṃ ca tattvataḥ draṣṭuṃ vā śakyate martyaiḥ praveṣṭuṃ kuta eva hi janmabhir bahubhiḥ pūtā narās tadgatacetasaḥ bhavanti vai bhāgavatās te viṣṇuṃ praviśanti ca anekajanmasaṃsāra- cite pāpasamuccaye nākṣīṇe jāyate puṃsāṃ govindābhimukhī matiḥ pradveṣaṃ yāti govinde dvijān vedāṃś ca nindati yo naras taṃ vijānīyād asurāṃśasamudbhavam pāṣaṇḍeṣu ratiḥ puṃsāṃ hetuvādānukūlatā jāyate viṣṇumāyāmbhaḥ- patitānāṃ durātmanām yadā pāpakṣayaḥ puṃsāṃ tadā vedadvijātiṣu viṣṇau ca yajñapuruṣe śraddhā bhavati te yathā yadā svalpāvaśeṣas tu narāṇāṃ pāpasaṃcayaḥ bhavanti te bhāgavatās tadā daityapate narāḥ bhrāmyatām atra saṃsāre narāṇāṃ karmadurgame hastāvalambado hy eko bhaktiprīto janārdanaḥ sa tvaṃ bhāgavato bhūtvā sarvapāpaharaṃ harim ārādhaya paraṃ bhaktyā prītim eṣyati keśavaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇā bhāgavatā bhavanti puruṣā guro yac ca bhāgavataiḥ kāryaṃ tan me kathaya bhārgava karmaṇā manasā vācā prāṇināṃ yo na hiṃsakaḥ bhāvabhaktaś ca govinde daitya bhāgavato hi saḥ yo brāhmaṇāṃś ca vedāṃś ca nityam envānumaṃsyati na ca drogdhā paraṃ vāde daitya bhāgavato hi saḥ sarvān devān hariṃ vetti sarvalokāṃś ca keśavam tebhyaś ca nānyam ātmānaṃ daitya bhāgavato hi saḥ devaṃ manuṣyam anyaṃ vā paśupakṣipipīlikān tarupāṣāṇakaṣṭhādi bhūmyambhogaganaṃ diśaḥ ātmānaṃ vāpi deveśān nātiriktaṃ janārdanāt yo bhajeta vijānīṣva taṃ vai bhāgavataṃ naram sarvaṃ bhagavato bhāvo yad bhūtaṃ bhavasaṃsthitam iti yo vai vijānāti sa tu bhāgavato naraḥ bhavabhītiṃ haraty eṣa bhaktibhāvena bhāvitaḥ bhagavān iti bhāvo yaḥ sa tu bhāgavato naraḥ bhāvaṃ na kurute yas tu sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam karmaṇā manasā vācā sa tu bhāgavato naraḥ bāhyārthanirapekṣo yo bhakto bhagavataḥ kriyām bhāvena niṣpādayati jñeyo bhāgavatas tu saḥ nārayo yasya na snigdhā na codāsī na vṛttayaḥ paśyataḥ sarvam evedaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhāgavato hi saḥ sutapteneha tapasā yajñair vā bahudakṣiṇaiḥ tāṃ gatiṃ na narā yānti yāṃ vai bhāgavatā gatāḥ yogacyutair bhāgavatair devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ arvāṅ nirīkṣyate yajñī kimu ye yogapāragāḥ yajñaniṣpattaye vedā yajño yajñapateḥ kṛte tattoṣaṇāya bhāvena tasmād bhāgavato bhava yena sarvātmanā viṣṇau bhaktyā bhāvo niveśitaḥ daityeśvara kṛtārthatvāc ślāghyo bhāgavato hi saḥ api naḥ sa kule dhanyo jāyate kulapāvanaḥ bhagavān bhaktibhāvena yena viṣṇur upāsitaḥ yaḥ kārayati devārcāṃ hṛdayālambanaṃ hareḥ sa naro viṣṇusālokyam upaiti dhūtakalmaṣaḥ yaś ca devālayaṃ bhaktyā viṣṇoḥ kārayati svayam sa saptapuruṣāṃl lokān viṣṇor nayati mānavaḥ yāvanty abdāni devārcā hares tiṣṭhati mandire tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke sa modate devārcā lakṣaṇopetā tadgṛhaṃ satataṃ divi niṣkāmaṃ ca mano yasya sa yāty akṣarasātmyatām puṣpāṇy atisugandhīni manojñāni ca yaḥ pumān prayacchati hṛṣīkeśe tadbhāvagatamānasaḥ dhūpāṃś ca vividhāṃs tāṃs tān gandhāḍhyaṃ cānulepanam dīpāvalyupahārāṃś ca yac cābhīṣṭam athātmanaḥ naraḥ so anudinaṃ yajñaṃ karoty ārādhanaṃ hareḥ yajñeśo bhagavān viṣṇur makhair api hi toṣyate bahūpakaraṇā yajñā nānāsaṃbhāravistarāḥ prāpyante te dhanayutair manuṣyair nālpasaṃcayaiḥ bhaktyā ca puruṣaiḥ pūjā kṛtā dūrvāṅkurair api harer dadāti hi phalaṃ sarvayajñaiḥ sudurlabham yāni puṣpāṇi hṛdyāni dhūpagandhānulepanam dayitaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ yac ca ye ca kauśeyavāsasī yāni cābhyavahārāṇi bhakṣyāṇi ca phalāni ca prayaccha tāni govinde bhavethāś caiva tanmanāḥ ādyantaṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ yathāśaktyā prasādaya ārādhya yāti taṃ devaṃ tasminn eva naro layam puṇyais tīrthodakair gandhair madhunā sarpiṣā tathā kṣīreṇa snāpayed īśam acyutaṃ jagataḥ patim dadhikṣīrahradān puṇyāṃs tato lokān madhucyutaḥ prayāsyasy asuraśreṣṭha nirvṛtiṃ cāpi śāśvatīm stotrair gītais tathā vādyair brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ manasaś caikatāyogād ārādhaya janārdanam ārādhya taṃ videhānāṃ puruṣāḥ saptasaptatiḥ haihayāḥ pañcapañcāśad amṛtatvam upāgatāḥ sa tvam ebhiḥ prakārais tam upavāsaiś ca keśavam toṣayādyo hi tuṣṭo asau viṣṇur dvandvapraśāntidaḥ upavāsair hṛṣīkeśaḥ kathaṃ tuṣyati bhārgava parihārāṃs tathācakṣva ye tyājyāś copavāsinām yad yat kāryaṃ yathā caiva keśavārādhane naraiḥ tat sarvaṃ vistarād brahman yathāvad vaktum arhasi smṛtaḥ saṃpūjito dhūpa- puṣpādyair dayitair hariḥ bhoginām upakārāya kiṃ punaś copavāsinām upāvṛttas tu pāpebhyo yas tu vāso guṇaiḥ saha upavāsaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sarvabhogavivarjitaḥ ekarātraṃ dvirātraṃ vā trirātram athavāparam upavāsī hariṃ yas tu bhaktyā dhyāyati mānavaḥ tannāmajāpī tatkarma- ratis tadgatamānasaḥ niṣkāmo daitya sa brahma param āpnoty asaṃśayam yaṃ ca kāmam abhidhyāyan keśavārpitamānasaḥ upoṣyati tam āpnoti prasanne garuḍadhvaje kathyate ca purā vipraḥ pulastyo brahmavādinā dālbhyena pṛṣṭo akathayad yathaitad arisūdana brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ strībhis tathā mune saṃsāragartapaṅkasthaiḥ sugatiḥ prāpyate katham anārādhya jagannāthaṃ sarvadhātāram acyutam nirvyalīkena cittena kaḥ prayāsyati sadgatim viṣayagrāhi vai yasya na cittaṃ keśavārpitam sa kathaṃ pāpapaṅkāṅkī naro yāsyati sadgatim yadi saṃsāraduḥkhārtaḥ sugatiṃ gantum icchasi tadārādhaya sarveśaṃ jagaddhātāram acyutam puṣpaiḥ sugandhair hṛdyaiś ca dhūpaiḥ sāgarucandanaiḥ vāsobhir bhūṣaṇair bhakṣyair upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ yadi saṃsāranirvedād abhivāñchasi sadgatim tadārādhaya govindaṃ yac ceṣṭaṃ tava cetasi puṣpāṇi yadi te na syuḥ śastaṃ pādapapallavaiḥ dūrvāṅkurair api brahmaṃs tadabhāve arcayācyutam sugandhipuṣpadīpādyair yaḥ kuryāt keśavālaye sarvatīrthaphalaṃ tasya saṃbhavet keśavārcayā sabāhyābhyantaraṃ yas tu mārjayed acyutālayam sabāhyābhyantaraṃ tasya kāyo niṣkalmaṣo bhavet puṣpapatrāmbubhir dhūpair yathāvibhavam acyutaḥ pūjitas tuṣṭim atulāṃ bhaktyāyāty ekacetasām yaḥ sadāyatane viṣṇoḥ kurute mārjanakriyām sa pāṃsubhūmer dehāc ca sarvapāpaṃ vyapohati yāvantyaḥ pāṃsukaṇikā mārjyante keśavālaye dināni divi tāvanti tiṣṭhaty astamalo naraḥ ahany ahani yat pāpaṃ kurute dvijasattama gocarmamātraṃ saṃmārjya hanti tat keśavālaye yaś copalepanaṃ kuryād viṣṇor āyatane naraḥ so api lokaṃ samāsādya modate ca śatakratoḥ mṛdā dhātuvikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā upalepanakṛd yāti vimānaṃ maṇicitritam udakābhyukṣaṇaṃ viṣṇor yaḥ karoti tathā gṛhe so api gacchati yatrāste bhagavān yādasāṃ patiḥ puṣpaprakaram atyarthaṃ sugandhaṃ keśavālaye upalipte naro dattvā na durgatim avāpnuyāt vimānam atividyoti sarvaratnamayaṃ divi samāpnoti naro dattvā dīpakaṃ keśavālaye yas tu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ tilapātraprado naraḥ dhvajaṃ tu viṣṇave dadyāt samam etat phalaṃ dvija vidhunvan hanti vātena dātur ajñānataḥ kṛtam pāpaṃ ketur gṛhe viṣṇor divārātram asaṃśayam gītavādyādibhir devaṃ ya upāste janārdanam gāndharvair gītanṛtyaiḥ sa vimānastho niṣevyate jātismaratvaṃ medhāṃ ca tathaivoparame smṛtim prāpnoti viṣṇvāyatane puṇyākhyānakathākaraḥ upoṣitaḥ pūjito vā dṛṣṭo vā namito api vā pradambha harate pāpaṃ ko na seved dhariṃ tataḥ vedavādakriyāyajña- snānatīrthaphalaṃ param aṣṭāṅgapraṇipātena praṇipatya hariṃ labhet pragamya hṛdā śirasā pādapadme mahītale niṣkalmaṣo bhavet sadyo na nāṭī pādapāṃsunā ekasya kṛṣṇasya krājataḥ praṇāmo daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthena tulyaḥ daśāśvamedhaiḥ punar eti janma kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya evaṃ deveśvaro bhaktyā yena viṣṇur upāsitaḥ sa prāpnoti gatiṃ ślāghyāṃ yāṃ yām icchati cetasā devatvaṃ manujaiḥ kaiścid gandharvatvaṃ tathāparaiḥ vidyādharatvam aparair ārādhyāptaṃ janārdanam śakraḥ kratuśateneśam ārādhya garuḍadhvajam devendratvaṃ gatas tasmān nānyaḥ pūjyatamaḥ kvacit devebhyo api hi pūjyas tu svagurur brahmacāriṇaḥ tasyāpi yajñapuruṣo viṣṇuḥ pūjyo dvijottama striyaś ca bhartāram ṛte pūjyam anyan na daivatam bhartur gṛhasthasya sataḥ pūjyo yajñapatir hariḥ vaikhānasānām ārādhyas tapobhir madhusūdanaḥ dhyeyaḥ parivrājakānāṃ vāsudevo mahātmanām evaṃ sarvāśramāṇāṃ hi vāsudevaḥ parāyaṇam sarveṣāṃ caiva varṇānāṃ tam ārādhyāpnuyād gatim śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ kāmyām upavāsāṃs tathāparān tat tam āśritya yān kāmān kurvītepsitam ātmanaḥ ekādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe phālgune māsi yo naraḥ japet kṛṣṇeti devasya nāma bhaktyā punaḥpunaḥ devārcane cāṣṭaśataṃ kṛtvaitat tu japec chuciḥ prātaḥ prasthānakāle ca utthāne skhalite kṣute pāṣaṇḍapatitāṃś caiva tathaivāntyāvasāyinaḥ nālapeta tathā kṛṣṇam arcayec chraddhayānvitaḥ idaṃ codāharet kṛṣṇe manaḥ saṃdhāya tatparaḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa kṛpālus tvam agatīnāṃ gatir bhava saṃsārāntarnimagnānāṃ prasīda madhusūdana evaṃ prasādyopāvāsaṃ kṛtvā niyatamānasaḥ pūrvāhna eva cānyedyur gavyaṃ saṃprāsya vai sakṛt snāto arcayitvā kṛṣṇeti punar nāma prakīrtayet vāridhārātrayaṃ caiva vikṣiped devapādayoḥ caitravaiśākhayoś caiva tadvaj jyeṣṭhe tu pūjayet martyaloke gatiṃ śreṣṭhāṃ dālbhya prāpnoti vai naraḥ utkrāntikāle kṛṣṇasya smaraṇaṃ ca tathāpnute āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe caiva māse bhādrapade tathā tathaivāśvayuje devam anena vidhinā naraḥ upoṣya saṃpūjya tathā keśaveti ca kīrtayet gomūtraprāśanāt pūrvaṃ svargalokagatiṃ vrajet ārādhitasya jagatām īśvarasyāvyāyātmanaḥ utkrāntikāle smaraṇaṃ keśavasya tathāpnuyāt kṣīrasya prāśanaṃ yas tu vidhiṃ cemaṃ yathoditam kārttikādi yathānyāyaṃ kuryān māsacatuṣṭayam tenaiva vidhinā brahman viṣṇor nāma prakīrtayet sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ viṣṇuṃ smarati ca kṣaye pratimāsaṃ dvijātibhyo dadyād dānaṃ yathecchayā cāturmāsye ca saṃpūrṇe puṇyaṃ śravaṇakīrtanam kathāṃ vā vāsudevasya tadgītīr vāpi kārayet evam etāṃ gatiṃ śreṣṭhāṃ devanāmānukīrtanāt kathitaṃ pāraṇaṃ yat te kārṣṇaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam ādhipatyaṃ tathā bhogāṃs tena prāpnoti mānuṣān dvitīyena tathā bhogān aindrān prāpnoti mānavaḥ viṣṇor lokaṃ tṛtīyena pāraṇena tathāpnuyāt evam etat samākhyātaṃ gatiprāpakam uttamam vidhānaṃ dvijaśārdūla kṛṣṇatuṣṭipradaṃ nṛṇām sugatidvādaśīm etāṃ śraddadhānas tu yo naraḥ upoṣya ca tathā nārī prāpnoti trividhāṃ gatim eṣā dhanyā pāpaharā tithir nityam upāsitā ārādhanāya śiṣṭaiṣā devadevasya cakriṇaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ ca śuklasya phālgunasyaiva sattama pāṣaṇḍapatitāṃś caiva tathaivāntyāvasāyinaḥ nāstikān bhinnavṛttīṃś ca pāpinaś cāpy anālapan nārāyaṇe gatamanāḥ puruṣo niyatendriyaḥ tiṣṭhan vrajan praskhalite kṣute vāpi janārdanam kīrtayet tatkriyākāle saptakṛtvaḥ prakīrtayet lakṣmyā samanvitaṃ devam arcayec ca janārdanam saṃdhyāvyuparame cendu- svarūpaṃ harim īśvaram rātriṃ ca lakṣmīṃ saṃcintya samyag arghyena pūjayet naktaṃ ca bhuñjīta naras tailakṣāravivarjitam tathaiva caitravaiśākha- jyeṣṭheṣu munisattama arcayīta yathāproktaṃ prāpte prāpte tu taddine niṣpāditaṃ bhaved ekam pāraṇaṃ dālbhya bhaktitaḥ dvitīyaṃ cāpi vakṣyāmi pāraṇaṃ dvijasattama āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe māsi prāpte bhādrapade tathā tathaivāśvayuje abhyarcya śrīdharaṃ ca śriyā saha samyak candramase dattvā bhuñjītārghyaṃ yathāvidhi dvitīyam etad ākhyātaṃ tṛtīyaṃ pāraṇaṃ śṛṇu kārttikādiṣu māseṣu tathaivābhyarcya keśavam bhūtyā samanvitaṃ dadyāc śaśāṅkāyārhanaṃ niśi bhuñjīta ca tathā proktaṃ tṛtīyam iti pāraṇam pratipūjāsu dadyāc ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca dakṣiṇām pratimāsaṃ ca vakṣyāmi prāśanaṃ kāyaśodhanam caturaḥ prathamān māsān pañcagavyam udāhṛtam kuśodakaṃ tathaivānyad uktaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam sūryāṃśutaptaṃ tadvac ca jalaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam gītavādyādikaṃ pāṭhyaṃ tathā kṛṣṇasya vā kathān kāriyīta ca devasya pāraṇe pāraṇe gate evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivat sapatnīkaṃ janārdanam nāpnotīṣtaviyogādīn pumān yoṣid athāpi vā janārdanaṃ salakṣmīkam arcayet prathamaṃ tataḥ saśrīkaṃ śrīdharaṃ bhaktyā tṛtīye bhūtikeśavau yāvanty etadvidhānena pāraṇenārcati prabhum tāvanti janmāny asukhaṃ nāpnotīṣṭaviyogajam devasya ca prasādena maraṇe prāpya tatsmṛtim kule satāṃ sphītadhane bhogabhuj jāyate naraḥ nāriṃ prāpnoti na vyādhiṃ narakaṃ ca na paśyati durgamaṃ yamamārgaṃ ca nekṣate dvijasattama śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ tāta yamamārgaṃ sudurgamam yathā sukhena saṃyānti mānavās tad vadasva me pratimāsaṃ tu nāmāni kṛṣṇasyaitāni dvādaśa kṛtopavāsaḥ susnātaḥ pūjayitvā janārdanam uccārayan naro abhyeti susukhenaiva tatpatham tato viprāya vai dadyād udakumbhaṃ sadakṣiṇaṃ upānadvastrayugmaṃ ca chattraṃ kanakam eva ca yad vai māsagataṃ nāma tatprītiś cāpi saṃvadet saṃvatsarānte apy athavā pratimāsaṃ dvijān budhaḥ vācayed udakumbhādyair dānaiḥ sarvān anukramāt keśavaṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu pauṣe nārāyaṇaṃ tathā mādhavaṃ māghamāse tu govindaṃ phālgune tathā viṣṇuṃ caitre atha vaiśākhe tathaiva madhusūdanam jyeṣṭhe trivikramaṃ devam āṣāḍhe vāmanaṃ tathā śrāvaṇe śrīdharaṃ caiva hṛṣīkeśeti cāparam nāma bhādrapade māsi gīyate puṇyakāṅkṣibhiḥ padmanābhaṃ cāśvayuje dāmodaram ataḥ param kārttike devadeveśaṃ stuvaṃs tarati durgatim iha vai svasthatāṃ prāpya maraṇe smaraṇaṃ tataḥ yāmyakleśam asaṃprāpya svargaloke mahīyate tato mānuṣyam āsādya nirātaṅko gatajvaraḥ dhanadhānyavati sphīte janma sādhukule arhati upavāsavratānīha keśavārādhanaṃ prati mamācakṣva mahābhāga paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me kāmān yān yān naro bhakto manasecchati keśavāt vratopavāsanāt prītas tāṃs tān viṣṇuḥ prayacchati ratnaparvatam āruhya yathā ratnaṃ mahāmune sattvānurūpam adatte tathā kṛtsnān manorathān mārgaśīrṣaṃ tu yo māsam ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet kurvan vai viṣṇuśuśrūṣāṃ sa deśe jāyate śubhe pauṣamāsaṃ tathā dālbhya ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet śuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ śaurer na rogī sa ca jāyate māghamāsaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ sa kule jāyate satām kṣapayed ekabhaktena śuśrūṣur yaś ca phālgunam saubhāgyaṃ svajanānāṃ sa sarveṣām eti sonnatim caitraṃ viṣṇuparo māsam ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyaṃ sa gārhasthyam avāpnuyāt yaḥ kṣaped ekabhaktena vaiśākhaṃ pūjayan harim naro vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ vrajet kṛṣṇārpitamanā jyeṣṭham ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet aiśvaryam atulaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pumān strī vābhijāyate āṣāḍham ekabhaktena yo nayed viṣṇutanmanāḥ bahudhānyo bahudhano bahuputraś ca jāyate kṣapayed ekabhaktena śrāvaṇaṃ viṣṇutatparaḥ dhanadhānyahiraṇyāḍhye kule sa jñātivardhanaḥ ekāhāro bhādrapadaṃ yaś ca kṛṣṇaparāyaṇaḥ dhanāḍhyaṃ sphītam acalam aiśvaryaṃ pratipadyate nayaṃś cāśvayujaṃ viṣṇuṃ pūjayed ekabhojanaḥ dhanavān vāhanāḍhyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate kārttike caikadā bhuṅkte yaś ca viṣṇuparo naraḥ śūraś ca kṛtavidyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate yas tu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇam ekabhakto bhaven naraḥ ahiṃsaḥ sarvabhūteṣu vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ namo astu vāsudevāyety ahaś cāṣṭaśataṃ japet atirātrasya yajñasya tataḥ phalam avāpnuyāt daśa varṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate tatkṣayād iha cāgatya māhātmyaṃ pratipadyate brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ strī śūdro vā yathoditān upavāsān imān kurvan phalāny etāny avāpnuyāt jagatpatiṃ jagadyoniṃ jaganniṣṭhaṃ jagadgurum jayaṃ śaraṇam abhyetya na janaiḥ śocyate janaḥ yasya nāmni smṛte martyaḥ samutkrānter anantaram prāpnoti śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ tataḥ pūjyataro hi saḥ nādir na madhyaṃ naivānto yasya devasya vidyate anāditvād amadhyatvād anantatvāc ca so avyayaḥ parāparaṃ sukṛtavatāṃ parāṃ gatiṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ prabhavan nidhānam avyayam sanātanaṃ yad amṛtam acyutaṃ dhruvaṃ praviśya taṃ harim amaratvam aśnute śṛṇu dālbhya paraṃ kāmyaṃ vrataṃ saṃtatidaṃ nṛṇām yam upoṣya na vicchedaḥ pitṛpiṇḍasya jāyate kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ caitramāse snāto niyatamānasaḥ kṛṣṇam abhyarcya pūjāṃ ca devakyāḥ kurute tu yaḥ nirāhāro japan nāma kṛṣṇasya jagataḥ pateḥ upaviṣṭo japasnāna- kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu pūjāyāṃ cāpi kṛṣṇasya sapta vārān prakīrtayet pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthān nālapec caiva nāstikān prabhāte tu punaḥ snāto dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām bhuñjīta kṛtapūjas tu kṛṣṇasyaiva jagatpateḥ vaiśākhajyeṣṭhayoś caiva pāraṇaṃ hi trimāsikam upoṣya devadeveśaṃ ghṛtena snāpayed dharim āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe caiva māse bhādrapade tathā upoṣite dvitīyaṃ vai pāraṇaṃ pūrvavat tu tat tathaivāśvayujaṃ cādiṃ kṛtvā māsatrayaṃ budhaḥ upoṣya snāpayed devaṃ haviṣā pāraṇe gate pauṣe māghe phālgune ca naras tadvad upoṣitaḥ caturthe pāraṇe pūrṇe ghṛtena snāpayed dharim evaṃ kṛtopavāsasya puruṣasya tathā striyaḥ na saṃtateḥ paricchedaḥ kadācid abhijāyate kṛṣṇāṣṭamīm imāṃ yas tu naro yoṣid athāpi vā upoṣyatīha sāhlādaṃ nṛloke prāpya nirvṛttim putrapautrasamṛddhiṃ ca mṛtaḥ svarge mahīyate ity etat kathitaṃ dālbhya mayā kṛṣṇāṣṭaṃīvratam prāvṛṭkāle tu niyamāñ śṛṇu kāmyān imān mama prāvṛṭkāle yadā śete vāsudevaḥ payonidhau bhogibhoge nijāṃ māyāṃ yoganidrāṃ ca mānayan viśiṣṭā na pravartante tadā yajñādikāḥ kriyāḥ devānāṃ sā bhaved rātrir dakṣiṇāyanasaṃjñitā yadā svapiti govindo yas tu māsaṃ catuṣṭayam adhaḥśāyī brahmacārī keśavārpitamānasaḥ namo namo astu kṛṣṇāya keśavāya namo namaḥ namo astu narasiṃhāya viṣṇave ca namo namaḥ iti prātas tathā sāyaṃ japed devakriyāparaḥ śamayaty atiduṣpāraṃ duritaṃ janmasaṃcitam madhu māṃsaṃ ca yo māsāñ caturas tān nirasyati devakriyāratir viṣṇor anusmaraṇatatparaḥ so api svargaṃ samabhyeti cyutas tasmāt tu jāyate arogī dhanadhānyāḍhyaḥ kulasaṃtatimān naraḥ samastamandirāṇāṃ ca yaḥ supte madhusūdane nirvṛttiṃ kurute so api devo vaimāniko bhavet anenaiva vidhānena naro viṣṇukriyāparaḥ ekāhāro bhaved yas tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate supte ca sarvalokeśe naktabhojī bhavet tu yaḥ sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke amaro bhavet śastaṃ tv anantaraṃ puṃsāṃ tataś caivekabhojanam naktabhojanatulyaṃ tu nopavāsaphalaṃ kvacit tailābhaṅgaṃ ca yo māsāṃś caturas tān nirasyati so apy aṅgalāvaṇyaguṇam ārogyaṃ ca naro labhet yas tv etāni samastāni māsān etān naraś caret sa viṣṇulokam āsādya viṣṇor anucaro bhavet caturbhiḥ pāraṇaṃ māsair niṣpādyaṃ haritatparaiḥ brāhmaṇān bhojayed dadyāt tatas tebhyaś ca dakṣiṇām pūjayec ca jagannāthaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim prīyasva deva govindety evaṃ caiva prasādayet iti dālbhya samākhyātaṃ cāturmāsye hi yad vratam devadevasya suptasya dvādaśīṃ śṛṇu cāparām yasyām anantasmaraṇād anantaphalabhāg bhavet māsi proṣṭhapade śukle dvādaśyāṃ jalaśāyinam praṇamyānantam abhyarcya puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ śuciḥ pāṣaṇḍādibhir ālāpam akurvan niyatātmavān viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā naktaṃ bhuṅkte tu yo naraḥ tiṣṭhan vrajan svapaṃś caiva kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu anantanāmasmaraṇaṃ kurvann uccāraṇaṃ tathā anenaiva vidhānena māsān dvādaśa vai kramāt upoṣya pāraṇe pūrṇe samabhyarcya jagadgurum gītavādyena hṛdyena prīṇayan vyuṣṭim aśnute anantaṃ gītavādyena yataḥ phalam udāhṛtam tenānantaṃ samabhyarcya tad eva labhate phalam evaṃ yaḥ puruṣaḥ kuryād anantārādhanaṃ śuciḥ nārī vā svargam abhyetya so aanantaphalam aśnute evaṃ dālbhya hṛṣīkeśo narair bhaktyā yathāvidhi phalaṃ dadāty asulabhaṃ salilenāpi pūjitaḥ na viṣṇur vittadānena puṣpair vā na phalais tathā ārādhyate suśuddhena hṛdayenaiva kevalam rāgādyapetaṃ hṛdayaṃ vāg duṣṭā nānṛtādinā hiṃsādirahitaḥ kāyaḥ keśavārādhanatrayam rāgādidūṣite citte nāspadī madhusūdanaḥ karoti na ratiṃ haṃsaḥ kadācit kardamāmbhasi na yogyā keśavastutyai vāg duṣṭā cānṛtādinā tamaso nāśanāyālaṃ nendor lekhā ghanāvṛtā hiṃsādidūṣitaḥ kāyaḥ keśavārādhane kutaḥ janacittaprasādāya na nabhas timirāvṛtam tasmāc chraddhasva bhāvena satyabhāvena ca dvija ahiṃsakena govindo nisargād eva toṣitaḥ sarvasvam api kṛṣṇāya yo dadyāt kuṭilāśayaḥ sa naivārādhayaty enaṃ sadbhāvenārcayācyutam rāgādyapetaṃ hṛdayaṃ kuru tvaṃ keśavārpitam tataḥ prāpsyasi duḥprāpyam ayatnenaiva keśavam bhagavan kathitaḥ samyak kāmyo ayaṃ keśavaṃ prati ārādhanavidhiḥ sarvo bhūyaḥ pṛcchāmi tad vada kule janma tathārogyaṃ dhanarddhiś ceha durlabhā tritayaṃ prāpyate yena tan me vada mahāmune mātāmahaṃ kāṇvam udāravīryaṃ maharṣim abhyarcya kulaprasūtim papraccha puṃsām atha yoṣitāṃ ca duṣvantaputro bharataḥ praṇamya yathāvad ācaṣṭa tato mahātmā sa rājavaryāya yathā kuleṣu prayānti sūtiṃ puruṣāḥ striyaś ca yathā ca samyak sukhino bhavanti pauṣe site dvādaśame ahni sārke tathārkṣayoge jagataḥ prasūtim saṃpūjya viṣṇuṃ vidhinopavāsī sraggandhadhūpānnavaropahāraiḥ gṛhṇīta māsaṃ pratimāsapūjām dānādiyuktaṃ vratam abdam ekam dadyāc ca dānaṃ dvijapuṅgavebhyas tad ucyamānaṃ vinibodha bhūpa ghṛtaṃ tilān vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ yavānnam ambhaḥkarakānnapānam chattraṃ payo annaṃ guḍaphāṇitāḍhyaṃ srakcandanaṃ vastram anukrameṇa māse ca māse vidhinoditena tasyāṃ tithau lokaguruṃ prapūjya aśnīta yāny ātmaviśuddhihetoḥ saṃprāśanānīha nibodha tāni gomūtram ambho ghṛtam āmaśākaṃ dūrvā dadhi vrīhiyavāṃs tilāṃś ca sūryāṃśutaptaṃ jalam ambu dārbhaṃ kṣīraṃ ca māsakramaśopayuñjyāt kule pradhāne dhanadhānyapūrṇe vivekavaty astasamastaduḥkhe prāpnoti janmāvikalendriyaś ca bhavaty arogo matimān sukhī ca tasmāt tvam apy etad amoghavid yo nārāyaṇārādhanam apramattaḥ kuruṣva viṣṇuṃ bhagavantam īśam ārādhya kāmān akhilān upaiti yadā ca śukladvādaśyāṃ nakṣatraṃ śravaṇaṃ bhavet tadā sā tu mahāpuṇyā dvādaśī vijayā smṛtā tasyāṃ snātaḥ sarvatīrthaiḥ snāto bhavati mānavaḥ saṃpūjya varṣapūjāyāḥ sakalaṃ phalam aśnute ekaṃ japtvā sahasrasya japtasyāpnoti yat phalam dānaṃ sahasraguṇitaṃ tathā vai vipra bhojanam yat kṣemam api vai tasyāṃ sahasraṃ śrāvaṇe tu tat anyasyām eva tithyāṃ śubhāyāṃ śrāvaṇaṃ yadā homas tathopavāsaś ca sahasrākhyaphalapradaḥ rohiṇyāś ca yadā kṛṣṇa- pakṣe aṣṭamyāṃ dvijottama jayantī nāma sā proktā sarvapāpaharā tithiḥ yad bālye yac ca kaumāre yauvane vārddhike ca yat saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu tat kṣālayati govindaṃ tasyām abhyarcya bhaktitaḥ homajapyādidānānāṃ phalaṃ ca śatasaṃmitam saṃprāpnoti na saṃdeho yac cānyan manasecchati upavāsaś ca tatrokto mahāpātakanāśanaḥ ekadaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe yadā rkṣaṃ vai punarvasuḥ nāmnā sātijayākhyātā tithīnām uttamā tithiḥ yo dadāti tilaprasthaṃ tṛṣkālaṃ vatsaraṃ naraḥ upavāsaṃ ca tasyāṃ yaḥ karoty etat samaṃ smṛtam tasyāṃ jagatpatir devaḥ sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ pratyakṣatāṃ prayāty alpaṃ tadānantaphalaṃ smṛtam sagareṇa kakutsthena duṃdhumāreṇa gādhinā tasyām ārādhitaḥ kṛṣṇo dattavān nikhilāṃ bhuvam ayane cottare prāpte yaḥ snāpayati keśavam ghṛtaprasthena pāpaṃ saḥ sakalaṃ vai vyapohati kapilāṃ vipramukhyāya dadāty anudinaṃ hi yaḥ ghṛtasnānaṃ ca devasya tasmin kāle samaṃ hi tat snāpyamānaṃ ca paśyati ye ghṛtenottarāyaṇe te yānti viṣṇusālokyaṃ sarvapāpavivarjitāḥ maitreyī brāhmaṇī pūrvaṃ yājñavalkyam apṛcchata praṇipatya mahābhāgaṃ yogeśvaram akalmaṣam pāpapraśamanāyālaṃ yat puṇyasyopavṛṃhakam manorathapradaṃ yac ca tad vrataṃ kathyatāṃ mama kāni dānāni śastāni snānāni ca yatavrata praśastās tithayaḥ kāś ca prāśanāni ca śaṃsa me sarvadānāni śastāni yāny uddiśya janārdanam dīyante vipramukhyebhyaḥ śraddhāpūtena cetasā tā eva tithayaḥ śastā yāsv abhyarcya janārdanam kriyante śradhayā samyag upavāsavratāḥ sadā prāpyate vividhair yajñair yat phalaṃ sādhvasādhubhiḥ upavāsais tad āpnoti samabhyarcya janārdanam manorathānāṃ saṃprāpti- kārakaṃ pāpanāśanam śrūyatāṃ mama dharmajñe vratānām uttamaṃ vratam yat kṛtvā na jaḍo nāndho badhiro na ca duḥkhitaḥ na caiveṣṭaviyogārtiṃ kaścit prāpnoti mānavaḥ na cāpriyo asya lokasya na daridro na durgatiḥ sapta janmāni bhavati sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate viṣṇuvratam idaṃ khyātaṃ bhāṣitaṃ viṣṇunā svayam pauṣaśukladvitīyādi kṛtvā dinacatuṣṭayam ṣaṇmāsapāraṇaprāyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt paramaṃ vratam pūrvaṃ siddhārthakaiḥ snānaṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ smṛtam vacayā ca tṛtīye ahni sarvauṣadhyā tataḥ param nāmnā kṛṣṇācyutākhyena tathānantena pūjayet tathaiva ca caturthe ahni hṛṣīkeśena keśavam devam abhyarcya puṣpaiś ca pattrair dhūpānulepanaiḥ udgacchataś ca bālendor dadyād arghyaṃ samāhitaḥ puṣpaiḥ pattraiḥ phalaiś caiva sarvadhānyaiś ca bhaktitaḥ dinakrameṇa caitāni candranāmāni kīrtayet śaśicandraśaśāṅkendu- saṃjñāni brahmavādini naktaṃ bhuñjīta matimān yāvat tiṣṭhati candramāḥ astaṃgate na bhuñjīta vratabhaṅgabhayāc chubhe evaṃ sarveṣu māseṣu jyeṣṭhānteṣu yaśasvini kartavyaṃ vai vrataśreṣṭhaṃ dvitīyādicaturdinam viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt pañcamyāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ evaṃ samāpayen māsaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ prathamapāraṇam pāraṇante ca devasya prīṇanaṃ bhaktitaḥ śubhe yathāśaktyā tu kartavyaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ vivarjayet āṣāḍhādidvitīyaṃ tu ṣaṇmāsena tapodhane pāraṇaṃ vai samākhyātaṃ vratasyāsya śubhapradam vratam etad dilīpena duṣvantena yayātinā tathānyaiḥ pṛthivīpālair upavāsavidhānataḥ caritaṃ munimukhyaiś ca ṛcīkacyavanādibhiḥ surambhayā sukaikeyyā śāṇḍilyā dhūmrapiṅgayā sudeṣṇayāthavā riṇyā matimatyā kṛtāśayā sāvitryā paurṇamāsyā ca vairiṇyā ca subhadrayā brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśām iti strībhir anuṣṭhitam urvaśyā rambhayā caiva saurabheyyā tathā vratam varāpsarobhir dharmajñe caritaṃ dharmavāṃchayā prathame pādapūjā syād dvitīye nābhipūjanam tṛtīye vakṣasaḥ pūjā caturthe śiraso hareḥ etac cīrtvā samastebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ mucyate sakalāṃś caiva saṃprāpnoti manorathān vratānām uttamaṃ hy etat svayaṃ devena bhāṣitam pāpapraśamanaṃ śastaṃ manorathaphalapradam yaṃ ca kāmam abhidhyāyan kriyate niyatavrataiḥ vratam etan mahābhāge taṃ tu pūrayate nṛṇām manorathān pūrayati sarvapāpaṃ vyapohati avyāhatendriyatvaṃ ca sapta janmāni yacchati māghe snātasya yat puṇyaṃ prayāge pāpanāśanam sakalaṃ tad avāpnoti śrutvā viṣṇuvrataṃ tv idam sākṣād bhagavatā proktaṃ paramaṃ pāpanāśanam śuklapakṣe tu pauṣasya saṃprāptidvādaśīṃ śṛṇu yām upoṣya samāpnoti sarvān eva manorathān pāṣaṇḍādibhir ālāpam akurvan viṣṇutatparaḥ pūjayet praṇato devam ekāgramatir acyutam pauṣādipāraṇaṃ māsaiḥ ṣaḍbhir jyeṣṭhāntakaṃ smṛtam prathame puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ nāma devasya gīyate dvitīye mādhavākhyaṃ tu viśvarūpaṃ tu phālgune puruṣottamākhyaṃ ca tataḥ pañcame cācyuteti ca ṣaṣṭhe jayeti devasya guhyaṃ nāma prakīrtyate pūrveṣu ṣaṭsu māseṣu snānaprāśanayos tilāḥ āṣāḍhādiṣu māseṣu pañcagavyam udāhṛtam snāne ca prāśane caiva praśastaṃ pāpanāśanam pratimāsaṃ ca devasya kṛtvā pūjāṃ yathāvidhi viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāc śraddadhānaḥ svaśaktitaḥ pāraṇānte ca devasya prīṇanaṃ bhaktipūrvakam kruvīta śaktyā govinde sadbhāvābhyarcano yataḥ naktaṃ bhuñjīta ca tatas tailakṣāravivarjitaṃ ekādaśyām uṣitvaivaṃ dvādaśyām athavā dine etām uṣitvā dharmajñe prīṇanaṃ devatatparaḥ sarvakāmān avāpnoti sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate yataḥ sarvam avāpnoti yad yad icchati cetasā tato lokeṣu vikhyātā saṃprāptidvādaśīti vai kṛtābhilaṣitā hy eṣā prārabdhā dharmatatparaiḥ pūrayaty akhilān kāmān saṃśrutā ca dine dine tasminn eva dine puṇye govindadvādaśīṃ śṛṇu yasyāṃ samyag anuṣṭhānāt prāpnoty abhimataṃ phalam pauṣamāse site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ samupoṣitaḥ saṃyak saṃpūjya govindaṃ nāmnā devam adhokṣajam puṣpadhūpopahārādyair upavāsaiḥ samāhitaḥ govindeti japan nāma punas tadgatamānasaḥ viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād yathāśakti tapodhane svapan vibuddhaḥ skhalito govindeti ca kīrtayet pāṣaṇḍādivikarmasthair ālāpaṃ ca vivarjayet gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ vāpi dadhi kṣīram athāpi vā godehataḥ samutpannaṃ saṃprāśnītātmaśuddhaye dvitīye ahni punaḥ snātas tathaivābhyarcya taṃ prabhum tenaiva nāmnā saṃstūya dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām tato bhuñjīta godeha- saṃbhūtena samanvitam evam evākhilān māsān upoṣya prayataḥ śuciḥ dadyād gavāhnikaṃ bhaktyā pratimāsaṃ svaśaktitaḥ pārite ca punar varṣe yathāśakti gavāhnikam dattvā paragave bhūyaḥ śṛṇu yat phalam aśnute suvarṇaśṛṅgāḥ pañca gāḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca vṛṣabhaṃ naraḥ pratimāsaṃ dvijāgrebhyo yad dattvā phalam aśnute tad āpnoty akhilaṃ samyag vratam etad upoṣitaḥ taṃ ca lokam avāpnoti govindo yatra tiṣṭhati govindadvādaśīm etām upoṣya divi tārakāḥ vidyotamānā dṛśyante lokair adyāpi śobhane upavāsavratānāṃ tu vaikalyaṃ yan mahāmune dānakarmakṛtaṃ tasya vipāko vada yādṛśaḥ yajñānām upavāsānāṃ vratānāṃ ca yatavrate vaikalyāt phalavaikalyaṃ yādṛśaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva me upavāsādinā rājyaṃ saṃprāpyaṃ te tathā vasu bhraṣṭaiśvaryā nirdhanāś ca bhavanti puruṣāḥ punaḥ rūpaṃ tathottamaṃ prāpya vratavaikalyadoṣataḥ kāṇāḥ kuṇṭhāś ca bhūyas te bhavanty andhāś ca mānavāḥ upavāsān naraḥ patnīṃ nārī prāpya tathā patim viyogaṃ vratavaikalyād ubhayaṃ tad avāpnute ye dravye saty adātāras tathānyenāhitāgnayaḥ kule ca sati duḥśīlā dauṣkulāḥ śīlinaś ca ye vastrānulepanair hīnā bhūṣaṇaiś cātirūpiṇaḥ virūparūpāś ca tathā prasādhanaguṇānvitāḥ te sarve vratavaikalyāt phalavaikalyam āgatāḥ guṇino api hi doṣeṇa saṃyuktāḥ saṃbhavanti te tasmān na vratavaikalyaṃ yajñavaikalyam eva vā upavāse ca kartavyaṃ vaikalyād vikalaṃ phalam kathaṃcid yadi vaikalyam upavāsādike bhavet kiṃ tatra vada kartavyam acchidraṃ yena jāyate akhaṇḍadvādaśīm etām aśeṣeṣv eva karmasu vaikalyapraśamāyālaṃ śṛṇuṣva gadato mama mārgaśīrṣe site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ niyataḥ śuciḥ kṛtopavāso deveśaṃ samabhyarcya janārdanam pañcagavyajalasnātaḥ pañcagavyakṛtāśanaḥ yavavrīhibhṛtaṃ pātraṃ dadyād viprāya bhaktitaḥ idaṃ coccārayed bhaktyā devasya purato hareḥ sapta janmāni yat kiṃcid mayā khaṇḍavrataṃ kṛtam bhagavaṃs tvatprasādena tad akhaṇḍam ihāstu me yathākhaṇḍaṃ jagat sarvam tvam eva puruṣottama tathākhilāny akhaṇḍāni vratāni mama santu vai evam evānumāsaṃ vai cāturmāsyavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ caturbhir eva māsais tu pāraṇaṃ prathamaṃ smṛtam prīṇanaṃ ca hareḥ kuryāt pārite pāraṇe tataḥ caitrādiṣu ca māseṣu caturṣv anyaṃ tu pāraṇam tatrāpi saktupātrāṇi dadyāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ śrāvaṇādiṣu māseṣu kārttikānteṣu pāraṇam yatnāt tu ghṛtapātrāṇi dadyād viprāya bhaktitaḥ evaṃ samyag yathānyāyam akhaṇḍadvādaśīṃ naraḥ yad upoṣyaty akhaṇḍaṃ sa vratasya phalam aśnute sapta janmasu vaikalyam yad vratasya kvacit kṛtam karoty avikalaṃ sarvam akhaṇḍadvādaśīvratam tasmād eṣātiyatnena naraiḥ strībhiś ca suvrate akhaṇḍadvādaśī samyag upoṣyā phalakāṃkṣibhiḥ evaṃ purā yājñavalkyaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ patnyā mahāmuniḥ ācaṣṭa puṇyaphaladam upavāsavidhiṃ param tathā tvam api viprarṣe keśavārādhane rataḥ vratopavāsaparamo bhavethā nānyamānasaḥ punaś caitan mahābhāga śrūyatāṃ gadato mama proktaṃ nareṇa devānāṃ tithimāhātmyam uttamam vijayātijayā caiva jayantī pāpanāśanī tathottarāyaṇaṃ śastaṃ sarvadā keśavārcane yad anyakāle varṣeṇa keśavāl labhyate phalam sakṛd evārcite kṛṣṇe tad etāsv api labhyate vijayātijayā caiva jayantī pāpanāśanī tathottarāyaṇaṃ caiva yac chastaṃ keśavārcane tat sarvaṃ kathayehādya tithimāhātmyam uttamam yatra saṃpūjitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarvapāpaṃ vyapohati ekādaśyāṃ site pakṣe puṣyarkṣaṃ yatra sattama tithau bhavati sā proktā viṣṇunā pāpanāśanī tasyāṃ saṃpūjya govindaṃ jagatām īśvareśvaram saptajanmakṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ yaś copavāsaṃ kurute tasyāṃ snāto dvijottama sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate dānaṃ yad dīyate kiṃcit samuddiśya janārdanam homo vā kriyate tasyām akṣayaṃ labhate phalam ekā ṛg devapurato japtā śraddhāvatā tathā ṛgvedasya samastasya japatā yacchate phalam sāmavedaphalaṃ sāma yajurvedaphalaṃ yajuḥ japtam ekaṃ muniśreṣṭha dadāty atra na saṃśayaḥ tārakā divi rājante dyotamānā dvijottama samabhyarcya tithāv asyāṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam yataḥ pāpam aśeṣaṃ vai nāśayaty atra keśavaḥ puṣyarkṣaikādaśī brahmaṃs tenoktā pāpanāśanī tathānyad api dharmajña śrūyatāṃ gadato mama padadvayaṃ jagaddhātur devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ pādapīṭhaṃ tatra nyastaṃ padadvayam vāsudevena viprendra bhūtānāṃ hitakāmyayā vāmam asya padaṃ brahman uttarāyaṇasaṃjñitam devādyaiḥ sakalair vandyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇāyanam tasmin yaḥ prayataḥ samyag devadevasya mānavaḥ karoty ārādhanaṃ tasya toṣam āyāti keśavaḥ katham ārādhanaṃ tasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ kriyate muniśārdūla tan mamākhyātum arhasi uttare tv ayane dālbhya snāto niyatamānasaḥ ghṛtakṣīrādinā devaṃ snāpayed dharaṇīdharam cāruvastropahāraiś ca puṣpadhūpānulepanaiḥ samabhyarcya tataḥ samyag brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ padadvayavrataṃ samyag gṛhṇīyād viṣṇutatparaḥ snāto nārāyaṇaṃ vakṣye bhuñjan nārāyaṇaṃ tathā bhuṅktvā nārāyaṇaṃ cāhaṃ gacchan nārāyaṇaṃ tataḥ svapan vibuddhaḥ praṇaman homaṃ kurvaṃs tathārcanam nārāyaṇasyānudinaṃ kariṣye nāmakīrtanam yāvad adyadināt prāptaṃ kramaśo dakṣiṇāyanam skhalite ahaṃ kṣute caiva vedanārto athavā sadā tāvan nārāyaṇaṃ vakṣye sarvam evottarāyaṇam yāvaj jīvavadhaṃ kiṃcid jñānato ajñānato api vā kariṣye ahaṃ tathā caiva kīrtayiṣyāmi taṃ prabhum yadā tadānṛtaṃ kiṃcid atha vakṣyāmi durvacaḥ ajñānād athavā jñānāt kīrtayiṣyāmi taṃ prabhum ṣaṇmāsam eṣa me jāpo nārāyaṇamayaḥ paraḥ taṃ smaran maraṇe yāti yāṃ gatiṃ sāstu me gatiḥ ṣaṇmāsābhyantare mṛtyur yady akasmād bhaven mama tan mayā vāsudevāya svayam ātmā niveditaḥ paramārthamayaṃ brahma vāsudevamayaṃ param yam ante saṃsmaran yāti sa me viṣṇuḥ parā gatiḥ yadā prātas tadā sāyaṃ madhyāhne vā mriye hy aham ṣaṇmāsābhyantare nyāsaḥ kṛto vratamayo mayā tathā kuru jagannātha sarvalokaparāyaṇa nārāyaṇa yathā nānyaṃ tvatto yāmi mṛte gatim evam uccārya ṣaṇmāsa- pāraṇaṃ pravaraṃ vratam tāvan niṣpādayed yāvat saṃprāptaṃ dakṣiṇāyanam tataś ca prīṇanaṃ kuryād yathāśaktyā jagadguroḥ bhojayed brāhmaṇān samyag dadyāt tebhyaś ca dakṣiṇām evaṃ vratam idaṃ dālbhya yaḥ pārayati mānavaḥ nārī vā sarvapāpebhyaḥ ṣaṇmāsād vipra mucyate ṣaṇmāsābhyantare cāsya maraṇaṃ yadi jāyate prāpnoty anaśanasyoktaṃ yat phalaṃ tad asaṃśayam padadvayaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya samyak tena tathārcitam harer nāma japan bhaktyā sa purā na janeśvara bhagavān ujjagau viṣṇuḥ purā gārgyāya pṛcchate phālgunāmalapakṣasya ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ naro vā yadi vā nārī samabhyarcya jagadgurum harer nāma japed bhaktyā sapta vārān nareśvara uttiṣṭhan prasvapaṃś caiva harim evānukīrtayet tato anyadivase prāpte dvādaśyāṃ prayato harim snātvā samyak tam abhyarcya dadyād viprāya dakṣiṇām harim uddiśya caivāgnau ghṛtahomakṛtakriyaḥ praṇipatya jagannātham iti vāṇīm udīrayet pātālasaṃsthā vasudhā yaṃ prasādya manorathān avāpa vāsudevo asau pradadātu manorathān yam abhyarcyāditiḥ prāptā sakalāṃś ca manorathān putrāṃś caivepsitān devaḥ pradadātu manorathān bhraṣṭarājyaś ca devendro yam abhyarcya jagatpatim manorathān avāpāgryān sa dadātu manorathān evam abhyarcya pūjāṃ ca niṣpādya haraye tataḥ bhuñjīta prayataḥ samyag haviṣyaṃ manujarṣabha phālgunaṃ caitravaiśākhau jyeṣṭhamāsaṃ ca pārthiva caturbhiḥ pāraṇaṃ māsair ebhir niṣpāditaṃ bhavet raktapuṣpais tu caturo māsān kurvīta cārcanam dahec ca guggulaṃ prāśya gośṛṅgakṣālanaṃ jalam haviṣyānnaṃ ca naivedyam ātmanaś caiva bhojanam tataś ca śrūyatām anyad āṣāḍhādau tu yā kriyā jātīpuṣpāṇi dhūpaś ca śastaḥ sarjaraso nṛpa prāśya darbhodakaṃ cātra śālyannaṃ ca nivedanam svayaṃ tad eva cāśnīyāc śeṣaṃ pūrvavad ācaret kārttikādiṣu māseṣu gomūtraṃ kāyaśodhanam sugandhaṃ cecchayā dhūpaṃ pūjābhṛṅgārakeṇa ca kāsāraṃ cātra naivedyam aśnīyāt tac ca vai svayam pratimāsaṃ ca viprāya dātavyā dakṣiṇā tathā prīṇanaṃ cecchayā viṣṇoḥ pāraṇe pāraṇe gate yathāśakti yathāprīti vittaśāṭhyaṃ vivarjayet sadbhāvenaiva govindaḥ pūjitaḥ prīyate yataḥ pāraṇānte yathāśaktyā snāpitaḥ pūjito hariḥ prīṇitaś cepsitān kāmān dadāty avyāhatān nṛpa eṣā dhanyā pāpaharā dvādaśī phalam icchatām yathābhilaṣitān kāmān dadāti manujeśvara pūrayaty akhilān bhaktyā yataś caiṣā manorathān manorathadvādaśīyaṃ tato lokeṣu viśrutā upoṣyaitāṃ tribhuvanaṃ prāptam indreṇa vai purā adityā cepsitāḥ putrā dhanaṃ cośanasā nṛpa dhaumyena cāpy adhyayanam anyaiś cābhimataṃ phalam rājarṣibhis tathā vipraiḥ strībhiḥ śūdraiś ca bhūpate yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyed vratam etad upoṣitaḥ taṃ tam āpnoty asaṃdigdhaṃ viṣṇor ārādhanodyataḥ aputro labhate putram adhano labhate dhanam rogābhibhūtaś cārogyaṃ kanyā prāpnoti satpatim samāgamaṃ pravasitair upoṣyaitām avāpnute sarvān kāmān avāpnoti mṛtaḥ svarge ca modate nāputro nādhano neṣṭa- viyogī na ca nirguṇaḥ upoṣyaitad vrataṃ martyaḥ strī jano vāpi jāyate ya eva vratasaṃcīrṇo viṣṇuloke mahīyate svargaloke sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ manujādhipa bhogān abhimatān bhuktvā svargaloke abhikāṅkṣitān iha puṇyavatāṃ nṝṇāṃ dhanināṃ sādhuśīlinām gṛheṣu jāyate rājan sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ aśokapūrṇimāṃ cānyāṃ śṛṇuśva vadato mama yām upoṣya naraḥ śokaṃ nāpnoti strī tathāpi vā phālgunāmalapakṣasya pūrṇimāsyāṃ nareśvara mṛjjalena naraḥ snātvā dattvā śirasi vai mṛdam mṛtprāśanaṃ tathā kṛtvā kṛtvā ca sthaṇḍilaṃ mṛdā puṣpaiḥ patrais tathābhyarcya bhūdharaṃ nānyamānasaḥ dharaṇīṃ ca tathā devīm aśokety abhidhīyate yathā viśokāṃ dharaṇīṃ kṛtavāṃs tvaṃ janārdanaḥ tathā māṃ sarvapāpebhyo mocayāśeṣadhāriṇi yathā samastabhūtānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ tvayy avasthitam tathā viśokaṃ kuru māṃ sakalecchāvibhūtibhiḥ dhyātamātre yathā viṣṇau svāsthyaṃ yātāsi medini tathā manaḥ svasthatāṃ me kuru tvaṃ bhūtadhāriṇi evaṃ stutvā tathābhyarcya candrāyārghyaṃ nivedya ca upoṣitavyaṃ naktaṃ vā bhoktavyaṃ tailavarjitam anenaiva prakāreṇa catvāraḥ phālgunādayaḥ upoṣyā nṛpate māsāḥ prathamaṃ tat tu pāraṇam āṣāḍhādiṣu māseṣu tadvat snānaṃ mṛdambunā tad eva prāśanaṃ pūjā tathaivendos tathārhaṇam caturṣv anyeṣu caivoktaṃ tathā vai kārttikādiṣu pāraṇaṃ tritayaṃ caiva cāturmāsikam ucyate prathamaṃ dharaṇī nāma stutyai māsacatuṣṭayam dvitīye medinī vācyā tṛtīye ca vasuṃdharā pāraṇe pāraṇe vastra- pūjayā pūjayen nṛpa dharaṇīṃ devadevaṃ ca ghṛtasnānena keśavam vastrābhāve tu sūtreṇa pūjayed dharaṇīṃ tathā ghṛtābhāve tathā kṣīraṃ śastaṃ vā salilaṃ hareḥ pātālamūlagatayā cīrṇam etan mahāvratam dharaṇyā keśavaprītyai tataḥ prāptā samunnatiḥ devena coktā dharaṇī varāhavapuṣā tadā upavāsaprasannena samuddhṛtya rasātalāt vratenānena kalyāṇi praṇato yaḥ kariṣyati tasya prasādam apy aham karomi tava medini tathaiva kurute pūjāṃ bhaktyā mama śubho janaḥ tathaiva tava kalyāṇi praṇato yaḥ kariṣyati vratam etad upāśritya pāraṇaṃ ca yathāvidhi sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sapta janmāntarāṇy asau viśokaḥ sarvakalyāṇa- bhājano matimāñ janaḥ sarvatra pūjyaḥ satataṃ sarveṣām aparājitaḥ yathāham evaṃ vasudhe bhavitā nirvṛteḥ padam tathā tvam api kalyāṇi bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ evam etan mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpopaśāntidam viśokākhyaṃ vrataṃ dhanyaṃ tat kuruṣva mahīpate strīṇāṃ dharmaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha upavāsaṃ bhavan mama kathayeha yathātattvam upavāsavidhiś ca yaḥ kaumārake gṛhasthāyā vidhavāyāś ca sattama dharmaṃ prabrūhy aśeṣeṇa bhagavan prītikārakam śrūyatām akhilaṃ brahman yady etad anupṛcchasi upakārāya ca strīṇāṃ triṣu lokeṣv anuttamam praśnam etat purā devī śailarājasutā patim papraccha śaṅkaraṃ brahman kailāsaśikhare sthitam kumārikābhir deveśa gṛhasthābhiś ca keśavaḥ vidhavābhis tathā strībhiḥ katham ārādhyate vada sādhu sādhvi tvayā pṛṣṭam etan nārāyaṇāśritam upavāsādi yat tattvaṃ śrūyatām asya yo vidhiḥ yogyaṃ patiṃ samāsādya nārī dharmam avāpnute duḥśīle api hi kāmārte nārī prāpnoti bhartari anārādhya jagannāthaṃ sarvalokeśvaraṃ harim katham āpnoti vai nārī patiṃ śīlaguṇānvitam sukalatrapradaṃ tasmād vratam acyutatuṣṭidam kartavyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tasya śrūyatāṃ varavarṇini yac cīrtvā sarvanārīṇāṃ śreṣṭham āpnoty asaṃśayam aihikaṃ ca sukhaṃ prāpya svarge bhuṅkte sukhāny api anujñāṃ prāpya pitṛto mātṛtaś ca kumārikā pūjayec ca jagannāthaṃ bhaktyā pāpaharaṃ harim triṣūttareṣu svṛkṣeṣu patikāmā kumārikā mādhavākhyaṃ tu vai nāma japen nityam atandritā priyaṅguṇā raktapuṣpair bandhūkakusumais tathā samabhyarcya tato dadyād raktam evānulepanam sarvauṣadhyā svayaṃ snātvā samabhyarcya jagatpatim namo astu mādhavāyeti homayen madhusarpiṣī sa devam uttarāyoge samabhyarcya janārdanam śobhanaṃ patim āpnoti pretya svargaṃ ca gacchati atibālye ca yat kiṃcit tayā pāpam anuṣṭhitam tasmāc ca mucyate devi sukhinī caiva jāyate abdenaikena tanvaṅgi dhūtapāpā yad icchati tad eva prāpnuyād bhadre nārāyaṇaparāyaṇā ṣaṇmāsaṃ prīṇanaṃ kāryaṃ bhaktyā śaktyā ca vai hareḥ pāraṇānte mahābhage tathā brāhmaṇatarpaṇam gārhasthye avasthitā nārī bhaktyā saṃpūjayet patim sa eva devatā tasyāḥ pūjyaḥ pūjyataraś ca saḥ tasmiṃs tuṣṭe paro dharmas tasyaiva paricaryayā toṣam āyāti sarvātmā paramātmā janārdanaḥ naiva tasyāḥ pṛthag yajño na śrāddhaṃ nāpy upoṣitam bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇenaiva prāpnoti strī yathepsitam tenaiva sāpy anujñātā tasya śuśrūṣaṇād anu toṣayej jagatām īśam anantam aparājitam vratair nānāvidhair devi aihikāmuṣmikāptaye viṣṇuvratādibhir divyais tathā dānair mano'nugaiḥ ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣekaiś ca brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ manojñair vividhair dhūpaiḥ puṣpavastrānulepanaiḥ gītavādyais tathā hṛdyair upavāsaiś ca bhāmini evam ārādhya govindam anujñātā yathāvidhi patinā sakalān kāmān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ patinā tv ananujñātā kiṃcit puṇyaṃ karoti yā viphalaṃ tad aśeṣaṃ vai tasyāḥ śailavarātmaje na ca prasādaṃ kurute bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ nānujñātā tu yā nārī patinārcati keśavam yā tu bhartṛparā nārī nārāyaṇam atandritā bhaktyā saṃpūjayed devaṃ toṣam āyāti keśavaḥ yā tu bhartrā parityaktā tathā yā mṛtabhartṛkā pāṣaṇḍānugato vāpi yasyā bhartā maheśvara prāyo dadāti nānujñāṃ viṣṇor ārādhane tadā katham ārādhanaṃ kāryaṃ viṣṇos tad vada śaṃkara yā tu bhartrā parityaktā sā saṃpūjya nijaṃ patim manasā tanmanaskā ca tasyaiva hitakāriṇī na nindākaraṇī tasya śreyo'bhidhyāyinī tathā tasyaiva sarvakāleṣu sarvakalyāṇam icchati ārādhayej jagannāthaṃ sarvadhātāram acyutam kṛtopavāsā puṣpādi nivedya sakalaṃ tataḥ bhartur manorathāvāptiṃ prārthayet prathamaṃ varam svayaṃ yathābhilaṣitaṃ prārthayet taṃ varaṃ tataḥ evaṃ bhartṛparityaktā yoṣid ārādhanaṃ hareḥ kurvāṇā sakalān kāmān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ bhartā karoti yac casyāḥ kiṃcit puṇyam aharniśam tasya puṇyasya saṃpūrṇam ardhaṃ prāpnoti sā śubhe yat tu sā kurute puṇyaṃ vinā doṣeṇa yojjhitā tat tasyāḥ sakalaṃ devi tasyārdhaṃ na labhet patiḥ bhartary evaṃ pravasite tyaktā ca patinā śubhe kurvītārādhanaṃ nārī upavāsādinā hareḥ etat tavoktaṃ yat pṛṣṭaṃ tvayāhaṃ girinandini vidhavānām ato dharmaṃ śrūyatāṃ viṣṇutuṣṭidam mṛte bhartari sādhvī strī brahmacaryavratoditā snātā pratidinaṃ dadyāt svabhartṛsalilāñjalim kuryād yānudinaṃ bhaktyā devānām api pūjanam atithes tarpaṇaṃ tadvad agnihotram amantrakam pūrtadharmāśritaṃ cānyat kuryān nityam atandritā nityakarma ṛte cāsyā neṣṭaṃ karma vidhīyate viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ caiva kuryān nityam upoṣitā dānādi vipramukhyebhyo dadyāt puṇyavivṛddhaye upavāsāṃś ca vividhān kuryāc chāstroditān śubhe lokāntarasthaṃ bhartāram ātmānaṃ ca varānane tārayaty ubhayaṃ nārī yetthaṃ dharmaparāyaṇā putraiśvaryasthitā nārī upavāsādinā harim yā toṣayati siddhiṃ sā putrebhyo api prayacchati śubhāṃl lokāṃs tathā bhartur ātmanaś ca yathepsitān sakalaṃ pūrayaty astaṃ pāpaṃ nayati cākhilam ātmanaś caiva bhartuś ca nārī paramikāṃ gatim dadāty ārādhya govindaṃ saputrā vidhavā ca yā tasmād ebhir vidhānais tu sarvakālaṃ tu yoṣitaḥ keśavārādhanaṃ kāryaṃ lokadvayaphalapradam ye narā mṛtapatnikās tair apy etad aśeṣataḥ pūrtadharmāśritaṃ kāryaṃ nityakarma ca kevalam putraiśvaryasthitaiḥ samyag brahmacaryaguṇānvitaiḥ viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ kāryaṃ tīrthasthair athavā gṛhe brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ strī śūdraś ca varānane anārādhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ nāpnoti paramāṃ gatim aiśvaryaṃ saṃtatiṃ śreṣṭhām ārogyaṃ dravyasaṃpadam dadāti bhagavān viṣṇur gatim agryāṃ sutoṣitaḥ evaṃ śailasutā proktā svayaṃ devena śaṃbhunā pṛṣṭena samyak kathitaṃ bhavato api mahāmune sarvavarṇais tathā strībhir anyair api janair hariḥ ārādhanīyo nātuṣṭe viṣṇau saṃprāpyate gatiḥ na durgatiṃ rauravādīn narakāṃś ca na gacchati yam ārādhyeśvaraṃ vandyaṃ kas taṃ viṣṇuṃ na pūjayet tasmād amuṣmikān kleśān narake yāś ca yātanāḥ sadaivodvijatā dālbhya samārādhyo janārdanaḥ bhagavan yātanā ghorāḥ śrūyante narakeṣu yāḥ tāsāṃ svarūpam atyugraṃ yathāvad vaktum arhasi śṛṇu dālbhyātighorāṇāṃ yātanānāṃ mayoditam svarūpaṃ nārakair yat tu narakeṣv anubhūyate yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi rauravo narako dvija aṅgārapūrṇamadhyo asau jvālāmālāpariṣkṛtaḥ tanmadhye patito yāti yojanāni sahasraśaḥ satyahānyānṛtī yāti tatra pāparatir naraḥ rauravād dviguṇaś caiva mahārauvarasaṃjñitaḥ taptatāmrapuṭāṅgāra- jvalatpāvakasaṃvṛtaḥ paropatāpinas tatra patanti narake narāḥ nāścaryaṃ dvijaśārdūla varṣalakṣayutāni ca kālasūtreṇa cchidyante cakrārūḍhāś ca mānavāḥ kālāṅgulisthena sadā āpādatalamastakāt kālasūtra iti khyāto ghoraḥ sa narakottamaḥ tatrāpi vañcakā yānti ye caivotkocajīvinaḥ taptakumbhas tathaivānyo narako bhṛśadāruṇaḥ tailakumbheṣu pacyante tatrāpy agnibhṛteṣu te devavedadvijātīnāṃ ye nindāṃ kurvate sadā saṃśṛṇvanti ca ye mūḍhā ye ca matsariṇo adhamāḥ karambhavālukākumbha- saṃjñaṃ ca narakaṃ śṛṇu paradāraratā ye tu patanti narake adhamāḥ hṛtaṃ yaiś ca jalaṃ te api tasmin yānti narādhamāḥ gonipāneṣu vighnāni mūḍhā ye cāpi kurvate karambhavālukākumbha- narake te patanti vai andhe tamasi duṣpāre śītārtiparikampitāḥ bhrāmyante mānavā gātraiḥ samastaiḥ sphuṭitāsthibhiḥ govadhaḥ strīvadhaḥ pāpaiḥ kṛtaṃ yaiś ca gavānṛtam te tatrātimahābhīme patanti narake narāḥ utpāṭyate tathā jihvā saṃdaṃśair bhṛśadāruṇaiḥ ākriśakānāṃ duṣṭānāṃ sadaivābaddhabhāṣiṇām karapatraiś ca pāṭyante yamasya puruṣais tathā paradāraparadravya- hiṃsakāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ āyasīṃ ca śilāṃ taptām aśeṣāṅgais tathā narāḥ paradāraratā evaṃ samāliṅganti pāpinaḥ sarvāṅgair vikṛtair raktam udgiranto atipīḍitāḥ yantreṣv anyeṣu pīḍyante jantupīḍākarā narāḥ vṛkaiḥ saṃbhakṣyate pṛṣṭhaṃ narāṇāṃ pāpakāriṇām janasya pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ yair bhakṣitaṃ pāpakāribhiḥ asipatravanair ghoraiś chidyante pāpakarmiṇaḥ sadbhāvapravaṇā yais tu bhagnā viśrambhino janāḥ ayomukhaiḥ khagair bhagnāḥ khaṇḍakhaṇḍaṃ tathāparaiḥ vrajanti pāpakarmāṇaḥ śvaśṛgālais tathāparaiḥ sūṣāyām api dhāsyante jvaladagnicayāvṛtāḥ pāṣāṇapeṣyaṃ piṣyante tathānye pāpakarmiṇaḥ devatātithibhṛtyāṇām adattvā bhuñjate tu ye mṛṣāgatās tathāivaikyaṃ trapuṣā sīsakena ca prayānti puruṣās tailaiḥ kvāthyante anye punaḥ punaḥ varṇadharmaparityāge naikyaṃ ye puruṣā gatāḥ te api pāpasamācārā varṇasaṃkarakāriṇaḥ svarūpaṃ nārakasyāgneḥ śṛṇuṣva kathayāmi te muktas tato anyavahnishtaḥ śete saṃprāpya nirvṛtim śastradhārās tathaivaitā mṛṇālaprastaraṃ naraḥ manyate nārakaiḥ śastrair vikṣato dvijasattama himakhaṇḍacayāchanno nivātaṃ manyate naraḥ vimukto nārakāc chītāt prakāśaṃ tamasas tamaḥ protā gudeṣu bhinnāṅgā ārtā rāvavirāviṇaḥ śūleṣu loheṣv apare triśūleṣu tathāpare yājyopādhyāyadāmpatya- suhṛnmitrasutādiṣu kṛto bhedo durācārair yair alīkoktibhāṣibhiḥ āyasāḥ kaṇṭakās tīkṣṇā narake kūṭaśālmalau teṣu protā durātmānaḥ paradārabhujo narāḥ kṛmikīṭajalaukādi- tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāsyavikṣatāḥ bhrāmyante cāndhatāmisre vṛthāmāṃsāśino hi ye etāṃś cānyāṃś ca narakāñ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ karmāntaraṃ jano bhuṅkte pariṇāmāṃś ca cetasaḥ yādṛk karma manuṣyāṇāṃ tādṛg viṣayarūpavat pariṇāmaṃ mano yāti śubhāśubhamayaṃ dvija atīvabhīṣaṇān itthaṃ śastrāgnibhayadān naraḥ kathaṃ na gacchen narakān etan me vaktum arhasi aho atikaṣṭapāpānāṃ vipāko narakasthitaiḥ puruṣair bhujyate brahmaṃs tanmokṣaṃ vada sattama puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ pākaḥ puṇya eva dvijottama cetasaḥ pariṇāmottaḥ svargasthair bhujyate naraiḥ tathaiva pākaḥ pāpānāṃ puruṣair narakasthitaiḥ bhujyate tāvad akhilaṃ yāvat pāpaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam yadā tu pāpasya jayaḥ kṣīyate sukṛtaṃ tadā śubhasya karmaṇo vṛddhau kṣayam āyāty aśobhanam jaye yateta puruṣas tasmāt sukṛtakarmaṇaḥ pāpaṃ karma vinā naiva narakaprāptir iṣyate jayāya dvādaśī śastā nṝṇāṃ sukṛtakarmaṇām yām upoṣya dvijaśreṣṭha na yāti narakaṃ naraḥ phālgunāmalapakṣasya ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ dvādaśyāṃ tu dvijaśreṣṭha pūjayen madhusūdanam ekādaśyāṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ viṣṇor nāmānukīrtanam pūjāyāṃ vāsudevasya kurvīta susamāhitaḥ namo nārāyaṇāyeti vācyaṃ ca svapatā niśi krodhaḥ prapañca īrṣyā ca dambho lobhaś ca varjitaḥ kāmo droho madaś cāpi mānamātsaryam eva ca sarvam etat parityajya viṣṇubhaktena cetasā asāratāṃ ca loke asmin saṃsāre bhāvayen matim kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca dambham īrṣyāṃ ca varjayet mānadrohādidoṣāṃś ca sarvān dhanamadodbhūtān bhāvayed viṣṇubhaktāṃś ca saṃsārāsāratāṃ tathā evaṃ bhāvitacittena prāṇināṃ hitam icchatā tathaiva kuryād dvādaśyāṃ nāmnām uccāraṇaṃ dvija yavapātrāṇi pūrvaṃ tu dadyān māsacatuṣṭayam āṣāḍhādidvitīyaṃ tu pāraṇaṃ yan mahāmate tatrāpi ghṛtapātrāṇi dadyāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ kārttikādiṣu māseṣu māghanteṣu tathā tilān viprāya dadyāt pātrashtān pratimāsam upoṣitaḥ nāmatrayam aśeṣeṣu māsi māsi dinadvayam tathaivoccārayed dadyād dvādaśyāṃ ca yavādikam praṇamya ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ kṛtapūjaḥ prasādayet viṣṇo namas te jagataḥ prasūte oṃ vāsudevāya namo namas te nārāyaṇa tvāṃ praṇato asmy acintya jayo astu me śāśvatapuṇyarāśeḥ prasīda puṇyaṃ jayam etu viṣṇo oṃ vāsudeva rddhim upaitu puṇyam nārāyaṇoṃ bhūtim upaitu puṇyam prayātu cāśeṣam aghaṃ vināśam viṣṇo puṇyodbhavo me astu vāsudevāstu me śubham nārāyaṇāstu dharmo me jahi pāpam aśeṣataḥ anekajanmajanitaṃ bālyayauvanavārddhike puṇyaṃ vivṛddhim āyātu yātu pāpaṃ tu saṃkṣayam ākāśādiṣu śabdādau śrotrādau mahadādiṣu prakṛtau puruṣe caiva brahmaṇy api ca sa prabhuḥ yathaika eva sarvātmā vāsudevo vyavasthitaḥ tena satyena me pāpaṃ narakārtipradaṃ kṣayam prayātu sukṛtasyāstu mamānudivasaṃ jayaḥ pāpasya hāniḥ puṇyaṃ ca vṛddhim abhyety anuttamām evam uccārya viprāya dattvā yat kathitaṃ tava bhuñjīta kṛtakṛtyas tu pāraṇe pāraṇe gate pāraṇānte ca devasya prīṇanaṃ śaktito dvija kurvītākhilapāṣaṇḍair ālāpaṃ ca vivarjayet ity etat kathitaṃ dālbhya sukṛtasya jayāvahā dvādaśī narakaṃ mṛtyo yām upoṣya na paśyati nāgnayo na ca śastrāṇi na ca lohamūkhāḥ khagāḥ nārakās taṃ prabādhante matir yasya janārdane nāmoccāraṇamātreṇa viṣṇoḥ kṣīṇo aghasaṃcayaḥ bhavaty apāstapāpasya narake gamanaṃ kutaḥ namo nārāyaṇa hare vāsudeveti kīrtayet na yāti narakaṃ martyaḥ saṃkṣīṇāśeṣapātakaḥ tasmāt pāṣaṇḍisaṃsargam akurvan dvādaśīm imām upoṣya puṇyopacayī na yāti narakaṃ naraḥ pāṣaṇḍibhir asaṃsparśam asaṃbhāṣaṇam eva ca viṣṇor ārādhanaparair naraiḥ kāryam upoṣitaiḥ kiṃ brūhi lakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ yādṛśān varjayed vratī kathaṃcid yadi saṃlāpa- darśanasparśanādikam upoṣitānāṃ pāṣaṇḍair narāṇāṃ vipra jāyate kiṃ tatra vada kartavyaṃ yenākhaṇḍaṃ vrataṃ bhavet śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ varṇāśramavibhāgajam ullaṅghya ye pravartante svecchayā kūṭayuktibhiḥ vikarmābhiratā mūḍhā yuktiprāgalbhyadurmadāḥ pāṣaṇḍinas te duḥśīlā narakārhā narādhamāḥ tāṃs tu pāṣaṇḍinaḥ pāpān vikarmasthāṃś ca mānavān vaiḍālavratikāṃś caiva nityam eva tu nālapet saṃbhāṣyaitāñ śuciṣadaṃ cintayed acyutaṃ budhaḥ idaṃ codāharet samyak kṛtvā tatpravaṇaṃ manaḥ śārīram antaḥkaraṇopaghātaṃ vācaś ca viṣṇur bhagavān aśeṣam śamaṃ nayatv astu mameha śarma pāpād anante hṛdi saṃniviṣṭe antaḥśuddhiṃ bahiḥśuddhiṃ śuddho antar mama yo acyutaḥ sa karotv amale tasmiñ śucir evāsmi sarvadā bāhyopaghātād anagho boddhā ca bhagavān ajaḥ śuddhiṃ nayatv anantātmā viṣṇuś cetasi saṃsthitaḥ etat saṃbhāṣya japtavyaṃ pāṣaṇḍibhir upoṣitaiḥ namaḥ śuciṣadety uktvā sūryaṃ paśyeta vīkṣitaiḥ śrūyate ca purā martyāḥ svecchayā svargagāminaḥ babhūvur anaghāḥ sarve svadharmaparipālanāt devāś ca balino martyair varṇakarmaṇy anuvrataiḥ yajñādhyayanadāneṣu vartamānaiś ca mānavaiḥ daiteyāś ca parābhāvam atuṣṭāv asurā yayuḥ tataś ca ṣaṇḍo markaś ca daityendrāṇāṃ purohitau cakratuḥ karma devānāṃ vināśāyātibhīṣaṇam tatrotpanno atikṛṣṇāṅgas tamaḥprāyo atidāruṇaḥ dambhādhāraḥ śāṭhyasāro nidrāprakṛtir ulvaṇaḥ mahāmoha iti khyātaḥ kṛtyarūpo vibhīṣaṇaḥ caturdhā sa vibhaktaś ca tābhām atra mahīyate vedadevadvijātīnām ekāṃśena sa nindanam karoty anyena na ratiṃ yogakarmasu vindati vikarmaṇy apareṇāpi saṃyojayati mānavān jñānāpahāram anyena karoti dvijasattama jñānabuddhyā tathājñānaṃ gṛhṇāty ajñānamohitaḥ vedavādavirodhena yā kathā sāsya rocate evaṃ sa tu mahāmohaḥ ṣaṇḍamarkopapāditaḥ dambhādidūṣito adharma- svarūpo atibhayaṃkara sa lokān vividhopāyair lokeṣv eva vyavasthitaḥ mohābhibhavaniḥsārāṇ karoti dvijasattama tanmohitānām acirād viveko yāti saṃkṣayam kṣīṇajñānā vikarmāṇi kurvanty aharaho dvija nijavarṇātmakaṃ dharmaṃ parityajya vimohitāḥ dharmabuddhyā tataḥ pāpaṃ kurvanty ajñānadurmadāḥ jñānāvalepas tatraiva tatas teṣāṃ prajāyate suhṛdbhir vāryamāṇās te paṇḍitaiś ca dayālubhiḥ prayacchanty uttaraṃ ṃūḍhāḥ kūṭayuktisamanvitam tatas te svayam ātmānam anyaṃ cālpamatiṃ naram vikarmaṇā yojayantaś cyavayanti svadharmataḥ pāṣaṇḍino durācārāḥ parānnaguṇavādinaḥ asaṃskṛtānnabhoktāro vrātyāḥ saṃskāravarjitāḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ pāpasaṃkalpā dāmbhikāḥ śaṭhabuddhayaḥ varṇasaṃkarakartāro māyāvyājopajīvinaḥ niḥśaucā vakramatayo nānyadastītivādinaḥ evaṃvidhās te sanmārgād vedaproktād bahiḥsthitāḥ kriyākalāpaṃ nindanta ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñitam ātmānaṃ ca parāṃś caiva kurvanti narakasthitān teṣāṃ darśanasaṃbhāṣa- sparśanāni naraiḥ sadā parityājyāni dṛṣṭe ca proktaḥ saṃbhāṣaṇe ca yaḥ saṃsparśe ca budhaḥ snātvā śuciḥ śuciṣadaṃ smaret bhavaty ataḥ sadaivaiṣām ālāpasparśanaṃ tyajet puṇyakāmo mahābhāgaḥ kiṃ punar yad upoṣitaḥ yato hi nindite karmaṇy abhyāso ratir eva ca pāṣaṇḍinām aśeṣāṇām aprītir vedakarmaṇi te hy adhogāminaḥ proktā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ aprāptir na tathā duḥkham aiśvaryāder dvijottama yathā manorathair labdhair vicyutir dharmahānijā aiśvaryād vittato vāpi saṃtater devalokataḥ abhīṣṭād anyato vāpi padād yena na vicyutim prāpnoti puruṣo brahman nārī vāpuṇyasaṃkṣayāt tan mamācakṣva viprarṣe duḥkham ebhyo hi vicyutiḥ satyam etan mahābhāga duḥkhaṃ prāptasya saṃkṣayaḥ aiśvaryād atha vittasya bandhuvargasukhasya vā tad etac chrūyatāṃ dālbhya yathā neṣṭāt paricyutiḥ sargāder jāyate samyag upavāsavatāṃ satām dvādaśarkṣāṇi viprarṣe pratimāsaṃ tu yāni vai tannāmāny acyutaṃ teṣu samyak saṃpūjayed budhaḥ puṣpair dhūpais tathāmbhobhir abhīṣṭair aparais tathā āditaḥ kṛttikāṃ kṛtvā kārttike munipuṅgava naivedyaṃ kṛsaraṃ pūrvam annaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam nivedayet kārttikādi saṃyāvaṃ ca tataḥ param āṣāḍhādau ca devāya pāyasaṃ vai nivedayet tenaivānnena viprarṣe brāhmaṇān bhojayed budhaḥ pañcagavyajalasnātas tasyaiva prāśanāc chuciḥ naivedyaṃ svayam aśnīyān naktaṃ saṃpūjite acyute evaṃ saṃvatsarasyānte tataḥ suptotthite acyute saṃyak saṃpūjya viprarṣe tam eva puruṣottamam praṇamya prārthayed vidvāñ śuciḥ snāto yathāvidhi namo namas te acyuta saṃkṣayo astu pāpasya vṛddhiṃ samupaitu puṇyam aiśvaryavittādi sadākṣayaṃ me akṣayā ca me saṃtatir acyutāstu yathācyutas tvaṃ parataḥ parasmāt sa brahmabhūtāt parataḥ parātman tathācyutaṃ me kuru vāñchitaṃ yan mayā padaṃ pāpaharāprameya acyutānanta govinda prasīda yad abhīpsitam tad akṣayam ameyātman kuruṣva puruṣottama evam ante samabhyarcya prārthayitvā tathāśiṣaḥ yathāvan muniśārdūla cyutiṃ nāpnoti mānavaḥ saṃtateḥ svargavittāder aiśvaryasya tathā mune yad vābhimatam atyantaṃ tato na cyavate naraḥ tasmāt sarvaprayatnena māsanakṣatrapūjane yatetākṣayakāmas tu sadaiva munipuṅgava atrāpi śrūyate siddhā kācit svarge mahāvratā nārī tapodhanā bhūtvā prakhyātā śāmbharāyaṇī samastasaṃdehaharā sadā svargaukasāṃ hi sā kasyacit tv atha kālasya devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ pūrvendracaritaṃ brahman papracchedaṃ bṛhaspatim pūrvendrā parataḥ pūrve ye babhūvuḥ sureśvarāḥ teṣāṃ caritam icchāmi śrotum āṅgirasāṃ vara evam uktas tadā tena devendreṇāmaladyutiḥ prāha dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ paramarṣir bṛhaspatiḥ nāhaṃ cirantanān vedmi devarāja sureśvarān ātmanaḥ samakālīnaṃ mām avaihi sureśvara tataḥ papraccha devendraḥ ko asmābhir munipuṅgava praṣṭavyo atra mahābhāga kṛtādivasatir divi bṛhaspatiś ciraṃ dhyātvā punar āha śacīpatim tapasvinīṃ mahābhāgāṃ smṛtvāsau śāmbharāyaṇīm na devā na ca gandharvā na cānye cirasaṃsthitāḥ cirantanānāṃ cariteṣv abhijñā tridaśeśvara ekaiva cirakālajñā dharmajñā śakra kevalam jānāty akhiladevendra- caritaṃ śāmbharāyaṇī ity uktas tena devendraḥ kautūhalasamanvitaḥ yayau yatra mahābhāgā tāpasī śāmbharāyaṇī sā tau dṛṣṭvā samāyātau devarājabṛhaspatī samyag arghyena saṃpūjya praṇipatya śubhavratā namo astu devarājāya tathaivāṅgirase namaḥ yad vāṃ kāryaṃ mahābhāgau sakalaṃ tad ihocyatām āvām abhyāgatau praṣṭuṃ tvām atrātivivekinīm yac ca kāryaṃ mahābhāge tat pṛṣṭā kathayeha nau yadi smarasi kalyāṇi pūrvendracaritāni nau tadākhyāhi mahābhāge devendrasya kutūhalāt yadi śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ tat kariṣye vimṛṣyatu yo vai pūrvaḥ surendrasya tataś ca prathamo hi yaḥ tasmāt pūrvataro yaś ca tasyāpi prathamāś ca ye teṣāṃ pūrvatarā ye ca vedmi tān akhilān aham teṣāṃ ca caritaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jānāmy āṅgirasāṃ vara manvantarāṇy anekāni sṛṣṭiṃ ca tridivaukasām saptarṣīn subahūn deva manūnāṃ ca sutān nṛpa tat pṛccha tvaṃ vadāmy eṣā pūrvendracaritaṃ mune evam ukte tatas tābhyāṃ pṛṣṭā sā śāmbharāyaṇī yathāvad ācaṣṭa tayoḥ pūrvendracaritaṃ dvija svāyambhuve yas tu manau manau svārociṣe tu yaḥ uttame tāmase caiva raivate cākṣuṣe tathā yo yo babhūva devendras tasya tasya tapasvinī tayor jagāda caritaṃ yathāvac chāmbharāyaṇī tataḥ kautūhalaparo devarāṭ tāṃ tapasvinīm uvāca jānāsi kathaṃ tvam etac chāmbharāyaṇi sarva eva hi devendrāḥ svargasthā ye manīṣiṇaḥ babhūvur etac caritam eteṣāṃ vedmi tena vai kiṃ kṛtaṃ vada dharmajñe tvayā yeneyam akṣayā svarloke vasatiḥ prāptā yathā nānyena kenacit aho sarvavratānāṃ tad upoṣitaṃ mahad vratam pradhānataram atyarthaṃ svargasaṃvāsadaṃ matam caritaṃ ca mayā teṣāṃ śrutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tathaiva ca evam uktā tatas tena devendreṇa yaśasvinī pratyuvāca mahābhāgā yathāvac chāmbharāyaṇī māsarkṣeṣv acyuto devaḥ pratimāsaṃ sureśvara yathoktavratayā samyak sapta varṣāṇi pūjitaḥ tasyeyaṃ karmaṇo vyuṣṭir acyutārādhanasya me devalokād abhimatā devarāja yad acyutiḥ svargaṃ dravyamayaiśvaryaṃ saṃtatiṃ vāpi yo acyutām naro vāñchati tenetthaṃ toṣaṇīyo acyutaḥ prabhuḥ etat te pūrvadevendra- caritaṃ sakalaṃ mayā svargavāsākṣayatvaṃ ca māsarkṣācyutapūjanāt yathāvat kathitaṃ deva pṛcchatas tridaśeśvara dharmārthakāmamokṣāṃs tu vāñchatāṃ vibudhādhipa viṣṇor ārādhanān nānyat paramaṃ siddhikāraṇam tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devarājabṛhaspatī tāṃ tathety ūcatuḥ sādhvīṃ ceratuś cāpi tad vratam tasmād dālbhya prayatnena pratimāsaṃ samāhitaḥ māsarkṣācyutapūjāyāṃ bhavethās tanmanāḥ sadā bhagavan prāṇinaḥ sarve viṣarogādyupadravaiḥ duṣṭagrahopaghātaiś ca sarvakālam upadrutāḥ ābhicārukakṛtyābhiḥ sparṣarogaiś ca dāruṇaiḥ sadā saṃpīḍyamānās te tiṣṭhanti munisattama yena karmavipākena viṣarogādyupadravāḥ na bhavanti nṛṇāṃ tan me yathāvad vaktum arhasi vratopavāsair yair viṣṇur nānyajanmani pūjitaḥ te narā muniśārdūla graharogādibhāginaḥ yair na tatpravaṇaṃ cittaṃ sarvadaiva naraiḥ kṛtam viṣagrahajvarāṇāṃ te manuṣyā dālbhya bhājanāḥ ārogyaṃ paramām ṛddhiṃ manasā yad yad icchati tat tad āpnoty asaṃdigdhaṃ paratrācyutatoṣakṛt nādhīn prāpnoti na vyādhīn na viṣagrahabandhanam kṛtyāsparśabhayaṃ vāpi toṣite madhusūdane sarvaduṣṭaśamas tasya saumyās tasya sadā grahāḥ devānām apradhṛṣyo asau tuṣṭo yasya janārdanaḥ yaḥ samaḥ sarvabhūteṣu yathātmani tathāpare upavādādinā tena toṣyate madhusūdanaḥ toṣite tatra jāyante narāḥ pūṛṇamanorathāḥ arogāḥ sukhino bhoga- bhoktāro munisattama na teṣāṃ śatravo naiva sparśarogābhicārukāḥ graharogādikaṃ vāpi pāpakāryaṃ na jāyate avyāhatāni kṛṣṇasya cakrādīny ātmayudhāni tam rakṣanti sakalāpadbhyo yena viṣṇur upāsitaḥ anārādhitagovindā ye narā duḥkhabhāginaḥ teṣāṃ duḥkhābhibhūtānāṃ kartavyaṃ yad dayālubhiḥ paśyadbhiḥ sarvabhūtasthaṃ vāsudevaṃ mahāmune samadṛṣṭibhir īśeśaṃ tan mama brūhy aśeṣataḥ kuśamūlasthito brahmā kuśamadhye janārdanaḥ kuśāgre śaṃkaraṃ vidyāt trayo devā vyavasthitāḥ gṛhītvā ca sa mūlāgrān kuśāñ śuddhān upaspṛśet mārjayet sarvagātrāṇi kuśāgrair dālbhya śāntikṛt śarīre yasya tiṣṭhanti kuśasthajalabindavaḥ naśyanti tasya pāpāni garuḍenaiva pannagāḥ viṣṇubhaktā viśeṣeṇa cidgatamānasaḥ rogagrahaviṣārtānāṃ kuryāc chāntim imāṃ śubhām nārasiṃhaṃ samabhyarcya śucau deśe kuśāsane mantrair etair yathā liṅgaṃ kuryād digbandham ātmanaḥ vārāhaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ ca vāmanaṃ viṣṇum eva ca dhyātvā samāhito bhūtvā dikṣu nāmāni vinyāset pūrve nārāyaṇaḥ pātu vārijākṣas tu dakṣiṇe pradyumnaḥ paścimasyāṃ tu vāsudevas tathottare īśānyām avatād viṣṇur āgneyyāṃ ca janārdanaḥ nairṛtyāṃ padmanābhaś ca vāyavyāṃ caiva mādhavaḥ ūrdhvaṃ govardhanadharo adharāyāṃ trivikramaḥ etābhyo daśadigbhyas tu sarvataḥ pātu keśavaḥ aṅguṣṭhāgre tu govindaṃ tarjanyāṃs tu mahīdharam madhyamāyāṃ hṛṣīkeśam anāmikyāṃ trivikramam kaṇiṣṭhāyāṃ nyased viṣṇuṃ karamadhye tu mādhavam evaṃ nyāsaṃ purā kṛtvā paścād aṅgeṣu vinyaset śikhāyāṃ keśavaṃ nyasya mūrdhni nārāyaṇaṃ nyaset cakṣurmadhye nyased viṣṇuṃ karṇayor madhusūdanam trivikramaṃ kapālasthaṃ vāmanaṃ karṇamūlayoḥ dāmodaraṃ dantavaktrau vārāhaṃ cibuke nyaset uttaroṣṭhe hṛṣīkeśaṃ padmanābhaṃ tathādhare jihvāyāṃ vāsudevaṃ ca tālvake garuḍadhvajam vaikuṇṭhaṃ kanṭhamadhyastham anantaṃ nāsikopari dakṣiṇe tu bhuje vipra vinyaset puruṣottamam vāmabhuje mahābhāgaṃ rāghavaṃ hṛdi vinyaset pītāmbaraṃ sarvatanau hariṃ nābhau tu vinyaset kare tu dakṣiṇe vipra tataḥ saṃkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset vāme vipra hariṃ vidyāt kaṭimadhye aparājitam pṛṣṭhe kṣitidharaṃ vidyād acyutaṃ skandhayor api mādhavaṃ bāhu kukṣau tu dakṣiṇe yogaśāyinam svayaṃbhuvaṃ meḍhramadhye ūrubhyāṃ tu gadādharam cakriṇaṃ jānumadhye tu jaṅghayor acyutaṃ nyaset gulpayor narasiṃhaṃ ca pādapṛṣṭhe amitaujasam śrīdharaṃ cāṅgulīṣu syāt padmākṣaṃ sarvasandhiṣu romakūpe guḍākeśaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ raktāsthimajjāsu manobuddhyor ahaṃkāreṣv evaṃ citte janārdanam nakheṣu mādhavaṃ caiva nyaset pādatale acyutam evaṃ nyāsavidhiṃ kṛtvā sākṣān nārāyaṇo bhavet tanur viṣṇumayī tasya yāvat kiṃcin na bhāṣate evaṃ nyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā yat kāryaṃ śṛṇu tad dvija pādamūle tu devasya śaṅkhaṃ tatraiva vinyaset vanamālāṃ tu vinyasya sarvadevābhipūjitām gadāṃ vakṣaḥsthale caiva cakraṃ caiva tu pṛṣṭhataḥ śrīvatsāṅgaṃ śiro nyasya pañcāṅgakavacaṃ nyaset āpādāmastake caiva vinyaset puruṣottamam oṃ apāmārjanako nyāsaḥ sarvavyādhivināśanaḥ viṣṇur ūrdhvam adho rakṣed vaikuṇṭho vidiśo diśaḥ pātu māṃ sarvato rāmo dhanvī cakrī ca keśavaḥ pūjākāle tu devasya japakāle tathaiva ca homārambheṣu sarveṣu trisaṃdhyāsu ca nityaśaḥ āyur ārogyam aiśvaryaṃ jñānaṃ vittaṃ phalaṃ bhavet yad yat sukhakaraṃ proktaṃ tat sarvaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati atha dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam vārāharūpiṇaṃ devaṃ saṃsmaraty aparājitam bṛhattanuṃ bṛhadgātraṃ bṛhaddaṃṣṭrasuśobhanam samastavedavedāṅgaṃ yuktāṅgaṃ bhūṣaṇair yutam uddhṛtya bhūmiṃ pātālād hastābhyām upagṛhṇatām āliṅgya bhūmiṃ śirasi mūrdhni jighrantam āsthitam ratnavaiḍūryamukhyābhir muktābhir upaśobhitam pītāmbaradharaṃ devaṃ śuklamālyānulepanam trayastriṃśakoṭidevaiḥ stūyamānaṃ mudāniśam nṛtyadbhir apsarobhiś ca gīyamānaṃ ca kinnaraiḥ itthaṃ dhyātvā mahātmānaṃ japen nityaṃ mahātmanaḥ suvarṇamaṇḍapāntasthaṃ padmaṃ dhyāyet sakesaram sakarṇikadalair iṣṭair aṣṭabhiḥ pariśobhitam karaṃ karahitaṃ devaṃ pūrṇacandrāptasuprabham taḍitsamaśaṭāśobhi kaṇṭhanālopaśobhitam śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣaḥsthaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ trilocanam javākusumasaṃkāśaṃ raktahastatalānvitam pītavastraparīdhānaṃ śuklayastrottarīyakam karaṃ karahitaṃ devaṃ pūrṇacandrāptasuprabham kaṭisūtreṇa haimena nūpureṇa virājitam vanamālādiśobhāḍhyaṃ muktāhāropaśobhitam anekasūryasaṃkāśaṃ mukuṭāṭopamastakam śaṅkhacakragṛhītābhyām udbāhubhyāṃ virājitam paṅkajābhaṃ caturhastaṃ tatpatrābhasulocanam prātaḥ sūryasamaprakhya- kuṇḍalābhyāṃ virājitam keyūrakāntisasyarddhi- muktikāratnaśobhitam jānūparinyastahastaṃ vararatnanakhāṅkuram jaṅghābharaṇasasyarddhi- visphuryatkaṅkanatviṣam muktāphalābdasamahad- dantapaṅktivirājitam campakāmukulaprakhya- sunāsāmukhapaṅkajam atiraktauṣṭhavadanaṃ vyāttāsyam atibhīṣaṇam vāmāṅkasthaṃ śivabhakta- śāntidāṃ sunitambinīm arhaṇīyāṃ sujātoruṃ sunāsāṃ śubhalakṣaṇām subhrūṃ sukeśīṃ suśroṇīṃ suśubhāṃ sudvijānanām supratiṣṭhāṃ suvadanāṃ caturhastāṃ vicintayet dukūle caiva cārvaṅgīṃ hāriṇīṃ sarvakāmadām taptakañcanasaṃkāśāṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām suvarṇakalaśaprakhya- pīnonnatapayodharām gṛhītapadmayugalaṃ udbāhubhyāṃ tathānyayoḥ gṛhītamātulaṅgākhyaṃ jāmbunadakarān tathā evaṃ devīṃ nṛsiṃhasya vāmāṅkopari saṃsmaret ativimalasugātraṃ raupyapātrastham annaṃ sulalitadadhikhaṇḍaṃ pāṇinā dakṣiṇena kalaśam amṛtapūrṇaṃ savyahaste dadhānaṃ tadatisakaladuḥkhaṃ vāmanaṃ bhāvayed yaḥ anyā bhāskarasaprabhābhir akhilair bhābhir diśo bhāsayan bhīmākṣasphuradaṭṭahāsavilasāddaṃṣṭrāgradīptānanaḥ dorbhiś cakradharau gadābjamukulau trāsāṃś ca pāśāṅkuśau bibhratpiṅgaśiro aruhoddhatasaṭaś cakravidhāno hariḥ manobhūtānīndriyāṇi guṇāḥ sattvaṃ rajas tamaḥ trailokyasyeśvaraṃ sarvam ahaṃkāre pratiṣṭhitāḥ oṃ namaḥ paramārthāya puruṣāya mahātmane arūpabahurūpāya vyāpine paramātmane namas te devadevāya suraśūra namo astu te lokādhyakṣa jagatpūjya paramātman namas te niṣkalmaṣāya śuddhāya sarvapāpaharāya ca namaskṛtvā pravakṣyāmi , yat tat sidhyatu me vacaḥ , varāhanarasiṃhāya vāmanāya mahātmane govindapadmanābhāya vāmadevāya bhūpate nārāyaṇāya devāya anantāya mahātmane garuḍadhvajāya kṛṣṇāya pītāmbaradharāya ca yogīśvarāya siddhāya guhyāya paramātmane janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya upendraśrīdharāya ca bhaktapriyāya vidhaye viṣvaksenāya śārṅgine hiraṇyagarbhapataye hiraṇyakaśipucchide cakrahastāya śūlāya tarjanyapatrāya dhīmate ādityāya upendrāya bhūtānāṃ jīvanāya ca vāsudevāya vandyāya varadāya mahātmane viṣūvṛcchravase tasmai kṣīrāmbunichiśāyine adhokṣajāya bhadrāya śrīdharāyādimūrtaye viśveśadvāramūrtiś ca mṛtyurāyohito asti saḥ nānārāgāṃś ca dakṣāṃś ca vikaṭāya mahābhītī jātupatiṃ vyagrahastaṃ vararatnanakhākaram nārāyaṇāya viśvāya viśveśāyāmbarāya ca dāmodarāya devāya anantāya mahātmane trivikramāya rāmāya vaikuṇṭhāya narāya ca namaskṛtvā pravakṣyāmi yat tat sidhyatu me vacaḥ varāhanarasiṃheśa vāmaneśa trivikrama hayagrīveśa sarveśa hṛṣīkeśa harāśubham aparājitacakrādyaiś caturbhiḥ paramāyudhaiḥ akhaṇḍitaprabhāvais tvaṃ sarvaduṣṭaharo bhava harāmukasya duritaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ durupoṣitam mṛtyubandhārtibhayadaṃ duriṣṭasya ca yat phalam parāpadhyānasahitaṃ prayuktaṃ cābhicāruka garasparśamahāyoga- prayogajarayājara oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥ kṣṛṇāya śārṅgiṇe namaḥ puṣkaranetrāya keśavāyādicakriṇe namaḥ kamalakiñjalka- pītanirmalavāsase mahāhavaripuskandha- ghṛṣṭacakrāya cakriṇe daṃṣṭroddhṛtakṣitidhṛte trayīmūrtimate namaḥ mahāyajñavarāhāya śeṣabhogoruśāyine taptahāṭakakeśānta jvalatpāvakalocana vajrādhikanakhasparśa divyasiṃha namo astu te kapila hemāśvaśīrṣa atiriktavilocana vidyutsphuritadaṃṣṭrāgra divyasiṃha namo astu te kāśyapāyātihrasvāya ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūṣita tubhyaṃ vāmanarūpāya sṛjate gāṃ namo namaḥ varāhāśeṣaduṣṭāni sarvapāpaharāṇi vai marda marda mahādaṃṣṭra marda marda ca tatphalam narasiṃha karālāsya dantaprāntānalojjvala bhañja bhañja ninādena duṣṭāny asyārtināśana ṛgyajuḥsāmagarbhābhir vāgbhir vāmanarūpadhṛk praśamaṃ sarvaduḥkhāni nayatv asya janārdanaḥ ekāhikaṃ dvyāhikaṃ ca tathā tridivasaṃ jvaram cāturthakaṃ tathātyugraṃ tathaiva satatajvaram doṣotthaṃ saṃnipātotthaṃ tathaivāgantukaṃ jvaram śamaṃ nayāśu govinda chittvā cchittvā tu vedanām netraduḥkhaṃ śiroduḥkhaṃ duḥkhaṃ codarasaṃbhavam anucchvāsam atiśvāsaṃ paritāpaṃ savepathuṃ gudaghrāṇāṃhrirogāṃś ca kuṣṭharogaṃ tathā kṣayam kāmalādīṃs tathā rogān pramehāṃś cātidāruṇān bhagaṃdarātisārāṃś ca mukharogaṃ savalgulim
