aśmarīmūtrakṛcchrāṃś ca rogān anyāṃś ca dāruṇān ye vātaprabhavā rogā ye ca pittasamudbhavāḥ kaphodbhavāś ca ye kecid ye cānye sāṃnipātikāḥ āgantavaś ca ye rogā lūtāvisphoṭakādayaḥ te sarve praśamaṃ yāntu vāsudevāpamārjitāḥ vilayaṃ yāntu te sarve viṣṇor uccāraṇena ca kṣayaṃ gacchantu cāśeṣās te cakrābhihatā hareḥ acyutānantagovinda- nāmoccāraṇabhīṣitāḥ naśyantu sakalā rogāḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmy aham sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ vāpi kṛtrimaṃ vāpi yad viṣam dantodbhavaṃ nakhabhavam ākāśaprabhavaṃ viṣam lūtādiprabhavaṃ yac ca viṣam atyantaduḥkhadam śamaṃ nayatu tat sarvaṃ kīrtito asya janārdanaḥ grahān pretagrahāṃś caiva tathā vai ḍākinīgrahān vetālāṃś ca piśācāṃś ca gandharvān yakṣarākṣasān śakunīpūtanādyāṃś ca tathā vaināyakagrahān mukhamaṇḍinikāṃ krūrāṃ revatīṃ vṛddharevatīm vṛddhikākhyān grahāṃś cogrāṃs tathā mātṛgrahān api bālasya viṣṇoḥ caritaṃ hantu bālagrahān imān vṛddhānāṃ ye grahāḥ kecid ye ca bālagrahāḥ kvacit narasiṃhasya te dṛṣṭyā dagdhā ye cāpi yauvane saṭākarālavadano narasiṃho mahāravaḥ grahān aśeṣān niḥśeṣān karotu jagato hitam narasiṃha mahāsiṃha jvālāmālojjvalānana grahān aśeṣān sarveśa khāda khādāgnilocana ye rogā ye mahotpātā yad viṣaṃ ye mahāgrahāḥ yāni ca krūrabhūtāni grahapīḍāś ca dāruṇāḥ śastrakṣateṣu ye doṣā jvālāgardabhakādayaḥ yāni cāryāṇi bhūtāni prāṇipīḍākarāṇi vai tāni sarvāṇi sarvātman paramātmañ janārdana kiṃcid rūpaṃ samāsthāya vāsudeva vināśaya kṣiptvā sudarśanaṃ cakraṃ jvālāmālāvibhīṣaṇam sarvaduṣṭopaśamanaṃ kuru devavarācyuta sudarśana mahācakra govindasya karāyudha jvalatpāvakasaṃkāśa sūryakoṭisamaprabha trailokyarakṣakartṛ tvaṃ tvaṃ duṣṭadānavadāraṇa tīkṣṇadhāra mahāvega chindhi cchindhi mahājvaram chindhi cchindhi mahāvyādhiṃ chindhi cchindhi mahāgrahān chindhi vātaṃ ca dhūtaṃ ca chindhi ghoraṃ mahāviṣam rujadāghaṃ ca śūlaṃ ca nimiṣajvālagardabham sudarśana mahājvāla chindhi cchindhi mamārayaḥ sarvaduṣṭāni rakṣāṃsi kṣapayātivibhīṣaṇa hāṃ hāṃ hūṃ hūṃ phaṭkāreṇa ṭhadvayena hatadviṣaḥ sudarśanasya mantreṇa grahā yānti diśo diśaḥ trailokyasyābhayaṃ kartum ājñāpaya janārdana sarvaduṣṭāni rakṣāṃsi kṣayaṃ yānti vibhīṣayā prācyāṃ pratīcyāṃ ca diśi dakṣiṇottaratas tathā rakṣāṃ karotu sarvātmā narasiṃhaḥ svagarjitaiḥ bhūmyantarikṣe ca tathā pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvato agrataḥ vyāghrasiṃhavarāheṣu andicorabhayeṣu ca rakṣāṃ karotu bhagavān bahurūpī janārdanaḥ yathā viṣṇuṛ jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānavam tena satyena duṣṭāni śamam asya vrajantu vai yathā viṣṇau smṛte samyak saṃkṣayaṃ yāti pātakam satyena tena sakalaṃ duṣṭam asya praśāmyatu paramātmā yathā viṣṇur vedānteṣv abhidhīyate tena satyena sakalaṃ duṣṭam asya praśāmyatu yathā yajñeṣvaro viṣṇur vedeṣv api tu gīyate tena satyena sakalaṃ yan mayoktaṃ tathāstu tat yathā yajñeśvaro viṣṇur yajñānte api gīyate tena satyena sakalaṃ yan mayoktaṃ tathāstu tat śāntir astu śivaṃ cāstu praśāmyatv asukhaṃ ca yat vāsudevaśarīrotthaiḥ kuśair nirmārjitaṃ mayā apāmārjati govindo naro nārāyaṇas tathā tavāstu sarvaduḥkhānāṃ praśamo vacanād dhareḥ idaṃ śāstraṃ paṭhed yas tu saptāhan niyataḥ śuciḥ śāntiṃ samastarogās te grahāḥ sarve viṣāni ca bhūtāni ca prayāntv īśe saṃsmṛte madhusūdane etat samastarogeṣu bhūtagrahabhayeṣu ca apamārjanakaṃ śastaṃ viṣṇunāmābhimantritam ete kuśā viṣṇuśarīrasaṃbhavā janārdano ahaṃ svayaṃ eva cāgataḥ hataṃ mayā duṣṭam aśeṣam asya svastho bhavaty eṣa vaco yathā hareḥ śāntir astu śivaṃ cāstu duṣṭam asya praśāmyatu yad asya duritaṃ kiṃcit tat kṣiptaṃ lavaṇārṇave svāsthyam asya sadaivāstu hṛṣīkeśasya kīrtanāt yata evāgataṃ pāpaṃ tatraiva pratigacchatu etad rogādipīḍāsu jantūnāṃ hitam icchatā viṣṇubhaktena kartavyam apamārjanakaṃ param anena sarvaduṣṭāni praśamaṃ yānty asaṃśayam sarvabhūtahitārthāya kuryāt tasmāt sadaiva hi sarvāparādhaśamanam apāmārjanakaṃ param etat stotram idaṃ puṇyaṃ paṭhed āyuṣyavardhanam vināśāya ca rogāṇām avamṛtyukṣayāya ca vyāghrāpasmārakuṣṭhādi piśācoragarākṣasāḥ tasya pārśvaṃ na gacchanti stotram etad yathā paṭhet smarañ japann idaṃ stotraṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ nityaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati surūpatā manuṣyāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ ca dvijasattama karmaṇā jāyate yena tan mamākhyātum arhasi surūpāṇāṃ sugātrāṇāṃ suveṣāṇāṃ tathā mune nyūnaṃ tathādhikaṃ vāpi kiṃcid aṅgaṃ prajāyate samastaiḥ śobhanair aṅgair narāḥ kecit tathā dvija kāṇāḥ kubjāś ca jāyante truṭitaśravaṇās tathā narāṇāṃ yoṣitāṃ caiva samastāṅgsurūpatā karmaṇā yena bhavati tat sarvaṃ kathayāmala lāvaṇyagativākyāni sati rūpe mahāmate prayānti cārutāṃ rūpaṃ tenoktaḥ paramo guṇaḥ vākyalāvaṇyasaṃskāra- vilāsalalitā gatiḥ viḍambanā kurūpāṇāṃ strīpuṃsām abhijāyate rūpakāraṇabhūtāya yateta matimāṃs tataḥ karmaṇā tan mamācakṣva karma yac cārurūpadam samyak pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā hīdam upavāsāśritaṃ dvija kathayāmi yathā proktaṃ vasiṣṭhena mahātmanā vasiṣṭham ṛṣim āsīnaṃ saptarṣipravaraṃ patim papracchārundhatī praśnaṃ yad etad bhavatā vayam tasyāḥ sa paripṛcchantyā jagāda munisattamaḥ yat tac chṛṇuṣva dharmajña mameha vadato akhilam śrūyatāṃ mama yat pṛṣṭas tvayāhaṃ brahmavādini surūpatā nṛṇāṃ yena yoṣitāṃ copajāyate anabhyarcya yathānyāyam anārādhya ca keśavam rūpādikā guṇāḥ kena prāpyante anyena karmaṇā tasmād ārādhanīyo vai viṣṇur eva yaśasvini paratra prāptukāmena rūpasaṃpatsutādikam yas tu vāñchati dharmajñe rūpaṃ sarvāṅgaśobhanam nakṣatrapuruṣas tena saṃpūjyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ nakṣatrāṅgaṃ yathāhāraḥ samupoṣyati yo harim surūpair akhilāṅgaiś ca rūpavān abhijāyate yoṣitā ca paraṃ rūpam icchantyā jagataḥ patiḥ sa evārādhanīyo atra nakṣatrāṅgo janārdanaḥ nakṣatrarūpī bhagavān pūjyate puruṣottamaḥ mune yena vidhānena tan mamākhyātum arhasi caitramāsaṃ samārabhya viṣṇoḥ pādādipūjanam yathā kurvīta rūpārthī tan niśāmaya tattvataḥ nakṣatram ekam ekaṃ vai snātaḥ samyag upoṣitaḥ nakṣatrapuruṣasyāṅgaṃ pūjayet sādhvī cakriṇaḥ mūle pādau tathā jaṅghe rohiṇīṣv arcayec chubhe jānunī cāśvinīyoga āṣāḍhe corusaṃjñite phālgunīdvitaye guhyaṃ kṛttikāsu tathā kaṭim pārśve bhadrapadāyugme dve kukṣī revatīṣu ca anurādha uraḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ śraviṣṭhāsv abhipūjayet bhujayugmaṃ viśākhāsu haste caiva karadvayam punarvasāv aṅgulīṃś ca āśleṣāsu tathā nakhān jyeṣṭhāyāṃ pūjayed grīvaṃ śravaṇe śravaṇe tathā puṣye mukhaṃ tathā svātau daśanān abhipūjayet hanvau śatabhiṣāyoge maghāyoge ca nāsikām mṛgottamāṅge nayane pūjayed bhaktitaḥ śubhe citrāyoge lalāṭaṃ ca bharaṇyāṃ ca tathā śiraḥ saṃpūjanīyā vidvadbhiś cādrāsu ca śiroruhāḥ nakṣatrayogeṣv eteṣu pūjito jagataḥ patiḥ nakṣatrapuruṣākhyo ayaṃ yathāvat puruṣottamaḥ pāpāpahāraṃ kurute samyac chraddhāvatāṃ satām aṅgopāṅgāni caivāsya pāpādīni yaśasvini surūpāny abhijāyante sapta janmāntarāṇi vai sarvāṇi caiva bhadrāṇi śarīrārogyam uttamam saṃtatiṃ manasaḥ prītiṃ rūpaṃ cātīvaśobhanam vāṅmādhūryaṃ tathā kāntiṃ yac cānyad abhivāñchitam dadāti nakṣatrapumān pūjitaś ca janārdanaḥ upoṣya samyag eteṣu krameṇa rkṣeṣu śobhane saṃpūjanīyo bhagavān nakṣatrāṅgo janārdanaḥ gandhapuṣpādisaṃyuktaṃ pūjayitvā yadāvidhi jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā idaṃ codāharet tataḥ svarūpam ārogyam atīva varcasaṃ susaṃtatiṃ tv asthitabhaktim acyutām api sarvam etaṃ protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva ekapuruṣa mahāpuruṣa ṛkṣapuruṣa namo astu te pratinakṣatrayoge ca bhojanīyā dvijottamāḥ nakṣatrajñāya viprāya dadyād dānaṃ ca śaktitaḥ pārite ca punar dadyāt strīpūṃsāṃ cāruhāsini chattropānadyugaṃ caiva saptadhānyaṃ sakāñcanam ghṛtapātraṃ ca dharmajñe yac cānyad ativallabham strī vā sādhvī sadā viṣṇor ārādhanaparāyaṇā anenaiva vidhānena saṃpūjyaitad avāpnuyāt sarvakāmān avāpnoti samārādhya janārdanam prakārair bahubhir brahman yān yān icchati cetasā nṝṇāṃ strīṇāṃ ca viprarṣe nānyac chokasya kāraṇam apatyād adhikaṃ kiṃcid vidyate hy atra janmani aputratā mahad duḥkham atiduḥkhaṃ kuputratā aputraḥ sarvaduḥkhānāṃ hetubhūto mato mama dhanyās te ye sutaṃ prāpya sarvaduḥkhavivarjitam śastaṃ praśāntaṃ balinaṃ parāṃ nirvṛtim āgatāḥ svakarmanirataṃ nityaṃ devadvijaparāyaṇam śāstrajñaṃ dharmatattvajñaṃ dīnānāthajanāśrayam vinirjitāriṃ sarvasya manohṛdayanandanam devānukūlatāyuktaṃ yuktaṃ samyag guṇena ca mitrasvajanasammāna- labdhanirvāṇam uttamam yaḥ prāpnoti sutaṃ tasmān nānyo dhanyataro bhuvi so aham icchāmi tac chrotuṃ tvattaḥ karma mahāmune yenedṛglakṣaṇaḥ putraḥ prāpyate bhuvi mānavaiḥ evam etan mahābhāga pitroḥ putrasamudbhavam duḥkhaṃ prayāty upaśamaṃ tena yeneha kenacit atrāpi śrūyatāṃ vṛttaṃ yat pūrvam abhavan mune utpattau kārtavīryasya haihayasya mahātmanaḥ kṛtavīryo mahīpālo haihayānām abhūt purā tasya śīladhanā nāma babhūva varavarṇinī patnī sahasrapravarā mahiṣī śīlamaṇḍanā sā tv aputrā mahābhāgā maitreyīṃ paryapṛcchata guṇavatputralābhāya kṛtāsanaparigrahām tayā ca pṛṣṭā vai samyag maitreyī brahmavādinī kathayām āsa paramaṃ nāmnānantavrataṃ vratam sarvakāmaphalāvāpti- kārakaṃ pāpanāśanam tasyāḥ sā putralābhāya rājaputrās tapasvinī yo ayam icchen naraḥ kāmaṃ nārī vā varavarṇini sa taṃ samārādhya vibhuṃ samāpnoti janārdanam mārgaśīrṣe mṛgaśiro bhīru yasmin dine bhavet tasmin saṃprāśya gomūtraṃ snāto niyatamānasaḥ puṣpair dhūpais tathā gandhair upahāraiḥ svaśaktitaḥ vāmapādam anantasya pūjayed varavarṇini anantaḥ sarvakāmānām anantaṃ bhagavān phalam dadātv anantaṃ ca punas tad evāstv anyajanmani anantapuṇyopacayaṃ karoty etan mahāvratam yathābhilaṣitāvāptiṃ kurvan mā kṣayam etu ca ity uccāryābhipūjyainaṃ yathāvad vidhinā naraḥ samāhitamanā bhūtvā praṇipātapuraḥsaram viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād anantaḥ prīyatām iti samuccārya tato naktaṃ bhuñjīyāt tailavarjitam tataś ca pauṣe puṣyarkṣe tathaiva bhagavatkaṭim vāmām abhyarcayet kṛtvā gomūtraprāśanaṃ budhaḥ anantaḥ sarvakāmānām iti coccārayed budhaḥ bhuñjīta ca tathā vipraṃ vācayitvā yathāvidhi māghe maghāsu tadvac ca bāhuṃ devasya pūjayet skandhaṃ ca phalgunīyoge phālgune māsi bhāmini caturṣv eteṣu gomūtra- prāśanaṃ nṛpanandini brāhmaṇāya tathā dadyāt tilān kanakam eva ca devasya dakṣiṇaskandhaṃ caitre citrāsu pūjayet tathaiva prāśanaṃ cātra pañcagavyam udāhṛtam vipre vācanake dadyād yāvan māsacatuṣṭayam vaiśākhe ca viśākhāsu bāhuṃ saṃpūjya dakṣiṇam tathaivoktayavān dadyāt tadvan naktaṃ bhujikriyā kaṭipūjāṃ ca jyeṣṭhāsu jyeṣṭhamūle śubhavrate āṣāḍhāsu tathāṣāḍhe kuryāt pādārcanaṃ śubhe padadvayaṃ ca śravaṇe śrāvaṇe subhru pūjayet ghṛtaṃ viprāya dātavyaṃ prāśanīyaṃ tathā dadhi kārttikānteṣu māseṣu prāśanaṃ dānam eva ca etad eva samākhyātaṃ devaṃ tadvac ca pūjayet guhyaṃ proṣṭhapadāyoge māsi bhādrapade arcayet tadvad āśvayuje pūjyaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāśvinīṣu vai kuryāt samāhitamanāḥ snānaprāśanaśaucavān anantaśirasaḥ pūjāṃ kārttike kṛttikāsu ca yasmin yasmin dine pūjā tatra tatra tadā dine nāmānantasya japtavyaṃ kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu ghṛtenānantam uddiśya pūrvamāsacatuṣṭayam kurvīta homaṃ caitrādau śālinā kulanandini kṣīreṇa śrāvaṇādau tu homaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam śastaṃ tu sarvamāseṣu haviṣyānnaṃ ca bhojanam evaṃ dvādaśabhir māsaiḥ pāraṇaṃ tritayaṃ śubhe pārite samavāpnoti sarvān eva manorathān putrārthibhir vittakāmair bhṛtyadārān abhīpsubhiḥ prārthayadbhiś ca kartavyam ārogyabalasaṃpadam etad vrataṃ mahābhāge puṇyaṃ svastyayanapradam anantavratasaṃjñaṃ vai sarvapāpapraṇāśanam tat kuruṣvaiva devi tvaṃ vrataṃ śīladhane varam viśiṣṭaṃ sarvalokasya yadi putram abhīpsasi iti śīladhanā śrutvā maitreyīvacanaṃ śubham cacāraitad vratavaraṃ susamāhitamānasā putrārthinyās tatas tasyā vratenānena suvrata viṣṇus tutoṣa tuṣṭe ca viṣṇau sā suṣuve sutam tasya vai jātamātrasya pravavāv anilaḥ śivaḥ nīrajaskam abhūd vyoma mudaṃ prāpākhilaṃ jagat devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca prajagur divi gandharvā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ dharme manaḥ samastasya dālbhya lokasya cābhavat tasya nāma pitā cakre tanayasyārjuneti vai kṛtavīryasutatvāc ca kārtavīryo babhūva saḥ tenāpi bhagavān viṣṇur dattātreyasvarūpavān ārādhito atimahatā tapasā dālbhya bhūbhṛtā tasya tuṣṭo jagannāthaś cakravartitvam uttamam dadau śauryabale cāti- sakalāny āyudhāni ca sa ca vavre varaṃ deva vadhas tvatto bhaved iti purānusmaraṇaṃ jñānaṃ bhītānāṃ cārtināśanam smaraṇād upakāritvaṃ jagato asya jagatpate tam āha devadeveśaḥ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇaḥ sarvam etan mahābhāga tava bhūpa bhaviṣyati yaś ca prabhāte rātrau ca tvāṃ naraḥ kīrtayiṣyati namo astu kārtavīryāyety abhidhāsyati caiva yaḥ tilaprasthapradānasya sa naraḥ puṇyam āpsyati anaṣṭadravyatā caiva tava nāmābhikīrtanaiḥ bhaviṣyati mahīpālety uktvā taṃ prayayau hariḥ sa cāpi varam āsādya prasannād garuḍadhvajāt pālayām āsa bhūpālaḥ saptadvīpāṃ vasuṃdharām teneṣṭaṃ vividhair yajñaiḥ samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ jitvārivargam akhilaṃ dharmataḥ pālitāḥ prajāḥ anantavratamāhātmyād āsādya tanayaṃ ca tam pitroḥ putrodbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāsīt svalpam api dvija evam etat samākhyātam anantākhyaṃ vrataṃ tava yac cīrtvā rājapatnī sā kārtavīryam asūyata yaś caitac chṛṇuyāj janma kārtavīryasya mānavaḥ strī vā duḥkham apatyotthaṃ sapta janmāni nāśnute rūpasaṃpat samākhyātā strīpuṃsāṃ jāyate śubhā samupoṣya jagannāthaṃ nakṣatrapuruṣaṃ harim vāso'tiśobhanaṃ cāru- vastrādyābharaṇojjvalam gṛhaṃ sarvaguṇopetam aśeṣopaskarānvitam karmaṇā yena viprarṣe toṣito madhusūdanaḥ dadāti bhagavān karma tan no vistarato vada yan māṃ pṛcchasi dālbhya tvaṃ gṛhopaskarabhūṣaṇam narāṇāṃ jāyate yena tat sarvaṃ kathayāmi te nandā bhadrā jayā riktā pūrṇā ca dvijasattama tithayo vai samākhyātāḥ pratipatkramasaṃjñayā pañcamī daśamī caiva tathā pañcadaśī tithiḥ pūrṇā etāḥ samākhyātāṣ tithayo munisattama mṛdā dhātuvikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā viṣṇor āyatane tāsu yaḥ karoty upalepanam pravātāvātaguṇavad varṣāsv atimanoramam anuliptaṃ śubhākāraṃ sugṛhaṃ labhate mune pūrṇaṃ dhānyahiraṇyādyair maṇimuktāphalojjvalam pratyāsannajalābhogaṃ gṛham āpnoti śobhanam sāmnatasvajanānāṃ yat sarveṣām uttamottamam tad āpnoti gṛhaṃ brahmann anulepanakṛn naraḥ yenānulipte tiṣṭhanti viṣṇvāyatanabhūtale brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśaḥ śūdrāḥ sādhvyas tathā striyaḥ tasya pūṇyaphalaṃ dālbhya śrūyatāṃ yat prajāyate apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ muktāhāragaṇojjvalam śreṣṭhaṃ sarvavimānānāṃ svarge dhiṣṇyam avāpnute yāvatyas tithayo liptaṃ divyābdāṃs tāvato dvija tasmin vimāne sa naraḥ strī vā tiṣṭhati sattama sugandhagandhasadvastra- sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ gandharvāpsarasāṃ saṃbhaiḥ pūjyamānaḥ sa tiṣṭhati liptaṃ ca yāvato hastān viṣṇor āyatanaṃ dvija tāvadyojanavistīrṇa- svargasthānādhipo hi saḥ pūjyamānaḥ suragaṇaiḥ śītoṣṇādivivarjitaḥ manojñagātro viprendras tiṣṭhaty astāghasaṃhatiḥ cyutas tasmād ihāgamya viśiṣṭe jāyate kule tato asya sadgṛhavaraṃ martyaloke abhijāyate na tatra tāvad dāridryaṃ nopasargā na vā kaliḥ na cāpi mṛtaniṣkrāntir yāvaj jīvaty asau dvija viṣṇuḥ samastabhūtāni sasarjaitāni yāni vai teṣāṃ madhye jagaddhātur atīveṣṭā vasuṃdharā kṛte saṃmārjane tasyās tathaivoparilepane prayāti paramaṃ toṣaṃ vaiṣṇavīyaṃ mahī yataḥ brahman yena vidhānena devāgāropalepalam kartavyaṃ puruṣaiḥ samyak strībhir vā tad udīraya riktāyās tu tither madhye kuryāt saṃkalpam ātmanaḥ upalepanakṛd vipro viṣṇor āyatane bhuvi dvitīye ahni tato devaṃ praṇamya yatamānasaḥ dharaṇīpitaraṃ viṣṇum idaṃ vākyam udīrayet tvaṃ sarvabhūtaprabhavo jagatpate tvayy etad īśeśa jagat pratiṣṭhitam tvam eva bhūtāni yatas tato ahaṃ tvām pūjayāmy adya mahīsvarūpam tvaṃ mahī jagatāṃ nātha sarvanātha namo astu te śuśrūṣitaḥ prasīdeśa bhuvo lepanakarmaṇā ity uccārya kṣitau kṣiptvā prathamaṃ dhāranītale puṣpāṇi vā dvijaśreṣṭha yaḥ karoty anulepanam na tasya jāyate bhaṅgo gārhasthyasya kadācana yā ca nārī karoty evaṃ yathāvad anulepanam nāpnoti sā ca vaidhavyaṃ gṛhabhaṅgaṃ kadācana kṛtvopalepanaṃ bhūyaḥ praṇipatya janārdanam snāto viṣṇuṃ samabhyarcya idaṃ vākyam udīrayet prasīda bhūdharānanta mayā yad upalepanam kṛtaṃ tena samastaṃ me nāśam abhyetu pātakam evaṃ saṃpūjya bhuñjīyād aparāhne dvijottama svanulipte mahābhāge bhuktvā limpec ca tat punaḥ pakṣe pakṣe trirātraṃ tu yaḥ karoty upalepanam sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaṃ gacchaty asaṃśayam tatkṣayāt svargeloke tu jāto gṛhavaraṃ yathā samāpnoti yathākhyātaṃ tat sarvaṃ tava sattama sarvābharaṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvopaskaradhānyavat gomahiṣyādisaṃbhogaṃ gṛham āpnoti mānavaḥ tasmād abhīpsatā samyag gārhasthyam avikhaṇḍitam viṣṇor āyatane kāryaṃ sarvadaivopalepanam saptadvīpavatīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yathendras tridivaṃ tathā alpopalepanād yasya māndhātā sakalāṃ mahīm avāpa viṣṇvāyatanaṃ nopalimpeta ko hi tat dīpaṃ prayacchati naro viṣṇor āyatane hi yaḥ sadakṣiṇasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam kārttike tu viśeṣeṇa kaumude māsi dīpakam dattvā yat phalam āpnoti dālbhya tat kena labhyate dālbhyānyad api vakṣyāmi purāvṛttam idaṃ śṛṇu vidarbharājatanayā lalitā yad uvāca ha vidarbharāṭ citraratho babhūvāstraviśāradaḥ tasya putraśataṃ rājño jajñe pañcadaśottaram ekaiva kanyā dālbhyāsīl lalitā nāmanāmataḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā bhrātṝṇāṃ pitur eva ca samastabhṛtyavargasya mātṝṇāṃ svajanasya ca tathaiva pauravargasya yaś cānyo dadṛśe śubhām tasya tasyāticārvaṅgī babhūveṣṭā dvijottama tāṃ dadau kāśirājāya sa pitā cāruvarmane upayeme ca tāṃ subhrūṃ cāruvarmā mahīpatiḥ śatāny anyāni bhāryāṇāṃ trīṇy āsaṃś cāruvarmaṇaḥ tāsāṃ madhye agramahiṣī lalitā tasya cābhavat sā ca nityaṃ jagaddhātur devadevasya cakriṇaḥ dīpavartiparā tadvat tailasyāharaṇodyatā viṣṇor āyatane tasyāḥ sahasraṃ dvijasattama dīpānāṃ vai prajajvāla divārātram atandritam tasyā dyutiparābhūtās tasyā lāvaṇyanirjitāḥ sarvāḥ sapatnyo lalitāṃ papracchur idam āditaḥ lalite vada bhadraṃ te bhadraṃ te lalite vada kautūhalaparāḥ sarvā yat pṛcchāmas tad ucyatām viṣaye sati vaktavyaṃ yan mayā tad ihocyatām nāhaṃ matsariṇī bhadrā na ca rāgādidūṣitā bhavatyo mama sarvāsāṃ bhavatīnām ahaṃ tathā apṛthagbhartṛsāmanyā devalokābhikāmukāḥ pūrvaṃ yūyam ahaṃ caiva bhavatīnāṃ sadharmiṇī na tathā puṣpadhūpeṣu na tathā dvijapūjane prayatnaṃ tava paśyāmo viṣṇor āyatane śubhe yathāhani tathā rātrau yathā rātrau tathāhani tava dīpapradānāya yathā subhru sadodyamaḥ tad etat kathayāsmākaṃ lalite kautukaṃ param manyāmo dīpadānasya bhavatyā viditaṃ phalam evam uktā tatas tābhir lalitā lalitaṃ vacaḥ vyājahāra sapatnīs tā na kiṃcid api bhāminī punaḥ punaś ca sā tābhir bahuṣo dālbhya coditā dākṣiṇyasārā lalitā kathāyām āsa bhāminī kautukaṃ bhavatīnāṃ ced atīvālpe api vastuni tad eṣā kathayāmy etad yad vṛttaṃ mama śobhanāḥ sauvīrarājasya purā maitreyo abhūt purohitaḥ tena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ devikātaṭe ahany ahani śuśrūṣāṃ puṣpadhūpopalepanaiḥ dīpadānādibhiś caiva cakre tatra sa vai dvijaḥ kārttike dīpako brahman pradattas tena vai tadā āsīn nirvāṇabhūyiṣṭho devārcāpurato niśi devatāyatane cāsaṃ tatrāham api mūṣikā pradīpavartiharaṇe kṛtabuddhir varānanāḥ gṛhītā ca mayā vartir vṛṣadaṃśo nanāda ca naṣṭā cāhaṃ tadā tasya mārjārasya bhayāturā vartiprāntena naśyantyā sa dīpaḥ prerito mayā jajvāla pūrvavad dīptyā tasminn āyatane punaḥ mṛtāhaṃ ca tato jātā vaidarbhī rājakanyakā jātismarā kāntimatī bhavatīnāṃ samā guṇaiḥ eṣa prabhāvo dīpasya kārttike māsi śobhanāḥ dattasya viṣṇvāyatane yasyeyaṃ vyuṣṭir uttamā asaṃkalpitam apy asya preraṇaṃ yat kṛtaṃ mayā viṣṇvāyatanadīpasya yasyedaṃ bhujyate phalam lobhābhibhūtā hartuṃ taṃ pradīpam aham āgatā avaśenaiva tadvartyā preraṇaṃ tatra me kṛtam tato jātismṛtir janma mānuṣyaṃ śobhanaṃ vapuḥ vaśyaḥ patiḥ pṛthivīśaḥ kiṃ punar dīpadāyinām etasmāt kāraṇād dīpān aham etān aharniśam prayacchāmi harer dhāmni jñātam asya hi yat phalam bhavatīnām idaṃ satyaṃ mayoktaṃ keśavālaye mūṣikatvād ahaṃ yena karmaṇā siddhim āgatā eṣa prabhāvo dīpasya kārttike māsi sattama viṣṇvāyatanadattasya jagāda lalitā yathā dine dine jagannātha keśaveti samāhitaḥ dadāti kārttike yas tu viṣṇvāyatanadīpakam jātismaratvaṃ prajñāṃ ca prākāśyaṃ sarvavastuṣu avyāhatendriyatvaṃ ca saṃprāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ śeṣakāle ca cakṣuṣmān medhāvī dīpado naraḥ jāyate narakaṃ vāpi tamaḥsaṃjñaṃ na paśyati ekādaśīṃ dvādaśīṃ vā pratipakṣaṃ ca yo naraḥ dīpaṃ dadāti kṛṣṇāya tasyāpi śṛṇu yat phalam suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyaṃ manojñam atiśobhanam dīpamālākulaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ so adhirohati tasmād āyatane viṣṇor dadyād dīpaṃ dvijottama tāṃś ca dattān na hiṃseta na ca tailaviyojitān kurvīta dīpahartā tu mūko andho jāyate yataḥ jāyate narakaṃ cāpi tapaḥsaṃjñaṃ sa paśyati andhe tāmasi duṣpāre narake patitān kila vikrośamānān kṣutkṣāmāñ jagāda yamakiṃkaraḥ vilāpair alam atrāpi kiṃ vo vilapite phalam yadā pramādibhiḥ pūrvam ātmātyantam upekṣitaḥ pūrvam ālocitaṃ naitat kim apy ante bhaviṣyati idānīṃ yātanābhogaḥ kiṃ vilāpaḥ kariṣyati deho dināni svalpāni viṣayāś cātidurdharāḥ etat ko na vijānāti yena yūyaṃ pramādinaḥ jantujanmasahasrebhya etasmin mānuṣyo yadi tatrāpy ativimūḍhatvāt kiṃ bhogān abhidhāvati viruddhaviṣayāsvāda- muditair hasitaṃ ca yat bhavadbhir āgataṃ duḥkhaṃ vilāpapariṇāmikam adyakālikayā buddhyā yad āgāmi na cintitam paritāpāya taj jātaṃ duḥkhaṃ karmavipākajam svalpam āyur manuṣyāṇāṃ tadante paratantratā bhujyate ca kṛtaṃ pūrvam etat kiṃ vo na cintitam yad abhūt paradāreṣu prītaye aṅgakucādikam yātanāduḥkharūpāya narake ca tad āgatam paradāramanohāri yad bhavadbhir agīyata hā māta ityādi rutaṃ tad idānīṃ vilapyate saṃdigdhaparalokānām aihike nihatātmanām mṛtānāṃ svakṛtaṃ karma paścāttāpāya kevalam muhūrtārdhasukhāsvāda- lubdhānām akṛtātmanām anekavarṣakoṭiṣu duḥkhadaṃ karma jāyate hā mātas tāta tāteti bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ vilapyate śubhāśubhaṃ nijaṃ karma tad adya hy atra bhujyate putradāragṛhakṣetra- hitāya satatodyatāḥ na kurvatni kathaṃ mūḍhāḥ svalpam apy ātmano hitam vañcito asau mayā labdham idam asmād upāyataḥ na vetti kaścid ātmārthaṃ vetti prakramato naraḥ na vetti sūryacandrādīn kālam ātmānam eva ca sākṣibhūtān aśeṣasya śubhasyehāśubhasya ca janmāny anyāni jāyante putradārādidehinām tadarthaṃ yat kṛtaṃ karma tasya janmaśatāni tat aho mohasya māhātmyaṃ mamatvaṃ narakeṣv api krandate mātaraṃ tātaṃ pīḍyamāno api yat svayam evam ākṛṣṭacittānāṃ viṣayāsvādatarṣulaiḥ nṝṇāṃ na jāyate buddhiḥ paramārthāvalokinī tathā ca viṣayāsaktiṃ karoty avirataṃ manaḥ ko atibhāro harer nāmni jihvāyāḥ parikīrtane vartitaile alpamaulye api yad agnir labhyate mudhā ato adhikataro lobhaḥ ko vaś citte abhavat tadā yeneyaṃ teṣu hasteṣu svātantrye sati dīpakaḥ mahāphalo viṣṇugṛhe na datto narakāpahaḥ na vo vilapite kiṃcid idānīṃ dṛśyate phalam asvātantrye vilapatāṃ svātantrye atipramādinām avaśyaṃpātinaḥ prāṇā bhoktā jīvo hy aharniśam dattaṃ ca labhate bhoktā samaye viṣayān iti etat svātantryavadbhir vo yuktam āsīt parīkṣitum idānīṃ kiṃ vilāpena sahadhvaṃ yad upāgatam yady etad anabhīṣṭaṃ vo yad duḥkhaṃ samupasthitam tad bhūyo api matiḥ pāpe na kartavyā kathaṃcana kṛte api pāpake karmaṇy ajñānād aghanāśanam kartavyam avyavasthitaṃ smaradbhir madhusūdanam nārakās tadvacaḥ śrutvā tām ūcur atiduḥkhitāḥ kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhās tṛṣayā parisphuṭitatālukāḥ bho bho sādho kṛtaṃ karma yad asmābhis tad ucyatām narakasthair vipāko ayaṃ bhujyate yasya dāruṇaḥ yuṣmābhir yauvanonmāda- muditair avivekibhiḥ dyūtodyotāya govinda- gṛhād dīpaḥ purā hṛtaḥ tenāsmin narake ghore kṣuttṛṣṇāparipīḍitāḥ bhavantaḥ patitās tīvra- śītavātavidāritāḥ etat te dīpadānasya pradīpaharaṇasya ca puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ ca kathitaṃ keśavāyatane dvija sarvatraiva hi dīpasya pradānaṃ dvija śasyate viśeṣeṇa jagaddhātuḥ keśavasya niveśane ye andhā mūkā niḥśrutā nirvivekā hīnās tais taiḥ sādhanair vipravarya tais tair dīpāḥ sādhulokapradattā devāgārād anyato vipraṇītāḥ āhlādaṃ cakṣuṣaḥ prītiṃ karoti manasas tathā keṣāṃcid darśanaṃ brahman manuṣyāṇām aharniśam udvejanīyā bhūtānām animittaṃ tathāpare vadante vipriyaṃ naiva prītiṃ kurvanti mānavāḥ etad yasya phalaṃ brahman dānasya tapaso athavā upavāsasya vā tan me yathāvad vaktum arhasi aprītidasya viprarṣe vipāko yasya karmaṇaḥ manuṣyāṇām aśeṣaṃ vai tan mamācakṣva sattama devabrāhmaṇavedeṣu yajñeṣu ca narādhamaiḥ yair jugupsā kṛtā dālbhya manasāpy atimānibhiḥ teṣāṃ saṃdarśanāt sarvo na sukhaṃ vindate dvija vadanty apy anukūlāni na teṣu prīyate janaḥ sparśād udvijate lokaḥ kaṭu teṣāṃ ca darśanam saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ ca nindā vai kṛtā vedadvijātike tasmān na nindāṃ vedādau na jugupsāṃ ca paṇḍitaḥ yajñādau ca naraḥ kuryād ya icchec chreya ātmanaḥ yais tu prītiḥ samasteṣu vedadevadvijātiṣu yajñādike caiva kṛtā dālbhya taddarśanaṃ nṛṇām āhlādaś cakṣuṣaḥ prītir manaso nirvṛtiḥ parā saṃbhāṣaṇe tathāhlādaḥ sarvalokasya jāyate stutāḥ praśastāḥ saṃprītyā pūjitā bahumānataḥ śreyaḥ paraṃ prayacchanti devā vedā makhā dvijāḥ lokadvaye api cāprītiṃ paśuputradhanakṣayam kurvanti dvijaśārdūla eta eva vininditāḥ eta eva samākhyātāḥ stavādigrahaṇe guṇāh nindāyāḥ śravaṇe doṣa eteṣām evam eva hi tasmāt stavyāḥ praśaṃsyāś ca devā vedā dvijātayaḥ yajñāś ca manasāpy eṣāṃ na nindām ācared budhaḥ anāyāsena bhagavan dānenānyena kenacit pāpaṃ praśamam āyāti yena tad vaktum arhasi śṛṇu dālbhya mahāpuṇyāṃ dvādaśīṃ pāpanāśanīm yām upoṣya paraṃ puṇyaṃ prāpnute śraddhayānvitaḥ māghamāse tu saṃprāpta āṣāḍhārkṣaṃ bhaved yadi mūlaṃ vā kṛṣṇapakṣasya dvādaśyāṃ niyatas tadā gṛhṇīyāt puṇyaphaladaṃ vidhānaṃ tasya me śṛṇu devadevaṃ samabhyarcya susnātaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ kṛṣṇanāmnā ca saṃstūya ekādaśyāṃ mahāmate upoṣito dvitīye ahni punaḥ saṃpūjya keśavam saṃstūya nāmnā ca tataḥ kṛṣṇākhyena punaḥ punaḥ dadyāt tilāṃs tu viprāya kṛṣṇo me prīyatām iti snānaprāśanayoḥ śastās tathā kṛṣṇatilā mune tilaprarohe jāyante yāvatsaṃkhyās tilā dvija tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate jātaś cehāpy arogo asau naro janmani janmani nāndho na badhiraś ceha na kuṣṭhī na jugupsitaḥ bhavaty etām uṣitvā tu tilākhyāṃ dvādaśīṃ naraḥ viṣṇoḥ prīṇanam atroktaṃ samāpte varṣapāraṇe pūjāṃ ca kuryād viprāya bhūyo dadyāt tathā tilān anena dālbhya vidhinā tiladānād asaṃśayam mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvair nirāyāsena mānavaḥ udbhṛtapulakaḥ sarvān nirāyāsena mānavaḥ dānavidhis tathā śraddhā sarvapātakaśāntaye nārthaḥ prabhūto nāyāsaḥ śārīro munisattama anantasyāprameyasya vyāpinaḥ paramātmanaḥ nāmnāṃ nakṣatrabhedena tithibhedena vā dvija dānabhedena cākhyāto vibhinnaphaladas tvayā viśeṣaḥ kṣetrabhedena kathyatāṃ yadi vidyate yatha rkṣatithibhedena teṣām eva punaḥ punaḥ viśeṣaḥ kathito nāmnāṃ viśeṣaphaladāyakaḥ tathā kṣetraviśeṣeṇa bhedaṃ nāmakṛtaṃ vada śṛṇu dālbhya yathākhyātam arjunāya mahātmane praṇipātaprasannena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā kṛte bhārāvataraṇe nivṛtte bhārate raṇe āgamya śibiraṃ viṣṇū rathasthaḥ prāha phālgunam iṣudhīgāṇḍivaṃ caiva samādāya tvarānvitaḥ avatīrya rathād vīra dūre tiṣṭḥa dhanaṃjaya avarokṣyāmy ahaṃ paścād avatīrṇe tatas tvayi etat kuru mahābāho mā vilambasva phālguna evam uktas tathā cakre vākyaṃ pārtho gadādhṛtaḥ avārohat tataḥ paścāt svayam eva janārdanaḥ avatīrṇe jagannāthe svasamutthena vahninā jajvāla sa rathaḥ sadyo bhasmībhūtaś ca tatkṣaṇāt sopaskarapatāko atha sadhvajaḥ saha vājibhiḥ sacchattro vahninā sadyo ratho bhasmalavīkṛtaḥ vahninā ca yathā kāṣṭhaṃ sadyo bhasmalavīkṛtam tad adbhutaṃ mahad dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ papraccha keśavam hṛṣṭaromā dvijaśreṣṭha bhayavismayagadgadaḥ āścaryaṃ puruṣavyāghra kim etan madhusūdana vināgninā ratho ayaṃ me dagdhas tṛṇacayo yathā bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādīnāṃ karṇādīnāṃ ca phālguna dagdho astrair vividhair eṣa pūrvam eva rathas tava madadhiṣṭhitatvāt kaunteya na śīrṇo ayaṃ tadābhavat pratyahan niśi cakreṇa mayā nyastena rakṣitaḥ so ayaṃ dagdho mahābāho tvayy adya kṛtakarmaṇi mayāvatārite cakre mā pārtha kuru vismayam kaṃ bhavantam ahaṃ vidyām atimānuṣaceṣṭitam karmaṇātyadbhutenāgnir dhūmenaiveha sūcitaḥ pūrvam eva yathākhyātaṃ raṇārambhe tavārjuna kālo asmi lokanāśāya pravṛtto ahaṃ yathādhunā tan mayā sādhitaṃ kāryaṃ tridaśānāṃ tathā bhuvaḥ bhārāvataraṇārthāya mama janma mahītale evam ukto arjunaḥ samyak praṇipatya janārdanam tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir udbhūtapulakas tataḥ namo astu te cakradharograrūpa namo astu te śārṅgadharāruṇākṣa namo astu te abhyudyatakhaḍga raudra namo astu vibhrāntagadāntakārin bhayena sanno asmi savepathena nāṅgāni me deva vaśaṃ prayānti vācaḥ samuccārayataḥ skhalanti keśā hṛṣīkeśa samucchvasanti kālo bhavān kālakarālakarmā yenaitad evaṃ kṣayam akṣayātman kṣatraṃ samudbhūtaruṣā samastam nītaṃ bhuvo bhāravirecanāya prasīda kartar jaya lokanātha prasīda sarvasya ca pālanāya sthitau samastasya ca kālarūpa kṛtodyameśāna jayāvyayātman na me dṛg eṣā tava rūpam etad draṣṭuṃ samarthā kṣubhito asmi cāntaḥ pūrvasvabhāvasthitavigraho api saṃlakṣyase atyantam asaumyarūpa smarāmi rūpaṃ tava viśvarūpaṃ yad darśitaṃ pūrvam abhūn mamaiva yasmin mayā viśvam aśeṣam āsīd dṛṣṭaṃ sayakṣoragadevadaityam sā me smṛtir darśanabhāṣanādi- prakurvato nātha gatā praṇāśam kālo aham asmīty udite tvayā tu samāgateyaṃ punar apy ananta kartā bhavān kāraṇam apy aśeṣam kāryaṃ ca niṣkāraṇa kartṛrūpa ādau sthitau saṃharaṇe ca deva viśvasya viśvaṃ svayam eva ca tvam brahmā bhavān viśvasṛg ādikāle viśvasya rūpo asi tathā visṛṣṭau viṣṇuḥ sthitau pālanabaddhakakṣo rudro bhavān saṃharaṇe prajānām ebhis tribhir nātha vibhūtibhedair yaś cintyate kāraṇam ātmano api vedāntavedoditam asti viṣṇoḥ padaṃ dhruvaṃ tat paramaṃ tvam eva yan nirguṇaṃ sarvavikalpahīnam anantam asthūlam arūpagandham paraṃ padaṃ vedavido vadanti tvam eva tac chabdarasādihīnam yathā hi mūle viṭapī mahādrumaḥ pratiṣṭhitaskandhavarograśākhaḥ tathā samastāmaramartyatiryag- vyomādiśabdādimayaṃ tvayīdam muñcāmi yāvat paramāyudhāni vairiṣv anantāhavadurmadeṣu dṛṣṭvā hi tāvat sahasā patanto nūnaṃ tavaivācyuta sa prabhāvaḥ hatā hatās te bhavato dṛśaiva mayā punaḥ keśava śastrapūgaiḥ kāh karṇabhīṣmapramukhān vijetuṃ yuṣmatprasādena vinā samarthaḥ triśūlapāṇir mama yaḥ purastān niṣūdayan vairibalaṃ jagāma jñātaṃ mayā sāṃpratam etad īśa tava prasādasya hi sā vibhūtiḥ yamendravitteśajaleśavahni- sūryātmako yaś ca mamāstrapūgaḥ nāśāya nābhūt patito api kāye tvatsaṃnidhānasya hi so anubhāvaḥ bālye bhavān yāni cakāra deva karmāṇy asahyāni surāsurāṇām tair eva jānīma na yat paraṃ tvāṃ doṣaḥ sa nirdoṣo manuṣyatāyāḥ tālocchritāgraṃ gurubhārasāram āyāmavistāravad adyajātaḥ pādāgravikṣepavibhinnabhāṇḍaṃ cikṣepa ko anyaḥ śakaṭaṃ yathā tvam anyena kenācyuta pūtanāyāḥ prāṇaiḥ samaṃ pītam asṛgvimiśram tvayā yathā stanyam atīvabālye goṣṭhe ca bhagnau yamalārjunau tau viṣānaloṣṇāmbunipātabhīmam āsphoṭya ko vā bhuvi manuṣo anyaḥ nanarta pādābjanipīḍitasya phaṇaṃ samāruhya ca kāliyasya sureśasaṃdeśavirodhavatsu varṣatsu megheṣu gavān nimittam dināni saptāsti ca kasya śaktir govardhanaṃ dhārayituṃ kareṇa pralambacāṇūramukhān nihatya kaṃsāsuraṃ yasya bibheti śakraḥ tam aṣṭavarṣo nijaghāna ko anyo nirāyodho nātha manuṣyajanmā bāṇārtham abhyudyatam ugraśūlaṃ nirjitya saṃkhye tripurārim ekaḥ sakārttikeyajvaram astrabāhuṃ karoti ko bāṇam anacyuto anyaḥ kaḥ pārijātaṃ surasundarīṇāṃ sadopabhogyaṃ vijitendrasainyaḥ svargān mahīm ucchritavīryadhairyaḥ samānayām āsa yathā prabho tvam hatvā hayagrīvam udāravīryaṃ niśumbhaśumbhau narakaṃ ca ko anyaḥ jagrāha kanyāpuram ātmano arthaṃ prāgjyotiṣākhye nagare mahātman sthitau sthitas tvaṃ paripāsi viśvaṃ tais tair upāyair avinītabhītaiḥ maitrī na yeṣāṃ vinayāya tāṃs tān sarvān bhavān saṃharate avyayātman hitāya teṣāṃ kapilādirūpiṇā tvayānuśastā bahavo anujīvāḥ yeṣāṃ na maitrī hṛdi te na neyā viśvopakārī vadha eva teṣām itthaṃ bhavān duṣṭavadhena nūnaṃ viśvopakārāya vibho pravṛttaḥ sthitau sthitaṃ pālanam eva viṣṇuḥ karoti hanty antagato antarudraḥ etāni cānyāni ca duṣkarāṇi dṛṣṭāni karmāṇi tathāpi satyam manyāmahe tvāṃ jagataḥ prasūtiṃ kiṃ kurma māyā tava mohanīyam tvaṃ sarvam etat tvayi sarvam etat tvattas tathaitat tava caitad īśa etat svarūpaṃ tava sarvabhūtaṃ vibhūtibhedair bahubhiḥ sthitasya prasīda kṛṣṇācyuta vāsudeva janārdanānanta nṛsiṃha viṣṇo manuṣyasāmānyadhiyā yadīśa dṛṣṭo mayā tat kṣamasvādideva na vedmi sadbhāvam ahaṃ tavādya sadbhāvabhūtasya carācarasya yo vai bhavān ko api nato asmi tasmai manuṣyarūpāya caturbhujāya devadeva jagannātha sarvapāpaharo bhava hetumātras tv ahaṃ tatra tvayaitad upasaṃhṛtam prasīdeśa hṛṣīkeśa akṣauhiṇyā daśāṣṭa ca tvayā grastā bhuvo bhūtyai hetubhūtā hi madvidhāḥ vayam anye ca govinda narāḥ krīḍanakās tava madvidhaiḥ karaṇair deva karoṣi sthitipālanam yad atra sad asad vāpi kiṃcid uccāritaṃ mayā bhaktimān iti tat sarvaṃ kṣantavyaṃ mama keśava evaṃ stutas tataḥ prāha prītimāṃs taṃ janārdanaḥ pariṣvajya mahābāhuṃ samāśvāsya ca phālgunam prvāca bhagavān devaḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā yas tvāṃ vetti sa māṃ vetti yas tvām anu sa mām anu abhedenātmanā vedmī tvām ahaṃ pāṇḍunandana mamāṃśatvaṃ mahābāho jagataḥ pālanecchayā bhuvo bhārāvatārārthaṃ pṛthak pārtha mayā kṛtam devadaityoragā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāpsarāḥ rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca paśupakṣisarīsṛpāḥ vṛkṣagulmādayaḥ śailāḥ sarvabhūtāni cārjuna mamaivāṃśāni bhūtāni viddhi sarvāṇy ariṃdama bhagavan sarvabhūtātman sarvabhūteṣu vai bhavān paramātmasvarūpeṇa sthitaṃ vedmi tad avyayam kṣetreṣu yeṣu yeṣu tvaṃ cintanīyo mayācyuta cetasaḥ praṇidhānārthaṃ tan mamākhyātum arhasi yatra yatra ca yan nāma prītaye bhavataḥ stutau prasādasumukho nātha tan mamāśeṣato vada sarvagaḥ sarvabhūto ahaṃ na hi kiṃcid mayā vinā carācare jagaty asmin vidyate kurusattama tathāpi yeṣu sthāneṣu cintanīyo aham arjuna stotavyo nāmabhir yais tu śrūyatāṃ tad vadāmi te puṣkare puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ gayāyāṃ ca gadādharam lohadaṇḍe tathā viṣṇuṃ stuvaṃs tarati duṣkṛtam kṣvāmācye kumāraṃ nepāle lokabhāvanam rāghavaṃ citrakūṭe tu prabhāse daityasūdanam vṛndāvane ca govindaṃ mā stuvan puṇyabhāg bhavet mandodapāne vaikuṇṭhaṃ māhantre cācyutaṃ vibhum jayaṃ jayantyāṃ tadvac ca jayantaṃ hastināpure vārāhaṃ kardamāle tu kāśmīre cakrapāṇinam janārdanaṃ ca kubjāmre mathurāyāṃ ca keśavam kubjake śrīdharaṃ tadvad gaṅgādvāre surottamam śālagrāme mahāyogiṃ hariṃ govardhanācale piṇḍārake caturbāhuṃ śaṅkhoddhāre ca śaṅkhinam vāmanaṃ ca kurukṣetre yamunāyāṃ trivikramam vanamālaṃ ca kiṣkindhāyāṃ devaṃ raivatake dvija kāśījale mahāyogaṃ devaṃ cāmitatejasam vaiśākhayūpe ajitaṃ virajāyāṃ viprakṣayam viśveśvaraṃ tathā śoṇe kapilaṃ pūrvasāgare śvetadvīpapatiṃ cāpi gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame bhūdharaṃ devikānadyāṃ prayāge caiva mādhavam naranārāyaṇākhyaṃ ca tathā badarikāśrame samudre dakṣiṇe stavyaṃ padmanābheti phālguna dvārakāyāṃ tathā kṛṣṇaṃ stuvaṃs tarati durgatim rāmaṃ nāma mahendrādrau hṛṣīkeśaṃ tathārbude aśvatīrthe hayagrīvaṃ viśvarūpaṃ himācale nṛsiṃhaṃ kṛtasauce ca vipāśāyāṃ dvijapriyam naimiṣe yajñapuruṣaṃ jambūmārge tathācyutam anantaṃ saindhavāraṇye daṇḍake śāṅgadhāriṇam utpalāvartake śauriṃ narmadāyāṃ śriyaḥ patim dāmodaraṃ raivatake nandāyāṃ jalaśāyinam sarvayogeśvaraṃ caiva sindhusāgarasaṃgame sahyādrau devadeveśaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ māgadhe vane sarvapāpaharaṃ vindhye uḍreṣu puruṣottamam hṛdaye cāpi kaunteya paramātmānam ātmanaḥ vaṭe vaṭe vaiśravaṇaṃ catvare catvare śivam parvate parvate rāmaṃ sarvatra madhusūdanam naraṃ bhūmau tathā vyomni kaunteya garuḍadhvajam vāsudevaṃ ca sarvatra saṃsmarañ jyotiṣāṃ patim arcayan praṇamaṃs tu tvaṃ saṃsmaraṃś ca dhanaṃjaya eteṣv etāni nāmāni naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate sthāneṣv eteṣu mannāmnām eteṣāṃ prīṇanaṃ naraḥ dvijānāṃ prīṇanaṃ kṛtvā svargaloke abhijāyate nāmāny etāni kaunteya sthānāny etāni cātmavān jayaṃ vai pañcapañcāśat trisandhyaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ trīṇi janmāni yat pāpam avasthātritaye kṛtam tat kṣālayaty asaṃdigdhaṃ jāyate ca satāṃ kule dviṣkālaṃ vā japann eva divārātrau ca yat kṛtam tasmād vimucyate pāpāt sadbhāvaparamo naraḥ japtāny etāni kaunteya sakṛcchraddhāsamanvitam mocayante naraṃ pāpād yat tatraiva dine kṛtam dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ jayaṃ kuru kulodvaha grahānukūlatāṃ caiva karoty āśu na saṃśayaḥ upoṣito matparamaḥ sthāneṣv eteṣu mānavaḥ kṛtāyatanavāsaś ca prāpnoty abhimataṃ phalam utkrāntir apy aśeṣeṣu sthāneṣv eteṣu śasyate anyasthānāc chataguṇam eteṣv anaśanādikam yas tu matparamaḥ kālaṃ karoty eteṣu mānavaḥ devānām api pūjyo asau mama loke mahīyate yan na tāpāya vai puṃsāṃ bhavaty āmuṣmikaṃ kṛtam tāpāya yac ca bhavati tad ācakṣva mahāmune upavāsaprabhāvaṃ ca kṛṣṇārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ kathayeha mama brahman na ca tṛpyāmi kathyate śrūyatāṃ dālbhya yat pṛṣṭāḥ kautukād bhavatā vayam āmuṣmikaṃ na tāpāya yac ca tāpāya jāyate upoṣitaprabhāvaṃ ca kṛṣṇārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ kathayāmi yathāvṛttaṃ pūrvam eva mahāmate vaidiśaṃ nāma nagaraṃ prakhyātam iha sattama tatra vaiśyo abhavat pūrvaṃ vīrabhadra iti śrutaḥ bhāryājāmātṛduhitṛ- putrapautrasnuṣānvitaḥ prabhūtabhṛtyavargaś ca bahuvyāpārakārakaḥ putrapautrādibharaṇa- vyāsaktamatir eva ca paralokaṃ prati matis tasya cātyantadurmukhā cakārānudinaṃ so atha nyāyānyāyair dhanārjanam sarvatrānyatra niḥsnehaḥ parasve cātitarṣulaḥ na juhoty udite kāle na dadāty atitṛṣṇayā babhūva codyamas tasya putrādibharaṇe paraḥ nityanaimittikānāṃ ca hāniṃ cakre svakarmaṇām tṛṣṇābhibhūto viprarṣe svavargabharaṇādhṛtaḥ kālena gacchatā so atha mṛto vindhyāṭavītaṭe yātanādehabhṛt preto grīṣmakāle abhavan mune taṃ dadarśa mahābhāgo divyajñānasamanvitaḥ vedavedāntavid vidvān pipīto nāma vai dvijaḥ bhāskarasyāṃśubhir dīptair dahyantam anivāraṇaiḥ prataptavālukāmadhye tṛṣā cātyantapīḍitam kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhaṃ śuṣkāsyaṃ stabdhodvṛttavilocanam niṣkrāntajihvam aṅgeṣu visphoṭaiḥ sarvataś citam niśvāsāyāsakhedena viralāsyam anādaram śrāntaṃ makṣikayākīrṇaṃ durdagdhaṃ cātidāruṇam nijena karmaṇā baddham asamarthaṃ palāyane taṃ tādṛśam atho dṛṣṭvā gārdabheyo mahāmuniḥ pipītaḥ prāha viprarṣiḥ kāruṇyastimitaṃ vacaḥ jānann api tathā prāptaṃ tadanuṣṭhānajaṃ phalam jantos tasyopakārāya sarvato hlādayann iva adhaḥ sūryāṃśubhis taptair bahubhir yānapāṃsubhiḥ upary arkakarair ugrais tṛṣā cārtas tathā kṣudhā anyais tathādhibhir ghorair aviṣahyair avāraṇaiḥ kathayeha yathātattvam ekākī dahyase katham tasyaitad vacanaṃ śrutvā pipītasya savedanam yātanāstha uvācedaṃ kṛcchrād ucchvāsya mastakam brahman nālocitaṃ pūrvaṃ katham ante bhaviṣyati aśāśvate śāśvatadhīs tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ dhanāpaṇagṛhakṣetra- putradārahite rataḥ nātmano ahaṃ hitārambhī tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ idaṃ kariṣye kṛtvedaṃ kariṣyāmy aparaṃ tv idam itīcchāśatasaro ahaṃ tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ juhomi yadi tan nāsti dadāmi yadi sīdati kuṭumbam iti mūḍho aham tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ śītoṣṇavarṣābhibhavaṃ lobhāt soḍḥaṃ mayāśubham tad eva hi na dharmārthaṃ tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇām adattvāpoṣitā hi ye te anyatra kvāpi vartante dahyāmy eko atra durmatiḥ putrabhṛtyakalatreṣu mama tv ādṛtamānasaḥ kṛtvā karmāṇy asādhūni dahyāmy eko atra durmatiḥ mṛte mayi dhane tasminn anyāyopārjite mayā nūnaṃ mameti vartante dahyāmy eko atra durmatiḥ na hi naḥ pūjitā gehān nirgatā dvijasattamāḥ svavargahitakāmasya tena dahyāmy aharniśam yan me na pūjitā devāḥ kuṭumbaṃ poṣītaṃ param ekākī tena dahyāmi ye puṣṭās te anyato gatāḥ nityanaimittikaṃ karma kṛte yeṣāṃ na ma kṛtam ekākī tena dahyāmi tair manye kvāpi ramyate yan me parijanasyārthe kṛtaṃ karma śubhāśubham ekākī tena dahyāmi gatās te phalabhoginaḥ dārāḥ putrāś ca bhṛtyāś ca pāpavyāptyā mayaidhitāḥ ekākī tena dahyāmi gatās te phalabhoginaḥ putradārādibhṛtyārthe mayānyāyārthasaṃcayāḥ kṛtās tenātra dahyāmi bhuñjate apy anyato gatāḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ mayā bhuktam anyais tatkarmasaṃcitam dahyāmy eko aham atyantaṃ tyaktas taiḥ phalabhogibhiḥ yan mamatvābhibhūtena mayā dhanam upārjitam anyasya te adya kasyāpi kevalaṃ mama duṣkṛtam antarduḥkhena dagdho antar bahir dahyāmi bhānunā nāntarduḥkhaṃ na vā bhānuḥ pāpam eva dvidhā sthitam kaṃcit karmasamuddhāraṃ paśyasy asukhasāgarāt mama yenāham āhlādam āpnuyāṃ munisattama alpakālikam uddhāraṃ tava paśyāmy asaṃśayam prakṣīṇaprāyam etat te sukṛtaṃ cāsti te param atīte daśame janmany acyutārādhanecchayā sukarmajayadāṃ bhadra dvādaśīṃ tvam upoṣitaḥ tava tasyāḥ prabhāveṇa pāpam atyantadurjayam alpair ahobhiḥ saṃkṣīṇaṃ navapātre yathā jalam yad anyaḥ kṣapayed varṣais tad dinair bhavataḥ kṣayam gataṃ pāpam ayaṃ tasyāḥ prabhāvo atyantadurlabhaḥ śamaṃ pāpasya kurute jayaṃ sukṛtakarmaṇaḥ satkarmajayadā hy eṣā tato vai dvādaśī smṛtā yac caitad vedanārtena bhavatā paridevitam tat tathā nātra saṃdeho mamatā pāpahetukī pāpam atra kṛtaṃ pretya bhadra tāpāya jāyate āhlādāya tathā puṇyam iha puṇyakṛtāṃ nṛṇām vīrabhadraṃ samāśvāsya yayāv itthaṃ mahāmuniḥ so apy alpenaiva kālena tato mokṣam avāptavān evaṃ dālbhya pare loke yad atrāsukṛtaṃ kṛtam tat tāpāya sukhāyoktaṃ yad atraiva śubhaṃ kṛtam upavāsaprabhāvaś ca kathitas te mahāmune yenālpair eva divasair bhūri pāpaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam tasmān nareṇa puṇyāya patitavyaṃ na pātake upavāsāś ca kartavyāḥ sadaivātmahitaiṣiṇā saṃsārāsāratāṃ jñātvā viṣayāṃś cātitarṣulān kartavyaṃ yan mahābhāga puruṣeṇa tad ucyatām saṃsārāsāratāṃ jñātvā viṣayāṃś cātitarṣulān gṛddhis teṣv eva saṃtyājyā tattyāgo guṇavān nṛṇām yeṣām abdasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrair api no naraḥ bhogāt tṛptiṃ samāpnoti kas tair bhogair virajyate yāvato vāñchate bhogān ahany ahani mānavaḥ teṣāṃ sahasrabhāge api dālbhya prāptiṃ na vindati atha cet tan avāpnoti sahasraguṇitān naraḥ tathāpy atṛpta evāntam antakāle gamiṣyati tṛptaye ye na saṃprāptāḥ prāpyante ye na vāñchitāḥ buddhimān indriyārtheṣu teṣv asaṅgī sadā bhavet yeṣāṃ tṛptir na bhogena tyāgaś caivopakārakaḥ upoṣitavidhānena bhogāntyāgas tato varaḥ kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni narais tasmān mumukṣubhiḥ niṣkāmair dālbhya kāryāṇi phalāya ca phalepsubhiḥ atrāpy udāharantīmaṃ munayo munisattama dasrābhyāṃ saha saṃvādam ailasya ca mahātmanaḥ ailaḥ purūravāḥ pūrvaṃ babhūva manujeśvaraḥ cakame yaṃ mahābhāgam urvaśī surasundarī saṃtyajya tridaśāvāsaṃ rūpaudāryaguṇānvitam bheje tam urvaśī dālbhya budhasya tanayaṃ nṛpam nāsatyadasrau rūpeṇa devānām adhikau tataḥ urvaśīlobhanaṃ tasya rūpaṃ draṣṭuṃ samutsukau pratiṣṭhānaṃ puraṃ tasya budhaputrasya dhīmataḥ jagmatuḥ sumahābhāgau tasya dvāstham athocatuḥ kṣatto asmadvacanād ailaṃ brūhi tvaṃ vasudhādhipam draṣṭuṃ tavāśvinau prāptau rūpasaṃpadguṇaṃ ṇrpa tadehy atra mahābhāga ihāsmān saṃpraveśaya āścaryabhūtaṃ lokeṣu urvaśīlobhanaṃ vapuḥ tat kautukaṃ na kurute kasya pārthivapuṅgava āvāṃ samāgatau tasmāt tvāṃ draṣṭuṃ manujottama dvāsthas tatheti tāv āha praviveśa ca satvaram ācacakṣe ca tad rājñe nāsatyavacanaṃ dvija tac chrutvā vacanaṃ rājā dvāstham āha muhūrtakam vilambyatāṃ mahābhāgau tau brūhi vacanān mama vyāyāmatailasaṃsarga- malino na vibhūṣitaḥ prasādhanaṃ ca kṛtvāhaṃ niṣkramāmi tvarānvitaḥ niṣkramya sa tato dvāstho yathoktaṃ bhūbhṛtakhilam samācaṣṭa tato dālbhya tau ca bhūyas tam ūcatuḥ aprasādhitam evāśu bhavantaṃ vasudhādhipa paśyāvas tava bhūyo api tvāṃ drakṣyāvaḥ prasādhitam ity ukto nirgatas tūrṇaṃ bhavanād avanīpatiḥ tailābhyaktatanur dālbhya vyāyāmaparidhānadhṛk sa praṇāmaṃ tayoḥ kṛtvā kiṃcin nataśirā nṛpaḥ provāca yan mayā kāryaṃ bhavatos tad ihocyatām saptadvīpavatī pṛthvī putradārabalaṃ dhanam yac cānyad api tat sarvaṃ yuvayor me niveditam ity udāhṛtam ākarṇya nṛpater aśvināv api aṅgopāṅgādikaṃ sarvaṃ śanakais tāv apaśyatām śirolalāṭabāhuṃ sa- nayanādivilokanam kṛtvā ca taṃ mahīpālam ūcatus tāv idaṃ surau praviśya snāhi bhūpāla yathārthaiś ca vibhūṣaṇaiḥ vibhūṣitaṃ tu bhūyas tvāṃ drakṣyāvo avāṃ nareśvara tatheti coktvā sa nṛpaḥ praviveśa mahāmune cakre ca sakalaṃ samyak snātvā dehaprasādhanam snāto anuliptaḥ sragdhārī suvastraḥ suvibhūṣitaḥ nāsatyadasrayoḥ pārśvam iyāya vasudhādhipaḥ bhūyo api tau yathā pūrvam aṅgopāṅgavilokanam cakratur nṛpates tasya smitabhinnauṣṭhasaṃpuṭau tau sahāsau samālakṣya sa tadā vasudhādhipaḥ hāsasya kāraṇaṃ deva- bhiṣajau tāv apṛcchata pṛcchantaṃ na tato dālbhya nṛpatiṃ hāsyakāraṇam yad ūcatur mahābhāgau tac chṛṇuṣva vadāmi te śṛṇu bhūpāla sakalaṃ hāsakāraṇam āvayoḥ yuṣmaddarśanasaṃbhūtaṃ kṣaṇāpacayahetukam asnātasyābhavad bhūpa yādṛśī te surūpatā sāṃprataṃ tādṛśī neyaṃ bhūṣitasyāpi bhūṣaṇaiḥ snātaḥ sragdāmadhārī tvaṃ svanuliptaḥ subhūṣitaḥ tathāpy asnāta eva prāc śobhano abhūn na sāṃpratam kiṃtu tatkāraṇaṃ yena vyāyāmamalināmbaraḥ śobhano aham abhūt pūrvam idānīṃ na vibhūṣitaḥ divyena cakṣuṣā bhūpa kālasyāsya ca tasya ca vayaḥpariṇatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ paśyāvo apacayapradām yathā hi nāḍikā pūrṇā galaty avirataṃ nṛpa nṝṇāṃ pariṇatas tadvac śarīragrahaṇād anu janmato anantaraṃ bālyaṃ paugaṇḍatvaṃ tataḥ param yauvanaṃ madhyadehitvaṃ vārddhakaṃ ca jarā nṛṇām sthūladṛṣṭyā tu paśyanti na tu te sūkṣmadarśinaḥ nimeṣaśatabhāgasya sahasrāṃśaḥ kṣaṇo nṛpa tasyāpy ayutabhāgāṃśo bhavaty apacayo nṛṇām sūkṣmātisūkṣmāpacayī bhavaty eṣa pumān nṛpa pariṇāmaṃ kramād yāti tṛptiṃ vāri pibann iva tad ahar jātabālyasya bālasyāpacayo hi saḥ pratikṣaṇāṃśayā vṛddhir bālatvaṃ hīyate tayā paugaṇḍe yauvane caiva vārddhake ca mahāmate hānikramaḥ sa evokto yo bālye kathitas tava kāntir yā nṛpa bālasya pogaṇḍasya hi sā kutaḥ tatkāntisaukumāryādyaiḥ śūnyam eva hi yauvanam kāntyādisaṃpado hāniḥ paramā nṛpa vārddhake tatrāpy anukṣaṇaṃ hānir hānir ā mṛtyuto nṛpa evaṃ pratikṣaṇāṃśāṃśo nṝṇām apacayapradaḥ kurvataḥ kimu kālas te mahāsnānaprasādhanam asmaddṛṣṭo bhavān yāvat praviṣṭo nijamandiram tāvad dhānim anuprāptaḥ kimu yāmārdhasaṃsthitaḥ yādṛśo adya bhavāṃs tādṛk tvaṃ na rūpī nareśvara paraśvaḥ śastanaṃ naiva caturthe ahni ca tanmayaḥ evaṃ samastabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca pratikṣaṇāṃśāpacayaṃ prāpnuvanti mahītale tasmān na kautukaṃ kāryaṃ bhavatā tu nareśvara yat te rūpam abhūt pūrvam aprasādhitaśobhanam rājā purūravā bhūyaḥ śrutvā vākyam idaṃ tayoḥ cintayitvā vacaḥ prāha saṃvegotkampimānasaḥ aho bhavadbhyāṃ kathitam anavasthitasaṃsthitam svarūpaṃ jagato devau yena trasto asmi sāṃpratam ajñānatimirāndhānāṃ madvidhānāṃ bhavadvidhāḥ pradīpabhūtāḥ saṃdeho vidyate nātra kaścana sadāpacayadoṣeṇa duṣṭakāyaiḥ surottamau yat kāryaṃ puruṣais tac ca kathyatāṃ hitakāmyayā atimūḍho adhruve kāye sadāpacayadharmiṇi naras tadupabhogyāni dhruvāṇi parimārgati āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ paridhānaṃ gṛhādikam vāñchaty aho atimohena susthiraṃ svayam asthiraḥ mūḍho adhruvaṃ dhruvamatiḥ kim ātmānaṃ na budhyate bālyāt paugaṇḍatāṃ gatvā yaḥ punar yauvanaṃ gataḥ bhuvaḥ śailaṃ samārūḍhaḥ samārūḍhas tato drumam ārohaṇaṃ sa kim anyad ṛkṣabhītaḥ kariṣyati bālyāt paugaṇḍatāṃ yāto yauvanād vṛddhatāṃ gataḥ vayo'vasthā tataḥ kānyā yad bhogāya sthirecchakaḥ tasmād etan manuṣyeṇa vicāryātmahitaiṣiṇā śreyasy āmuṣmike yatnaḥ kartavyo aharniśaṃ nṛpa bhogeṣv asaktiḥ satataṃ tathaivātmāvalokanam śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ kapilaḥ prāha pārthivaḥ sarvatra samadarśitvaṃ nirmamatvam asaṅgitā śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ prāha pañcaśikho muniḥ āgarbhajanmabālyādi- vayo'vasthādivedanam śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇām aṅgāriṣṭho abravīn nṛpaḥ adhyātmikādiduḥkhānām atyantādipratikriyā śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ janako hy āha mokṣavit abhinnayor bhedakaraḥ pratyayo yaḥ parātmanoḥ hiraṇyagarbhas tacchāntiṃ śreyaḥ paramam abravīt kartavyam iti yat karma ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñitam kriyate tat paraṃ śreyo jaigīṣavyo abravīn muniḥ hāniṃ sarvavidhitsānām ātmanaḥ sukhahetukīm śreyaḥ paraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ devalo apy āha tattvavit yad yat tyajati kāmānāṃ tat sukhasyābhipūryate etad eva paraṃ śreyo vijñānaṃ hitakāminām kāmānusārī puruṣaḥ kāmān anu vinaśyati aśreyasaṃ paraṃ caitad yad bhūpālātikāmitā evaṃ vijñātatattvārthaḥ sanako yogināṃ varaḥ narendra prāha viprāṇāṃ paramārthaparaṃparam kriyākalāpaphaladam ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñitam amuṣmin madhyamaṃ śreyaḥ prāhuḥ sapta rṣayo nṛpa ihaiva phaladaṃ kāmyaṃ karma yat kriyate naraiḥ tad āhur aparaṃ śreyo ṛcīkacyavanādayaḥ dve karmaṇī naraśreṣṭha brahmaṇā samudāhṛte pravṛttākhyaṃ nivṛttaṃ ca svargamuktiphale hi te pravṛttam api mokṣāya karma pārthiva jāyate karma svarūpato bhraṣṭam anākāṅkṣya phalaṃ kṛtam sāmānyaṃ cāparaṃ śreyaḥ sarvavarṇāśrameṣu yat tac chṛṇuṣva mahīpāla vadato mama tattvataḥ satyaṃ vaktavyaṃ nityaṃ maitreṇa bhāvyaṃ kāryaṃ ca tyājyaṃ nityam āyāsakāri loke amuṣmin yad dhitaṃ ca tathāsmiṃs tasminn ātmā yojanīyo anudhīraiḥ tīrthasnānaiḥ sopavāsair ajasraṃ pātre dānair homajāpaiś ca nityam śuddhir neyo devatābhyarcanaiś ca śuddho apy ātmā saṅgadoṣād aśuddhaḥ śuddhaṃ vastraṃ saṅgadoṣād aśuddhaṃ bhūyaḥ śuddhiṃ śodhyamānaṃ paryāti etaj jñātvā na pramādo manuṣyaiḥ śuddhe hy ātmany ātmavidbhir vidheyaḥ ity uktvā tau narendraṃ tau tena cārghyādinā pṛthak samyak saṃpūjitau yātau nāka pṛṣṭham athāśvinau sa cāpy anityatām evam avagamya nareśvaraḥ niṣkāmo anudinam eva avagamya nareśvaraḥ niṣkāmo anudinaṃ yajñair iyāja puruṣottamam bhogāsaṅgi mano dālbhya yadāsīt tasya bhūpateḥ tad eva bhagavaddhyāna- paraṃ cakre mahāmune tatyājārtheṣu mamatām ahaṃkāraṃ tathātmani samatāṃ sarvabhūteṣu saṃprāpa pṛthivīpatiḥ yasyātmany api viprarṣe nāhaṃmāno asti kutracit madāvalepo pūpādau tasya syād iti kā kathā evaṃ dālbhya manuṣyeṇa samatām anutiṣṭhatā sarvabhogeṣu saṃtyājyo dhyeyaś ca puruṣottamaḥ kutra tiṣṭhati govindo bāhyanivṛtacetasi tasmān niḥsaṅgacittena śakyaś cintayituṃ hariḥ prītidveṣādayas tyaktvā maharṣe yasya cetasā priyātithis taddhṛdaye viṣṇur mokṣaphalapradaḥ kāryārambheṣu sarveṣu duḥsvapneṣu ca sattama amaṅgalyeṣu sarveṣu yaj japtavyaṃ tad ucyatām yenārambhāś ca sidhhyanti duḥsvapnaṃ copaśāmyati amaṅgalānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratighātaś ca jāyate janārdanaṃ bhūtapatiṃ jagadguruṃ smaran manuṣyaḥ satataṃ mahāmune duṣṭāny aśeṣāṇy apahanti sādhayaty aśeṣakāryāṇi tathā yadīcchati śṛṇuṣva cānyad vadato mamākhilaṃ vadāmi yat te dvijavarya maṅgalam sarvārthasiddhiṃ pradadāti yaḥ sadā nihanty aśeṣāṇi ca pātakāni pratiṣṭhitaṃ yatra jagac carācaraṃ jagac ca yo yo jagataś ca hetuḥ jagac ca pāty atti ca yaḥ sa sarvadā mamāstu maṅgalyavivṛddaye hariḥ vyomāmbuvāyvagnimahīsvarūpair vistāravān yo aṇutaro aṇubhāgāt sa sthūlasūkṣmaḥ satateśvareśvaro yasmāt parastāt puruṣād anantād anādimadhyād akhilaṃ na kiṃcit sa hetuhetuḥ parameśvareśvaro hiraṇyagarbhācyutarudrarūpī sṛjaty aśeṣaṃ paripāti hanti guṇāśrayī yo bhagavān sa sarvadā paraḥ surāṇāṃ paramo asurāṇāṃ paro munīnāṃ paramo yatīnām paraḥ samastasya ca yaḥ sa devo dhyāto yatīnām apakalmaṣair yo dadāti muktiṃ parameśvareśvaraḥ manobhir ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ sa sarvadā surendravaivasvatavittapāmbupa- svarūparūpī paripāti yo jagat sa śuddhasattvaḥ parameśvareśvaro yannāmakīrtanato vimucyate anekajanmārjitapāpasaṃcayaiḥ pāpendhanāgniḥ sa sadaiva nirmalo yenoddhṛteyaṃ dharaṇī rasātalād aśeṣasattvasthitikāraṇād idam bibharti viśvaṃ jagataḥ sa mūlavān pādeṣu vedā jaṭhare carācaraṃ romasv aśeṣā munayo mukhe makhāḥ yasyeśvareśasya sa sarvadā prabhur samastayajñāṅgamayaṃ vapur vibhor yasyāṅgam īśeśvarasaṃstutasya varāharūpo bhagavān sa sarvadā vikṣobhya sarvodadhitoyasaṃpadaṃ dadhāra dhātrīṃ jagataś ca yodbhavaḥ yajñeśvaro yajñapumān sa sarvadā pātālamūleśvarabhogisaṃhatau vinyasya pādau pṛthivīṃ ca bibhrataḥ yasyopamānaṃ na babhūva so acyuto vighargharaṃ yasya ca bṛṃhato muhuḥ sanandanādyair janalokasaṃsthitaiḥ śrutaṃ jayetyuktiparaiḥ sa sarvadā ekārṇavād yasya mahīyaso mahīm ādāya vegena samutpatiṣyataḥ nutaṃ vapur yogivaraiḥ sa sarvadā hato hiraṇyākṣamahāsuraḥ purā purāṇapuṃsā parameṇa yena varāharūpaḥ sa patiḥ prajāpater daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ surabhītināśanaṃ kṛtvā vapur divyanṛsiṃharūpiṇaṃ trātaṃ jagad yena sa sarvadā prabhur daityendravakṣaḥsthaladāradāruṇaiḥ karoruhaiḥ śatrurujānukāribhiḥ ciccheda lokasya bhayāni cāvyayo dantāntadīptidyutinirmalāṇi cakāra sarvāṇi diśaṃ mukhāni ninādavitrāsitadānavo hy asau yannāmasaṃkīrtanato mahābhayād vimokṣam āpnoti na saṃśayaṃ naraḥ samastalokārtiharo nṛkesarī saṭākalāpabhramaṇānilahatāḥ sphuṭanti yasyāmbudharāḥ samantataḥ sa divyasiṃhaḥ sphuritākulekṣaṇo yadīkṣaṇajyotiṣi raśmimaṇḍalaṃ pralīnam eva na rarāja bhāsvataḥ kutaḥ śaśāṅkasya sa siṃharūpadhṛṅ dravanti daityāḥ praṇamanti devatā naśyanti rakṣāṃsy apayānti cārayaḥ yatkīrtanāt so adbhutarūpakesarī aśeṣadeveśanareśvareśvaraiḥ sadā stutaṃ yac caritaṃ mahādbhutam sa sarvalokārtiharo mahāharir ṛkkāritaṃ yo yajuṣātiśāntimat sāmadhvanidhvastasamastapātakam cakre jagad vāmanakaḥ sa sarvadā yatpādavinyāsapavitratāṃ mahī yayau viyad ṛgyajuṣām udīraṇāt sa vāmano divyaśarīradhṛk sadā yasmin prayāte surabhūbhṛto adhvaraṃ nanāma khedād avaniḥ sasāgarā sa vāmanaḥ sarvajaganmayaḥ sadā mahādyutau daityapater mahādhvaraṃ yasmin praviṣṭe kṣubhitaṃ mahāsuraiḥ sa vāmano antasthitasaptalokadhṛṅ samastadeveṣṭimayaṃ mahādyutir dadhāra yo rūpam atīndriyaṃ prabhuḥ trivikramākrāntajagattrayaḥ sadā saṅghaiḥ surāṇāṃ divi bhūtale sthitais tathā manuṣyair gagane sa sarvadā stutaḥ kramād yaḥ pradade sa sarvadā krāntvā dharitrīṃ gaganaṃ tathā divaṃ marutpater yaḥ pradadau triviṣṭapam sa devadevo bhuvaneśvareśvaro anugrahaṃ cāpi baler anuttamaṃ cakāra yaś cendrapadopalakṣaṇaṃ surāṃś ca yajñasya bhujaḥ sa sarvadā rasātalād yena purā samāhṛtāḥ samastavedā varavājirūpiṇā sa kaiṭabhārir madhusūdano mahān niḥkṣatriyāṃ yaś ca cakāra medinīm anekaśo bāhuvanaṃ tathāchinat yaḥ kārtavīryasya sa bhārgavottamo nihatya vāliṃ ca kapīśvaraṃ hi yo nibadhya setuṃ jaladhau daśānanam jaghāna cānyān rajanīcarān asau cikṣepa bālaḥ śakaṭaṃ babhañja yo yamalārjunau kaṃsam ariṃ jaghāna mamarda cāṇūramukhaṃ sa sarvadā prātaḥ sahasrāṃśumarīcinirmalaṃ kareṇa bibhrad bhagavān sudarśanam kaumodakīṃ cāpi gadām anuttamāṃ himendukundasphaṭikābhrakomalaṃ mukhānilāpūritam īśvareśvaraḥ madhyāhnakāle ca sa śaṅkham uttamam tathāparāhne pravikāsipaṅkajaṃ vakṣaḥsthalena śriyam udvahad vibhuḥ vistāripadmotpalapatralocano sarveṣu kāleṣu samastadeśeṣv aśeṣakāryeṣu tatheśvareśvaraḥ sarvaiḥ svarūpair bhagavān anādimān etat paṭhan dālbhya samastapāpair vimucyate viṣṇuparo manuṣyaḥ sidhyanti kāryāṇi tathāsya sarvāṇy arthān avāpnoti tathā yatheṣṭam duḥsvapnaṃ praśamam upaiti paṭhyamāne stotre asmiñ śravaṇavidhau sadotthitasya prārambho drutam upayāti siddhim īśaḥ pāpāni kṣapayati cāsya vāsudevaḥ maṅgalyaṃ paramam idaṃ sadārthasiddhiṃ nirvighna tv adhikaphalaṃ sadā dadāti kiṃ loke tad iha paratra cāsti puṃsām yad viṣṇupravaṇadhiyā na dālbhya sādhyam devendras tribhuvanam artham ekapiṅgaḥ sarvarddhiṃ tribhuvanagāṃ ca kārtavīryaḥ vaidehaḥ paramapadaṃ prasādya viṣṇuṃ saṃprāptaḥ sakalaphalaprado hi viṣṇuḥ sarvārambheṣu dālbhyaitad duḥsvapneṣu ca paṇḍitaḥ japed ekamatir viṣṇau tathāmaṅgalyadarśane śamaṃ prayānti duṣṭāni grahapīḍāś ca dāruṇāḥ karmārambhāś ca sidhyanti puṇyam āpnoti cottamam harir dadāti bhadrāṇi maṅgalyastutisaṃstutaḥ karoty akhilarūpaiś ca rakṣām akṣataśaktidhṛk kurvīta kiṃ pumān sthānaṃ kaḥ pumān brahmaṇo balam brahmaṇaś ca kathaṃ bhedo jñeyo abhinnaphalapradaḥ svakarmaṇā dhanaṃ labdhvā nityanaimittikāḥ kriyāḥ kurvīta śuddhim āsthāya svecchayā ca tathā paraḥ tyaktvā rāgādikān doṣān samaḥ sarvatra vai bhavet sarvatra maitrīṃ kurvīta dadyād iṣṭāni cārthinām kuryād dīneṣu karuṇāṃ duḥśīlān parivarjayet muditāṃ dharmaśīleṣu bhāvanāṃ munisattama ekatra vā jagannāthe bhāvanāṃ puruṣottame niḥśeṣārthamalāpetāṃ śuddhāṃ kurvīta paṇḍitaḥ śarīrabāhyatāṃ śaśvad dhiṃsāṃ kurvīta na kvacit nindāvamānam anyeṣāṃ yac cānyad upaghātakam śarīravāṅmanaḥśuddhiṃ kurvīta ca sadātmanaḥ bhūtānām upakāraś ca tapobhiś cātmakarṣaṇam eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena dālbhyākhyāto mayā tava adharmaś cāyam evokto viparīto manīṣibhiḥ ete yatra guṇāḥ pūrvaṃ kathitā jñānasaṃyutāḥ brahmaṇaḥ sāśrayaḥ śuddha upacārāt tad eva saḥ ekasyaiva satas tasya brahmaṇo dvijasattama nāmnāṃ bahutvaṃ lokānām upakārakaraṃ śṛṇu nimittaśaktayo nāmno bhedatas tadudīraṇāt vibhinnāny eva sādhyante phalāni kurunandana yacchakti nāma tat tasya tat tasminn eva vastuni sādhakaṃ puruṣavyāghra saumyakrūreṣu vastuṣu vāsudevācyutānanta- satyājyapuruṣottamaiḥ paramātmeśvarādyaiś ca stuto nāmabhir avyayaḥ nimittabhāvaṃ bhagavān vimukter yāty adhokṣajaḥ tathānyakāryasaṃsiddhau yad yat tat tan niśāmaya dhanakṛd dharmakṛd dharmī dharmātmā viśvakṛc chuciḥ śuciṣad viṣṇur abjākṣaḥ puṣkarākṣo hy adhokṣayaḥ śuciśravāḥ śipiviṣṭo yajñeśo yajñabhāvanaḥ nāmnām ity evam ādīnāṃ samuccāraṇato naraḥ dharmaṃ mahāntam āpnoti pāpabandhakṣayaṃ tathā tathārthaprāptaye brahman devanāmāni me śṛṇu yeṣāṃ samuccāraṇato vittam āpnoti bhaktimān śrīdaḥ śrīśaḥ śrīnivāsaḥ śrīdharaḥ śrīniketanaḥ śriyaḥ patiḥ śrīparamaḥ śrīmāñ śrīvatsalāñcchanaḥ nṛsiṃho duṣṭadāmano jayo viṣṇus trivikramaḥ stutaḥ prayacchate cārtham evam ādibhir acyutaḥ kāmyaḥ kāmapradaḥ kāntaḥ kāmapālas tathā hariḥ ānando mādhavaś caiva kāmasaṃsiddhaye nṛpa rāmaḥ paraśurāmaś ca nṛsiṃho viṣṇur eva ca vikramaś caivam ādīni japyāny arijigīṣubhiḥ vidyām abhyasatā nityaṃ japtavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ dāmodaraṃ bandhagato nityam eva japan naraḥ keśavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ puṣkarākṣaṃ tathā japet netrabādhāsu sarvāsu hṛṣīkeśaṃ bhayeṣu ca acyutaṃ cāmṛtaṃ caiva japed auṣadhakarmaṇi bhrājiṣṇum agnihānau ca japed ālambane sthitam saṃgrāmābhimukhaṃ gacchan saṃsmared aparājitam pātālanarasiṃhaṃ ca jalaprataraṇe smaret cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ caiva śārṅginaṃ khaḍginaṃ tathā kṣemārthe prasavan rājan dikṣu prācyādiṣu smaret ajitaṃ cādhikaṃ caiva sarvaṃ sarvaśvaraṃ tathā saṃsmaret puruṣo bhaktyā vyavahāreṣu sarvadā nārāyaṇaṃ sarvakālaṃ kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu devabādhāṭavīṣu ca asyuvairinirodheṣu vyāghrasiṃhādisaṃkaṭe andhakāre ca tīvre ca narasiṃham anusmaret taraty akhiladurgāṇi tāpārto jalaśāyinam garuḍadhvajānusmaraṇād āpadbhyo mucyate naraḥ jvaraduṣṭaśiroroga- viṣavīryaṃ praśāmyati snāne devārcane home praṇipāte pradakṣiṇe kīrtayed bhagavannāma vāsudeveti tatparaḥ sthagane vittadhānyāder apadhyāne ca duṣṭaje kurvīta tanmanā bhūtvā anantācyutakīrtanam nārāyaṇaṃ śārṅgadharaṃ śrīdharaṃ puruṣottamam vāmanaṃ khaḍginaṃ caiva duḥsvapneṣu ca saṃsmaret ekārṇavāhiparyaṅka- śāyinaṃ ca naraḥ smaret vāyvagnīgṛhadāhāya pravṛddhāv upalakṣya ca vidyārthī mohavibhrānti- vegāghūrṇitamānasaḥ manuṣyo muniśārdūla sadāśvaśirasaṃ smaret balabhadraṃ samṛddhyarthī sīrakarmaṇi kīrtayet jagatsūtim apatyārthī stuvan bhaktyā na sīdati japtavyaṃ suprajākhyaṃ tu devadevasya sattama dampatyor ātmasaṃbandhe vivāhākhye punaḥ punaḥ śrīśaṃ sarvābhyudayike karmaṇi saṃprakīrtayet ariṣṭānteṣv aśeṣeṣu viśokaṃ ca sadā japet marutpratāpāgnijala- bandhanādiṣu mṛtyuṣu svātantryaparatantreṣu vāsudevaṃ japed budhaḥ sarvārthaśaktiyuktasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ yad vābhirocate nāma tat sarvārtheṣu kīrtayet sarvārthasiddhim āpnoti nāmnām ekārthatā yataḥ sarvāṇy etāni nāmāni parasya brahmaṇo anagha evam etāni nāmāni devadevasya kīrtayet yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyet taṃ tam āpnoty asaṃśayam sarvān kāmān avāpnoti samārādhya jagadgurum tanmayatvena govindam ity etad dālbhya nānyathā tanmayo vāñchitān kāmān yad avāpnoti mānavaḥ nimittaśaktiḥ sā tasya na bhedo dālbhya mānasaḥ vāṅmanaḥkāyikaṃ dveṣaṃ yac ca kurvan prayāty adhaḥ svarūpaśaktiḥ sā tasya matibhedakṛtaṃ na tad sa śākto nirguṇaḥ śuddho brahmabhūto jagadguruḥ karmabhir nāmabhir jīvo dṛśyate dālbhya naikadhā yathā ca gaṅgāsalilaṃ sitam atyantanirmalam ekasvarūpam adhyātmaṃ puṇyāpuṇyavibhedibhiḥ bhrāntijñānānvitair miśraṃ sitāsitaviceṣṭitaiḥ dṛśyate naikadhā dālbhya prāṇibhir bhinnabuddhibhiḥ tāpārtās tāpaśamanam atiprītyatiśītalam kaphadoṣānvitair nāti- prītiyuktair niraṃśubhiḥ strīyogyam etan netīti prītyaprītisamanvitaiḥ madhyasthabuddhyā caivānye nātiśītātitāpibhiḥ pavitram ity etad iti puṇyabuddhyā tathāparaiḥ mṛṣṭam etad itīty anyair matsyāḍhyam iti cāparaiḥ tulyabuddhyāpi caivānyair heyabuddhyā tathāparaiḥ nātivegātivegaṃ ca hṛṣṭodvignais tathāparaiḥ kim eteneti caivānyaiḥ paradārābhilāṣibhiḥ dālbhya saṃdṛśyate cānyair jantubhir bhāyakātaraiḥ tad eva pūyaṃ paśyanti pretādyā hṛtipāpinaḥ etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhir viśeṣair bahujantubhiḥ viśeṣavat karmabhedād ekam eva hi dṛśyate naite gaṅgāmbhaso bhedāḥ prītyaprītipradāyinaḥ prāṇināṃ cetaso bhedād dālbhyaite karmayonayaḥ samastakarmaṇā dālbhya saṃkṣaye bhayam ety asau viśeṣakāraṇābhāvād viśeṣābhāva eva hi viṣṇvākhyam evaṃ tad brahma śuddham atyantanirmalam abhedaṃ bahudhā bhinnaṃ dṛśyate karmabhedibhiḥ yogibhir dṛśyate śuddhaṃ rāgādyupaśamāmalaiḥ rāgibhir viṣayākāraṃ tad eva brahma dṛśyate karmamārgāśritaiḥ karma- bhoktṛtve ca tatheṣyate kim apy astīti caivānyair avivekibhir ucyate sarvam etat tad eveti vadanty advaitavādinaḥ pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyam eveti vadanty anye duruktibhiḥ vadanty anye tad evāhaṃ nāstīty anye vadanti tat tiryaṅmanuṣyadevākhyaṃ tad anyair abhidhīyate vandyabuddhyā tu tat kaiścid dhyeyabuddhyā tathāparaiḥ gamyabuddhyā tathānyaiś ca labhyabuddhyā ca jantubhiḥ gṛhyate tat paraṃ brahma ripubuddhyā tathāparaiḥ ātmaputrasuhṛdbhartṛ- parabuddhyā tathāparaiḥ parabuddhyā ca naikadhā prāṇibhiḥ karmavaiṣamya- bhinnabuddhibhir avyayam tad brahma gṛhyate dālbhya paramārthaṃ nibodha me bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇa- pradhānapuruṣātmakam aparaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ paraṃ dālbhya niśāmaya aheyam akṣaraṃ śuddham asaṃbhūtinirañjanam viṣṇvākhyaṃ paramaṃ brahma yad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ yathaitad bhavatā proktaṃ dharmārthādes tu sādhanam patnī nṝṇāṃ muniśreṣṭha yoṣitas ca tathā naraḥ tac chrotum icche viprarṣe vidhavā strī na jāyate upoṣītena yenāgryā patnyā ca rahito naraḥ aśūnyaśayanā nāma dvitīyāṃ śṛṇu tāṃ mama yām upoṣya na vaidhavyaṃ prayāti strī dvijottama patnīviyuktaś ca naro na kadācit prajāyate śete jagatpatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śriyā sārdhaṃ yadā dvija aśūnyaśayanā nāma tadā grāhyā hi sā tithiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣadvitīyāyāṃ śrāvaṇe dvijasattama idam uccārayen nāma praṇamya jagataḥ patim śrīvatsadhāriṇaṃ śrīśaṃ bhaktyābhyarcya śriyā saha śrīvatsadhāriñ śrīkānta śrīdhāma śrīpate acyuta gārhasthyaṃ mā praṇāśaṃ me yātu dharmārthakāmadam agnayo mā praṇaśyantu mā praṇaśyantu devatāḥ pitaro mā praṇaśyantu matto dāmpatyabhedataḥ lakṣmyā prayujyate deva na kadācid yathā bhavān tathā kalatrasaṃbandho deva mā me vibhidyatām lakṣmyā na śūnyaṃ varada yathā te śayanaṃ sadā śayyā mamāpy aśūnyāstu tathaiva madhusūdana evaṃ prasādya pūjāṃ ca kṛtvā lakṣmyās tathā hareḥ phalāni dadyāc chayyāyām abhīṣṭāni jagatpateḥ naktaṃ praṇamyāyatane havir bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ brāhmaṇāya dvitīye ahni śaktyā dadyāc ca dakṣiṇām evaṃ karoti yaḥ samyag naro māsacatuṣṭayam tasya janmatrayaṃ dālbhya gṛhabhaṅgo na jāyate aśūnyaśayanaś cāsau dharmakarmārthasādhakaḥ bhavaty avyāhataiśvaryaḥ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ nārī ca dālbhya dharmajñā vratam etad yathāvidhi yā karoti na sā śocyā bandhuvargasya jāyate vaidhavyaṃ durbhagatvaṃ vā bhartṛtyāgaṃ ca sattama nāpnoti janmatritayam etac cīrtvā pativratā upavāsāśritaṃ samyag lokadvayaphalapradam kathitaṃ bhavatā sarvaṃ yat pṛṣṭo asi mayā dvija anyad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ tad bhavān prabravītu me saṃsārahetuṃ muktiṃ ca saṃsārān munisattama avidyāprabhavaṃ karma hetubhūtaṃ dvijottama saṃsārasyāsya tanmuktiḥ saṃkṣepāc chrūyatāṃ mama svajātivihitaṃ karma lobhadveṣavivarjitam kurvataḥ kṣīyate pūrvaṃ manyubandhaś ca neṣyate apūrvasaṃbhavābhavāt kṣayaṃ yāty ādikarmaṇi dālbhya saṃsāravicchedaḥ kāraṇābhāvasaṃbhavaḥ bhavaty asaṃśayaṃ cānyac śrūyatām atra kāraṇam saṃsārān mucyate dālbhya samāsād vadato mama gṛhītakarmaṇā yena puṃsāṃ jātir dvijottama tatprāyaścittabhūtaṃ vai śṛṇu karmakṣayāvaham brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāntyānāṃ ca sattama svajātivihitaṃ karma rāgadveṣādivarjitam jātipradasya kṣayadaṃ tad evādyasya karmaṇaḥ jñānakāraṇabhāvaṃ ca tad eva pratipadyate pumāṃś cādhigatajñāno bhedaṃ nāpnoti sattama brahmaṇā viṣṇusaṃjñena parameṇāvyayātmanā etat te kathitaṃ dālbhya saṃsārasya samāsataḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavamuktiś ca jāyate yogino yathā iti dālbhyaḥ pulastyena yathāvat pratibodhitaḥ ārādhayām āsa hariṃ lebhe kāmāṃś ca vāñchitān tathā tvam api daityendra keśavārādhanaṃ kuru ārādhya taṃ jagannāthaṃ na kaścid avasīdati iti śukravacaḥ śrutvā prahlādo madhusūdanam ārādhya prāptavān kṛtsnaṃ trailokaiśvaryam ūrjitam etan mayoktaṃ sakalaṃ tava bhūmipa pṛcchataḥ anārādhyācyutaṃ devaṃ kaḥ kāmān prāpnute naraḥ ambarīso narapatir viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam śrutvā babhūva satataṃ keśavārpitamānasaḥ evaṃ tvam api kauravya yadi muktim abhīṣyasi bhogān vā vilupān devāt tasmād ārādhayācyutam dadāti vāñchitān kāmān sakāmair arcito hariḥ muktiṃ dadāti govindo niṣkāmair abhipūjitaḥ bhagavān avatīrṇo abhūn martyalokaṃ janārdanaḥ bhārāvataraṇārthāya bhuvo bhūtapatir hariḥ mānuṣatve ca govindo mama pūrvapitāmahaiḥ cakāra prītim atulāṃ sāmānyapuruṣo yathā sārathyaṃ kṛtavāṃś caiva teṣāṃ sarveśvaro hariḥ nistīrṇo yena bhīṣmaugho kurusainyamahodadhiḥ upakārī mahābhāgaḥ sa teṣāṃ sarvavastuṣu keśavaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ sutānāṃ janako yathā dhanyās te kṛtapuṇyāś ca mama pāṇḍusutā matāḥ viviśur ye pariṣvaṅge govindabhujapañjaram rājyahetor arīñ jaghnur akasmāt pāṇḍunandanāḥ saptalokaikanāthena ye abhavann ekaśāyinaḥ ātmānam avagacchāmi bhagavan dhūtakalmaṣam jātaṃ nirdhūtapāpe asmin kule viṣṇuparigrahe evaṃ devavaras teṣāṃ prasādasumukho hariḥ pṛcchatāṃ kaccid ācaṣṭe kiṃcid guhyaṃ mahātmanām guhyaṃ janārdanaṃ yāṃs tu dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ papraccha dharmān akhilāṃs tan mamākhyātum arhasi dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu yad guhyaṃ madhusūdanaḥ teṣām avocad bhagavāñ śrotum icchāmi tat tv aham bahūni dharmaguhyāni dharmaputrāya keśavaḥ purā provāca rājendra prasādasumukho hariḥ śaratalpagatād bhīṣmād dharmāñ śrutvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pṛṣṭavān yaj jagannāthaṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu pañcamenāśvamedhena yadā snāto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tadā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ praśnam etam apṛcchata bhagavan vaiṣṇavā dharmāḥ kiṃphalāḥ kiṃparāyaṇāḥ kiṃ kṛtyam adhikṛtyaite bhavatotpāditāḥ purā yadi te pāṇḍuṣu sneho vidyate madhusūdana śrotavyāś cen mayā dharmās tatas tān kathayākhilān pavitrāś caiva ye dharmāḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanāḥ tava vaktracyutā deva sarvadharmeṣv anuttamāḥ yāñ śrutvā brahmahā goghnaḥ pitṛghno gurutalpagaḥ surāpo vā kṛtaghnaś ca mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ etan me kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sabhāmadhye arisūdana vasiṣṭhādyair mahābhāgair munibhir bhāvitātmabhiḥ tato ahaṃ tava deveśa pādamūlam upāgataḥ dharmān kathaya tān deva yady ahaṃ bhavataḥ priyaḥ śrutā me mānavā dharmā vāsiṣṭhāś ca mahāmate parāśarakṛtāś caiva tathātreyasya dhīmataḥ śrutā gārgyasya śaṅkhasya likhitasya yamasya ca jāpāleś ca mahābāho muner dvaipāyanasya ca umāmaheśvarāś caiva jātidharmāś ca pāvanāḥ guṇeś ca guṇabāhoś ca kāśyapeyās tathaiva ca bahvāyanakṛtāś caiva śākuneyās tathaiva ca agastyagītā maudgalyāḥ śāṇḍilyāḥ saurabhās tathā bhṛgor aṅgirasaś caiva kaśyapoddālakās tathā saumantūgrāyaṇāgrāś ca pailasya ca mahātmanaḥ vaiśampāyanagītāś ca piśaṅgamakṛtāś ca ye aindrāś ca vāruṇāś caiva kauberā vātsyapauṇakāḥ āpastambāḥ śrutā dharmās tathā gopālakasya ca bhṛgvaṅgiraḥkṛtāś caiva sauryā hārītakās tathā yājñavalkyakṛtāś caiva tathā saptarṣayaś ca ye etāś cānyāś ca vividhāḥ śrutā me dharmasaṃhitāḥ bhagavañ śrotum icchāmi tava vaktrād viniḥsṛtān evam uktaḥ sa pārthena pratyuvāca janārdanaḥ bahumānāc ca prītyā ca dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram iṣṭas tvaṃ hi mahābāho sadā mama yudhiṣṭhira paramārthaṃ tava brūyāṃ kiṃ punar dharmasaṃhitām paramajñānibhiḥ siddhair yuñjadbhir api nityaśaḥ praśāntasyeva dīpasya gatir mama duratyayā sarvavedamayaṃ brahma pavitram ṛṣibhiḥ stutam kathayiṣyāmi te rājan dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtām vara evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena ṛṣayo amitatejasaḥ samājagmuḥ sabhāmadhye śrotukāmā harer giram devagandharvaṛṣayo guhyakāś ca mahāyaśāḥ vālakhilyā mahātmāno munayaḥ saṃmitavratāḥ pāvanān sarvadharmebhyo rahasyān dvijasattama vaiṣṇavān akhilān dharmān yaḥ paṭhet pāpanāśanān bhaveyur akṣayās tasya lokāḥ satpuṇyabhāginaḥ kṛṣṇadṛṣṭihataṃ cāsya kilbiṣaṃ saṃpraṇaśyati vaiṣṇavasya ca yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ kautūhalasamāviṣṭaḥ papracchedaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yamalokasya cādhvānam antaraṃ mānuṣasya ca kīdṛśaṃ kiṃpramāṇaṃ vā kathaṃ vāntaṃ janārdana taranti puruṣāḥ kṛṣṇa kenopāyena saṃśame tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vismito madhusūdanaḥ pratyuvāca mahātmānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram sādhu sādhur ayaṃ praśnaḥ śrūyatāṃ bho yudhiṣṭhira ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ narādhipa yamalokasya cādhvānam antaraṃ mānuṣasya ca tāmrapātram ivātaptaṃ śūlavyāmiśrakaṇṭakam dvādaśādityasaṃkāśaṃ bhairavaṃ duratikramam na tatra vṛkṣā na cchāyā pānīyaṃ ketanāni ca yatra viśramate śrāntaḥ puruṣo adhvānako nṛpa yāmyair dūtair nīyamāno yamasyājñākarair balāt avaśyaṃ ca mahārāja sa gantavyo mahāpathaḥ naraiḥ strībhis tathā tiryaiḥ pṛthivyāṃ jīvasaṃjñakaiḥ ekaviṃśac ca narakā yamasya viṣaye smṛtāḥ ye tu duṣkṛtakarmāṇas te patanti pṛthak pṛthak narako rauravo nāma mahāraurava eva ca kṣuradhārā mahāraudraḥ sūkaras tāla eva ca vajrakumbho mahāghoraḥ śālmalo atha vimohanaḥ kīṭādaḥ kṛmibhakṣaś ca śālmaliś ca mahādrumaḥ tathā pūyavahaḥ pāpā rudhirāndho mahattamaḥ agnijvālo mahānādaḥ saṃdāmśaḥ śunabhojanaḥ tathā vaitaraṇī coṣṇā asipattravanaṃ tathā viṣṇos tad vacanaṃ śrutvā papāta bhuvi pāṇḍavaḥ sa saṃjñaś ca muhūrtena bhūyaḥ keśavam abravīt bhītaś cāsmi mahābāho śrutvā mārgasya vistaram kenopāyena taṃ mārgaṃ taranti puruṣāḥ sukham brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradānāni nānārūpāṇi pārthiva yo dadyāc chraddhayā yuktaḥ sukhaṃ yāti mahāpatham upānahapradā yānti sukhaṃ chāyāsu cchattradāḥ na teṣām aśubhaṃ kiṃcic śūlādi na ca kaṇṭakāḥ upānahau yo dadāti pātrabhūte dvijottame aśvataryaḥ pradātāram upatiṣṭhanti taṃ naram vitṛṣṇāś cāmbudātāras tarpitāś cānnadās tathā auprāvṛtā vastradāś ca nagnā vai yānty avastradāḥ hiraṇyadāḥ sukhaṃ yānti puruṣāḥ svābhyalaṃkṛtāḥ gopradā yānti ca sukhaṃ vimuktāḥ sarvakilbiṣaiḥ bhūmidāḥ sukham adhante sarvakāmaiḥ sutarpitāḥ yānti caivāparikliṣṭā narāḥ śayyāsanapradāḥ tataḥ sukhataraṃ yānti vimāneṣu gṛhapradāḥ kṣīrapradā hi divyābhiḥ sasarpibhis tathaiva ca gopradātā labhet tṛptiṃ tasmin deśe sudurlabhām ārāmaropī cchāyāsu śītalāsu sukhaṃ vrajet sugandhigandhino yānti gandhamālyapradā naraḥ adattadānā gacchanti padbhyāṃ yānena yānadāḥ dīpapradāḥ sukhaṃ yānti dīpayantaś ca tatpatham vimānair haṃsayuktais tu yānti māsopavāsinaḥ cakravākaprayuktena pañcarātropavāsinaḥ tato barhiṇayuktena ṣaḍrātram upavāsinaḥ trirātram ekabhaktena kṣapayed yas tu pāṇḍava anantaraṃ ca yo aśnīyāt tasya lokā yathā mama panīyaṃ paralokeṣu pāvanaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam pānīyasya pradānena tṛptir bhavati śāśvatī pānīyasya guṇā divyāḥ pretaloke sukhāvahāḥ tatra puṇyodakā nāma nadī teṣāṃ pravartate śītalaṃ salilaṃ tatra pibanti hy amṛtopamam ye ca duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ pūyaṃ teṣāṃ pravartate eṣā nadī mahārāja sarvakāmadughā śubhā adhvani khinnagātras tu dvijo yaḥ kṣuttṛṣṇānvitaḥ pṛcchan sadānnadātāram abhyeti gṛham āśayā taṃ pūjaya prayatnena so atithir brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ pitaro devatāś caiva ṛṣayaś ca tapodhanāḥ pūjitāḥ pūjite tasmin nirāśe tu nirāśakāḥ tam eva gacchantam anuvrajanti devāś ca sarve pitaras tathaiva tasmin dvije pūjite pūjitās te gate nirāśe pratiyānti nāśam ahany ahani dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira āgamiṣyati yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati na tathā haviṣo homair na puṣpair nānulepanaiḥ agnau vā suhute rājan yathā hy atithipūjane kapilāyāṃ tu dattāyāṃ yat phalaṃ jyeṣṭhapuṣkare tat phalaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha viprāṇāṃ pādaśaucane dvijapādodakaklinnā yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī tāvat puṣkarapātreṣu pibanti pitaro jalam devamālyāpanayanaṃ dvijocchiṣṭāpamārjanam śrāntasaṃvāhanaṃ caiva dīnasya paripālanam ekaikaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha gopradānād viśiṣyate pādaśaucaṃ tathābhyaṅgaṃ dīpam annaṃ pratiśrayam dadanti ye mahārāja nopasarpanti te yamam svāgatenāgnayaḥ prītā āsanena śatakratuḥ pitaraḥ pādaśaucena annādyena prajāpatiḥ abhayasya pradānena bhavet prītir mamātulā yeṣāṃ taḍāgāni bahūdakāni prapāś ca kūpāś ca pratiśrayāś ca annapradānaṃ madhurā ca vāṇī yamasya te nirvacanā bhavanti savṛṣaṃ gośataṃ tena dattaṃ bhavati śāśvatam pāpaṃ karma ca yat kiṃcid brahmahatyāsamaṃ bhavet śochayet kapilāṃ dattvā etad vai nātra saṃśayaḥ prāsādā yatra sauvarṇā vasordhārā ca syandate gandharvāpsaraso yatra tatra gacchanti gopradāḥ prayacchate yaḥ kapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ kanakāgraśṛṅgīm yān yān hi kāmān abhivāñchate asau tāṃs tān avāpnoty amalāṃś ca lokān yāvad vatsasya dvau pādau śiraś caiva pradṛśyate tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati tasmin kāle pradātavyā vidhinā yā mayoditā antarikṣagato vatso yāvad yonyāṃ pradṛśyate tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati yāvanti tasya romāṇi tāvadvarṣāṇi mānavaḥ haṃsayuktena yānena yuktenāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ gandharvāpsarasodgītaiḥ svargaloke mahīyate tiladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi yaś cāsyā vidhir uttamaḥ suvarṇanābhiṃ yaḥ kṛtvā sukhūraṃ kṛṣṇamārgaṇām kutapaprastarasthāṃ tu tilāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ tilaiḥ prasthādi tāṃ dadyāt sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtām sasamudradrumā caiva saśailavanakānanā caturantā bhaved dattā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇājine tilāṃ kṛtvā kṛṣṇāṃ vā yadi vetarām rājateṣu tu pātreṣu koṇeṣu madhusarpiṣī prīyatāṃ dharmarājeti yad vā manasi vartate yāvaj jīvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tena dānena pūyate dhanaṃ prāpnoti puṇyena maunenājñāṃ prayacchati upabhogaṃ tu dānena jīvitaṃ brahmacaryayā ahiṃsayā paraṃ rūpam dīkṣayā kulajanma ca phalamūlāśanād rājyaṃ svargaḥ parṇāśano bhavet payobhakṣa divaṃ yānti snānena draviṇādhikāḥ śākaṃ sādhayato rājyaṃ nākapṛṣṭham anāśanāt sthaṇḍile ca śayānasya gṛhāṇi śayanāni ca cīravalkaladhāriṇāṃ vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca śayanāsanayānāni ye gatā hi tapovanam agnipraveśī niyataṃ brahmaloke mahīyate rasānāṃ pratisaṃhārāt saubhāgyam abhijāyate āmiṣapratiṣedhāt tu bhavaty āyuṣmatī prajā udavāsaṃ vased yas tu nāgānām adhipo bhavet satyavādī naraśreṣṭha devataih saha modate kīrtir bhavati dānena ārogyaṃ cāpy ahiṃsayā dvijaśuśrūṣayā rājyaṃ dvijatvaṃ cāpi puṣkalam dvijaśuśrūṣayā rājyaṃ divyarūpam avāpnute annapānapradānena kāmabhogais tu tṛpyate dīpālokapradānena cakṣuṣmāñ jāyate naraḥ gandhamālyapradānena tuṣṭir bhavati puṣkalā keśaśmaśrūn dhārayato hy agrā bhavati saṃtatiḥ vākśaucaṃ manasaḥ śaucaṃ yac ca śaucaṃ jalāśrayam tribhiḥ śaucair upeto yaḥ sa svargī nātra saṃśayaḥ tāmrāyasānāṃ bhaṇḍānāṃ dātā ratnādhipo bhavet labhate tu paraṃ sthānaṃ balavān puṣyate sadā dhānyaṃ krameṇārjitavittasaṃcayaṃ vipre suśīle te prayacchate yaḥ vasuṃdharā tasya bhavet sutuṣṭā dhārā vasūnāṃ pratimuñcatīha puṣpopabhogaṃ ca phalopabhogaṃ yaḥ pādapaṃ sparśayate dvijāya sa śrīsamṛddhaṃ bahuratnapūrṇaṃ labhaty adhiṣṭhānavaraṃ samṛddham indhanāni ca yo dadyād dvijebhyaḥ śiśirāgame kāyāgnidīptiṃ saubhāgyam aiśvaryaṃ cādhigacchati chattrapradānena gṛhaṃ variṣṭhaṃ rathaṃ tathopānahasaṃpradānāt dhuryapradānena gavām tathaiva lokān avāpnoti puraṃdarasya svargīyam apy āha hiraṇyadānam tathā variṣṭhaṃ kanakapradānam naiveśikaṃ sarvaguṇopapannaṃ prayacchate yaḥ puruṣo dvijāya svādhyāyacāritraguṇānvitāya tasyāpi lokāḥ pravarā bhavanti yo brahmadeyāṃ pradadāti kanyāṃ bhūmipradānaṃ ca karoti vipre hiraṇyadānaṃ ca tathā viśiṣṭaṃ sa śakro lokaṃ labhate durāpam sucitravastrābharaṇopadhānaṃ dadyān naro yaḥ śayanaṃ dvijāya rūpānvitāṃ dakṣavatīṃ manojñāṃ bhāryām ayatnopacitāṃ labhet saḥ lavaṇasya tu dātāras tilānāṃ sarpiṣas tathā tejasvino abhijāyante bhoginaṣ cirajīvinaḥ svarge apsarobhiḥ saha bhuktabhogas tataś cyutaḥ śīlavatīṃ sa bhāryām rūpānvitāṃ dakṣavatīṃ suraktāṃ sukhena dharmeṇa tathāpi kāle tasyaiva sārdhaṃ suralokam eti tasyaiva cānyat punar eti janma kīdṛgvidhāsv avasthāsu dattaṃ dānaṃ janārdana ihalokeṣv anubhavet puruṣas tad bravīhi me garbhasthāsyāthavā bālye yauvane vārddhake api vā avasthāṃ kṛṣṇa kathaya paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me vṛthājanmāni catvāri vṛthādānāni ṣoḍaśa aputrāṇāṃ vṛthā janma ye ca dharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ parapākaṃ ca ye aśnanti paradāraratāś ca ye pary asthānaṃ vṛthā dānaṃ sadoṣaṃ parikīrtitam ārūḍhapatite caiva anyāyopārjitaṃ ca yat vyarthaṃ cābrāhmaṇe dānaṃ patite taskare tathā guroś cāprītijanake kṛtaghne grāmayājake brahmabandhau ca yad dattaṃ yad dattaṃ vṛṣalīpatau vedavikrayiṇe caiva yasya copapatir gṛhe strīnirjiteṣu yad dattaṃ vyālagrāhe tathaiva ca paricārake ca yad dattaṃ vṛthādānāni ṣoḍaśa tamovṛtas tu yo dadyād bhayāt krodhāt tathaiva ca vṛthā dānaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ bhuṅkte garbhastha eva tu serṣyāmanyumanāś caiva dambhārthaṃ cārthakāraṇāt yo dadāti dvijātibhyaḥ sa bālatve tad aśnute yaḥ śuddhiḥ prayato bhūtvā prasannamānasendriyaḥ pradadāti dvijātibhyo yauvanasthas tad aśnute deśe deśe ca pātre ca yo dadāti dvijātiṣu manasā parituṣṭena yauvanasthas tad aśnute tasmāt sarvāsv avasthāsu sarvadānāni pārthiva dātavyāni dvijātibhyaḥ svargamargam abhīpsatā trailokya kṛṣṇa bhūtānāṃ sarvalokātmako hy asi nṝṇāṃ yaduvaraśreṣṭha tuṣyase kena karmaṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjitair nityaṃ pūjito ahaṃ na saṃśayaḥ nirbhartsitaiś ca nirbhagnas tasyāhaṃ sarvakarmasu viprāparā gatir mahyaṃ yas tān pūjayate nṛpa tam ahaṃ tena rūpeṇa prapaśyāmi yudhiṣṭhira kāṇāḥ kubjāś ca khañjāś ca daridrā vyādhitāś ca ye nāvamanyed dvijān prājño mama rūpaṃ hitaṃ tathā bahavo api na jānante narā jñānabahiṣkṛtāḥ yathāhaṃ dvijarūpeṇa carāmi pṛthivītale ye kecit sāgarāntāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ kīrtitā dvijāḥ tad rūpaṃ hi paraṃ mahyaṃ yo arcayed arcayet tu saḥ tadrūpān ghnanti ye viprān vikarmasu ca yuñjanti apreṣaṇe preṣayanto dāsatvaṃ kārayanti hi mṛtāṃs tān karapattrena yamadūtā mahābalāḥ nikṛntanti yathā kāṣṭhaṃ sūtramārgeṇa śilpinaḥ ye caivāślakṣṇayā vācā tarjayanti narādhamāḥ vadanti krodhaniḥsparśaṃ pādenābhihananti ca mṛtāṃs tān yamalokeṣu nihatya dharaṇītale uraḥ pādena cākramya krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ agnivarṇaiś ca saṃdaṃśair jihvām uddharate yamaḥ pāpāś ca nārake vahnau dhāsyante yamakiṃkaraiḥ ye tu viprān nirīkṣanti pāpāḥ pāpena cakṣuṣā abrahmaṇyāḥ śruter bāhyā nityaṃ brahmadviṣo narāḥ teṣāṃ ghorā mahākāyā vajratuṇḍā bhayānakāḥ uddharanti muhūrtena cakṣuḥ kākā yamājñayā yas tāḍayati viprāṃs tu kṣataṃ kuryāt saśoṇitam asthibhaṅgaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt prāṇair vāpi viyojayet brahmaghnaḥ so anupūrveṇa narake vasudhādhipa kīlair vinihataḥ pāpo mīrāyāṃ pacyate bhṛśam subahūni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ kleśabhāg bhavet ravān muñcati durbuddhir na tasmai niṣkṛtiḥ smṛtā tasmād viprā naraśreṣṭha namaskāryāś ca nityaśaḥ annapānapradānais tu pūjārhāḥ satataṃ dvijāḥ āmantrayitvā yo viprān gandhair mālyaiś ca mānavaḥ tarpayec chraddhayā yuktaḥ sa mām arcayate sadā sa māṃ prasādayec caiva sa ca māṃ paritoṣayet tapodamānviteṣv eva nityaṃ pūjāṃ prayojayet ye brāhmaṇāḥ so aham asaṃśayaṃ nṛpa teṣv arciteṣv arcito ahaṃ yathāvat teṣv eva tuṣṭeṣv aham eva tuṣṭo vairaṃ ca tair yasya mamāpi vairam sugandhidhūpādibhir abhyarcya vipraṃ , tam acyutaṃ nārcayate sadaiva , yo bhakṣatoyādibhir annapānair , anulepācamanapradānaiḥ , yaḥ pūjayed bhojayitvā dvijāgryān , saṃpūjayitvā paritoṣayec ca , arghyādinā ye abhipūjya , pūjayanti sadācyutam , tenaiva mām eva sadā , pūjayanti na saṃśayaḥ , virūpāś ca surūpāś ca , vijanān niṣkalān api , kṛpayā bhāvitātmāno , ye arcayanti dvijottamān , anasūyā hitātmāno , viprān ārādhate kvacit , asaṃśayaṃ sadā bhaktyā , mām evārcayate hi saḥ , tataḥ pavitram atulaṃ , na puṇyam adhikaṃ tataḥ , yaś candanaiḥ sāgarugandhamālyair abhyarcayed dārumayīṃ mamārcām nāsau mamārcām arcayate arcayan vai viprārcanād arcita eva cāham vipraprasādān madha eva cāhaṃ vipraprasādād asurāñ jayāmi vipraprasādāt puruṣottamatvaṃ vipraprasādād ajito asmi nityam sāyaṃ prātaś ca yaḥ saṃdhyām upāste askannamānasaḥ japan hi pāvanīṃ devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram sa tayā pāvito devyā brāhmaṇaḥ pūtakilbiṣaḥ na sīdet pratigṛhṇānaḥ pṛthivīṃ tu sasāgarām ye cānye dāruṇāḥ kecid grahāḥ sūryādayo divi te cāsya saumyā jāyante śivāḥ śivatamāh sadā yatratatragataṃ cainaṃ dāruṇāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ghorarūpā mahākāyā na karṣanti dvijottamam yāvantaś ca pṛthivyāṃ hi cīrṇavedavratā dvijāḥ acīrṇavratavedā vā vikarmapatham āśritāḥ teṣāṃ tu pāvanārthaṃ hi nityam eva yudhiṣṭhira dve saṃdhye hy upatiṣṭheta tad askannaṃ mahāvratam nāsti kiṃcin naravyāghra duṣkṛtaṃ brāhmaṇasya tu yatra sthitaḥ sadādhyātme dve saṃdhye hy upatiṣṭhati pūrṇāhutiṃ vā prāpnoti juhute ca trayo aghnayaḥ dahanti duṣkṛtaṃ tasya agnayo nātra saṃśayaḥ evaṃ sarvasya viprasya kilbiṣaṃ nirdahāmy aham ubhe saṃdhye hy upāsinas tasmāt sarvaśucir dvijaḥ daive pitrye ca yatnena niyoktavyo ajugupsitaḥ jugupsitas tu tac chrāddhaṃ dahaty agnir ivendhanam purāṇaṃ mānavā dharmāḥ sāṅgo vedaś cikitsitam ājñāsiddhāni catvāri na hantavyāni hetubhiḥ hatvā hy etāni saṃmūḍhaḥ kalpaṃ tamasi pacyate na brāhmaṇaṃ parīkṣeta śrāddhakāle hy upasthite sumahān parivādo hi brāhmaṇānāṃ parīkṣaṇe kāṇāḥ kuṇṭhāś ca ṣaṇḍāś ca daridrā vyādhitās tathā sarve śrāddhe niyoktavyā miśritā vedapāragaiḥ akṣayaṃ tu bhavec chrāddham etad dharmavido viduḥ brāhmaṇo hi mahad bhūtaṃ janmanā saha jāyate lokā lokeśvarāś cāpi sarve brāhmaṇapūjakāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kupitā hanyur bhasma kuryuś ca tejasā lokān anyān sṛjeyuś ca lokapālāṃs tathāparān brāhmaṇā hi mahātmāno virajāḥ svargasaṃkramāḥ brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādād asurāḥ salileśayāḥ apeyaḥ sāgaro yais tu kṛtaḥ kopān mahātmabhiḥ yeṣāṃ kopāgnir adyāpi daṇḍake nopaśāmyati ete svargasya netāro bhūmidevāḥ sanātanāḥ ebhiś cādhikṛtaḥ panthā devayānaḥ sa ucyate te pūjyās te namaskāryās teṣu sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam te vai lokān imān sarvān dhārayanti parasparam pramāṇaṃ sarvalokānāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇaḥ tān apāśritya tiṣṭhante trayo lokāḥ sanātanāḥ gūḍhasvādhyāyatapaso brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśitavratāḥ vidyāsnātā vratasnātā anapāśrityajīvinaḥ āśīviṣā iva kruddhā upacaryā hi brāhmaṇāḥ tapasā dīpyamānās te daheyuḥ sāgarān api brāhmaṇeṣu ca tuṣṭeṣu tuṣyante sarvadevatāḥ brāhmaṇānāṃ namaskāraiḥ sūryo divi virājate brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādāt pateyur api devatāḥ dhuri ye nāvasīdanti praṇīte yajñavahnayaḥ bhojanācchādanair dānais tārayanti tapodhanāḥ te gatiḥ sarvabhūtānām adhyātmagaticintakāḥ ādimadhyāvasānānāṃ jñānānāṃ chinnasāmśayāḥ parāparaviśeṣajñā netāraḥ paramāṃ gatim avadhyā brāhmaṇās tasmāt pāpeṣv api ratāḥ sadā yaś ca sarvam idaṃ hanyād brāhmaṇaṃ vāpi tatsamam so agniḥ so arko mahātejā viṣaṃ bhavati kopitaḥ bhūtānāṃ agrabhug vipro varṇaśreṣṭhaḥ pitā guruḥ na skandate na vyathate na ca naśyati karhicit variṣṭham agnihotrād dhi brāhmaṇasya mukhe hutam avidyo vā savidyo vā brāhmaṇo mama daivatam praṇītaś cāpraṇītaś ca yathāgnir daivataṃ mahat evaṃ vidvān avidvān vā brāhmaṇo daivataṃ mahat śmaśāneṣv api tejasvī pāvako naiva duṣyati havyakavyavyapeto api brāhmaṇo naiva duṣyati sarvathā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyāḥ sarvathā daivataṃ mahat tasmāt sarvaprayatnena rakṣed āpatsu brāhmaṇān śakro api hi dvijendrāṇāṃ bibheti vibudhādhipaḥ dānaṃ devāḥ praśaṃsanti iti dharmavido viduḥ nānādānavidhiṃ tasmāc śṛṇuṣva susamāhitaḥ hiraṇyadānaṃ godānaṃ pṛthivīdānam eva ca etāni vai pavitrāṇi tārayanti paratra ca yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cāsti dayitaṃ gṛhe tat tad guṇavate deyaṃ tad evākṣayam icchatā suvarṇadānaṃ godānaṃ pṛthivīdānam eva ca etat prayacchamāno vai sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate yad dadāsi viśiṣṭebhyo yac cāśnāsi dine dine tat te vittam ahaṃ manye śeṣaṃ kasyāpi rakṣasi tulyanāmāni śastāni trīṇi tulyaphalāni ca nityaṃ deyāni rājendra gāvaḥ pṛthvī sarasvatī tadvaj
