jalam amitraghna tat tulyaphalanāmataḥ dattvā tṛptim avāpnoti yatratatrābhijāyate saṃkalpavihito yo artho brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradīyate arthibhyo hy arthahetubhyo manasvī tena jāyate sīdate dvijamukhyāya yo arthine na prayacchati amarthe sati durbuddhir narakāyopapadyate dhenavo anaḍuhaś caiva chattraṃ vastram upānahau deyāni yācamānebhyaḥ pānam annaṃ tathaiva ca evaṃ dānaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ vyuṣṭimat tārakaṃ param eṣa te vihito yajñaḥ śraddhāpūtaḥ sadakṣiṇaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ sa ca yajñeṣu dadatām anasūyayā dānavidbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthā yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ yair dānais tarpayiṣyanti śraddhāpūtair dvijottamān yathā hi sukṛte kṣetre phalaṃ vindati kṣetrikaḥ evaṃ dattvā brāhmaṇebhyo dātā phalam upāśnute brāhmaṇāś caiva vidyante satyavanto bahuśrutāḥ na dadāti ca dānāni moghaṃ tasya dhanārjanam utthāyotthāya boddhavyaṃ kim adya sukṛtaṃ mayā dattaṃ vā dāpitaṃ vāpi votsāhyam api vā kṛtam utthāyotthāya dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira āgamiṣyati yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati yac ca vedamayaṃ pātraṃ yac ca pātraṃ tapomayam asaṃkīrṇaṃ ca yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati adhyāyaṃ tapaso vakṣye tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu tapaso hi paraṃ nāsti tapasā vindate phalam ṛṣayas tapa āsthāya modante daivataiḥ saha tapasā prāpyate svargaṃ tapasā prāpyate yaśaḥ āyuḥprakarṣaṃ bhogāṃś ca tapasā vindate naraḥ jñānaṃ vijñānam āstikyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ rūpam uttamam tapasā labhyate sarvaṃ manasā yad yad icchati nātaptatapaso yānti brahmalokaṃ kadācana yat kāryaṃ kiṃcid āsthāya puruṣas tapyate tapaḥ sarvaṃ tat samavāpnoti paratreha ca mānavaḥ surāpaḥ pāradārī ca bhrūṇahā gurutalpagaḥ tapasā tarate sarvaṃ sarvataś ca vimucyate api sarveśvaraḥ sthāṇur viṣṇuś caiva sanātanaḥ brahmā hutāśanaḥ śakras tapasyanti sanātanāḥ ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhvaretasām tapasā divi modante sametā daivataiḥ saha tapasā prāpyate rājyaṃ śakraḥ sarvasureśvaraḥ tapasā pālayan sarvam ahany ahani vṛtrahā sūryācandramasau devau sarvalokahite ratau tapasaiva prakāśete nakṣatrāṇi grahās tathā na cāsti tat sukhaṃ loke yad vinā tapasā kila tapasaiva sukhaṃ sarvam iti dharmavido viduḥ viśvāmitraś ca tapasā brāhmaṇatvam upāgataḥ sarvaṃ ca tapasābhyeti sarvaṃ ca sukham aśnute tapas tapyati yo araṇye munir mūlaphalāśanaḥ ṛcam ekāṃ api paṭhan sa yāti paramāṃ gatim tasmāt tapaḥ samāsthāya prārthayed yad abhīpsitam satyam eva paraṃ brahma satyam eva paraṃ tapaḥ satyam eva paro yajñaḥ satyam eva paraṃ śrutam satyaṃ deveṣu jāgarti muktiḥ satyataroḥ phalam tapo yaśaś ca puṇyaṃ ca pitṛdevarṣipūjanam ādyo vidhiś ca vidyā ca sarvaṃ satye pratiṣṭhitam satyaṃ yajñas tathā vedā mantrā devī sarasvatī vratacaryā tathā satyam oṃkāraḥ satyam eva ca satyena vāyur abhyeti satyena tapate raviḥ satyena cāgnir dahati svargaṃ satyena gacchati satyena cāpaḥ kṣipati parjanyaḥ pṛthivītale pāraṇaṃ sarvavedānāṃ sarvatīrthāvagahanah satyaṃ ca vadato loke tat samaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ aśvamedhasahasraṃ ca satyaṃ ca tulayā dhṛtam aśvamedhasahasrād dhi satyam etad viśiṣyate munayaḥ satyaniratā munayaḥ satyavikramāḥ munayaḥ satyaprapathāḥ parāṃ siddhim ito gatāḥ satyena devāḥ prīyante pitaro brāhmaṇās tathā satyam āhuḥ paraṃ dharmaṃ tasmāt satyaṃ na lopayet munayaḥ satyaniratās tasmāt satyaṃ viśiṣyate svarge satyaparā nityaṃ modante devatā iva apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair vimānair upayānti te vaktavyaṃ hi sadā satyaṃ na satyād vidyate param etat pramāṇaṃ yaḥ kuryāt sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet agādhe vimale śuddhe satyatīrthe hrade śubhe snātavyaṃ manasā yuktaiḥ snānaṃ tat paramaṃ smṛtam ātmārthe ca parārthe vā putrārthe vāpi pārthiva ye anṛtaṃ nābhibhāṣante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ api cedaṃ purā gītaṃ dharmavidbhir yudhiṣṭhira yaḥ satyavādī puruṣo nānṛtaṃ paribhāṣate saṃprāpya virajāṃl lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥ śucīnāṃ śrīmatāṃ gehe jāyate sumahāmatiḥ vidyārogyasukhaiśvaryair yukto yogaparo bhavet ādityacandrāv analānilau ca dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca ahaś ca rātriś ca ubhe ca saṃdhye dharmaś ca jānāti narasya vṛttam tasmān na vācyam anṛtaṃ hi sadbhir evaṃvidhair dharmavido vadanti satyaṃ vadaṃs tejasā dīpyamāno na hīyate dharmayaśo arthakāmaiḥ eṣa vāṇīkṛto dharmo vaidiko dharmaniścaye evam etad yathānyāyaṃ satyādhyāye prakīrtitam tat pramāṇaṃ budhaḥ kuryān na satyād vidyate param sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ pravakṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhira upoṣitaiś ca kaunteya yat prayojyaṃ yathāvidhi phalaṃ yad upavāsasya tan nibodha ca pāṇḍava avāpnoti yathā kāmān upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ mayaite nṛpate kāmyā vihitā hitam icchatā upavāsā manuṣyāṇāṃ mayy evārpitacetasām pañcamīṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhīṃ ca paurṇamāsīṃ ca pāṇḍava upoṣya rūpavān dhanyaḥ subhagaś caiva jāyate aṣṭamīṃ caiva kaunteya śuklapakṣe caturdaśīm upoṣya vyādhirahito vīryavāṃś caiva jāyate mārgaśīrṣaṃ tu yo māsaṃ nityam ekāśano bhavet kṛṣibhāgī bhaved rājan bahuputraś ca jāyate pauṣamāse tu rājendra bhaktenaikena yaḥ kṣapet subhago darśanīyaś ca jñānabhāgī ca jāyate pitṝn uddiśya māghaṃ tu yaḥ kṣaped ekabhojanam māsena puruṣavyāghra so anantyaṃ phalam aśnute bhagadaivatamāsaṃ tu yaḥ kṣaped ekabhojanam strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti vaśyāś cāsya bhavanti tāḥ caitraṃ tu puruṣavyāghra yaḥ kṣaped ekabhojanam māsena puruṣavyāghra maunan tu phalam aśnute bhagadaivatamāsaṃ tu yaḥ kṣaped ekabhojanaḥ strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti vaśyāś cāsya bhavanti tāḥ caitraṃ tu puruṣavyāghra yaḥ kṣaped ekabhojanaḥ suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhye kule mahati jāyate nistared ekabhaktena vaiśākhaṃ yo narādhipa naro vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ vrajet jyeṣṭhamāsam apānīyam ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet aiśvaryaṃ puruṣavyāghra strībhāgī copajāyate āṣāḍhaṃ bharataśreṣṭha ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet śūraś ca bahudhānyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate śrāvaṇaṃ tu naravyāghra bhaktenaikena yaḥ kṣapet yatra yatropapadyeta tatra syāj jñātivardhanaḥ māsaṃ bhādrapadaṃ rājann ekabhaktena yaḥ kṣapet dhanāḍhyo vīryavāṃś caiva aiśvaryaṃ pratipadyate yaḥ kṣaped ekabhaktena māsam āśvayujaṃ naraḥ dhanavān vāhanāḍhyaś ca bahuputraś ca jāyate kārttikaṃ tu naro māsaṃ nityam ekāśano bhavet śūraś ca bahubhāryaś ca kīrtimāṃś caiva jāyate ete māsā naraśreṣṭha ekabhaktena kīrtitāḥ tithīnāṃ niyamāṃś caiva tāñ śṛṇuṣva narādhipa pakṣe pakṣe caturthaṃ tu bhaktaṃ yaḥ kṣapayen naraḥ vipulaṃ dhanam āpnoti bhagavān agnir abravīt māse māse caturthaṃ tu bhaktam ekaṃ tu yaḥ kṣapet kṛṣibhāgī yaśobhāgī tejasvī cāpi jāyate pakṣe pakṣe trirātraṃ tu yaḥ kṣapen narapuṅgava gaṇe ghoṣe pure grāme māhātmyaṃ pratipadyate māse māse trirātraṃ tu bhaktenaikena yaḥ kṣapet gaṇādhipatyaṃ labhate niḥsapatnam akaṇṭakam yas tu sāyaṃ tathā kalyaṃ bhuṅkte naivāntarā pibet ahiṃsānirato nityaṃ juhvāno jātavedasam ṣaḍbhir eva tu varṣais tu sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ aṣṭamena tu bhaktena rājan saṃvatsaraṃ nayet gavāmayasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ haṃsasārasayuktena vimānena sa gacchati pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu svargaloke mahīyate ārto vā vyādhito vāpi gacched anaśanaṃ tu yaḥ pade pade yajñaphalaṃ tasya mannāmakīrtanāt divyaṛkṣaprayuktena vimānena sa gacchati śatam apsarasāṃ caiva ramayantīha taṃ naram sahasraśatasaṃyukte vimāne sūryavarcase ārūḍhastrīśatākīrṇe viharan sukham edhate na kruddho vyādhito nārtaḥ prasannamanasendriyaḥ gacched anaśanaṃ yas tu tasyāpi śṛṇu yat phalam śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ svargaloke mahīyate svasthaḥ saphalasaṃkalpaḥ sukhī vigatakalmaṣaḥ strīsahasrasamākīrṇe suprabhe sukham edhate yāvanti romakūpāni tasya gātreṣu bhārata tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi divyāni divi modate nāsti vedāt paraṃ śāstraṃ nāsti mātṛsamo guruḥ na dharmāt paramo lābhas tapo nānaśanāt param brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paraṃ nāsti divi ceha ca pāvanam upavāsais tathā tulyaṃ tapo hy anyan na vidyate upoṣya vidhivad devās tridivaṃ pratipedire munayaś ca parāṃ siddhim upavāsair avāpnuvan divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā kṣāntam ekena bhaktena yena vipratvam āgataḥ cyavano jamadagniś ca vasiṣṭho gautamo bhṛguḥ sarve hy ete divaṃ prāptāḥ kṣamāvanto bahuśrutāḥ vidhinānena rājendra yo mayā parikīrtitaḥ paṭheta yo vai śṛṇuyāc ca bhaktyā na vidyate tasya narasya pāpam upadravair mucyate sarvāṅgikair na cāpi pāpair abhibhūyate naraḥ brāhmaṇatvaṃ suduṣprāpaṃ nisargād brāhmaṇo bhavet kṣatriyo vāthavā vaiśyo nisargād eva jāyate duṣkṛtena tu duṣṭātmā sthānād bhraśyati mānavaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ sthānaṃ samāsādya tasmād rakṣeta paṇḍitaḥ yas tu vipratvam utsṛjya kṣatriyatvaṃ niṣevate brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatrayonyāṃ prasūyate vaiśyakarmāṇi vā kurvan vaiśyayonau prajāyate śūdrakarmāṇi kurvāṇaḥ śūdratvam upapadyate sa tatra durgatiṃ prāpya sthānād bhraṣṭo yudhiṣṭhira śūdrayonim anuprāpto yadi dharmaṃ na sevate mānuṣyāt sa paribhraṣṭas tiryagyonau prajāyate adharmasevanān mūḍhas tamopahatacetanaḥ jātyantarasahasrāṇi tatraiva parivartate tasmāt prāpya śubhaṃ sthānaṃ pramādān na tu nāśayet śūdrānnenāvaśeṣeṇa yo mriyej jaṭhare dvijaḥ āhitāgnis tathā yajvā sa śūdragatibhāg bhavet kṣatrānnenāvaśeṣeṇa kṣatratvam upapadyate vaiśyānnenāvaśeṣeṇa vaiśyatvam upapadyate tāṃ yoniṃ labhate vipro bhuktvānnaṃ yasya vai mṛtaḥ brāhmaṇatvaṃ śubhaṃ prāpya durlabhaṃ yo avamanyate bhojyābhojyaṃ na jānāti sa bhavet kṣatriyo dvijaḥ karmaṇā yena medhāvī śūdro vaiśyo abhijāyate tat te vakṣyāmi nikhilaṃ yena varṇottamo bhavet śūdrakarma yathoddiṣṭaṃ śūdro bhūtvā samācaret yathāvat paricaryāṃ tu triṣu varṇeṣu nityadā kurute avimanā yas tu sa śūdro vaiśyatāṃ vrajet kṣatriyatvaṃ yathā vaiśyas tad vakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ caukṣaḥ pāpajanadveṣṭā śeṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ agnihotram upādāya juhvānaś ca yathāvidhi sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyakule jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ kṣatriyo brahmayonyāṃ tu jāyate śṛṇu tad yathā dadāti yajate yajñair vidhivac cāptadakṣiṇaiḥ adhīte svargam anvicchaṃs tretāgniśaraṇaḥ sadā ārtahastaprado nityaṃ prajā dharmeṇa pālayan ṛtukāle tu svāṃ bhāryām abhigacchan vidhānataḥ sarvātithyaṃ trivargasya dīyatāṃ bhujyatām iti śūdrāṇāṃ yācakānāṃ ca nityaṃ siddhim iti bruvan gobrāhmaṇasya cārthāya raṇe cābhimukho hataḥ tretāgnimantrapūtātmā kṣatriyo brāhmaṇo bhavet vidhijñaḥ kṣatriyakule yājakaḥ sa tu jāyate prāpyate avikalaḥ svargo varṇaiḥ satpatham āsthitaiḥ brāhmaṇatvaṃ suduṣprāpaṃ kṛcchreṇāsādyate naraiḥ tasmāt sarvaprayatnena rakṣed brāhmaṇyam uttamam suvarṇaṃ paramaṃ dānaṃ suvarṇaṃ dakṣiṇā parā etat pavitraṃ paramam etat svastyayanaṃ mahat daśa pūrvāparān vaṃśān ātmānaṃ ca viśāmyate api pāpaśataṃ kṛtvā dattvā vipreṣu tārayet suvarṇaṃ ye prayacchanti narāḥ śuddhena cetasā devatās te prayacchanti samastā iti naḥ śrutam agnir hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇaṃ ca hutāśanaḥ tasmāt suvarṇaṃ dadatā dattāḥ sarvāś ca devatāḥ agnyabhāve ca kurvanti vahnisthāneṣu kāñcanam sarvavedapramāṇajñā vedaśrutinidarśanāt ye tv enaṃ jvālayitvāgnim ādityodayanaṃ prati dadyur vai vratam uddiśya sarvān kāmān avāpnuyuḥ suvarṇadaḥ svargaloke kāmān iṣṭān upāśnute virajāmbarasaṃvītaḥ pariyāti yatas tataḥ vimānenārkavarṇena bhāsvareṇa virājatā apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇe bhāsvatā svena tejasā haṃsabarhiṇayuktena kāmagena narottamaḥ divyagandhavahaḥ svarge parigacched itas tataḥ tasmāt svaśaktyā dātavyaṃ kāñcanaṃ mānavair bhuvi na hy ataḥ paramaṃ loke sadyaḥ pāpavimocanam suvarṇasya tu śuddhasya suvarṇaṃ yaḥ prayacchati bahūny abdasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate lokāṃs tu sṛjatā pūrvaṃ gāvaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā prītyarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tasmāt tā mātaraḥ smṛtāḥ tās tu dattvā saurabheyīḥ svargaloke mahīyate tasmāt tā varṇayiṣyāmi dānaṃ cāsāṃ yathāvidhi yādṛśī vidhinā yena dātavyā yādṛśāya ca dvijāya poṣaṇārthaṃ tu homadhenukṛte na vai prathamā gaurakapilā dvitīyā gaurapiṅgalā tṛtīyā raktakapilā caturthī nīlapiṅgalā pañcamī śuklapiṅgākṣī ṣaṣṭhī tu śuklapiṅgalā saptamī citrapiṅgākṣī aṣṭamī babhrurohiṇī navamī śvetapiṅgākṣī daśamī śvetapiṅgalā tādṛśā ye apy anaḍvāhaḥ kapilās te prakīrtitāḥ brāhmaṇo vāhayet tāṃs tu nānyo varṇaḥ kadācana dhenuṃ dattvā suvratāṃ sopadhānāṃ kalyāṇavatsāṃ ca payasvinīṃ ca yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti dhenvā duhyeta kāmān nṛpa varṣāṇi tāvat prayacchate yaḥ kapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ kanakāgraśṛṅgīm tais tair guṇaiḥ kāmdughā hi bhūtvā naraṃ pradātāram upaiti sā gauḥ gosahasraṃ tu yo dadyāt sarvakāmair alaṃkṛtam parāṃ vṛddhiṃ śriyaṃ prāpya svargaloke mahīyate daśa cobhayataḥ pretya mātāmahapitāmahaiḥ gacchet sukṛtināṃ lokān gāvo dattvā yathāvidhi dāyādalabdhair arthair yo gavāḥ krītvā prayacchati tasyāpi cākṣayā lokā bhavantīha paratra ca yo dyūtena dhanaṃ jitvā krītvā gāvaḥ prayacchati sa gacched virajāṃl lokān gopradānaphalārjitān pratigṛhya tu yo dadyād gāvaḥ śuddhena cetasā sa gatvā durgamaṃ sthānam amaraiḥ saha modate yaś cātmavikrayaṃ kṛtvā gāvo dadyād yathāvidhi sa gatvā virajāṃl lokān sukhaṃ vasati devavat saṃgrāme yas tanuṃ tyaktvā gāvaḥ krītvā prayacchati dehavikrayamūlyas tāḥ śāśvatāḥ kāmadohanāḥ rūpānvitāḥ śīlavayopapannāḥ sarvāḥ praśastā hi sugandhavatyaḥ yathā hi gaṅgā saritāṃ variṣṭhā tathārjunīnāṃ kapilā variṣṭhā antarjātāḥ sukrayajñānalabdhāḥ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā sodakāḥ sodvahāś ca kṛcchrotsṛṣṭāḥ poṣaṇāyābhyupetā dvārair etair goviśeṣā variṣṭhāḥ tisro rātryaś cāpy upoṣyeha dātā tṛptā gā vai tarpitebhyaḥ prayacchet vatsaiḥ pītāḥ sopadhānās tryahaṃ ca dattvā gā vai gorasair vartitavyam loke jyeṣṭhā lokavṛttāntavṛttā vedair gītāḥ somaniṣyandabhūtāḥ saumyāḥ puṇyāḥ kāmadāḥ prāṇadāś ca gāvo dattvā sarvadā santi santaḥ na caivāsāṃ dānamātraṃ praśastaṃ pātraṃ kālo goviśeṣo vidhiś ca dṛṣṭvā gāvaḥ pāvakādityabhūtāḥ svādhyāyāḍhye pātravarye viśiṣṭe vaitānasthaṃ satyavākyaṃ kṛtajñaṃ goṣu kṣāntaṃ gośaraṇyaṃ suvṛttaṃ śastaṃ pātraṃ gopradānasya bhūmes tathā suvarṇasya ca sarvakālam bhikṣādānaṃ cādhikaṃ saṃpraśastaṃ pāthodānaṃ cānnadānaṃ tathā ca bhikṣate bahubhṛtyāya śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye dātavyā gauḥ prayatnena ekāpy atiphalā hi sā tāṃ ced vikrīṇate rājan vacasā kaluṣīkṛtām nāsau praśasyate vipro brāhmaṇo naiva sa smṛtaḥ tasyādharmapravṛttasya lubdhasyānṛtavādinaḥ havyakavyavyapetasya na deyā gauḥ kathaṃcana jīrṇāṃ caivopabhuktāṃ ca jaratkūpam ivāphalām tamaḥ praviśate dātā dvijaṃ kleśena yojayan duṣṭāḥ kṛśāś caiva pālayatīś ca naitādṛśā dānayogyā bhavanti kleśair vipraṃ yo aphalaiḥ saṃyunakti gacchet sa tiryag viphalāṃś ca lokān anaḍvāhaṃ suvrataṃ yo dadāti halasya voḍhāram anantavīryam yugaṃdharaṃ balavantaṃ yuvānaṃ prāpnoti lokān daśadhenudasya prayacchate yaḥ puruṣo dvijāya svādhyāyacāritraguṇānvitāya balena yuktaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tu nīlaṃ ṣaḍāṅgavaṃ prītikaraṃ surūpam yuvānaṃ balinaṃ śyāmaṃ śatena saha yūthapam gavendraṃ brāhmaṇendrāya bhūriśṛṅgam alaṃkṛtam vṛṣabhaṃ ye prayacchanti śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye te gatvā tadgavāṃ lokaṃ devalokān mahattaram tatra sthitvā tu suciraṃ sarvakāmaiḥ sutarpitāḥ aiśvarye te abhijāyante jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ sadakṣiṇāṃ kāñcanarūpyaśṛṅgīṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ kanakottarīyām dhenuṃ tilānāṃ kanakottarīyām lokā vasūnām acalā bhavanti tilālābhe tu yo dadyād ghṛtadhenuṃ yatavrataḥ sa durgāt tārito dhenvā brahmaloke mahīyate ghṛtālābhe tu yo dadyāj jaladhenuṃ yatavrataḥ sa sarvaṃ tarate durgaṃ jalaṃ divyaṃ samaśnute brāhmaṇāś caiva gāvaś ca kulam ekaṃ dvidhākṛtam ekatra mantrās tiṣṭhanti havir ekatra tiṣṭhati upagamya tu yo dadyād gāvaḥ śuddhena cetasā yāvanti tāsāṃ romāṇi tāvat svarge mahīyate śṛṇu tvaṃ me gavāṃ lokā yādṛśā yatra vā sthitāḥ manojñā ramaṇīyāś ca sarvakāmadughāḥ sadā puṇyāḥ pāpaharāś caiva gavāṃ lokā na saṃśayaḥ atyantasukhinas tatra sarvapāpavivarjitāḥ pramodante mahāsthāne narā vigatakalmaṣāḥ te vrajante vimāneṣu grahā divi gatā iva evaṃ yair dattasatkārāḥ surabhyaś cārcitāḥ sadā kāmarūpā mahātmānaḥ pūtā vigatakilbiṣāḥ tulyaprabhāvā devais te modante apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ gandharvair upagīyante gośaraṇyā na saṃśayaḥ brahmaṇyāḥ sādhuvṛttāś ca dayāvanto anukampinaḥ ghṛṇinaḥ śubhakarmāṇo modante te amaraiḥ saha yathaiva salile matsyaḥ salilena sahohyate gobhiḥ pāpakṛtaṃ karma dṛḍham eva mayohyate mātaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ prajāsaṃrakṣaṇe smṛtāḥ brahmaṇā lokasāreṇa gāvaḥ pāpabhayāpahāḥ tāsu dattāsu rājendra kiṃ na dattaṃ bhaved iha kṛśāya tu viśeṣeṇa vṛttiglānāya sīdate bhūdānena samaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati iti dharmavidaḥ prāhus tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svarge vasati bhūmidaḥ ācchettā cānumantā ca tāny eva narake vaset atidānaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ bhūmidānam ihocyate acalā hy akṣayā bhūmiḥ sarvān kāmān prayacchati bhūmidaḥ svargam āruhya śāśvatīr edhati samāḥ punaś ca janma saṃprāpya bhaved bhūmipatir dhruvam yathā bhūmiḥ sadā devī dātāraṃ kurute patim evaṃ sadakṣiṇā dattā kurute gaur janādhipam api pāpakṛtaṃ prāpya pratigṛhṇīta bhūmidam mahīṃ dadan pavitrī syāt puṇyā hi jagatī yataḥ nāma vai priyadatteti guhyam etat sanātanam tad asyāḥ satataṃ prītyai kīrtanīyaṃ prayacchatā yat kiṃcit kurute pāpaṃ puruṣo vṛttikarṣitaḥ api gocarmamātreṇa bhūmidānena śudhyati suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇimuktāvasūni ca sarvān etān mahāprājña dadāti vasudhāṃ dadan tapo yajñāḥ śrutaṃ śīlam alobhaḥ satyavāditā gurudaivatapūjā ca nātikramanti bhūmidam bhartur niḥśreyase yuktās tyaktātmāno raṇe hatāḥ brahmalokagatāḥ santo nātikrāmanti bhūmidam phalakṛṣṭāṃ mahīṃ dattvā sodakāṃ saphalānvitām sodakaṃ vāpi śaraṇaṃ prāpnoti mama saṃpadam ratnopakīṛṇāṃ vasudhāṃ yo dadāti dvijātaye muktaḥ sa kaluṣaiḥ sarvaiḥ svargaloke mahīyate ikṣubhiḥ saṃtatāṃ bhūmiṃ yavagodhūmaśāḍbalām ye prayacchanti viprebhyo nopasarpanti te yamam sarvakāmadughāṃ dhenuṃ sarvasasyasamudbhavām yo dadāti dvijendrāya brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati bhūmidānaṃ naraḥ kurvan mucyate mahato bhayāt na bhūyo bhūmidānād dhi dānam anyad viśiṣyate puṇyāṃ sarvarasāṃ bhūmiṃ yo dadāti nararṣabha na tasya lokāḥ kṣīyante bhūmidasya mahātmanaḥ yathā janitrī puṣṇāti kṣīreṇa svasutaṃ nṛpa evaṃ sarvaguṇā bhūmir dātāram anupuṣyati agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair iṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ na tat phalaṃ avāpnoti yad dattvā vasudhāṃ nṛpa mṛtyor hi kiṃkarā daṇḍā hy agnitāpāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ghorāś ca vāruṇāḥ pāśā nopasarpanti bhūmidam pitaraḥ pitṛlokasthā devaloke divaukasaḥ saṃtarpayanti dātāraṃ bhūmeḥ prabhavatāṃ vara kṛśāya kṛśabhṛtyāya vṛttikṣīṇāya sīdate bhūmiṃ vṛttikārīṃ dattvā sattrī bhavati mānavaḥ siṃhāsanaṃ tathā cchattraṃ varāśvā varavāraṇāḥ bhūmidānasya puṣpāṇi phalaṃ svargaṃ tathaiva ca ādityā iva dīpyante tejasā divi mānavāḥ ye prayacchanti vasudhāṃ brāhmaṇāyāhitāgnaye yathā bījāni rohanti prakīrṇāni mahītale tathā kāmādhirohanti bhūmidānaguṇārjitāḥ āsphoṭayanti pitaraḥ pravalganti pitāmahāḥ bhūmido naḥ kule jātaḥ sa naḥ saṃtārayiṣyati ādityā vasavo rudrā hy aśvinau vasubhiḥ saha śūlapāṇiś ca bhagavān abhinandanti bhūmidam sa naḥ kulasya puruṣaḥ sa no bandhuḥ sa no gatiḥ sa dātā sa ca vikrānto yo dadāti vasuṃdharām dātāram anugṛhṇāti yathā dattena rocate pūrvadattāṃ haran bhūmiṃ narakāyopapadyate vindhyāṭavīṣv atoyāsu śuṣkakoṭaravāsinaḥ kṛṣṇasarpā hi jāyante ye haranti vasuṃdharām patanty aśrūṇi rudatāṃ dīnānām avasīdatām brāhmaṇānāṃ hṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ hanyāt tripuruṣaṃ kulam sādhubhyo bhūmim ākṣipya na bhūtiṃ vindate kvacit dattvā hi bhūmiṃ sādhubhyo vindate bhūtim uttamām pūrvadattāṃ dvijātibhyo yatnād rakṣa yudhiṣṭhira mahīṃ mahībhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha dānāc chreyo anupālanam yatraiṣaḥ paṭhyate śrāddhe bhūmidānasya saṃstavaḥ na tatra rakṣasāṃ bhāgo nāsurāṇāṃ kathaṃcana akṣayaṃ tu bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ tasmād viśrāvayed enaṃ śrāddheṣu brāhmaṇān sadā evam etad yathoddiṣṭaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam bhūmidānaṃ mahārāja sarvapāpāpahaṃ śubham agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair iṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ na tat phalam avāpnoti saṃgrāme yad avāpnuyāt iti yajñavidaḥ prāhur yajñakarmaviśāradāḥ tasmāt tat te pravakṣyāmi yat phalaṃ śastrajīvinām dharmalābho arthalābhaś ca yaśolābhas tathaiva ca yaḥ śūro vadhyate yuddhe vimṛdan paravāhinīm tasya dharmārthakāmāś ca yajñāś caivāptadakṣiṇāḥ paraṃ hy abhimukhaṃ hatvā tadyānaṃ yo adhirohati viṣṇukrāntaṃ sa yajata evaṃ yudhyan raṇājire aśvamedhān avāpnoti caturas tena karmaṇā yas tu śastram anutsṛjya vīryavān vāhinīmukhe saṃmukho vartate śūraḥ sa svargān na vivartate rājānaṃ rājaputraṃ vā senāpatim athāpi vā hanyāt kṣatreṇa yaḥ śūras tasya loko akṣayo dhruvaḥ yāvanti tasya śastrāṇi bhindanti tvacam āhave tāvato labhate lokān sarvakāmadugho akṣayān vīrāsanaṃ vīraśayyā vīrasthānasthitiḥ sthirā gavārthe brāhmaṇārthe vā svāmyarthe tu kṛtaṃ ca yaiḥ te gacchanty amalaṃ sthānaṃ yathā sukṛtinas tathā abhagnaṃ yaḥ paraṃ hanyād bhagnaṃ ca parirakṣati yasmin sthite palāyanti so api prāpnoti svargatim ūrdhvaṃ tiryak ca yaś cārvāk prāṇān saṃtyajate yudhi hatāśvaś ca pated yuddhe sa svargān na nivartate yasya cihnīkṛtaṃ gātraṃ śaraśaktyṛṣṭitomaraiḥ devakanyās tu taṃ vīraṃ ramayanti ramanti ca varāpsaraḥsahasrāṇi śūram āyodhane hatam tvaritāny abhidhāvanti mama bhartā mameti ca hatasyābhimukhasyājau patitasyānivartinaḥ hriyate yat parair dravyaṃ naramedhaphalaṃ tu tat bhūyo gatiṃ pravakṣyāmi raṇe ye abhimukhā hatāḥ śakyaṃ tv iha samṛddhais tu yaṣṭuṃ kratuśatair naraiḥ ātmadehaṃ tu viprārthe tyaktuṃ yuddhe suduṣkaram yāṃ yajñasaṃghais tapasā ca viprāḥ svargaiṣiṇas tatra cayaiḥ prayānti kṣaṇena tām eva gatiṃ prayānti mahāhave svāṃ tanuṃ saṃtyajantaḥ sarvāṃś ca vedān saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca vane ca vāsam etān guṇān eka evātiśete saṃgrāmadhāmny ātmatanuṃ tyajed yaḥ imāṃ giraṃ citrapadāṃ śubhākṣarāṃ subhāṣitāṃ vṛtabhidāṃ divaukasām camūmukhe yaḥ smarate dṛḍhasmṛtir na hanyate hanti ca so araṇe ripūn eṣa puṇyatamaḥ svargyaḥ suyajñaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ kṣatriyasya viśeṣataḥ bhūyaś caiva pravakṣyāmi bhīṣmavākyam anuttamam yādṛśāya prahartavyaṃ yādṛśaṃ parivarjayet ātatāyinam āyāntam api vedāntagaṃ raṇe jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyān na tena brahmahā bhavet hatāśvaś ca na hantavyaḥ pānīyaṃ yaś ca yācate vyādhito durbalaś caiva rathahīnas tathaiva ca bhagnadhanvācchinaguṇaḥ prāṇepsuḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bruvan vimuktakeśo dhāved yo yaś conmattākṛtir bhavet parṇaśākhātṛṇagrāhī tavāsmīti ca yo vadet brāhmaṇo asmīti yaś cāha bālo vṛddho napuṃsakaḥ tasmād etān parihared yathoddiṣṭān raṇājire hato na hanyate sadbhir hatā eva hi bhīravaḥ amāṃsabhakṣaṇe rājan yo dharmaḥ kurupuṅgava tan me śṛṇu yathātathyaṃ yaś cāsya vidhir uttamaḥ māsi māsy aśvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ na ca khādati yo māṃsaṃ samam etad yudhiṣṭhira sadā yajati sattreṇa sadā dānaṃ prayacchati sadā tapasvī bhavati madhumāṃsavivarjanāt sarvavedā na tat kuryuḥ sarvadānāni caiva hi yo māṃsarasam āsvādya sarvamāṃsāni varjayet duṣkaraṃ hi rasajñena māṃsasya parivarjanam caturvratam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ prāṇināṃ mṛtyubhīruṇām tadā bhavati loke asmin prāṇināṃ jīvitaiṣiṇām viśvāsyaś copagamyaś ca na hi hiṃsārudir yadā duṣṭarāṃs tarate maāṃ māṃsasya parivarjanāt prāṇā yathātmano abhīṣṭā bhūtānām api te tathā ātmaupamyena gantavyaṃ buddhimadbhir mahātmabhiḥ ahiṃsā paramo dharmaḥ satyam eva ca pāṇḍava ahiṃsā caiva satyaṃ ca dharmo hi paramaḥ smṛtaḥ na hi māṃsaṃ tṛṇāt kāṣṭhād upalād vāpi jāyate jīvād utpadyate māṃsaṃ tasmād garhanti tad budhāḥ yadi vai khādako na syān na tadā ghātako bhavet lobhād vā buddhimohād vā yo māṃsāny atti mānavaḥ nirghṛṇaḥ sa hi mantavyaḥ saddharmaparivarjitaḥ svamāṃsaṃ paramāṃsena yo vardhayitum icchati udvignavāse vasati yatratatrābhijāyate dhanena krāyako hanti upabhogena khādakaḥ ghātako vadhabandhābhyām ity eṣa trividho vadhaḥ bhakṣayitvā tu yo māṃsaṃ paścād api nivartate tasyāpi sumahān dharmo yaḥ pāpād vinivartate varam ekasya sattvasya dadyād akṣayadakṣiṇām na tu viprasahasrasya gosahasraṃ sakāñcanam yo dadyāt kāñcanaṃ meruṃ kṛtsnāṃ vāpi vasuṃdharām abhakṣaṇaṃ ca māṃsasya na tu tulyaṃ yudhiṣṭhira idam anyat pravakṣyāmi purāṇam ṛṣinirmitam śrūyate ca purākalpe hy ṛṣīṇāṃ vrīhayaḥ paśuḥ yajante yena vai yajñān ṛṣayaḥ puṇyakarmiṇaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saṃśayaṃ pṛṣṭo vasū rājā tataḥ purā abhakṣyaṃ bhakṣyam iti vai māṃsam āha narādhipa ākāśān medinīṃ prāptas tataḥ sa pṛthivīpatiḥ etad eva punaś coktvā viveśa dharaṇītalam kaumudaṃ tu viśeṣeṇa śuklapakṣe narādhipa varjayet sarvamāṃsāni dharmo hy atra vidhīyate caturo vārṣikān māsān yo māṃsaṃ parivarjayet catvāri bhadrāṇy āpnoti kīrtir āyur yaśo balam apy ekam iha yo māsaṃ sarvamāṃsāni varjayet atītya sarvaduḥkhāni sukhaṃ jīven nirāmayaḥ yo hi varṣaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ tapas tapyet sudāruṇam apy ekaṃ varjayen māsaṃ māṃsam etat samaṃ matam yo varjayati māṃsāni māsaṃ pakṣam athāpi vā sa vai hiṃsānivṛttas tu brahmaloke mahīyate sarvakālaṃ tu māṃsāni varjitāni maharṣibhiḥ manvā kṣupeṇa śvetena tathaivekṣvākunāpi ca bhṛguṇā nalarāmābhyāṃ dilīparaghupauravaiḥ āyuṣā caiva gārgyeṇa janakaiś cakravartibhiḥ dhundhumārāmbarīṣābhyāṃ nahuṣeṇa ca dhīmatā gādhinā purukutsena kuruṇā puruṇā tathā mucukundena māndhātrā sagareṇa mahātmanā śibinā cāśvapatinā vīrasenādibhis tathā saṃjayenātha bhīṣmeṇa puṣkareṇātha pāṇḍunā suvarṇaṣṭhīvinā caiva duṣvantanṛgarohitaiḥ etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhiḥ sarvair māṃsaṃ na bhakṣitam śaratkaumudikaṃ māsaṃ tataḥ svargaṃ gatā nṛpāḥ sarvakāmasamṛddhās te vasanti divi saṃsthitāḥ brahmaloke ca pūjyante jvalamānāḥ śriyāvṛtāḥ upāsyamānā gāndharvaiḥ strīsahasrasamanvitāḥ tad evam uttamaṃ dharmam ahiṃsālakṣaṇaṃ śubhan ye rakṣanti mahātmāno nākapṛṣṭhe vasanti te madhu māṃsaṃ ca ye nityaṃ varjayantīha mānavāḥ janmaprabhṛti madyaṃ ca sarve te munayaḥ smṛtāḥ āpannaś cāpado mucyed baddho mucyeta bandhanāt vyādhito mucyate rogād duḥkhān mucyeta duḥkhitaḥ yaś cainaṃ paṭhate nityaṃ prayatnād bharatarṣabha ghoraṃ saṃtarate durgaṃ svargavāsaṃ ca vindati tiryagyoniṃ na gacchec ca rūpavāṃś caiva jāyate etat te kathitaṃ rājan māṃsasya parivarjanam pravṛttau ca nivṛttau ca pramāṇam ṛṣisattamaiḥ gobrāhmaṇahitārthāya cāturvarṇyahitāya ca aśiṣṭanigrahārthāya śiṣṭānāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca yudhiṣṭhirasya rājarṣer evaṃ nārāyaṇo abravīt pañca rūpāṇi rājāno dhārayanty amitaujasaḥ agner indrasya somasya yamasya varuṇasya ca tān na hiṃsen na cākrośen nākṣipen nāpriyaṃ vadet devā mānuṣarūpeṇa caranti pṛthivīm imām indrāt prabhutvaṃ jvalanāt pratāpaṃ krauryaṃ yamād vaiśravaṇāt prabhāvam sattvasthitiṃ rāmajanārdanābhām ādāya rājñaḥ kriyate śarīram na cāpi rājā mantavyo manuṣyo ayam iti prabho mahatī devatā hy eṣā nararūpeṇa tiṣṭhati svayam indro naro bhūtvā pṛthivīm anuśāsati na hi pālayituṃ śakto manuṣyaḥ pṛthivīm imām yat prajāpālanaiḥ puṇyaṃ prāpnuvantīha pārthivāḥ na tat kratusahasreṇa prāpnuvanti dvijottamāḥ adhītahutataptasya karmaṇaḥ sukṛtasya ca ṣaṣṭhaṃ labhati bhāgaṃ tu prajā dharmeṇa pālayan grāmādhipatyaṃ nagarādhipatyaṃ deśādhipatyaṃ pṛthivīpatitvam na prāpnuvantīha manuṣyamātrā ye devatānāṃ na bhavanti bhāgāḥ na tad asti vrataṃ loke yad rājñaś caritopamam na tad vedarahasyaṃ vā yad rājñaḥ phalato adhikam evaṃvṛttās tu rājāno devabhāgā na mānuṣāḥ caturvedyaṃ hutacana yo hiṃseta narādhipaḥ daṇḍasyaite bhayād bhītā na khādanti parasparam jadaṇḍabhayāt ke na durvanti hi pātakam yamadaṇḍabhayād anye na durvanti parasparam nābhīto yajate kāṃścan nābhīto daṇḍam icchati ya eva devā hantāras tāṃl loko arcayate bhṛśam hantā śakraś ca rudraś ca hantā vaiśravaṇo yamaḥ varuṇo vāyur ādityaḥ parjanyo agnir bṛhaspatiḥ etān devān namasyanti pratāpapraṇatā janāḥ na brahmāṇaṃ na dhātāraṃ na pūṣāṇaṃ kathaṃcana daṇḍagrastaṃ jagat sarvaṃ vaśyatvam anugacchati nāyaṃ klībasya loko asti na paraḥ pārthivottama na hi paśyāmi jīvantaṃ rājan kaṃcid ahiṃsayā udake jantavo nityaṃ pṛthivyāṃ ca phaleṣu ca na hatvā lipyate rājā prajā dharmeṇa pālayan yadi daṇḍo na vidyeta durvinītās tatho narāḥ hanyuḥ paśūn manuṣyāṃś ca yājñiyāni haviṃṣi ca vṛkavat kṣapayeyuś ca yo yasya balavattaraḥ tasmāt prāṇihite daṇḍe hiṃsādoṣo na bādhate naivostrā na balīvardā nāśvāśvataragardabhāḥ yuktā vaheyur yānāni daṇḍaś cen nodyato bhavet satyaṃ kilaitad yad uvāca śakro daṇḍaḥ prajā rakṣati sādhuvṛttaḥ yasyāgnayaḥ pratimāsasya bhītāḥ saṃtarjitā daṇḍabhayāj jvalanti yatra śyāmo lohitākṣo daṇḍaś carati pāpahā prajās tatra na muhyante netā cet sādhu paśyati daṇḍanītau sunītāyāṃ sarve sidhyanty upakramāḥ daṇḍaś cen na pravarteta vinaśyeyur imāḥ prajāḥ vṛkavad bhakṣayeyuś ca yo yasya balavattaraḥ kākādyāś ca purodāśaṃ śvā caivāvalihed dhaviḥ svāmyaṃ ca na syāt kasmiṃścit pravartetādharottaram cāturvarṇyavimokṣāya durvinītabhayāya ca daṇḍena niyato loko dharmasthānaṃ ca rakṣati sarvo daṇḍajito loko durlabho hi śucir janaḥ daṇḍasya hi bhayād bhītā narās tiṣṭhanti śāsane ti api bhogāya kalpante daṇḍenoparipīḍitāḥ gurur ātmavatāṃ śāstā śāstā rājā durātmanāṃ ihapracchannapāpānāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ pāpānām atha mūḍhānāṃ paradravyāpahāriṇām paradāraratā ye ca ye ca pātakasaṃjñitāḥ teṣāṃ tu śāsanārthāya mayaitat samudāhṛtam brāhmaṇyaṃ duṣkaraṃ jñātvā tasya daṇḍaṃ nipātayet karmānurūpo daṇḍaḥ syād gohiraṇyādiko bhavet avadhyo brāhmaṇo rājan strī vṛddho bāla eva ca yaś cared aśubhaṃ karma pāpaṃ rājavigarhitam pātakeṣu ca varteta nigrahaṃ tasya kārayet śiraso muṇḍanaṃ kṛtvā gomayenānulepayet kharayānena nagaraṃ ḍiṇḍimena tu bhrāmayet rājanirdiṣṭadaṇḍasya prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate eṣa te kathito daṇḍo brāhmaṇasya yudhiṣṭhira kṣatriyasya tu yo daṇḍas taṃ vakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ paradravyādiharaṇe paradārābhimardane pātakeṣu ca sarveṣu yo hi varteta kṣatriyaḥ tasya daṇḍaṃ pravakṣyāmi tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu hastapādaparicchedaṃ karṇanāsāvakartanam sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā pararāṣṭrāya preśayet rājyaṃ kāṅkṣeta yo mūḍho rājapatnīm athāpi vā śarais tu rājā vidhyeta śakticakragadādibhiḥ kṣatriyasya tu duṣṭasya daṇḍa eṣa vidhīyate vaiśyasyāpi ca yo daṇḍas taṃ pravakṣyāmi bhārata pātakeṣv eva krūreṣu yas tu vaiśyaḥ pravartate paradāre paradravye tasya nigraham ādiśet śūlāyāṃ bhedanaṃ tasya vṛkṣaśākhāvalambanam etad vaiśyasya nirdiṣṭaṃ śūdrasyāpy anupūrvaśaḥ śūle śūdrasya yo duṣṭas tasyaikasya vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ kuñjareṇābhimardeta mīnīyām atha pācayet etac chūdrasya nirdiṣṭaṃ nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate naikasyārthe kulaṃ hanyān na rāṣṭraṃ na ca grāmakam dhanalobhān na moktavyo rāgād vā śāsanaṃ vinā ekaṃ suśiṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ kośaṃ praveśayet yudhiṣṭhirasya rājarṣer evaṃ nārāyaṇo abravīt samāsena yathānyāyaṃ daṇḍanītim anuttamām uttamādhamakāryeṣu sameṣu viṣameṣu ca rājadharmāṃs tu paśyeta viṣṇunā samudāhṛtān etān dharmāñ jagannāthaḥ pāṇḍuputrāya pṛcchate jagāda puruṣavyāghra kim anyac chrotum icchasi bhagavan vahatāṃ bhaktiṃ devadeve janārdane yat phalaṃ kathitaṃ tajjñais tan me vistarato vada yat phalaṃ vahatāṃ bhaktim acyute bhavati prabho na tad varṇayituṃ śakyaṃ hariḥ sarvepsitapradaḥ yādṛk sattvaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tādṛg ārādhya keśavam phalam icchanti tādṛc ca labhyate tair nareśvara muktikāmā narā muktiṃ svargaṃ devatvam īpsavaḥ gandharvayakṣasiddhānāṃ vṛṇvanty anye salokatām varṣeṣv abhīpsavo viṣṇuṃ pātāleṣu tathāpare bhogān abhīpsavo viṣṇuṃ toṣayaṇti narādhipa tathāpare naraiśvaryam ārogyaṃ guṇavad bhuvi prārthayanty acyutaṃ devam ārādhya jagato gatim dharmopadeśād acalāṃ vahan bhaktiṃ janārdane saśarīro gataḥ svargaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tathaiva janakaḥ kṛṣṇe viniveśya svamānasam avāpa paramāṃ siddhiṃ vasuḥ prāyāt tripiṣṭapam anye ca ye ye munayo ye ye ca vasudhādhipāḥ avāpur atulān kāmāṃs te te saṃtoṣya keśavam anārādhya jagannāthaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim sadgatiḥ kena saṃprāptā bhogāś cāpi manoramāḥ drauṇibrahmāstranirdagdhas tava rājan pitāmahaḥ viṣṇoḥ kāryamanuṣyasya darśanād utthitaḥ punaḥ nāmasaṃkīrtanād yasya pāpam anyair upadravaiḥ samaṃ vināśam āyāti devaḥ ko abhyadhikas tataḥ rāṣṭrasya śaraṇaṃ rājā pitarau bālakasya ca dharmaḥ samastamartyānāṃ sarvasya śaraṇaṃ hariḥ muktihetum anādyantam ajam akṣayam acyutam namasyan sarvalokasya namasyo jāyate naraḥ na hi tasya guṇāḥ sarve sarvair munigaṇair api vaktuṃ śakyā viyuktasya sattvādyair akhilair guṇaiḥ śrutaṃ mayā yathā pūrvam āryako me yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saśarīro gataḥ svargaṃ jitam ātmīyakarmabhiḥ yat tv etad bhagavān āha sa yathā pāṇdupūrvajaḥ dharmopadeśād govindam ārādhayata tad vada purā śāsati dharmajñe dharmaputre yudhiṣṭhire tasyaiva vaiśvadevānte caṇḍālo abhyāgamat kila samupetya gṛhaṃ tasya dharmaputrasya vismitaḥ uvāca śvapaco dvāḥsthaṃ praśrayāvanatasthitaḥ kasyaitad bhavanaṃ divyaṃ maṇiratnavibhūṣitam śuddhasphaṭikasopānaṃ maṇikāñcanatoraṇam aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ dine dine yudhiṣṭhiram ṛte bhūpaṃ bhuñjate kasya veśmani katham etan na jānīṣe candrabimbam ivāparam yudhiṣṭhirasya bhavanaṃ devarājagṛhopamam abalasya balaṃ rājā bālasya ruditaṃ balam balaṃ mūrkhasya vai maunaṃ taskarasyānṛtaṃ balam gaccha jalpa svarājānaṃ pratīhāra vaco mama duḥkhārtaḥ kāryavān rājaṃś caṇḍālo dvāri tiṣṭhati kenāpi hetumātreṇa bhavantaṃ duṣṭam āgataḥ ity ukto dharmarājasya pratīhāro yathoditam nivedayām āsa tathā dharmarājo abravīd idam kiṃ rūpaṃ kīdṛśaṃ śīlaṃ ko asyārthaḥ kiṃ prayojanam brūhi dvāḥstha yathāvan me naras tiṣṭhati kīdṛśaḥ kākakokilakṛṣṇāṅgo bhagnanāsāruṇekṣaṇaḥ yavamadhyaḥ kṛśagrīvo vakrapādo mahāhanuḥ brūhi gaccha durācāraṃ caṇḍālaṃ pāpakarmiṇam devakāryasya velāyāṃ dutas tvaṃ pratyupasthitaḥ caṇḍālapatitau dṛṣṭvā naraḥ paśyeta bhāskaram snātas tv etāv athālokya sacailasnānam arhati ity ājñapte tathoktas tu caṇḍālas tena vai tataḥ pratyuvāca pratīhāram īṣan manyupariplutaḥ kiṃ devakāryeṇa narādhipasya kṛtvā hi manyuṃ viṣayasthitānām tad devakāryaṃ sa ca yajñahomo yad aśrupātā na patanti rāṣṭre idaṃ vacanam avyagraṃ pratīhāra tvarā mama nivedaya svarājendraṃ yatheṣṭaṃ sa karotu vai ity uktaḥ satvaraṃ gatvā dharmarājaṃ tathā tathaṃ kathayām āsa tat sarvaṃ cāṇḍālena yad īritam suśobhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ na bhaved antyajātiṣu cintayitvā tato rājā nirjagāma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ity etad vacanaṃ śrutvā nirjagāma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pratyuvāca ca caṇḍālam īṣan kopasamanvitaḥ kutas te bhayam utpannaṃ yena tvaṃ gṛham āgataḥ āvādhākāraṇaṃ sarvaṃ yathāvat kathayasva me tad ahaṃ te pratijñāya caṇḍakarmakarakṣaṇam apāsya devakāryārthaṃ praviśyāmy antaraṃ punaḥ na bhuñjate brāhmaṇā me sarvāś codvijate janaḥ prāṇihiṃsā ca no vṛttir deva puṣṇāti me anṛtam anekajanmasāhasrīṃ prāpya saṃsārapaddhatim mānuṣye kutsitāṃ jātim āpanno muṣito asmi bhoḥ karmabhūmim imāṃ rājan prārthayanti divaukasaḥ tāṃ saṃprāpya vṛthājanmā muṣṭo asmi kurusattama duḥkhe duḥkhādhikān paśyet sukhe paśyet sukhādhikān ātmānaṃ śokaharṣābhyāṃ śatrubhyām iva nārpayet so aham icchāmi vijñātum atiduṣkṛtakarmakṛt vaktum arhasi dharmajña kaḥ pāpiṣṭhataro mayā adhvānam upari śrāntaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ gṛham āgatam anarcayitvā yo bhuṅkte sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva vikalaṃ netradurbalam yo nābhyuddharate putraḥ sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā godhanasya tṛṣārtasya jalārthaṃ paridhāvataḥ vighnam ācarate yas tu sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā vivāhayitvā yaḥ kanyāṃ kulajāṃ śīlamaṇḍanām vinā tyajati doṣeṇa sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā āśākāras tv adātā yo dātuś ca pratiṣedhakaḥ dattaṃ ca yaḥ kīrtayati sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā bahubhṛtyair daridraiś ca dhanaṃ santaṃ dvijottamaiḥ yācito na prayacched yaḥ sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyaḥ śūdro api vā naraḥ svadharmaṃ saṃtyajed yas tu sa pāpiṣṭhataras tvayā kṛtārtho ahaṃ gamiṣyāmi yaśodharmam avāpnuhi tuṣṭo asmy ahaṃ svayā yonyā mattaḥ proktās tvayādhamāḥ devatānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ ca kṛtaṃ mayā sāṃprataṃ deśakālo ayaṃ tvam evātra bhavātithiḥ caṇḍālo ahaṃ mahārāja patito lokavarjitaḥ kathaṃ nihīno varṇebhyo bhokṣyāmi bhavato gṛhe caṇḍālo bhava pāpo vā śatrur vā pitṛghātakaḥ deśakālābhyupetaṃ tvāṃ bharaṇīyaṃ hi vedmy aham daśasūnāsamaṃ cakraṃ daśacakrasamo dhvajaḥ daśadhvajasamā veśyā daśaveśyāsamo nṛpaḥ daśa sūnāsahasrāṇi kurute yo hi saunikaḥ tena tulyaḥ smṛto rājā ghoras tasya pratigrahaḥ nānāgotrādicaraṇā bhuñjate brāhmaṇā mama na te vadanti vāgduṣṭaṃ yathaitat kīrtitaṃ tvayā lobhātmāno na jānīyur brāhmaṇā rājakilbiṣam varaṃ svamāṃsam attavyaṃ na tu rājapratigraham rājakilbiṣadagdhānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ yudhiṣṭhira chinnānām iva bījānāṃ punarjanma na vidyate rājapratigraho ghoro madhvāsvādo viṣopamaḥ budhena pratihartavyaḥ svamāṃsasyeva bhakṣaṇam adhītya caturo vedān sarvaśāstrārthatattvavit narendrabhavane bhuṅktvā viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ nindase sarvarājāno na cātmānaṃ praśaṃsasi dhairyavān ātmano anindyo nāśvāsārthaṃ ca pṛcchasi vimuktakrodhaharśaś ca ko apy atra pratibhāsi naḥ anindyo nindyarūpeṇa mahātmā tvaṃ hi me mataḥ ko bhavān brūhi satyaṃ me kimartham iha cāgataḥ bhavān upendraḥ śakro vā śarvo vā tvaṃ pinākadhṛk athavā nindyarūpeṇa pitā nas tvam ihāgataḥ jñāto asmi pṛthivīpāla tuṣṭaś ca tava darśanāt nandantu bhūmibhāgās te yeṣu tvaṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ nirjitya parasainyāni kṣitiṃ dharmeṇa pālaya svalpam apy astu te velāṃ mā govindojjhitaṃ manaḥ kiṃ me rājyena bhos tāta viṣayair jīvitena vā yo ahaṃ sūnāsahasrais tu daśabhiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ mā viṣādaṃ naraśreṣṭha samupaihi yudhiṣṭhira yajñeśvaraṃ yajñamūrtiṃ tvaṃ ca viṣṇuṃ samāśritaḥ yeṣāṃ na viṣaye viprā yajñair yajñapatiṃ harim yajanti bhūbhujas teṣām etat sūnoditaṃ phalam yeṣāṃ pāṣaṇḍasaṃkīrṇaṃ na rāṣṭraṃ brāhmaṇotkaṭam te tu sūnāsahasrāṇāṃ daśānāṃ bhāgino nṛpāḥ yeṣāṃ na yajñapuruṣaḥ kāraṇaṃ puruṣottamaḥ te tu pāpasamācārāḥ sūnāpāpaughabhāginaḥ tvaṃ tu matprabhavas tāta viṣṇubhaktas tathaiva ca iṣṭir vaiśvānarī pāpam upahaṃsyati te akhilam avaśyaṃ viṣaye kaścid brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśritavrataḥ iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ kḷptāṃ nirvaped abdaparyaye tasya ṣaḍbhāgamātreṇa tvaṃ pāpaṃ nirdahiṣyasi sa tvaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te varaṃ yan manasecchasi samyak śraddhāsamācārād aham ārādhitas tvayā atha pātakabhītas tvaṃ sarvabhāvena bhārata vimuktānyasamārambho nārāyaṇaparo bhava paraḥ parāṇām ādyo asau jñeyo dhyeyo janārdanaḥ tadartham api karmāṇi kurvan pāpaṃ vyapohati lobhādivyāptahṛdayo yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ vilayaṃ yāti tat sarvam acyute hṛdaye sthite śamāyālaṃ jalaṃ vahnes tamaso bhāskarādayaḥ kṣāntiḥ kaler aghaughasya nāmasaṃkīrtanaṃ hareḥ prasanno yadi me tāta varārho yadi cāpy aham varaṃ tad ekam evaitaṃ prāptum icchāmy ahaṃ pitaḥ jāgratsvapnasuṣupteṣu yogasthasya sadā mama yā kācin manaso vṛttiḥ sā bhavatv acyutāśrayā yā yā jāyeta me buddhir yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ pitaḥ sā sā chinattu saṃdehān kṛṣṇāptau paripanthinaḥ yathā govindam ārādhya saśarīraḥ surālayam prāpnuyām iti me tāta prayaccha pravaraṃ varam evam etad aśeṣaṃ te matprasādād bhaviṣyati nāsti govindabhaktānāṃ vāñchitaṃ bhuvi durlabham iti dharmopadeśena sarvadevavaraṃ harim ārādhya pāṇḍavo yātaḥ saśarīraḥ surālayam bhūyaś ca śṛṇu rājendra janakena mahātmanā yad gītaṃ vahatā bhaktiṃ jñānam āsādya keśave sarvatra samadṛṣṭiṃ taṃ janakaṃ mithileśvaram paśyantam acyutamayaṃ sarvaṃ ca sacarācaram dvijarūpaṃ samāsthāya devadevo janārdanaḥ upatasthe mahābhāgaṃ pratyuvāca ca pārthivam rājañ janaka bhadraṃ te yad bravīmi nibodha tat kuruṣva ca mahābuddhe yadi sādhu mataṃ tava pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpālaḥ pālayitvā pitā tava svargaṃ gatas tathā bhrātā samyak satyadhvajo nṛpaḥ tvaṃ punar nirabhīmānaḥ sarvatra samadarśanaḥ ripumitrādivargeṣu katham etad bhaviṣyati mitreṣu mitravan na tvaṃ nāhiteṣv arivad bhavān madhyasthabhāg na caiva tvaṃ tathodāsīnavṛttiṣu śabdādayo ye viśayās te vairāgyaphalā nṛpa nītyā vihīnas tu bhavān kathaṃ rājyaṃ kariṣyati sarvair nītiṃ samāsthāya yathā te prapitāmahaiḥ kṛtaṃ rājyaṃ tathā bhūpa kuru mātijaḍo bhava tava prajñā matā hy eṣā mama moho mahīpate trivargasādhanaṃ prajñā na dharmādivirodhinī samyag āha bhavān vipra vācyam evaṃ bhavadvidhaiḥ mamāpi śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ bhavato yadi rocate yadā sarvagato viṣṇuḥ paramātmā prajāpatiḥ tadā mitrādimadhyastha- saṃjñā keṣu nipātyatām pitā mātā tathā bhrātā yadā nānyaj janārdanāt pitṛmātṛmayīṃ saṃjñāṃ tadā kutra karomy aham so ahaṃ bravīmi yad vākyaṃ tan nibodha dvijottama anekarūparūpo ayaṃ viṣṇur evākhilaṃ jagat viṣṇuḥ pitā me jagataḥ pratiṣṭhā viṣṇur mātā viṣṇur evāgrajo me viṣṇur gatir viṣṇumayas tathāsmi viṣṇau sthito asmy akṣagataś ca viṣṇuḥ yo me mamatvopagataḥ sa viṣṇur yaś cāribhūto mama so api viṣṇuḥ divaṃ viyad bhūḥ kakubhaś ca viṣṇur bhūtāni viṣṇur bhuvanāni viṣṇuḥ paśyāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyac śṛṇomi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyat spṛśāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyaj jighrāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyat rasāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyan manye ca viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyat jighrāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyac namāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyat budhyāmi viṣṇuṃ na paraṃ tato anyat sarvaṃ hi viṣṇur na paraṃ tato anyat viṣṇuḥ samastaṃ na paraṃ tato asti viṣṇuḥ samastaṃ na paraṃ ca devaḥ viṣṇuḥ sthārīyān na paraṃ tato asti viṣṇur laghīyān na paraṃ tato asti viṣṇur garīyān na paraṃ tato anyat yathā na viṣṇuvyatiriktam anyac śṛṇomi paśyāmi tathā spṛśāmi satyena tenopaśamaṃ prayāntu doṣā vimukteḥ paripanthino ye na me asti bandhur na ca me asti śatrur na bhūtavargo na jano madanyaḥ tvaṃ cāhaṃ anye ca śarīrabhedair vibhinnam īśasya hareḥ svarūpam mūrtāmūrtiviśeṣaṃ tu paśyatas tanmayaṃ dvija krodhaharṣādayo bhāvāḥ sthāsyanti hṛdaye katham sa tvaṃ prasīda moho ayam atha cen mama suvrata tathāpi mā ruṣaṃ kārṣīr acikitsyā hi mohitāḥ bahurūpas tato rūpaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam darśayām āsa suprīto janakāya janārdanaḥ tatas taddarśanād bhūpaṃ śirasā praṇataṃ prabhuḥ ādyaḥ prajāpatipatiḥ pratyuvācācyuto hariḥ varaṃ varaya bhūpāla parituṣṭo asmi te anagha mayy arpitamanobuddheḥ sadaivāhaṃ na durlabhaḥ yadi deva prasanno asi samyag ārādhito mayā tad vṛṇomi varaṃ bhaktis tvayy evāstu sadā mama evaṃ bhaviṣyatīty uktvā gato antardhānam īśvaraḥ so api lebhe layaṃ viṣṇau bhaktyā yogisudurlabham iti kṛṣṇe naravyāghra kurvan bhaktiṃ naraḥ sadā prāpnoti puruṣavyāghra muktiṃ cāpy atidurlabhām jagaddhātur anantasya vāsudevasya bhārgava mamāvatārān akhilāñ śrotum icchā pravartate yathā yathā hi kṛṣṇasya katheyaṃ kathyate tvayā jāyate manasaḥ prītir udbhūtapulakas tathā manaḥprītir anāyāsād apuṇyacayasaṃkṣayaḥ prāpyate puruṣair brahmañ śṛṇvadbhir bhagavatkathām sa kuruṣvāmalamate prasādapravaṇaṃ manaḥ avatārān sureśasya viṣṇor icchāmi veditum jagadguruṃ jagadyonim anantam udakeśayam nārāyaṇaṃ purākalpe pṛṣṭavān kamalodbhavaḥ vinirjagmur mukhebhyas tu brahmaṇo vyaktajanmanaḥ oṃkārapravaṇā vedā jagmus te ca rasātalam ekārṇave jagaty asmin brahmaṇy amitatejasi kṛṣṇanābhihradodbhūta- kamalodaraśāyini bhogiśayyāśayaḥ kṛṣṇo dvitīyāṃ tanum ātmanaḥ kṛtvā mīnamayīṃ sadyaḥ praviveśa rasātalam vedamūrtis tato vedān āninye brahmaṇo antikam madhukaiṭabhābhyāṃ ca punar bhogiśayyāgato hariḥ hṛtān hayaśirā bhūtvā vedān āhṛtavān rasāt āhṛteṣv atha vedeṣu devadevaṃ pitāmahaḥ tuṣṭāva praṇato bhaktyā tasya cāvir babhau hariḥ athāmaraguruṃ viṣṇum anantam ajam avyayam uvāca prakaṭībhūtaṃ praṇipatyābjasaṃbhavaḥ namaḥ sūkṣmātisūkṣmāya namas tubhyaṃ trimūrtaye bahurūpādimadhyānta pariṇāmavivarjita jagadīśasya sarvasya jagataḥ sarvakāmada aham ātmabhavo deva tvayādhyakṣo nirūpitaḥ so aham icchāmi taṃ jñātum ātmānaṃ prabhavāvyayam viśvasya ca virūpasya sthāvarasya carasya ca yadi te anugrahakṛtā mayi buddhir janārdana tan māṃ bhakta iti jñātvā kathayātmānam acyuta kathayāmi tavātmānam anākhyāgodaraṃ param na vācāṃ viṣaye yo asāv aviśeṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ prasādasumukhaḥ so aham imaṃ yacchāmi te varam anākhyātasvarūpaṃ māṃ bhavāñ jñāsyati yogataḥ bhakto māṃ tattvato vetti mayi bhaktiś ca te parā majjijñāsā parā brahmaṃs tena jātā matis tava evam uktas tato brahmā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā viṣṇoḥ svarūpaṃ jijñāsur yuyojātmānam ātmanā sa dadarśātisūkṣmaṃ ca sūkṣmajyotiṣy ajaṃ vibhum niyutārdhārdhamātreṇa vyāptāśeṣacarācaram ātmānam indrarudrārka- candrāśvivasumārutān khādīny atha ca śabdādīn dadṛśe ca sa tanmayān ye vyaktā ye tathāvyaktā bhāvā ye cāpi pauruṣāḥ tāṃś ca tatrātisūkṣmo api dṛṣṭavān akhilān vibhuḥ tataḥ praṇamya deveśam ajam ārtiharaṃ harim pitāmahaḥ prahvatanur vākyam etad uvāca ha jñātaṃ svarūpam ajñāta- svarūpa bhagavaṃs tava mayā na yad vāgviṣaye tatrasthaṃ cākhilaṃ jagat dhanyo asmy anugṛhīto asmi svarūpaṃ yan mayā tava bhagavañ jñātam ajñātam anantāja namo astu te yadi prasādaṃ deva tvaṃ prakaroṣi mamāparam paramaṃ cāvatāreṣu yad rūpaṃ tad vadasva me keṣu keṣu mayā jñeyaḥ sthāneṣu tvam adhokṣaja saṃbhūtayo mamācakṣva yā bhaviṣyanti te bhuvi devaloke nṛloke vā pātāle khe anyato api vā saṃbhūtayo yās tu bhavān kariṣyati vadasva tāḥ tvaṃ kartā sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃhartā ceśvareśvaraḥ tavāpi kartā nānyo asti svecchayā krīḍate bhavān ahaṃ vedmi bhavantaṃ hi na tavānyo asti veditā yan māṃ tvaṃ pṛcchasi brahman avatārāśritaṃ param tat te samyak pravakṣyāmi nibodha mama suvrata mama prakṛtyā saṃyogaḥ svecchayā saṃpravartate deveṣu nṝṣu tiryakṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca mamāvatārāḥ kāryārthaṃ jagataś copakāriṇaḥ yadā yadā hi dharmasya glāniḥ samupajāyate abhyutthānam adharmasya tadātmāṅgaṃ sṛjāmy aham paritrāṇāya sādhūnāṃ vināśāya ca duṣkṛtāṃ dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya saṃbhavāmi yuge yuge pūrvotpanneṣu bhūteṣu nṛdevādiṣu cāpy aham anupraviśya dharmasya karomi paripālanam praviśya ca tathā pūrvaṃ tanuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara jagato asya jagatsṛṣṭiṃ karomi sthitipālanam devatve devikā ceṣṭā tiryaktve mama tāmasī icchayā mānuṣatve ca vicarāmi nṛceṣṭayā pratikṣaṇaṃ ca bhūteṣu sṛjāmi jagataḥ sthitim karomi vidyamāneṣu dharmasaṃsthāpaneṣu ca yad vai dharmopakārāya yac ca duṣṭanivarhaṇam caritaṃ mānuṣādīnāṃ tad vai jānīhi matkṛtam yac ca pṛcchasi māṃ brahman kāḥ kāḥ saṃbhūtayas tava tāḥ śṛṇuṣva samāsena yā bhaviṣyanti sāṃpratam matsyena bhūtvā pātālāt tava vedāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ madhukaiṭabhābhyāṃ ca hṛtā dattāśvaśirasā mayā tvam apy atra mahābhāga madaṃśaḥ kamalodarāt mannābhisaṃbhavāj jātaḥ prajāsṛṣṭikaraḥ paraḥ ekārṇavaṃ ca yad idaṃ brahman paśyasy aśeṣataḥ asmin vasumatīṃ devīṃ magnāṃ pātālam āgatām vedapādo yūpadaṃṣṭraḥ kratudantaś citīmukhaḥ agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ ahorātrekṣaṇadharo vedāṅgaśrutibhūṣaṇaḥ ājyanāsaḥ śruvastuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvaro mahān prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhir ācitaḥ dakṣiṇāhṛdayo yogī mahāsattramayo mahān upakarmeṣṭiruciraḥ pravargāvartabhūṣaṇaḥ nānācchandogatipatho brahmoktikarmavikramaḥ bhūtvā yajñavarāho aham iti brahman rasātalāt pṛthivīm uddhariṣyāmi sthāpayaiṣyāmi ca sthitau parvatānāṃ nadīnāṃ ca dvīpādīnāṃ ca yā sthitiḥ tāṃ ca tadvat kariṣyāmi śailādīnām anukramāt hiraṇyākṣaṃ ca durvṛttaṃ kaśyapasyātmasaṃbhavam tenaiva ghātayiṣyāmi rūpeṇāhaṃ prajāpate utpādya pṛthivīṃ samyak sthāpayitvā yathā purā sṛṣṭiṃ tataḥ kariṣyāmi tvām āviśya prajāpatim jānāsi kāpilaṃ rūpaṃ prathamaṃ pauruṣaṃ mama sarvavidyāpraṇetāraṃ tvayā vedeṣu darśitam ravimaṇḍalamadhyastham agner yat paramaṃ padam tata utsṛjya rūpāṇi amarādivibhedataḥ vyāpayiṣyāmi lokāṃs tu bhūlokādīm aśeṣataḥ sṛṣṭaṃ jagad idaṃ deva- mānuṣyādiviśeṣaṇam hiraṇyakaśipur daityas tāpayiṣyati vikramāt vyaṃsayitvā varāṃs tasya tais tair hetubhir ātmavān nṛsiṃharūpaṃ kṛtvāhaṃ ghātayiṣyāmi taṃ ripum kṣīrābdau kūrmarūpo ahaṃ devānāṃ kamalodbhava mandaraṃ dhārayiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhenāmṛtamanthane hariṣyati ca devānāṃ yajñabhāgān yadā baliḥ tadāhaṃ vāmano bhūtvā gatvā tasya mahādhvaram vañcayitvāsurapatiṃ kariṣyāmi tripiṣṭapam baliṃ cāpi kariṣyāmi pātālatalavāsinam atrer dattvā varaṃ caiva tasya putratvam āgataḥ dattātreyo bhaviṣyāmi nihaṃsyāmi tathāsurān sattvānām upakārāya pradhānapuruṣāntaram darśayiṣyāmi lokeṣu kāpilaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ kārtavīryādibhiś cānyaiś caturdaśabhir anvitāḥ bhaviṣyanti madaṃśena tretāyāṃ cakravartinaḥ tataś ca bhārgavo rāmo gṛhītaparaśur dvijaḥ bhūtvā kṣatriyahīnāṃ ca kariṣyāmi vasuṃdharām punaś ca rāghavo rāmo bhūtvā daśarathātmajaḥ baddhvā mahodadhiṃ kartā rākṣasānāṃ kulakṣayam uttīrya ca paraṃ pāraṃ laṅkām āsādya durjayām nihatya rāvaṇaṃ vīraṃ varadānena darpitam māyāvināṃ mahāvīryaṃ rakṣasāṃ vanaśāyinām lakṣmaṇānucaro rāmaḥ kariṣyāmi kulakṣayam aṣṭāviṃśatime prāpte dvāpare kaṃsam ucchritam keśinaṃ dhenukaṃ caiva śakuniṃ pūtanāṃ tathā ariṣṭaṃ ca haniṣyāmi muruṃ narakam eva ca niśumbhaṃ sahayagrīvaṇ tathānyāṃś cāsureśvarān haniṣyāmi sudurvṛttāṃl lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā pravarṣati sa devendre mahobhaṅgavirodhite govardhanaṃ girivaraṃ dhārayiṣyāmi bāhunā bhārākrāntām imām urvīṃ dhanaṃjayasahāyavān ghātayitvākhilān bhūpāṃl laghvīṃ kartāsmi sattama prāpte kaliyuge kṛtsnam upasaṃhṛtya vai kulam dvārakāṃ plāvayiṣyāmi utsrakṣyāmi manuṣyatām dvitīyo yo mamāṃśas tu rāmo anantaḥ sa lāṅgalī so api saṃtyajya vasudhāṃ rasātalam upeṣyati tataḥ kaliyuge ghore saṃprāpte abjasamudbhava śuddhodanasuto buddho bhaviṣyāmi vimatsaraḥ bauddhaṃ dharmam upāśritya kariṣye dharmadeśanām narāṇām atha nārīṇāṃ dayāṃ bhūteṣu darśayan raktāmbarā hy āñjitākṣāḥ praśāntamanasas tataḥ śūdrā dharmaṃ pravakṣyanti mayi buddhatvam āgate eḍūkacihnā pṛthivī na devagṛhabhūṣitā bhavitrī prāyaśo brahman mayi buddhatvam āgate skandhadarśanamātraṃ hi paśyantaḥ sakalaṃ jagat śūdrāḥ śūdreṣu dāsyanti mayi buddhatvam āgate alpāyuṣas tato martyā mohopahatacetasaḥ narakārhāṇi karmāṇi kariṣyanti prajāpate svādhyāyeṣv avasīdanto brāhmaṇāḥ śaucavarjitāḥ antyapratigrahādānaṃ kariṣyanty alpamedhasaḥ na śroṣyanti pituḥ putrāḥ śvaśrūśvaśurayoḥ snuṣāḥ na bhāryā bhartur īśasya na bhṛtyā vinayasthitāḥ varṇasaṃkaratāṃ prāpte loke asmin dasyutāṃ gate brāhmaṇādiṣu varṇeṣu bhaviṣyaty adharottaram dharmakañcukasaṃvītā vidharmarucayas tathā mānuṣān bhakṣayiṣyanti mlecchāḥ pārthivarūpiṇaḥ tataḥ kaliyugasyānte vedo vājasaneyakaḥ daśa pañca ca vai śākhāḥ pramāṇena bhaviṣyati tato ahaṃ saṃbhaviṣyāmi brāhmaṇo haripiṅgalaḥ kalkī viṣṇuyaśaḥputro yājñavalkyapurohitaḥ mlecchān utsādayiṣyāmi gṛhītāstraḥ kuśāyudhaḥ sthāpayiṣyāmi maryādāś cāturvarṇye yathoditāḥ tathāśrameṣu sarveṣu brahmacārivratādikāḥ sthāpayitvā tataḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ saddharmavartmani kalkirūpaṃ parityajya divam eṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ bhūyaḥ pūrvavat saṃpravartsyate varṇāśramāś ca dharmeṣu dveṣu sthāsyanti sattama evaṃ sarveṣu kalpeṣu sarvamanvantareṣu ca mamāvatārāḥ śataśo ye bhavanti jagaddhitāḥ saṃkarṣaṇātmajaś caiva kalpānte ca rasātalāt samutpatsyet tadā rudraḥ kālāgnir iti yaḥ śrutaḥ tataḥ kṣayaṃ kariṣyāmi jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam bhūyaś caiva hi svapsyāmi jagaty ekārṇave sthite tvadrūpī ca tato bhūtvā jagat srakṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ etat saṃkṣepato brahman mayākhyātaṃ yathātatham aṃśāvataraṇaṃ sarvaṃ mattaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu yad dṛśyaṃ yac ca vai spṛśyaṃ yad ghreyaṃ rasyate ca yat yac chravyaṃ yac ca mantavyaṃ bodhavyaṃ cāham aṃśagaḥ yat tu buddheḥ parataram anākhyeyam anopamam tad ahaṃ brahma nirdvandvaṃ yad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ idaṃ janmarahasyaṃ me yo naraḥ kīrtayiṣyati sulabho ahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi tasya janmani janmani paṭhann etad brahmahā tu surāpo gurutalpagaḥ steyī kṛtaghno goghnaś ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate garbhiṇī janayet putraṃ kanyā vindati satpatim labhante abhimatān kāmān narās tāṃs tān yathepsitān iti devātidevena brahmaṇo vyaktajanmanaḥ rahasyam idam ākhyātaṃ tavāpi kathitaṃ mayā viṣṇuḥ sarvagato anantaḥ sarvaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhitam sa ca sarvam idaṃ rājan na tato vidyate param etat pavitraṃ paṭhitaṃ tathā duḥsvapnanāśanam jātismaratvaṃ prajñāṃ ca dadāti paṭhatāṃ nṛṇām mayā hi devadevasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ śrutāḥ saṃbhūtayaḥ sarvā gadatas tava suvrata yadi prasanno bhagavān anugrāhyo asmi vā yadi tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi nṝṇāṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam svapnā hi sumahābhāga dṛśyante ye śubhāśubhāḥ phalāni te prayacchanti tadguṇāny eva bhārgava yad yat puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ ca nṝṇām atiśubhapradam duḥsvapnopaśamāyālaṃ tan me vistarato vada idam eva mahārāja pṛṣṭavāṃs te pitāmahaḥ bhīṣmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ devavrataṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam vinayenopasaṃgamya paryapṛcchad yudhiṣṭhiraḥ duḥsvapnadarśanaṃ ghoram avekṣya bharatarṣabha prayataḥ kiṃ japej japyaṃ vibuddhaḥ kim anusmaret pitāmaha mahābuddhe buddher bhedo mahān ayam tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi brūhi me vadatāṃ vara śṛṇu rājan mahābāho vartayiṣyāmi te akhilam duḥsvapnadarśane japyaṃ yad vai nityaṃ samāhitaiḥ atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam gajendramokṣaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ kṛṣṇasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ sarvaratnamayaḥ śrīmāṃs trikūṭo nāma parvataḥ sutaḥ parvatarājasya sumeror bhāskaradyuteḥ kṣīrodajalavīcyagrair dhautāmalaśilātalaḥ utthitaḥ sāgaraṃ bhittvā devarṣigaṇasevitaḥ apsarobhiḥ samākīrṇaḥ śrīmān prasravaṇākulaḥ gandharvaiḥ kiṃnarair yakṣaiḥ siddhacāraṇapannagaiḥ vidyādharaiḥ sapatnikaiḥ saṃyataiś ca tapasvibhiḥ mṛgair dvīpair dvijaiś caiva vṛtaḥ sauvarṇarājataiḥ puṃnāgaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca puṣpitair upaśobhitaḥ cūtanīpakadambaiś ca candanāgarucampakaiḥ śālais tālais tamālaiś ca kuṭajaiś cārjunais tathā evaṃ bahuvidhair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvataḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ nānādhātūjjvalaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ prasravadbhiḥ samantataḥ mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ siṃhair mātaṃgaiś ca sadāmadaiḥ jīvaṃjīvakasaṃghuṣṭaṃ cakoraśikhināditam tasyaikaṃ kāñcanaṃ śṛṅgaṃ sevate yad divādaraḥ nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ nānāgandhasamākulam dvitīyaṃ rājataṃ śṛṅgaṃ sevate yan niśākaraḥ pāṇḍurāmbudasaṃkāśaṃ tuṣāracayasaṃnibham vajrendranīlavaiḍūrya- tejobhir bhāsayan nabhaḥ tṛtīyaṃ brahmasadanaṃ prakṛṣṭaṃ śṛṅgam uttamam na tat kṛtaghnāḥ paśyanti na nṛśaṃsā na nāstikāḥ nātaptatapasaḥ śailaṃ taṃ vai paśyanti mānavāḥ tasya sānumataḥ pṛṣṭhe saraḥ kāñcanapaṅkajam kāraṇḍavasamākīrṇaṃ rājahaṃsopaśobhitam mattabhramarasaṃghuṣṭaṃ phullapaṅkajaśobhitam kumudotpalakalhāra- puṇḍarīkopaśobhitam utpalaiḥ śatapattraiś ca kāñcanaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam pattrair maṇidalaprakhyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kāñcanasaṃnibhaiḥ gulmaiḥ kīcakaveṇūnāṃ samantāt parivāritam tasmin sarasi duṣṭātmā virūpo antarjalāśayaḥ āsīd grāho gajendrāṇāṃ durādharṣo mahābalaḥ atha dantojjvalamukhaḥ kadācid gajayūthapaḥ ājagāmāsitābhrābhaḥ kareṇuparivāritaḥ madasrāvī mahāraudraḥ pādacārīva parvataḥ vāsayan madagandhena girim airāvatopamaḥ sa gajo añjanasaṃkāśo madāc calitamānasaḥ gandhahastīti vikhyātaḥ saraḥ samabhigamya tat tṛṣitaḥ sa jalaṃ prāpya kusumākaraśītalam apibat sahasā rājan kareṇuparivāritaḥ salīlaṃ paṅkajavane yūthamadhyagato avrajat gṛhītas tena raudreṇa grāheṇāvyaktamūrtinā paśyantīnāṃ kareṇūnāṃ krośantīnāṃ ca dāruṇam kriyate paṅkajavane grāheṇātibalīyasā gajaś cākarṣate tīraṃ grāhaś cākarṣate jalam tayor dvandva mahāyuddhaṃ divyavarṣasahasrikam vāruṇaiḥ saṃyataḥ pāśair niḥprayatnagatiḥ kṛtaḥ veṣṭyamānaḥ sughorais tu pāśair nāgo dṛḍhais tathā visphurjya ca yathāśakti vikruśya ca mahāravān vyathitaḥ saṃnirutsāho gṛhīto ghorakarmaṇā paramāpadam āpanno manasācintayad dharim sa tu nāgavaraḥ śrīmān nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ tam eva paramaṃ devaṃ gataḥ sarvātmanā tadā ekāgraṃ cintayām āsa viśuddhenāntarātmanā janmajanmāntarābhyāsād bhaktimān garuḍadhvaje ādyaṃ devaṃ mahātmānaṃ pūjayām āsa keśavam navameghapratīkāśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam sahasraśubhanāmānam ādidevam ajaṃ param digbāhuṃ sarvamūrdhānaṃ bhūpādaṃ gaganodaram ādityacandranayanaṃ samagraṃ lokasākṣiṇam bhagavantaṃ prasanno ahaṃ viṣṇum apratimaujasam pragṛhya puṣkarāgreṇa kāñcanaṃ kamalottamam āpadvimokṣam anvicchan gajaḥ stotram udairayat oṃ namo mūlaprakṛtaye , ajitāya mahātmane , anāśritāya devāya , niḥspṛhāya namo namaḥ , nama ādyāya bījāya , śivāya ca praśāntāya , ārṣeyāya pravartine , niścalāya yaśasvine , anantarāya caikāya , sanātanāya pūrvāya , avyaktāya namo namaḥ , purāṇāya namo namaḥ , namo guhyāya gūḍhāya , guṇāyāguṇavartine , atarkyāyāprameyāya , anantāya namo namaḥ , namo devātidevāya , aprabhāya namo namaḥ , namo jagatprasthitāya , govindāya namo namaḥ , namo astu padmanābhāya , sāṃkhyayogodbhavāya ca , viśveśvarāya devāya , śivāya haraye namaḥ , namo astu tasmai devāya , nirguṇāya guṇātmane , nārāyaṇāya viśvāya , devānāṃ paramātmane , namo namaḥ kāraṇavāmanāya nārāyaṇāyāmitavikramāya śrīśārṅgacakrāsigadādharāya namo astu tasmai puruṣottamāya ādyāya vedanilayāya mahodarāya siṃhāya daityanidhanāya caturbhujāya brahmendrarudramunicāraṇasaṃstutāya devottamāya varadāya namo acyutāya nāgendrabhogaśayanāsanasupriyāya gokṣīrahemaśukanīlaghanopamāya pītāmbarāya madhukaiṭabhanāśanāya viśvāya cārumukuṭāya namo akṣarāya bhaktipriyāya varadīptasudarśanāya nābhiprajātakamalasthacaturmukhāya kṣīrodakārṇavaniketayaśodhanāya nānāvicitramukuṭāṅgadabhūṣaṇāya sarveśvarāya varadāya namo varāya viśvātmane paramakāraṇakāraṇāya phullāravindavimalāyatalocanāya devendradānavaparīkṣitapauruṣāya yogeśvarāya vijayāya namo varāya lokāyanāya tridaśāyanāya brahmāyanāyātmabhavāyanāya dharmāyanāyaikajalāyanāya mahāvarāhāya sadā nato asmi acintyam avyaktam anantarūpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ kāraṇam ādidevam yugāntaśeṣaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye yogeśvaraṃ cāruvicitramaulim ājñeyamaukhyaṃ prakṛteḥ parastham kṣetrajñam ātmaprabhavaṃ vareṇyaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye adṛśyam acchedyam anādimadhyaṃ maharṣayo brahmavidaḥ sureśam vadanti yaṃ vai puruṣaṃ sanātanaṃ taṃ vāsudevaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye yad akṣaraṃ brahma vadanti sarvagaṃ niśāmya yaṃ mṛtyumukhāt pramucyate tam īśvaraṃ tṛptam anopamair guṇaiḥ parāyaṇaṃ viṣṇum upaimi śāśvatam kāryaṃ kriyākāraṇam aprameyaṃ hiraṇyanābhaṃ varapadmanābham mahābalaṃ vedanidhiṃ surottamaṃ vrajāmi viṣṇuṃ śaraṇaṃ janārdanam vicitrakeyūramahārhaniṣkaṃ ratnottamālaṃkṛtasarvagātram pītāmbaraṃ kāñcanabhakticitraṃ mālādharaṃ keśavam abhyupaimi bhavodbhavaṃ vedavidāṃ variṣṭhaṃ yogātmānaṃ sāṃkhyavidāṃ variṣṭham ādityacandrāśvivasuprabhāvaṃ prabhuṃ prapadye acyutam ātmabhūtam śrīvatsāṅkaṃ mahādevaṃ vedaguhyam anuttamam prapadye sūkṣmam acalaṃ bhaktānām abhayapradam prabhavaṃ sarvalokānāṃ nirguṇaṃ parameśvaram prapadye muktasaṃgānāṃ yatīnāṃ paramāṃ gatim bhagavantaṃ surādhyakṣam akṣaraṃ puṣkarekṣaṇam śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ bhaktyā prapadye brāhmaṇapriyam trivikramaṃ trilokeśam ādyam ekam anāmayam bhūtātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ prapadye madhusūdanam ādidevam ajaṃ śambhuṃ vyaktāvyaktaṃ janārdanam kṣetrajñaṃ puruṣaṃ yajñaṃ triguṇātītam avyayam nārāyaṇam aṇīyāṃsaṃ prapadye parameśvaram ekāya lokatrayāya parataḥ paramātmane namaḥ sahasraśirase anantāya mahātmane vareṇyam anaghaṃ devam ṛṣayo vedapāragāḥ kīrtayanti ca yaṃ sarve taṃ prapadye sanātanam namas te puṇḍarīkākṣa bhaktānām abhayaprada subrahmaṇya namas te astu trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam bhaktiṃ tasyānusaṃcintya nāgasyāmoghasaṃstavam prītimān abhavad rājañ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ sāṃnidhyaṃ kalpayām āsa tasmin sarasi mādhavaḥ grāhagrastaṃ gajaṃ taṃ ca saṃgṛhya salilāśayāt ujjahārāprameyātmā tarasaivārisūdanaḥ sthalasthaṃ dārayām āsa grāhaṃ cakreṇa mādhavaḥ mokṣayām āsa ca gajaṃ pāśebhyaḥ śaraṇāgatam sa hi devalaśāpena hūhū gandharvasattamaḥ gajatvam agamat kṛṣṇān mokṣaṃ prāpya divaṃ gataḥ śāpād vimuktaḥ sadyaś ca gajo gandharvatāṃ gataḥ grāho api yakṣatāṃ yāto yaḥ kṛṣṇena nipātitaḥ tasyāpi śāpamokṣo asau jaigīṣavyakṛto abhavat prītimāṃs trāti govindaḥ sadyaḥ saṃsārasāgarāt kruddho api nighnan devatvam arātīnāṃ prayacchati tau ca svaṃ svaṃ vapuḥ prāpya praṇipatya janārdanam gandharvarāṭ tathā yakṣaḥ parāṃ nirvṛtim āgatau idaṃ caiva mahābāho devadevo abhyabhāṣata dṛṣṭvā muktau gajagrahau bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ yo grāhaṃ nāgarājaṃ ca māṃ caiva praṇidhānavān smariṣyati saraś cedaṃ yuvayor mokṣaṇaṃ tathā gulmaṃ kīcakaveṇūnāṃ taṃ ca śailavaraṃ tathā aśvatthaṃ bhāskaraṃ gaṅgāṃ naimiṣāraṇyam eva ca saṃsmariṣyanti ye martyāḥ samyak śroṣyanti vāpi ye na te duḥsvapnapāpasya bhoktāro matparigrahāt sarvapāpaiḥ pramokṣyante kalyāṇānāṃ ca bhāginaḥ bhaviṣyanti tathā puṇyāṃ gatiṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ duḥsvapnaṃ ca nṛṇāṃ teṣāṃ susvapnaṃ ca bhaviṣyati kaurmaṃ mātsyaṃ ca vārāhaṃ vāmanaṃ tārkṣyam eva ca nārasiṃhaṃ tathā rūpaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakam etāni prātar utthāya saṃsmariṣyanti ye narāḥ sarvapāpavinirmuktās te yānti paramāṃ gatim evam uktvā tu rājendra devadevo janārdanaḥ aspṛśad gajagandharvaṃ grāhayakṣaṃ ca taṃ tadā tena spṛṣṭāv ubhau sadyo divyamālyāmbarānvitau vimāne abhimate prāpya jagmatus tridaśālayam tato devapatiḥ kṛṣṇo mokṣayitvā gajottamam ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamāno hi guhyair vedapadākṣaraiḥ gataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇur durvijñeyagatiḥ prabhuḥ gajendramokṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve cendrapurogamāḥ brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā sarve prāñjalayo abhavan vavandire mahātmānaṃ prabhuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim vismayotphullanayanāḥ prajāpatipuraḥsarāḥ ya idaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ prātar utthāya mānavaḥ prāpnuyāt paramāṃ siddhiṃ duḥsvapnas tasya naśyati gajendramokṣaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapramocanam śrāvayet prātar utthāya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate śraddhayā hi kuruśreṣṭha smṛtena kathitena ca gajendramokṣaṇeneha dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt mayā te kathitaṃ divyaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam kīrtayasva mahābāho mahāduḥsvapnanāśanam kīrtyamānaṃ ca viprebhyaḥ śṛṇu bhaktyā yathoditam gajendramokṣaṇaṃ śrutvā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīṣmād bhagīrathīputrāt pūjayām āsa keśavam ye cāpi pāṇḍuputrasya samīpasthā dvijottamāḥ te api bhīṣmasya pārśvasthaṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇemire varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varapadmanābhaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ brahmanidhiṃ sureśam taṃ devaguhyaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ vavandire brahmavidāṃ variṣṭham etat puṇyaṃ mahārāja narāṇāṃ pāpakarmaṇām duḥsvapnadarśane ghore śrutvā pāpāt pramucyate bhaktimān puṇḍarīkākṣe gajo duḥkhād vimocitaḥ tathā tvam api rājendra prapadya śaraṇaṃ harim vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ prāpsyase paramāṃ gatim mahāmate mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśārada akṣīṇakarmabandhas tu puruṣo dvijasattama maraṇe yaj japañ japyaṃ yac ca bhāvaṃ anusmaran paraṃ padam avāpnoti tan me vada mahāmune śrīvatsāṅkaṃ jagadbījam anantaṃ lokabhāvanam purā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ nāradaḥ paryapṛcchata bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa śraddadhānair jitendriyaiḥ kathaṃ bhaktair vicintyo asi maraṇe pratyupasthite kiṃ vā japyaṃ japen nityaṃ kalyam utthāya mānavaḥ svapan vibudhyan dhyāyaṃś ca tan me brūhi sanātana śrutvā tasya tu devarṣer vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ provāca bhagavān viṣṇur nāradaṃ jagato gatiḥ hanta te kathayiṣyāmi mune divyām anusmṛtim maraṇe yām anusmṛtya prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim oṃkāram āditaḥ kṛtvā mām anusmṛtya manmanāḥ ekāgraprayato bhūtvā idaṃ mantram udīrayet avyaktaṃ śāśvataṃ devam anantaṃ puruṣottamam prapadye prāñjalir viṣṇum acyutaṃ parameśvaram purāṇaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇum adbhutaṃ lokabhāvanam prapadye puṇḍarīkākṣam īśaṃ bhaktānukampinam lokanāthaṃ prapanno asmi akṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam bhagavantaṃ prapanno asmi bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhum sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānām anantabalapauruṣam padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ papadye satyam avyayam hiraṇyagarbhaṃ bhūgarbham amṛtaṃ viśvatomukham ābhāsvaram anādyantaṃ prapadye bhāskaradyutim sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ tārkṣyavāhanam prapadye sūkṣmam acalaṃ vareṇyam abhayapradam nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ haṃsaṃ yogātmānaṃ sanātanam śaraṇyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ prapadye dhruvam īśvaram yaḥ prabhuḥ sarvalokānāṃ yena sarvam idaṃ tatam carācaragurur devaḥ sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu yasmāj jātaḥ purā brahmā padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ prasīdatu sa no viṣṇuḥ pitā mātā pitāmahaḥ yaḥ purā pralaye prāpte naṣṭe loke carācare ekas tiṣṭhati yogātmā sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu caturbhiś ca caturbhiś ca dvābhyāṃ pañcabhir eva ca hūyate ca punar dvābhyāṃ sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu parjanyaḥ pṛthivī sasyaṃ kālo dharmaḥ kriyā phalam guṇākaraḥ sa no babhrur vāsudevaḥ prasīdatu yogāvāsa namas tubhyaṃ sarvāvāsa varaprada yajñagarbha mahābhāga pañcayajña namo astu te caturmūrte jagaddhāma lakṣmyāvāsa varaprada sarvāvāsa namas te astu sākṣibhūta jagatpate ajeya khaṇḍaparaśo viśvamūrte vṛṣākape trigarte pañcakālajña namas te jñānasāgara avyaktād aṇḍam utpannam avyaktādyaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ yasmāt parataraṃ nāsti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ cintayanto hi yaṃ nityaṃ brahmeśānādayaḥ prabhum niścayaṃ nādhigacchanti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ jitendriyā mahātmāno jñānadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ yaṃ prāpya na nivartante tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ekāṃśena jagat sarvaṃ yo avaṣṭabhya vibhuḥ sthitaḥ agrāhyo nirguṇaḥ śāstā tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ divākarasya saumyaṃ hi madhye jyotir avasthitam kṣetrajñam iti yaṃ prāhuḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu avyaktam anavasthāno durvijñeyaḥ sanātanaḥ āsthitaḥ prakṛtiṃ bhuṅkte sa mahātmā prasīdatu kṣetrajñaḥ pañcadhā bhuṅkte prakṛtiṃ bahubhir guṇaiḥ manoguṇāṃś ca yo bhuṅkte sa mahātmā prasīdatu sāṃkhyā yogāś ca ye cānye siddhāś caiva maharṣayaḥ yaṃ viditvā vimucyante sa mahātmā prasīdatu namas te sarvatobhadra sarvato'kṣiśiromukha nirvikāra namas te astu sākṣibhūta hṛdi sthita atīndriya namas tubhyaṃ liṅgebhyas tvaṃ pramīyase ye tu tvāṃ nābhijānanti saṃsāre saṃsaranti te rāgadveṣavinirmuktaṃ lobhamohavivarjitam aśarīraṃ śarīrasthaṃ samaṃ sarveṣu dehiṣu avyaktaṃ buddhyahaṃkārau mahābhūtendriyāṇi ca tvayi tāni na teṣu tvaṃ teṣu tvaṃ tāni na tvayi sraṣṭā bhoktāsi kūṭastho guṇānāṃ prabhur īśvaraḥ akartā heturahitaḥ prabhuḥ svātmany avasthitaḥ namas te puṇḍarīkākṣa punar eva namo astu te īśvaro asi jagannātha kim ataḥ param ucyate bhaktānāṃ yad dhitaṃ deva tad dhyāya tridaśeśvara mā me bhūteṣu saṃyogaḥ punar bhavatu janmani ahaṃkāreṇa buddhyā vā tathā sattvādibhir guṇaiḥ mā me dharmo hy adharmo vā punar bhavatu janmani viṣayair indriyair vāpi mā me bhūyāt samāgamaḥ pṛthivīṃ yātu me ghrāṇaṃ yātu me rasanā jalam cakṣur hutāśanaṃ yātu sparśo me yātu mārutam śabdo hy ākāśam abhyetu mano vaikārikaṃ tathā ahaṃkāraś ca me buddhiṃ tvayi buddhiḥ sametu ca viyogaḥ sarvakaraṇair guṇair bhūtaiś ca me bhavet sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva prakṛtiṃ praviśantu me niṣkevalaṃ padaṃ caiva prayāmi paramaṃ tava ekībhāvas tvayaivāstu mā me janma bhavet punaḥ namo bhagavate tasmai viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave tvanmanas tvadgatapṛāṇas tvadbhaktas tvatparāyaṇaḥ tvām evānusmare deva maraṇe pratyupasthite pūrvadehakṛtā ye me vyādhayas te viśantu mām ārdayantu ca duḥkhāni pravimuñcāmi yad ṛṇam upatiṣṭhantu me rogā ye mayā pūrvasaṃcitāḥ anṛṇo gantum icchāmi tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ahaṃ bhagavatas tasya mama cāsau sureśvaraḥ tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati namo bhagavate tasmai yena sarvam idaṃ tatam tam eva ca prapanno asmi mama yo yasya cāpy aham imām anusmṛtiṃ nityaṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ pāpanāśanīm svapañ jāgrat paṭhed yas tu trisaṃdhyaṃ vāpi yaḥ smaret maraṇe cāpy anuprāpte yas tv imāṃ samanusmaret api pāpasamācāraḥ so api yāti parāṃ gatim arcayann api yo devaṃ gṛhe vāpi baliṃ dadet juhvad agniṃ smared vāpi labhate sa parāṃ gatim paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ śrāvayec chraddadhānaṃs tu ye cānye mām upāśritāḥ nama ity eva yo brūyān madbhaktaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ tasya syur akṣayā lokāḥ śvapākasyāpi nārada kiṃ punar ye yajante māṃ sādhavo vidhipūrvakam dhyāyanti ca yathānyāyaṃ te yānti paramāṃ gatim aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ yaḥ sahasraṃ samācaret nāsau tat padam āpnoti madbhaktair yad avāpyate iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ tapo adhītaṃ vratāni niyamāś ca ye sarvam etad vināśāntaṃ jñānasyānto na vidyate tasmāt pradeyaṃ sādhubhyo dharmyaṃ sattvābhayaṃkaram dānādīny antavantīha madbhakto nāntam aśnute yo dadyād bhagavajjñānaṃ kuryād vā dharmadeśanām kṛtsnāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ dadyān na tu tulyaṃ kathaṃcana kāntāravanadurgeṣu kṛcchreṣv āpatsu saṃbhrame dasyubhiḥ saṃniruddhaś ca nāmabhir māṃ prakīrtayet varāho rakṣatu jale viṣameṣu ca vāmanaḥ rāmo rāmaś ca rāmaś ca trāyantāṃ dasyudoṣataḥ aṭavyāṃ nārasiṃhas tu sarvataḥ pātu keśavaḥ baddhaḥ parikaras tena mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati sakṛd uccāritaṃ yena harir ity akṣaradvayam janmāntarasahasrāṇi tapojñānasamādhibhiḥ narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate gatvā gatvā nivartane candrasūryādayo grahāḥ adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ na vāsudevāt param asti maṅgalaṃ na vāsudevāt paramaṃ pavitram na vāsudevāt param asti daivataṃ na vāsudevaṃ praṇipatya sīdati tasmān mām eva devarṣe dhyāyasvātandritaḥ sadā avāpsyasi tataḥ siddhiṃ padaṃ drakṣyasi ca dhruvam evaṃ sa devadevena nāradaḥ pratibodhitaḥ cakāra keśave bhaktiṃ tasmāt tvaṃ kuru bhūpate yaḥ paṭhet parayā bhaktyā sa gacched viṣṇusāmyatām etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam pāpaṃ praṇaśyate yena puṇyaṃ yena vivardhate yaj japan sugatiṃ yāti śṛṇvaṃś ca mama tad vada kaścid āsīd dvijadrogdhā piśunaḥ kṣatriyādhamaḥ parapīḍārucir duṣṭaḥ svabhāvād eva nirghṛṇaḥ paribhūtāḥ sadā tena pitṛdevadvijātayaḥ paradāreṣu caivāsya babhūvābhirataṃ manaḥ sa tv āyuṣi parikṣīṇe jajñe ghoro niśācaraḥ tena vai karmadoṣeṇa svena pāpakṛtāṃ varaḥ krūrair eva tato vṛttiṃ rākṣasatve viśeṣataḥ cakāra karmabhiḥ pāpaḥ sarvaprāṇivihiṃsakaḥ tasya pāparatasyaivaṃ jagmur varṣaśatāni vai tena vai karmadoṣeṇa nānyā vṛttir arocata yad yat paśyati sattvaṃ sa tat tad ādāya rākṣasaḥ cakhāda puruṣavyāghra bāhugocaram āgatam evaṃ tasyātiduṣṭasya kurvataḥ prāṇināṃ vadham jagāma sumahān kālaḥ pariṇāmaṃ tathā vayaḥ sa dadarśa tapasyantaṃ tāpasaṃ saṃśritavratam ūrdhvabāhuṃ mahābhāgaṃ kṛtarakṣaṃ samantataḥ taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa tu durbuddhir brāhmaṇaṃ rākṣasādhamaḥ samabhyadhāvad vegena samādātuṃ cikhādiṣuḥ tena rakṣā ca yā dikṣu brāhmaṇenābhavat kṛtā tayā nirastaṃ tad rakṣo nipapātāvidūrataḥ bhagavan kīdṛśīṃ rakṣāṃ sa cakāra dvijottamaḥ yayā nirdhūtavīryo asau nirasto rajanīcaraḥ ekāgracitto govinde taj japaṃs tatparāyaṇaḥ tapaś cacāra vipro asau praviṣṭo viṣṇupañjaram viṣṇupañjaram icchāmi śrotuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara sadā sarvabhayebhyas tu rakṣā yā paramābhavat tripuraṃ jaghnuṣaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā viṣṇupañjaraḥ śaṃkarasya kuruśreṣṭha rakṣaṇāya nirūpitaḥ vāgīśena tu śakrasya balaṃ hantuṃ prayāsyataḥ tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi tan nibodha mahīpate viṣṇuḥ prācyāṃ sthitaś cakrī viṣṇur dakṣiṇato gadī pratīcyāṃ śārṅgadhṛg viṣṇur viṣṇuḥ khaḍgī mamottare hṛṣīkeśo vikoṇeṣu tacchidreṣu janārdanaḥ kroḍarūpī harir bhūmau narasiṃho ambare mama kṣurāntam amalaṃ cakraṃ bhramaty etat sudarśanam asyāṃśumālā duḥprekṣā hantu pretaniśācarān gadā ceyaṃ sahasrārcir udvamatpāvakolvaṇā rakṣobhūtapiśācānāṃ ḍākiṇīnāṃ ca nāśanī śārṅgavisphūrjitaṃ caiva vāsudevasya madripūn tiryaṅmanuṣyakūṣmāṇḍa- pretādīn hantv aśeṣataḥ khaḍgadhārājvalajjyotsnā- nirdhūtā ye samāhatāḥ te yāntu saumyataṃ sadyo garuḍeneva pannagāḥ ye kūṣmāṇḍās tathā yakṣā ye daityā ye niśācarāḥ pretā vināyakāḥ krūrā manuṣyā jambhakāḥ khagāḥ siṃhādayo ye paśavo dandasūkāś ca pannagāḥ sarve bhavantu te saumyāḥ kṛṣṇaśaṅkharavāhatāḥ cittavṛttiharā ye me ye janāḥ smṛtihārakāḥ balaujasāṃ ca hartāraś chāyāvibhraṃśakāś ca ye ye copabhogahartāro ye ca lakṣaṇanāśakāḥ kūṣmāṇḍās te praṇaśyantu viṣṇucakrarayāhatāḥ buddhisvāsthyaṃ manaḥsvāsthyaṃ svāsthyam aindriyakaṃ tathā mamāstu devadevasya vāsudevasya kīrtanāt pṛṣṭhe purastān mama dakṣiṇottare vikoṇagaś cāstu janārdano hariḥ tad īḍyam īśānam anantam īśvaraṃ janārdanaṃ praṇipatito na sīdati yathā paraṃ brahma haris tathā paraṃ jagatsvarūpaś ca sa eva keśavaḥ ṛtena tenācyutanāmakīrtanāt praṇāśam etu trividhaṃ mamāśubham ity asāv ātmarakṣārthaṃ nyastavān viṣṇupañjaram tenāsādhyaḥ sa duṣṭānāṃ babhūva nṛpa rakṣasām etayārakṣayā rakṣo nirdhūtaṃ bhuvi pātitam japyāvasāne vipro asau dadarśa vigataujasam dṛṣṭvā ca kṛpayāviṣṭaḥ samāśvāsya niśācaram papracchāgamane hetuṃ taṃ cācaṣṭa yathātatham kathayitvā ca tat sarvaṃ rākṣasaḥ punar abravīt prasīda vipravarya tvaṃ nirviṇṇasyātipāpinaḥ pāpapraśamanāyālam upadeśaṃ prayaccha me bahūni pāpāni mayā kṛtāni bahavo hatāḥ kṛtāḥ striyaś ca me bahvyo vidhavā hataputrikāḥ anāgasāṃ ca sattvānām anekānāṃ kṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ so aham icchāmi viprarṣe prasādāt tava suvrata pāpasyāsya kṣayaṃ kartuṃ kuru me dharmadeśanām kathaṃ krūrasvabhāvasya satas tava niśācara sahasaiva samāyātā jijñāsā dharmavartmani tvām attum āgataḥ kṣipto rakṣayā kṛtayā tvayā tatsaṃsparśāc ca me brahman sādhv etan manasi sthitam kā sā rakṣā na tāṃ vedmi vedmi nāsyāḥ parāyaṇam kiṃtv asyāḥ saṃgam āsādya nirvedaṃ prāpitaṃ param sa kṛpāṃ kuru dharmajña mayy anukrośam āvaha yathā pāpāpanodo me bhavaty ārya tathā kuru ity evam uktaḥ sa muniḥ sadayas tena rakṣasā pratyuvāca mahābhāga vimṛśya suciraṃ tadā yat tvam ātthopadeśārthaṃ nirviṇṇaḥ svena karmaṇā yuktam etan na pāpānāṃ nivṛtter upakārakam kariṣye yātudhānānāṃ na tv ahaṃ dharmadeśanām tāṃs tvaṃ pṛccha dvijān saumya ye vai pravacane ratāḥ evam uktvā yayau vipraś cintām āpa ca rākṣasaḥ kathaṃ pāpāpanodaḥ syād ity asau vyākulendriyaḥ na tadā khādate sattvān kṣudhā saṃpīḍito api san ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā kāle jantum ekam abhakṣayat sa kadācit kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ paryaṭan vipine vane dadarśātha phalāhāram agrataḥ kauśikaṃ dvijam taṃ jagrāha ca bhakṣārthaṃ ṣaṣṭhe kāle bubhukṣitaḥ guror arthe phalāhāram āgataṃ brahmacāriṇam gṛhīto rakṣasā tena sa tadā munidārakaḥ nirāśo jīvite prāha sāmapūrvaṃ niśācaram bho bhadramukha yatkāryaṃ gṛhīto aham iha tvayā tad bravīhi yathātattvam ayam asmy anuśādhi mām ṣaṣṭhe kāle mamāhāraḥ kṣudhitasya tvam āgataḥ niḥśūkasyātipāpasya nirghṛṇasya dvijadruhaḥ yady avaśyaṃ tvayādhyāhaṃ bhakṣaṇīyo niśācara āyāsyāmi tad adyaiva nivedya gurave phalam gurumūle tad āgatya yat phalagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam mamātra niṣṭhāṃ prāptasya tat pāpāya niveditam sa tvaṃ muhūrtamātraṃ mām atraiva pratipālaya nivedya gurave yāvad ihāgacchāmy ahaṃ phalam ṣaṣṭhe kāle na me brahman kaścid grahaṇam āgataḥ pramucyate nibodhaitad iti me pāpajīvikām eka evātra mokṣasya tava hetuḥ śṛṇuṣva tam muñcāmy aham asaṃdigdhaṃ yadi tat kurute bhavān guror yan na virodhāya yan na dharmoparodhakam tat kariṣyāmy ahaṃ rakṣo yan na vrataharaṃ mama mayā nisargato brahmañ jātidoṣād viśeṣataḥ nirvivekena pāpena pāpaṃ karma sadā kṛtam ā bālyān mama pāpeṣu na puṇyeṣu rataṃ manaḥ tatpāpasaṃcayān mokṣaṃ prāpnuyāṃ yena tad vada yāni pāpāni karmāṇi bālatvāc caritāni me duṣṭāṃ yonim imāṃ prāpya tanmuktiṃ kathaya dvija yady etad dvijaputra tvaṃ mamākhyāsyasy aśeṣataḥ tat kṣudhārtāt samārtas tvaṃ niyataṃ mokṣam āpsyasi na caitat pāpaśīlo aham adya tvāṃ kṣutpipāsitaḥ ṣaṣṭhe kāle nṛśaṃsātmā bhakṣayiṣyāmi nirghṛṇaḥ evam ukto munisutas tena ghoreṇa rakṣasā cintām avāpa mahatīm aśaktas tad udīritum vimṛśya suciraṃ vipraḥ śaraṇaṃ jātavedasam jagāma jñānadānāya saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ yadi śuśrūṣito vahnir guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇād anu vratāni vā sucīrṇāni saptārciḥ pātu māṃ tataḥ na mātaraṃ na pitaraṃ gauraveṇa yathā gurum yathāham avagacchāmi tathā māṃ pātu pāvakaḥ yathā guruṃ na manasā karmaṇā vacasāpi vā avajānāmy ahaṃ tena pātu satyena pāvakaḥ ity evaṃ śapathān satyān kurvatas tasya tat punaḥ saptārciṣā samādiṣṭā prādurāsīt sarasvatī sā covāca dvijasutaṃ rākṣasagrahaṇākulam mā bhair dvijasutāhaṃ tvāṃ mokṣayāmy atisaṃkaṭāt yad asya rakṣasaḥ śreyo jihvāgre ahaṃ sthitā tava tat sarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi tato mokṣam avāpsyasi adṛśyā rakṣasā tena proktvetthaṃ taṃ sarasvatī adarśanam itā so api dvijaḥ prāha niśācaram śrūyatāṃ tava yac chreyas tathānyeṣāṃ ca pāpinām samastapāpaśuddhyarthaṃ puṇyopacayadaṃ ca yat prātar utthāya satataṃ madhyāhne ahnaḥ kṣaye api vā ayaṃ śastaḥ sadā jāpaḥ sarvapāpopaśāntidaḥ hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam praṇato asmi jagannāthaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu viśveśvaram ajaṃ viṣṇum aprameyaparākramam praṇato asmi prajāpālaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu viṣṇum acyutam īśānam anantam aparājitam praṇato asmi mahātmānaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu carācaraguruṃ nāthaṃ govindaṃ śeṣaśāyinam praṇato asmi paraṃ devaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu govardhanadharaṃ dhīraṃ gobrāhmaṇahite sthitam praṇato asmi gadāpāṇiṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu śaṅkhinaṃ cakriṇaṃ śāntaṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ sragdharaṃ param praṇato asmi patiṃ lakṣmyāḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu dāmodaram udārākṣaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam avyayam praṇato asmi stutaṃ stutyaiḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ śauriṃ mādhavaṃ madhusūdanam praṇato asmi dharādhāraṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu keśavaṃ keśihantāraṃ kaṃsāriṣṭanisūdanam praṇato asmi caturbāhuṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ śrīśaṃ śrīdharaṃ śrīniketanam praṇato asmi śriyaḥ kāntaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu yam īśaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhyāyanti yatayo akṣaram vāsudevam anirdeśyaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ samastālambanebhyo ayaṃ saṃhṛtya manaso gatim dhyāyanti vāsudevākhyaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ sarvagaṃ sarvabhūtaṃ ca sarvasyādhātam īśvaram vāsudevaṃ paraṃ brahma tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ paramātmānam avyaktaṃ yaṃ prayānti sumedhasaḥ karmakṣaye akṣayaṃ devaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ puṇyapāpavinirmuktā yaṃ praviśya punarbhavam na yoginaḥ prāpnuvanti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ brahmā bhūtvā jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam yaḥ sṛjaty acyuto devas tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ brahmatve yasya vaktrebhyaś caturvedamayaṃ vapuḥ sūtaṃ prabho purā jajñe tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ brahmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ jagadyoniṃ janārdanam sraṣṭṛtve saṃsthitaṃ sṛṣṭau praṇato asmi sanātanam yaḥ pāti sṛṣṭaṃ ca vibhuḥ sthitāv asurasūdanaḥ tam ādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato asmi sanātanam dhṛtā mahī hatā daityāḥ paritrātās tathāmarāḥ yena taṃ viṣṇum ādyeśaṃ praṇato asmi sanātanam yajñair yajanti yaṃ viprā yajñeśaṃ yajñabhāvanam taṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato asmi sanātanam varṇāśramān sthitāv ādyo yaḥ sthāpayati vartmani tam ādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato asmi sanātanam kalpānte rudrarūpo yaḥ saṃharaty akhilaṃ jagat tam ādipuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato asmi janārdanam pātālavīthībhūrādīṃs tathā lokān bibharti yaḥ tam antapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato asmi janārdanam saṃbhakṣayitvā sakalaṃ yathā sṛṣṭam idaṃ jagat yo nṛtyaty atiraudrātmā praṇato asmi janārdanam surāsurāḥ pitṛgaṇā yakṣagandharvarākṣasāḥ yasyāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham samastadevāḥ sakalā mānuṣāṇāṃ ca jātayaḥ yasyāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham vṛkṣagulmādayo yasya tathā paśumṛgādayaḥ ekāṃśabhūtā devasya sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham yasmān nānyat paraṃ kiṃcid yasmin sarvaṃ mahātmani yaḥ sarvam avyayo anantaḥ sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca viṣṇur eva tathā pāpaṃ mamāśeṣaṃ praṇaśyatu yathā viṣṇumayaṃ sarvaṃ yat sarvendriyagocaram yac ca jñānaparicchedyaṃ pāpaṃ naśyatu me tathā pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca karma viṣṇumayaṃ yathā anekajanmakarmotthaṃ pāpaṃ naśyatu me tathā yan niśāyāṃ tathā prātar yac ca madhyāparāhṇayoḥ saṃdhyayoś ca kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā tiṣṭhatā vrajatā yac ca śayyāsanagatena ca kṛtaṃ yad aśubhaṃ karma kāyena manasā girā ajñānato jñānato vā vāsudevasya kīrtanāt tat sarvaṃ vilayaṃ yātu toyasthaṃ lavaṇaṃ yathā paradāraparadravya- vāñchādrohodbhavaṃ ca yat paripīḍodbhavaṃ nindāṃ kurvato yan mahātmanām yac ca bhojye tathā peye yac ca kaṇḍūyanādiṣu tad yātu vilayaṃ toye yathā lavaṇabhājanam yad bālye yac ca kaumāre yat pāpaṃ yauvane mama vayaḥpariṇatau yac ca yac ca janmāntareṣu me tan nārāyaṇagovinda- harikṛṣṇeśakīrtanāt prayātu vilayaṃ toye yathā lavaṇabhājanam viṣṇave vāsudevāya haraye keśavāya ca janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya namo bhūyo namo namaḥ idaṃ sārasvataṃ stotram aśeṣāghavināśanam paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpavināśanam idaṃ yaḥ prātar utthāya praṇipatya janārdanam japaty ekamanāḥ pāpaṃ samastaṃ sa vyapohati yas tu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaḥ japaty etan naraḥ puṇyaṃ kṛtvā manasi keśavam śārīraṃ mānasaṃ vāgjaṃ jñānato ajñānato api vā kṛtaṃ tena tu yat pāpaṃ sapta janmāntarāṇi vai mahāpātakam alpaṃ vā tathā yac copapātakam sakalaṃ nāśayaty etat tathānyat puṇyam ṛcchati viprāya suviśiṣṭāya tilapātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa ahany ahani yo dadyāt paṭhaty etac ca tat samam aviplutamatiś cānte saṃprāpya smaraṇaṃ hareḥ viṣṇulokam avāpnoti satyam etan mayoditam yathainaṃ paṭhati nityaṃ stavaṃ sārasvataṃ pumān api pāpasamāyukto mokṣaṃ prāpnoty asāv api yathaitat satyam uktaṃ me nātrālpam api vai mṛṣā rākṣasagrastasarvāṅgaṃ tathā mām eṣa muñcatu evam uccārite muktaḥ sa tadā tena rakṣasā akāmena dvijo bhūyas tam āha rajanīcaram etad bhadramukhākhyātaṃ tava pātakanāśanam viṣṇoḥ sārasvataṃ stotraṃ yaj jagāda sarasvatī hutāśanena prahitā mama jihvāgrasaṃsthitā jagādemaṃ stavaṃ viṣṇoḥ sarvapāpapraśāntidam anenaiva jagannāthaṃ tvam ārādhaya keśavam tataḥ pāpāpanodaṃ tu stute prāpsyasi keśave aharniśaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ stavenānena rākṣasa stauhi bhaktiṃ parāṃ kṛtvā tataḥ pāpād vimokṣyase stuto hi sarvapāpāni nāśayiṣyaty asaṃśayam bhaktyā rākṣasaśārdūla sarvapāpaharo hariḥ tataḥ praṇamya taṃ vipraṃ prasādya ca niśācaraḥ śālagrāmaṃ mahārāja tadaiva tapase yayau tatrāharniśam evaitaj japañ japyaṃ narādhipa devakriyāratir bhūtvā tapas tepe sa rākṣasaḥ ārādhya ca jagannāthaṃ sa tatra puruṣottamam sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokam avāptavān tathā tvam api rājarṣe sarvapāpapraśāntidam ārādhaya hṛṣīkeśaṃ japan sārasvataṃ stavam ya etat paramaṃ stotraṃ vāsudevasya mānavaḥ paṭhiṣyati sa sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyo mokṣam āpsyati brahmann asāre saṃsāre rogādivyāptamānasaḥ śabdādilubdhaḥ puruṣaḥ kiṃ kurvan nāvasīdati sve mahimni sthitaṃ devam aprameyam ajaṃ vibhum śokamohavinirmuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati aprāṇacitikaṃ brahma vedānteṣu prakāśitam ādyaṃ puruṣam īśānaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati aśanādyair asaṃspṛṣṭaṃ sevitaṃ yogibhiḥ sadā sarvadoṣavinirmuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati dhāmatrayavinirmuktaṃ suprabhātaṃ sunirmalam niṣkalaṃ śāśvataṃ devaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati kṣarākṣaravinirmuktaṃ janmamṛtyuvivarjitam abhayaṃ satyasaṃkalpaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati amṛtaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ yaṃ paśyanti manīṣiṇaḥ jñeyākhyaṃ paramātmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati atulaṃ sukhadharmāṇaṃ vyomadehaṃ sanātanam dharmādharmavinirmuktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati vyāsādyair munibhiḥ sarvair dhyānayogaparāyaṇaiḥ arcitaṃ bhāvakusumair viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati viṣṇvaṣṭakam idaṃ puṇyaṃ yogināṃ prītivardhanam yaḥ paṭhet parayā prītyā sa gacched viṣṇusātmyatām etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam kurvan bhaktiṃ hṛṣīkeśe mānavo bhṛgunandana nirvāṇaṃ samavāpnoti yādṛśaṃ tad vadasva me dṛśyante puruṣā bhaktim udvahanto janārdane tathāpy anekadehārti- manastāpāturā mune smṛtamātraḥ surendrasya yo artihā madhusūdanaḥ tasyāpi karmābhiratā duḥkhabhājaḥ kathaṃ narāḥ kaiś ca dānair jagatsvāmī svāmī nārāyaṇo nṛṇām upakārāya bhaktānāṃ jāyate sa mahāmune tvadyukto ayam anupraśno mahārāja śṛṇuṣva tam yathā pṛṣṭam idaṃ samyak kathyamānaṃ yathākhilam pṛthivīṃ ratnasaṃpūrṇāṃ yaḥ kṛṣṇāya prayacchati tasyāpy anyamanaskasya sulabho na janārdanaḥ nārādhyate acyuto dānair na homair bhāvavarjitaiḥ aikātmyaṃ puruṣair yāti tanmayair eva mādhavaḥ śrūyate ca purākhyāto rājoparicaro vasuḥ iyāja subahūn yajñāñ śraddhāpūtena cetasā sa vipraśāpād rājarṣiḥ kasmiṃścit kāraṇāntare ākāśacārī sahasā praviveśa rasātalam rasātalam anuprāptas tathāpi jagataḥ prabhum tuṣṭāva tanmayo bhūtvā divyair mantrair janārdanam devānām eṣa yajñāṃśair yajvī pakṣavivardhanaḥ cedirāḍ iti daityānāṃ matir āsīd rasātale anena vividhair yajñais tarpitas tridaśeśvaraḥ jaghāna daityān vadhyo ayaṃ prāpto asmadgocaraṃ ripuḥ iti saṃmantrya te daityāś cedirājajighāṃsavaḥ tatsamīpam anuprāptā gṛhītavividhāyudhāḥ paramāmarṣasaṃyuktās tatas te cedipuṅgavam hantuṃ na śekuḥ śastrais tu yatnavanto api pārthivam sa cāpi vasur āsīnaḥ keśavārpitamānasaḥ jajāpa mantram oṃkāraṃ praṇavaṃ dvādaśākṣaram dadarśa ca sa viśveśaṃ dhyānāvasthitamānasaḥ kṛtvānyaviṣayatyāgi cittam atyantaniścalam prāg īśam akṣaraṃ dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jagadgurum saṃcintya vāsudevākhyam anirdeśyaṃ parāyaṇam tato antaryāmirupeṇa prākṛtena ca saṃsthitam
