brahmaviṣṇuśivānāṃ ca svarūpaiḥ saṃsthitaṃ tridhā punaś ca devagandharva- siddhādimanujādiṣu sthāvarānteṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣv eva samāsthitam dikṣv ambaradharābhūbhṛt- toyavāyvanalādiṣu dṛśyādṛśyeṣu caiveśaṃ cintayām āsa pārthivaḥ sarvatra dṛṣṭvā taṃ devam ātmany api ca sarvagam sarvaṃ ca tanmayaṃ dṛṣṭvā virarāma samādhitaḥ indriyāṇīndriyārtheṣu pūrvavat sa narādhipaḥ viniveśya tato apaśyad asurān udyatāyudhān tān sa dṛṣṭvā gṛhītārghya ekaikasyaiva pārthivaḥ pādyapūrveṇa vidhinā pūjayām āsa bhaktimān prasādaṃ kuru bhadraṃ vo bhagavāñ jagataḥ patiḥ vāsudevo bhavān prāpto mamānugrahakāmyayā ity evaṃ cedirājo asāv ekaikasya ca dānavān pūjayām āsa pādyādi nivedya vacasā tathā te api taṃ cedirājānaṃ papracchur asurās tadā kva vāsudevo atra vayaṃ prāptā dākṣāyaṇīsutāḥ ity evaṃ vadato daityān sa jagāda punar vasuḥ praṇāmanamro rājendra sarvadarśī mahāmatiḥ vāsudevo jagat sarvaṃ yac ceṅgaṃ yac ca neṅgati brahmādiṣu tṛṇānteṣu sa evaiko jagadguruḥ ahaṃ bhavanto devādyā manuṣyāḥ paśavaś ca ye te api devā jagaddhātur vyatiriktā na keśavāt tenaiva māyā vitatā vaiṣṇavī bhinnadarśanī tayā svāṅgeṣu devo asau pradarśayati sarvaśaḥ tad yūyam aham anye ca yac ca sthāvarajaṅgamam vāsudevātmakaṃ sarvam iti matvā namo astu vaḥ ity uktās tena te daityā na śaktā manujeśvaram yatnavanto api taṃ hantuṃ prayayuḥ svān athālayān tataḥ purohitaṃ sarve kāvyaṃ nītiviśāradam sametya te yathāvṛttaṃ sarvam asmai nyavedayan asmākam atyantaripur ayaṃ prāpto rasātalam devānām upakṛd brahman yajvā cedipatir vasuḥ asmatpakṣakṣayāyaiṣa devānāṃ pakṣavardhanaḥ tatra yat pratipattavyaṃ tan no brūhi mahāmate svagocaram ariḥ prāptaḥ śatrupakṣopakārakaḥ na hantavya itīdaṃ ko nītimān pravadiṣyati tasmāt pragṛhya divyāni sarvāstrāṇy amarārdanāḥ nipātayata taṃ gatvā cedirājaṃ svagocare sarvam etan mahābhāga tasminn asmābhir udyataiḥ kṛtaṃ na śakito hantuṃ niryatno api hi pārthivaḥ kiṃ tad yogaphalaṃ tasya kiṃ vā japaphalaṃ mune tapaso vā muniśreṣṭha vistarāt tad vadasva naḥ nityaṃ saṃcintayaty eṣa yogayukto janārdanam sāsya rakṣā parā manye ko hinasty acyutāśrayam kīrtitaḥ saṃsmṛto dhyātaḥ pūjitaḥ saṃstutas tathā aihikāmuṣmikīṃ rakṣāṃ karoti bhagavān hariḥ yad durlabhaṃ yad aprāpyaṃ manaso yan na gocare tad apy aprārthitaṃ dhyāto dadāti madhusūdanaḥ śarīrārogyam arthāṃś ca bhogāṃś caivānuṣaṅgikān dadāti dhyāyatāṃ nityam apavargaprado hariḥ yad idaṃ cedirājānaṃ hantum icchatha dānavāḥ tad asya keśavāc cittam upāyenāpanīyatām tatas te tadvacaḥ śrutvā dānavāḥ kurupuṅgava brahmarūpapraticchannā jagmur yatra sthito vasuḥ dadṛśus te mahātmānaṃ praṇataṃ cedipuṅgavam kṛtapūjaṃ jagaddhātur vāsudevasya pārthivam saṃstutāv udyataṃ śāntaṃ sarvatra samadarśinam kṛṣṇārpitamanovṛttiṃ jānubhyām avaniṃgatam tataḥ saṃśṛṇvatāṃ teṣāṃ tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam tannāmasmaraṇodbhūta- pulakaś cedipuṅgavaḥ jagāda yaṃ sa rājarṣiḥ stavaṃ kṛṣṇasya śaunaka śṛṇvatāṃ dānavendrāṇāṃ tan me pāpaharaṃ vada śṛṇu yad devadevasya viṣṇor adbhutakarmaṇaḥ stotraṃ jagāda rājāsau rasātalatalaṃ gataḥ staumi devam ajaṃ nityaṃ pariṇāmavivarjitam avṛddhikṣayam īśānam acyutaṃ parataḥ param kalpanākṛtanāmānam anirdeśyam ajaṃ vibhum mūlahetum ahetuṃ tvāṃ vāsudevaṃ namāmy aham paramārthaparair īśaś cintyate yaḥ prajākaraiḥ taṃ vāsudevam īśeśaṃ namāmy adya guṇaṃ param yasmād idaṃ yatra cedam idaṃ yo viśvam avyayam taṃ vāsudevam amalaṃ namāmi parameśvaram jñeyaṃ jñātāram ajaraṃ bhoktāraṃ prakṛteḥ prabhum puruṣasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ nato asmi puruṣaṃ param pradhānādiviśeṣānta- svarūpam ajam avyayam sthūlasūkṣmamayaṃ sarvaṃ- vyāpinaṃ taṃ namāmy aham sraṣṭā pālayitā cānte yaś ca saṃhārakārakaḥ trayīmayaṃ taṃ triguṇaṃ nato asmi puruṣottamam ābrahmasthāvarānte ca yo jagaty atra saṃsthitaḥ vyaktarūpī ca taṃ devaṃ nato ahaṃ viṣṇum avyayam namo namo astu te deva jagatām īśvareśvara paramārtha parācintya vidhātaḥ parameśvara tvam ādir anto madhyaṃ ca jagato asya jagatpate jagat tvayi jagac ca tvaṃ jagat tvatto jaganmaya tavāgnir āsaṃ vasudhāṅghriyugmaṃ nabhaḥ śiraś candraravī ca netre samastalokā jaṭharaṃ bhujāś ca diśaś catasro bhagavan namas te yad bhūgataṃ yad gaganāntarāle yad vā nabhasy akhilalokagaṃ ca yat sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ paratas tato api yad asti yan nāsti ca tat tvam īśa vedāś ca vedyaṃ ca bhagavān ananto vedāntavedyaś ca samastaheto vadanti tat tvā munayaḥ pareśaṃ tvayi prasanne paramārthadṛśye namo hṛṣīkeśa tavāprameya namaś ca tubhyaṃ paramārthasāra viṣṇo namas te astu parāpareśa kṛṣṇācyutānanta jagannivāsa namo astu tubhyaṃ parameśvarāya namas tathāntaḥkāraṇasthitāya pradhānabhūtāya namaś ca tubhyam vyaktasvarūpeṇa ca saṃsthitāya saṃhṛtya viśvaṃ jalaśāyine namo namaś ca te kaiṭabhasūdanāya svanābhipadmodaraśāyine ca brahmasvarūpopanatāya caiva sraṣṭre namaḥ pālayitre sthitau ca sarveśa tubhyaṃ puruṣottamāya rudrāya cānte kṣayahetave te nato asmi saṃhārakarāya viṣṇo jaya prapannārtiharāprameya jayāgnivasvaśvimaya prajeśa rudrendracandrastuta devadeva jayāmarāṇām ariśātanāya jitaṃ tvayā sarvaga sarvasāraṃ sarvātmabhūtākhila vedavedya jitaṃ jitākṣāmalacittadṛśya carācarādhāra dharādhareḍya yajñāśrayo yajñapumān aśeṣa deveśa martyāsurayajñabhoktaḥ tvam īḍyamāno abhimataṃ dadāsi dharādhareśācyuta vāsudeva namas te devadeva tvaṃ yathā pāsy akhilaṃ jagat sthitau tathā samastebhyo doṣebhyo māṃ samuddhara kṛṣṇācyuta hṛṣīkeśa sarvabhūteśa keśava mahātmaṃs trāhi māṃ bhaktaṃ vāsudeva prasīda me iti stotrāvasāne taṃ cedirājaṃ tato asurāḥ jahasuḥ satalākṣepaṃ procuś ca dvijarūpiṇaḥ prājñaḥ kila prajāpālaś cedirāṭ saṃśruto bhuvi tas asya jñānam akhilaṃ viparītārtham īdṛśam kva vāsudevaḥ kva bhavān imām antyāṃ daśāṃ gataḥ yo bhavān vipraśāpena rasātalatalāśrayaḥ bhaviṣyati smṛto devas trātā kila tavācyutaḥ yo asāv āpyāyyate viprair adhvareṣu haviḥsravaiḥ yo anyatras trāṇakāmo vā yajñabhāgam abhīpsate sa trātā tava govindo bhaviṣyaty ativismayaḥ yadā tvaṃ bhagavadbhakto vipraśāpān nipātitaḥ tadā sa vāsudevas te kva gato alpaśruto avyayaḥ na vāsudevo na harir na govindo na keśavaḥ śāpaṃ dadatsu vipreṣu paritrāṇaparo bhavet sa tvam ārtapralāpebhyo viramādya yadīcchasi kubuddhim etāṃ saṃtyajya svapauruṣaparo bhava na vayaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ nānantaṃ nācyutaṃ harim saṃśritā na ca sīdāmaḥ svapauruṣam upāśritāḥ yady asmadvacanaṃ vīra na mohena viśaṅkase tadāśrayasva svaṃ vīryaṃ parityajya vimūḍhatām ity udīritam ākarṇya sa teṣāṃ cedipuṅgavaḥ ajñānapaṭalacchannān hṛdayena śuśoca tān uvāca cedirājo vai hṛdaye kṛtamatsaraḥ aho moho ayam eteṣām ahaṃkārasamudbhavaḥ yena sarveśvare viṣṇāv eteṣām āvṛtā matiḥ prakāśaṃ ca sa tān āha dānavān prītipūrvakam pāpatas tatparitrāṇaṃ cikīrṣur vasudhādhipaḥ maivaṃ bho bhagavadbhaktiṃ kurudhvaṃ dvijasattamāḥ saṃsārābdhau manuṣyāṇām ekaḥ poto janārdanaḥ yūyaṃ vayaṃ tathaivānye tasya sarve vibhūtayaḥ brahmādisthāvarāntaṃ hi tasya devasya vistṛtiḥ sukhaduḥkhamayo nṝṇāṃ vipākaḥ karmaṇāṃ ca yaḥ saṃśuddhihetuḥ svacchandāt so api viprāḥ pravartate parīkṣāṃ ca jagannāthaḥ karoty adṛḍhacetasām narāṇām arthavidhvaṃsa- nikāśeṣu janārdanaḥ alpayatnena cāyānti vimuktiṃ keśavāśrayāt tadvighātāya śakrādyā yatante vighnahetubhiḥ yadā janārdane bhaktiṃ vahan sīdati mānavaḥ nirviṇṇacetāḥ śaithilyaṃ manasaḥ kurute tadā devānāṃ mahatī śaṅkā bhaktiyuktā janārdane muktibhājo bhaviṣyantīty atas te paripanthinaḥ prāyo bhavanti govinde bhaktivyāghātahetavaḥ vighnāś cittavighātā hi vimuktiparipanthinaḥ satyaṃ śatena vighnānāṃ sahasreṇa tathā tapaḥ vighnāyutena govinde nṝṇāṃ bhaktir nivāryate svaṃ cāpi karma puruṣaḥ śubhāśubham upāgatam bhuṅkte kim atra devasya garhyate yena keśavaḥ maryādāṃ ca kṛtāṃ tena yo bhinatti sa mānavaḥ na viṣṇubhakto mantavyaḥ sādhu dharmārcano hariḥ na puṣpair na ca dhūpena nopahārānulepanaiḥ toṣaṃ prayāti govindaḥ svakarmābhyarcito yathā brāhmaṇā devadevena mukhāt sṛṣṭā mahātmanā devānām api saṃpūjya bhūmidevā dvijottamāḥ anuvṛttiḥ sadā kāryā teṣāṃ varṇair anuvrataiḥ te pūjyās te namaskāryās toṣaṇīyāś ca yatnataḥ teṣu tuṣṭeṣv aśeṣāṇāṃ devānāṃ prītir uttamā teṣāṃ mayā yad ajñānāj jñānād vā kṛtam apriyam tenāpi tuṣṭa evāhaṃ viṣṇor aṃśā dvijottamāḥ kriyāvān mama poto ayaṃ bhūtalād yo rasātale patitasyātibhīme asmin duruttāre bhavārṇave rasātalatalottāraṃ na hi vāñchāmy ahaṃ dvijāḥ saṃsāragartād uttāraṃ vṛṇomy ārādhanād dhareḥ yathāhaṃ nābhivāñchāmi bhogān ārādhya keśavam tena satyena viṣṇur me sarvadoṣān vyapohatu yathā na mātā na pitā nātmā na suhṛdaḥ sutāḥ kṛṣṇālāpāt priyatarās tathā māṃ pātu keśavaḥ yathā viṣṇumayaṃ sarvam etat paśyāmy ahaṃ jagat tathā mama manodoṣān aśeṣān sa vyapohatu jātā viṣṇuvilomeṣu bhavatsv api dayā mama yathā tenādya satyena bhavantaḥ santu tanmayāḥ yathā nāhaṃ bhavaddveṣān na saṃharṣād bravīmy aham kṛpayaiva tathā sarve bhavantaḥ santu tanmayāḥ yo yo na bhakto govinde tatra tatra kṛpā yathā mamārivarge api tathā bhaktir vo astu janārdane evam uccārite teṣāṃ daityānāṃ tatkṣaṇāt tathā tasmin rājany abhūn maitrī tathānyeṣu ca jantuṣu devadeve apy abhūd bhaktir bhāvo naṣṭas tathāsuraḥ svarūpadhāriṇaś cainaṃ praṇamyāsurapuṅgavāḥ pratyūcuḥ pārthivaṃ viṣṇu- bhaktaṃ sadbrahmacāriṇam cedibhūpāla bhadraṃ te bhavato atulavikrama saṃsāre tvatsamaiḥ saṅgaḥ puṇyabhājāṃ pravartate vayaṃ svajātidoṣeṇa devapakṣavirodhinaḥ bhavantam āgatā hantuṃ devaprīṇanatatparam yadā na śaktito hantum asmābhis tvaṃ nirāyudhaḥ viṣṇudhyānamahārakṣā- kakṣāntaragataḥ prabho tyājayadbhis tathā bhaktiṃ keśavād iti darśitam vaiphalyam atipuṇyeṣu viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇā nṛṇām sa tvaṃ devātidevasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ anugrāhyo yathā teyam acyute niścalā matiḥ diṣṭyā krodhābhibhūtānām asmākaṃ tvannivarhaṇe matir jātā yataḥ prāptā tvatsaṅgād durlabhā matiḥ kuruṣva ca prasādaṃ tvaṃ praṇatānāṃ nareśvara śatrāv api kṛpāśīlaṃ yan no duṣṭam abhūn manaḥ diśāṃ vaimalyaṃ vimalaṃ cakṣuṣaś copapāditam bhavatā duṣṭatāṃ etām āsurīm apamārjatā duṣṭāḥ sma varṣapūgāni yad yātāni vṛthaiva naḥ viṣayākṣiptacittānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktim akurvatām karmabhūmau manuṣyāṇāṃ tad eva viphalaṃ dinam yad acyutakathālāpa- dhyānārcārahitaṃ gatam ity uktvā te asurā bhūyaḥ prasādya ca tathā vasum viṣṇau bhaktiparā yātās tīvrasaṃyogino alayan sa cāpi cedirāṭ tasmād devadevena cakriṇā pātālād uddhṛtaḥ paścāt saṃsāragahanād api ity etat sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi yathāvasīdanti narā bhaktimanto api keśave dṛḍhā janārdane bhaktir yadaivāvyabhicāriṇī tadā kiyat svargasukhaṃ saiva nirvāṇahetukī ity etad asuraiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃvādaṃ yaḥ purā vasoḥ paṭhiṣyaty akhilaṃ bhaktyā sa tallokam upaiṣyati jagatprabhuṃ devadevam aśeṣeśam janārdanam praṇipatyāham etaṃ tvāṃ yat pṛcchāmi tad ucyatām yair upāyaiḥ pradānair vā narāṇām amarārcitaḥ prītimān puṇḍarīkākṣo bhavaty ācakṣva tan mama ye svadharme sthitā varṇā viprādyāḥ kurunandana vidharmeṣu na vartante prītimāṃs teṣu keśavaḥ brahmacārigṛhasthādyā na cyavanty āśramāc ca ye svadharmato haris teṣāṃ prītimān eva sarvadā ye na dambhena vartante narā bhūteṣv alolupāḥ tyaktagrāmyādisaṃgāś ca teṣu prītiḥ parā hareḥ dātāro nāpahartāraḥ parasvānām amāyinaḥ ye narās teṣu govindaḥ putreṣv iva sadā hitaḥ yeṣāṃ narāṇāṃ na matir jihvā vāsatyam ujjhati te priyā vāsudevasya ye ca dvijaparāyaṇāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā ye na hiṃsānuvartinaḥ te narā vāsudevasya priyāḥ pāṇḍukulodvaha sarvadeveṣu ye viṣṇuṃ sarvabhūteṣv avasthitam manyante vāsudevasya te priyāḥ putravat sadā brahmādyaṃ sthāvarāntaṃ ca bhūtagrāmaṃ janārdanāt ye ca paśyanty abhedena te viṣṇoḥ satataṃ priyāḥ devavedadvijātīnāṃ nindāyāṃ ye na mānavāḥ prītibhājo bhavantīṣṭās te sadā śārṅgadhanvinaḥ priyāṇām atha sarveṣāṃ devadevasya sa priyaḥ āpatsv api sadā yasya bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī tasmāt priyatvaṃ kṛṣṇasya vāñchatā nijadharmajaiḥ guṇair ātmā sadā yojyo na dūre guṇino hariḥ yeṣāṃ na gṛddhiḥ pārakye dāre dravye ca cetasaḥ hiṃsāyāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ smṛtayo yeṣāṃ sanmārgasevinām paropakārasaktānāṃ te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ kalikalmaṣadoṣeṇa yeṣāṃ nopahatā matiḥ pāṣaṇḍānugatā naiva te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ yeṣāṃ kleśo guror arthe devaviprodbhavo api vā na vivitsāsamudbhūtas te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ svapantaḥ saṃsthitā yāntas tiṣṭhantaś ca janārdanam ye cintayanty avirataṃ te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ yathātmani tathāpatye yeṣāṃ adrohiṇī matiḥ samastasattvajāteṣu te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ devapūjām anudinaṃ guruviprārthasatkriyām ye kurvanti narā viddhi te kṛṣṇenāvalokitāḥ suvarṇaṃ ratnam athavā pārakyaṃ vijane vane vilokya naiti yo lobhaṃ taṃ avaihi hareḥ priyam devān pitṝṃs tathāpannān atithīñ jāmayo adhvagān yo bibharti vijānīhi taṃ naraṃ bhagavatpriyam na krodham eti kruddhebhyaḥ sahate yo nirākriyām taṃ vijānīhi bhartavyaṃ devadevasya śārṅginaḥ paralokapratīkāra- karaṇāya sadodyamam kurvann ālakṣyatām eti keśavenāvalokitaḥ nātmasaṃstavam anyeṣāṃ na nindāṃ cārthalipsayā karoti puruṣavyāghra yasya nārāyaṇo hṛdi sarvabhūtadayāṃ satyam akrodhaṃ dharmaśīlatām bhajante puruṣā deve govinde hṛdaye sthite na kalau na paradravye paradārāśritā matiḥ narāṇāṃ jāyate rājan govinde hṛdayasthite kṣamāṃ karoti kruddheṣu dayāṃ mūḍheṣu mānavaḥ mudaṃ ca dharmaśīleṣu govinde hṛdaye sthite yadā bibhety adharmāder dharmādīṃś ca yadecchati tadā kuruvaraśreṣṭha naraḥ kṛṣṇena vīkṣitaḥ putradāragṛhakṣetra- dravyāder mamatāṃ naraḥ nāyāsyati jagannāthe hṛṣīkeśe parāṅmukhe kalau kṛtayugaṃ teṣāṃ kleśās teṣāṃ sukhādhikāḥ yeṣāṃ śarīragrahaṇe hariśuśrūṣaṇe matiḥ yadā necchati pāpāni yadā puṇyāni vāñchati jñeyas tadā manuṣyeṇa hṛdaye asya hariḥ sthitaḥ paramārthe matiḥ puṃsām asāre tu bhavārṇave kathaṃ bhavati rājendra viṣvaksena parāṅmukhe śraddadhāno dayāśīlaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ parārthe mānavaḥ kṛṣṇe prasanne nṛpa jāyate vahato api sadā kṛṣṇe bhaktim avyabhicāriṇīm pāṇiṣv asamadṛgbuddheḥ sulabho naiva keśavaḥ ye dāmbhikā bhinnavṛttā ye ca dharmadhvajocchrayāḥ durlabho bhagavān devas teṣāṃ suyatatām api kāmalobhāśritaṃ yeṣāṃ cittaṃ krodhādidūṣitam teṣāṃ janmasahasre api na matiḥ keśavāśrayā heyāṃ kṛṣṇāśrayāṃ vṛttiṃ manyante hetusaṃśritāḥ aviyopahatajñānā ye ajñāne jñānamāninaḥ vedavādavirodhena kūṭayuktim apāśritāḥ ye keśavas taddhṛdaye na kadācit priyātithiḥ mānuṣaṃ taṃ manuṣyatve manyamānāḥ kubuddhayaḥ karmāṇi ye asya nindanti na teṣāṃ niṣkṛtir nṛṇām kecid vadanti taṃ devaṃ manuṣyaṃ cālpamedhasaḥ tiryaktvaṃ cāpare viṣṇuṃ māyayā tasya mohitāḥ devatvam api kṛṣṇasya yasya nindā mahātmanaḥ stutiṃ tasya kathaṃ śaktāḥ kartum īśasya mānavāḥ vyāpitvaṃ śāśvatatvaṃ ca janmabhāvavivarjitam yadāsya procyate kāsya stutir arthe tathā sthitau sarveśvareśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ procyate yadi paṇḍitaḥ tathāpi svalpam evoktaṃ bhūtārthe katamā stutiḥ ābrahmastambaparyante saṃsāre yasya saṃsthitiḥ nindāpi tasya na nṛbhiḥ kartum īśasya śakyate yadā kāṇāś ca kūṇṭhāś ca mūḍho durbuddhir āturaḥ sarvagatvāt sa evaikas tadāsau nindyate katham sraṣṭā pālayitā hartā jagato asya jagac ca saḥ yaṣṭā yājayitā yājyaḥ sa eva bhagavān hariḥ dātā dānaṃ tathādātā kartā kāryaṃ tathā kriyāḥ hantā ghātayitā hiṃsyo hāryaṃ hartā ca yaḥ svayam sarvakāraṇabhūtasya tasyeśasya mahātmanaḥ kaḥ karoti stutiṃ viṣṇor nindāṃ vā pṛthivīpate tasmāt sarveśvaro viṣṇur na stotuṃ na ca ninditum śakyate sarvabhūtatvāc cokṣācokṣasvarūpiṇā stuteḥ pādād yato nānyad utkṛṣṭam upalabhyate tasyāpy uccāraṇeneśo na stotuṃ śakyate hariḥ bhūtārthavādastutaye na nindāyai vidhīyate yato ataḥ sarvabhūtasya kā nindā tasya kā stutiḥ yena sarvātmanā tatra hṛdayaṃ saṃniveśitam api maunavatas tasya sulabho ayaṃ janārdanaḥ tasmāt tvaṃ kuruśārdūla svadharmaparipālanam kuru viṣṇuṃ ca hṛdaye sarvavyāpinam īśvaram tanmanā bhava tadbhaktas tadyājī taṃ namaskuru viṣṇor evaṃ priyatvaṃ tvam āśu yāsyasi pārthiva yaṃ stuvan stavyatām eti vandyamānaś ca vandyatām tam īśvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ hṛdaye saṃniveśaya saṃpūjya yaṃ pūjyatamo bhavaty atra jagattraye tam īśvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ hṛdaye kuru pārthiva svavarṇakarmābhirataḥ kuru citte janārdanam eṣa śāstrārthasadbhāvaḥ kim uktair bahuvistaraiḥ yasmin prasannacittas tvaṃ yasmin kopam upaiṣi ca tāv ubhāv api tadbhūtau cintayan siddhim eṣyasi yatra yatra sthitaṃ cetaḥ prītyā snehena vā tava taṃ taṃ cintaya govindaṃ manasaḥ sthairyakāraṇāt svapan vibuddhyann uttiṣṭhan sthito bhuñjan piban vrajan sarvagaṃ sarvakartāraṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvatra cintaya yathāgnisaṃgāt kanakam apadoṣaṃ prajāyate saṃśliṣṭaṃ vāsudevena manuṣyāṇāṃ tathā manaḥ yajvino yaṃ namasyanti yaṃ namasyanti devatāḥ yogino yaṃ namasyanti taṃ namasyaṃ namāmy aham bhūyaś ca śṛṇu rājendra yaj jagāda janārdanaḥ nāgaparyaṅkaśayane pṛṣṭaḥ kṣīrābdhikanyayā purā śayānaṃ govindaṃ prāvṛṭkāle mahodadhau śeṣabhogimahābhoge vīcyambukaṇaśītale vakṣaḥsthalasthitā devī jaganmātā jagatpatim ananyāsaktadṛṣṭiṃ ca kim apy ekāgramānasam śrīvatsavkṣasaṃ lakṣmīḥ karasaṃvāhanādṛtā yoganidrāvasānastham acyutaṃ jagataḥ patim papraccha puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ puṇḍarīkakarā harim sṛṣṭaṃ jagad idaṃ sarvaṃ bahuśaś copasaṃhṛtam tvayā jagatpate cātra kiṃ kaścid dayitas tava devān manuṣyān gandharvān yakṣavidyādharāsurān sṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭān nirghṛṇatvād upasaṃharate bhavān kaścid eteṣu bhūteṣu devādiṣu tavācyuta dveṣo asti prītir athavā samaḥ sarvatra vā bhavān samo asmi sarvabhūteṣu na me dveṣyo asti na priyaḥ tathāpi guṇagṛhyo ahaṃ pratyekahṛdayasthitaḥ antarātmani sarvasya lokasyāham avasthitaḥ puṇyāpuṇyakṛtau teṣu prītidveṣau śubhe mama puṇyaṃ prītyanubhāvena sādhu buddhiṣu vartate dveṣānubhāvenāpuṇyaṃ phaladaṃ teṣu bhāmini śrūyatāṃ ca mahābhāge nareṣu śubhacāriṣu satataṃ yeṣu me prītis tathāprītir varānane pralayotpattitattvajñā ātmajñānaparāś ca ye ete svakarmaṇā bhadre mama prītipathaṃ gatāḥ vāṅmanaḥkāyikīṃ hiṃsāṃ ye na kurvanti kutracit sarvamaitrā narā lakṣmi dayitās te sadā mama svakīyadravyasaṃtuṣṭā nivṛttāś cauryakarmaṇaḥ satyaśīladayāyuktā narā mama sadā priyāḥ mātṛsvasṛsutātulyān paradārāṃś ca ye narāḥ manyante te ca me lakṣmi dṛḍhaṃ priyatamāḥ sadā na kāmān na ca saṃrambhān na dveṣād ye ca bhāmini saṃtyajanti svakaṃ karma te atīva dayitā mama viśvāsyāḥ sarvabhūtānām ahiṃsrāś ca dayālavaḥ tyaktānṛtakathā devi manuṣyā dayitā mama dharmalabdhāṃs tu ye bhogān bhuñjate nātikīkaṭāḥ paralokāvirodhena te mamātipriyā narāḥ na lobhe na ca kārpaṇye na steye na ca matsare yeṣāṃ matir manuṣyāṇāṃ te atīva dayitā mama dharmalabdheṣu dāreṣu ṛtukālābhigāminaḥ gṛhasthakarmābhiratā narās te dayitā mama pararandhreṣu jātyandhāḥ paradāreṣv apuṃsakāḥ parāpavāde ye mūkā dayitās te narā mama parāpavādaṃ nindāṃ ca paramarmāvaghaṭṭanam ye na kurvanti puruṣās te devi mama vallabhāḥ satyāṃ ślakṣṇāṃ nirābādhāṃ madhurāṃ prītidāyinīm ye vācam īrayanti sma te manuṣyā mama priyāḥ ye brāhmaṇārthe saṃtyajya sadyaḥ svam api jīvitam yatante parayā bhaktyā te devi dayitā mama sākṣād devam ivāyāntaṃ yā patiṃ nityam arcati pādaśaucādibhir nārī tasyā nāhaṃ sudurlabhaḥ pūrṇacandram ivodyataṃ bhartāraṃ yā gṛhāgatam hṛṣṭā paśyati tāṃ viddhi dayitāṃ yoṣitaṃ mama te bhaktā ye sadā viprān pūjayanty abdhisaṃbhave yathāvibhavato bhaktyā svakarmābhiratā narāḥ śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ manasāpi na ye narāḥ samullaṅghya pravartante te bhaktā mama bhāmini brahmarūpadharasyāsyān mama vedā viniḥsṛtāḥ manvādirūpiṇaś caiva samastāḥ smṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ śrutiḥ smṛtir mamaivājñā tām ullaṅghya yajec chubhe sarvasvenāpi māṃ devi nāpnoty ājñāvighātakṛt yaḥ svadharmān na calati hiṃsādhau yo na sajyate vahatas tasya madbhaktiṃ sadaivāhaṃ na durlabhaḥ etad devi mayākhyātaṃ yat pṛṣṭo aham iha tvayā priyāṇāṃ mama sarveṣāṃ śṛṇu yo atitaraṃ priyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdraś ca varavarṇini svadharmād acalan devi dayāvān sarvajantuṣu satyavāc chaucasaṃpanno na drohī na ca matsarī vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ śānto dayitaḥ satataṃ mama evaṃ śrīr devadevena prāg uktā harimedhasā tavāpi hi naraśreṣṭha yathāvat kathitaṃ mayā saṃvādam etad devasya saha lakṣmyā jagatpateḥ yaḥ śṛṇoti sa pāpebhyaḥ samastebhyaḥ pramucyate bhūyo akhilaṃ jagaddhātur vāsudevasya bhārgava samyagārādhanāyālaṃ kriyāyogaṃ bravīhi me yat phalaṃ keśavasyārcāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya labhen naraḥ yac ca devakulaṃ viṣṇoḥ kārayitvā phalaṃ labhet yad dīpadhūpapuṣpāṇāṃ gandhānāṃ ca nivedane dhvajādidāne yat puṇyaṃ yat puṇyaṃ gītavādite tathā pavitrapaṭhane jayaśabdādyudīraṇe saṃmārjanādau yat puṇyaṃ namaskāre pradakṣiṇe śīrṇasphuṭitasaṃskāra- karaṇe cāpi yat phalam tan me vistarataḥ sarvaṃ bhagavan vaktum arhasi yaiś copavāsair bhagavān narair ārādhyate hariḥ teṣāṃ phalaṃ ca yat kṛtsnaṃ tan mamācakṣva vistarāt saṃkṣepāt pūrvam evaitad bhavataḥ kathitaṃ mayā vistareṇa mahārāja śrūyatāṃ bruvato mama aditir nāma devānāṃ mātā paramaduścaram tapaś cacāra varṣāṇāṃ sahasraṃ pṛthivīpate ārādhanāya kṛṣṇasya vāgyatā vāyubhojanā daityair nirākṛtān dṛṣṭvā tanayān kurunandana vṛthāputrāham asmīti nirvedāt praṇatā harim tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ paramārthāvabodhinī śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇatā bhaktavatsalam devadaityanṛpaśvāpa- vyomavāyvādirūpiṇam namaḥ smṛtārtināśāya namaḥ puṣkaramāline namaḥ paramakalyāṇa- kalyāṇāyādivedhase namaḥ paṅkajanetrāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye namaḥ paṅkajasaṃbhūti- saṃbhavāyātmayonaye śriyaḥ kāntāya dāntāya dāntadṛśyāya cakriṇe namaḥ śaṅkhāsihastāya namaḥ kanakaretase tathātmajñānavijñāna- yogacittātmayogine nirguṇāya viśeṣāya haraye brahmarūpiṇe jagat pratiṣṭhitaṃ yatra jagatā yo na dṛśyate namaḥ sthūlātisūkṣmāya tasmai devāya śaṅkhine yaṃ na paśyanti paśyanto jagad apy akhilaṃ narāḥ apaśyadbhir jagad yac ca dṛśyate svahṛdi sthitaḥ bahirjyotiṣi lakṣyo yo lakṣyate jyotiṣaḥ paraḥ yasminn etad yataś caitad yaś caitad akhilaṃ jagat tasmai samastajagatām ādhārāya namo namaḥ ādyaḥ prajāpatipatir yaḥ pitṝṇāṃ paraḥ patiḥ patiḥ surāṇāṃ yas tasmai namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase yaḥ pravṛttair nivṛttaiś ca karmabhir vibhur ijyate svargāpavargaphalado namas tasmai gadādhṛte yaś cintyamāno manasā sadyaḥ pāpaṃ vyapohati namas tasmai viśuddhāya parasmai harimedhase yaṃ praviśyākhilādhāram īśānam ajam avyayam na punar janmamaraṇe prāpnuvanti namāmi tam yo yajñe yajñaparamair ijyate yajñasaṃsthitiḥ taṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ namāmi prabhum īśvaram gīyate sarvavedeṣu vedavidbhir vidāṃ gatiḥ yas tasmai vedavedyāya viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ yato viśvaṃ samudbhūtaṃ yasmiṃś ca layam eṣyati viśvodbhavapratiṣṭhāya namas tasmai mahātmane brahmādistambaparyantaṃ vinā yena tatām imām māyāṃ nālaṃ samuttartuṃ tam upendraṃ namāmy aham yam ārādhya viśuddhena manasā karmaṇā girā haraty avidyām akhilāṃ tam upendraṃ namāmy aham viṣādatoṣaroṣādyair yo ajasraṃ sukhaduḥkhajaiḥ nṛtyaty akhilabhūtasthas tam upendraṃ namāmy aham yo annatoyasvarūpastho bibharty akhilam īśvaraḥ viśvaṃ viśvapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ taṃ namāmi prajāpatim mūrtaṃ tamo asuramayaṃ tadvadhād vinihanti yaḥ rātrijaṃ sūryarūpī ca tam upendraṃ namāmy aham kapilādisvarūpastho yaś cājñānamayaṃ tamaḥ hanti jñānapradānena tam upendraṃ namāmy aham yasyākṣiṇī candrasūryau sarvalokaśubhāśubham paśyete karma satataṃ tam upendraṃ namāmy aham yasmin sarveśvare sarvaṃ satyam etan mayoditam nānṛtaṃ tam ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ namāmi prabhavāvyayam yathaitat satyam uktaṃ me bhūyaś cāto janārdanaḥ satyena tena sakalāḥ pūryantāṃ me manorathāḥ evaṃ stuto atha bhagavān vāsudeva uvāca tām adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tasyāḥ saṃdarśane sthitaḥ manorathāṃs tvam adite yān icchasy abhipūritān tāṃs tān prāpsyasi dharmajñe matprasādād asaṃśayam śṛṇuṣva ca mahābhāge varaṃ yas te hṛdi sthitaḥ taṃ prayacchāmi niyataṃ mātra kāryā vicāraṇā maddarśanaṃ hi viphalaṃ na kadācid bhaviṣyati yadi deva prasannas tvaṃ bhaktāyā bhaktavatsala trailokyādhipatiḥ putras tad astu mama vāsavaḥ hṛtarājyo hṛtaś cāsya yajñabhāgo mahāsuraiḥ tvayi prasanne varada taṃ prāpnotu suto mama hṛtaṃ rājyaṃ na duḥkhāya mama putrasya keśava sapatnād āyatibhraṃśo bādhāṃ naḥ kurute hṛdi kṛtaḥ prasādo hi mayā tava devi yathepsitaḥ svāṃśena caiva te garbhe saṃbhaviṣyāmi kaśyapāt tava garbhasamudbhūtaḥ sutas te ye surārayaḥ tān ahaṃ nihaniṣyāmi nirvṛtā bhava nandini prasīda devadeveśa namas te viśvabhāvana nāhaṃ tvām udareṇeśa voḍhuṃ śakṣyāmi keśava yasmin pratiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ yo viśvaṃ svayam īśvara tad ahaṃ nodareṇa tvāṃ voḍhuṃ śakṣyāmi durdharam satyam āttha mahābhāge mayi sarvam idaṃ jagat pratiṣṭhitaṃ na māṃ śaktā voḍhuṃ sendrā divaukasaḥ kintv ahaṃ sakalāṃl lokān sadevāsuramānuṣān jaṅgamājaṅgamaṃ sarvaṃ tvāṃ ca devi sakāśyapām dhārayiṣyāmi bhadraṃ te tava garbhaśayo adite na te glānir na te khedo garbhasthe bhavitā mayi dākṣāyaṇi prasādaṃ te karomy anyaiḥ sudurlabham garbhasthe mayi putrāṇāṃ tava yo arir bhaviṣyati tejasas tasya hāniṃ ca kariṣye mā vyathāṃ kṛtāḥ evam uktvā tataḥ sadyo gato antardhānam īśvaraḥ sāpi kālena taṃ garbham avāpa kurusattama garbhasthite tataḥ kṛṣṇe cacāla sakalā kṣitiḥ cakampire mahāśailā jagmuḥ kṣobham athābdhayaḥ yato yato aditir yāntī dadāti lalitaṃ padam tatas tataḥ kṣitiḥ khedān nanāma vasudhādhipa daityānām api sarveṣāṃ garbhasthe madhusūdane babhūva tejaso hānir yathoktaṃ parameṣṭhinā nistejaso asurān dṛṣṭvā samastān asureśvaraḥ prahrādam atha papraccha balir ātmapitāmaham tāta nistejaso daityā nirdagdhā iva vahninā kim ete sahasaivādya brahmadaṇḍahatā iva duriṣṭaṃ kiṃ nu daityānāṃ kiṃ kṛtyā vairinirmitā nāśāyaiṣāṃ samudbhūtā yena nistejaso asurāḥ ity āsuravaras tena pṛṣṭaḥ pautreṇa pārthiva ciraṃ dhyātvā jagādedam asurendraṃ tadā balim calanti girayo bhūmir jahāti sahajāṃ dhṛtim sadyaḥ samudrāḥ kṣubhitā daityā nistejasaḥ kṛtāḥ sūryādayo yathā pūrvaṃ tathā gacchanti na grahāḥ devānāṃ ca parā lakṣmīḥ kāraṇair anumīyate mahad etan mahābāho kāraṇaṃ dānaveśvara na hy alpam iti mantavyaṃ tvayā kāryaṃ surārdana ity uktvā dānavapatiṃ prahrādaḥ so asurottamaḥ atyantabhakto deveśaṃ jagāma manasā harim sa dhyānapathagaṃ kṛtvā prahrādaḥ svaṃ mano asuraḥ vicārayām āsa tato yato devo janārdanaḥ sa dadarśodare adityāḥ prahrādo vāmanākṛtim antaḥsthān bibhrataṃ sapta lokān ādiprajāpatim tad antaś ca vasūn rudrān aśvinau marutas tathā sādhyān viśve tathādityān gandharvoragarākṣasān virocanaṃ satanayaṃ baliṃ cāsuranāyakam jambhaṃ kujambhaṃ narakaṃ bāṇam anyāṃs tathāsurān ātmānam urvīgaganaṃ vāyum ambho hutāśanam samudrādridrumasarit- sarāṃsi paśavo mṛgān vayomanuṣyān akhilāṃs tathaiva ca sarīsṛpān samastalokasraṣṭāraṃ brahmāṇaṃ bhavam eva ca grahanakṣatratārāś ca dakṣādyāṃś ca prajāpatīn saṃpaśyan vismayāviṣṭaḥ prakṛtisthaḥ kṣaṇāt punaḥ prahrādaḥ prāha daityendraṃ baliṃ vairocaniṃ tadā vatsa jñātaṃ mayā sarvaṃ yadarthaṃ bhavatām iyam tejaso hānir utpannā tac chṛṇu tvam aśeṣataḥ devadevo jagadyonir ayonir jagadādikṛt anādir ādir viśvasya vareṇyo varado hariḥ parāparāṇāṃ paramaḥ paraḥ paravatām api prabhuḥ pramāṇaṃ mānānāṃ saptalokaguror guruḥ sthitiṃ kartuṃ jagannāthaḥ so adityā garbhatāṃ gataḥ prabhuḥ prabhūṇām paramaḥ parāṇām anādimadhyo bhagavān anantaḥ trailokyam aṃśena sanātham eṣa kartuṃ mahātmāditijo avatīrṇaḥ na yasya rudro na ca padmayonir nendro na sūryendumarīcimiśrāḥ jānanti daityādhipa yat svarūpaṃ sa vāsudevaḥ kalayāvatīrṇaḥ yo asau kalāṃśena nṛsiṃharūpī jaghāna pūrvaṃ pitaram aśeṣaḥ yaḥ sarvayogīśamanonivāsaḥ sa vāsudevaḥ kalayāvatīrṇaḥ yam akṣaraṃ vedavido viditvā viśanti taṃ jñānavidhūtapāpāḥ yasmin praviṣṭā na punar bhavanti taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇamāmi devam bhūtāny aśeṣāṇi yato bhavanti yathormayas toyanidher ajasram layaṃ ca yasmin pralaye prayānti taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇamāmy acintyam na yasya rūpaṃ na balaṃ prabhāvo na ca svabhāvaḥ paramasya puṃsaḥ vijñāyate sarvapitāmahādyais taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇamāmy acintyam rūpasya cakṣur grahaṇe tvag eṣā sparśagrahītrī rasanā rasasya śrotraṃ ca śabdagrahaṇe narāṇāṃ ghrāṇaṃ ca gandhagrahaṇe niyuktam na ghrāṇacakṣuḥśravaṇādibhir yaḥ sarveśvaro veditum avyayātmā śakyas tam īḍyaṃ manasaiva devaṃ grāhyaṃ nato ahaṃ harim īśitāram yenaikadaṃṣṭrāgrasamuddhṛteyaṃ dharācalā dhārayatīha sarvam grastvā sa śete sakalaṃ jagad yas tam īḍyam īśaṃ praṇato asmi viṣṇum aṃśāvatīrṇena ca yena garbhe hṛtāni tejāṃsi mahāsurāṇām namāmi taṃ devam anantam īśam aśeṣasaṃsārataroḥ kuṭhāram devo jagadyonir ayaṃ mahātmā sa ṣoḍaśāṃśena mahāsurendra surendramātur jaṭharaṃ praviṣṭo hṛtāni vas tena bale vapūṃṣi tāta ko ayaṃ harir nāma yato na bhayam āgatam santi me śataśo daityā vāsudevabalādhikāḥ vipracittiḥ śibiḥ śaṅkur ayaḥśaṅkus tathaiva ca ayaḥśirā aśvaśirā bhaṅgakāro mahāhanuḥ pratāpī praghasaḥ śaṃbhuḥ kurkurākṣaś ca durjayaḥ ete cānye ca me santi daiteyā dānavās tathā mahābalā mahāvīryā bhūbhāradharaṇakṣamāḥ yeṣām ekaikaśaḥ kṛṣṇo na vīryārdhena saṃmitaḥ pautrasyaitad vacaḥ śrutvā prahrādo daityapuṅgavaḥ dhig dhig ity āha sa baliṃ vaikuṇṭhākṣepavādinam vināśam upayāsyanti manye daiteyadānavāḥ yeṣāṃ tvam īdṛśo rājā durbuddhir avivekavān devadevaṃ mahābhāgaṃ vāsudevam ajaṃ vibhum tvām ṛte pāpasaṃkalpaṃ ko anya evaṃ vadiṣyati ya ete bhavatā proktāḥ samastā daityadānavāḥ sabrahmakās tathā devāḥ sthāvarāntāś ca bhūtayaḥ tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca jagac cedaṃ sādridrumanadīnadam samudradvīpalokāś ca yac ceṅgaṃ yac ca neṅgati yasyātivandyavandyasya vyāpinaḥ paramātmanaḥ ekāṃśāṃśakalājanma kas tam evaṃ pravakṣyati ṛte vināśābhimukhaṃ tvām ekam avivekinam durbuddhim ajitātmānaṃ vṛddhānāṃ śāsanātigam śocyo ahaṃ yasya vai gehe jātas tava pitādhamaḥ yasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putro devadevāvamanyakaḥ tiṣṭhatv anekasaṃsāra- saṃhṛtāghavināśanī kṛṣṇe bhaktir ahaṃ tāvad avekṣyo bhavato na kim na me priyataraḥ kṛṣṇād api deho ayam ātmanaḥ iti jānāty ayaṃ loko bhavāṃś ca ditijādhamaḥ jānann api priyataraṃ prāṇebhyo api hariṃ mama nindāṃ karoṣi ca katham akurvan gauravaṃ mama virocanas tava gurur gurus tasyāpy ahaṃ bale mamāpi sarvajagatāṃ gurur nārāyaṇo guruḥ nindāṃ karoṣi tasmiṃs tvaṃ kṛṣṇe guruguror gurau yasmāt tasmād ihaiśvaryād acirād bhraṃśam eṣyasi mā devo mā jagannātho bale māsau janārdanaḥ bhavatv aham avekṣyas te prītimān atra me guruḥ etāvanmātram apy atra nindatā jagato gurum nāpekṣitā vayaṃ yasmāt tasmāc chāpaṃ dadāmi te yathā me śirasaś chedād idaṃ gurutaraṃ bale tvayoktam acyutākṣepi rājyabhraṣṭas tathā pata yathā na kṛṣṇād aparaṃ paritrāṇaṃ bhavārṇave tathācireṇa paśyeyaṃ bhavantaṃ rājyavicyutam iti daityapatiḥ śrutvā guror vacanam apriyam prasādayām āsa guruṃ praṇipatya puṇaḥ punaḥ prasīda tāta mā kopaṃ kuru mohahate mayi balāvalepamattena mayaitad vākyam īritam mohopahatavijñānaḥ pāpo ahaṃ ditijottama yac chapto asmi durācāras tat sādhu bhavatā kṛtam rājyabhraṃśaṃ vasubhraṃśaṃ saṃprāpsyāmīti na tv aham viṣaṇṇo asmi yathā tāta tavaivāvinaye kṛte trailokyarājyam aiśvaryam anyad vā nātidurlabham saṃsāre durlabhās tāta guravo ye bhavadvidhāḥ tat prasīda na me kopaṃ kartum arhasi daityapa tvatkopahetuduṣṭo ahaṃ paritapye na śāpataḥ vatsa kopena moho me janitas tena te mayā śāpo datto vivekaś ca mohenāpahṛto mama yadi mohena me jñānaṃ nākṣiptaṃ syān mahāsura tat kathaṃ sarvagaṃ jñānan hariṃ kaṃcic chāpāmy aham yo ayaṃ śāpo mayā datto bhavato asurapuṅgava bhāvyam etena nūnaṃ te tasmāt tvaṃ mā viṣīdathāḥ adyaprabhṛti deveśe bhagavaty acyute harau bhavethā bhaktimān īśaḥ sa te trātā bhaviṣyati śāpaṃ prāpya ca māṃ vīra saṃsmarethāḥ smṛtas tvayā tathā tathā yatiṣyāmi śreyasā yokṣyate yathā evam uktvā sa daityendro virarāma mahāmatiḥ ajāyata sa govindo bhagavān vāmanākṛtiḥ avatīrṇe jagannāthe tasmin sarvam aśīśamat yad āsuram abhūd duḥkhaṃ devānām adites tathā vavur vātāḥ sukhasparśā nīrajaskam abhūn nabhaḥ dharme ca sarvabhūtānāṃ tadā matir ajāyata nodvegaś cāpy abhūd dehe manujānāṃ janeśvara tathā hi sarvabhūtānāṃ bhūmyambaradivaukasām taṃ jātamātraṃ bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ jātakarmādikāḥ kṛtvā kriyās tuṣṭāva pārthiva jayādyeśa jayājeya jaya sarvātmakātmaka jaya janmajarāpeta jayānanta jayācyuta jayājita jayāśeṣa jayāvyakta sthite jaya paramārthārtha sarvajña jñāna jñeyātmaniḥsṛta jayāśeṣajagatsākṣiñ jaya kartar jagadguroḥ jagato jagadante anta sthitau pālayitā jaya jayākhila jayāśeṣa jayākhilahṛdi sthita jayādimadhyāntamaya sarvajñānamayottama mumukṣubhir anirdeśya svayaṃdṛṣṭa jayeśvara yogibhir muktiphalada damādiguṇabhūṣaṇaiḥ jayātisūkṣma durjñeya jagat sthūla jaganmaya jaya sthūlātisūkṣma tvaṃ jayātīndriya sendriya jaya svamāyāyogastha śeṣabhogaśayākṣara jayaikadaṃṣṭrāprāntānta samuddhṛtavasuṃdhara nṛkesariñ jayārāti- vakṣaḥsthalavidāraṇa sāṃprataṃ jaya viśvātman māyāvāmana keśava nijamāyāpaṭacchanna jagaddhātar janārdana jayācintya jayāneka- svarūpaikavidha prabho vardhasva vardhitāneka- vikāraprakṛte hare tvayy eṣā jagatām īśa saṃsthitā dharmapaddhatiḥ na tvām ahaṃ na ceśāno nendrādyās tridaśā hare jñātum īśā na munayaḥ sanakādyā na yoginaḥ tvanmāyāpaṭasaṃvīte jagaty atra jagatpate kas tvāṃ vetsyati sarveśaṃ tvatprasādaṃ vinā naraḥ tvam evārādhito yasya prasādasumukhaḥ prabho sa eva kevalaṃ deva vetti tvāṃ netaro janaḥ tad īśvareśvareśāna vibho vardhasva bhāvana prabhāvāyāsya viśvasya viśvātman pṛthulocana evaṃ stuto hṛṣīkeśaḥ sa tadā vāmanākṛtiḥ prahasya bhāvagambhīram uvācābjasamudbhavam stuto ahaṃ bhavatā pūrvam indrādyaiḥ kaśyapena ca mayā ca vaḥ pratijñātam indrasya bhuvanatrayam bhūyaś cāhaṃ stuto adityā tasyāś cāpi pratiśrutam yathā śakrāya dāsyāmi trailokyaṃ hatakaṇṭakam so ahaṃ tathā kariṣyāmi yathendro jagataḥ patiḥ bhaviṣyati sahasrākṣaḥ satyam etad bravīmi te tataḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ brahmā hṛṣīkeśāya dattavān yajñopavītaṃ bhagavān dadau tasmai bṛhaspatiḥ āṣāḍham adadad daṇḍaṃ marīcir brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ kamaṇḍaluṃ vasiṣṭhaś ca kauśyaṃ vedam athāṅgirāḥ akṣasūtraṃ ca pulahaḥ pulastyaḥ sitavāsasī upatasthuś ca taṃ vedāḥ praṇavasvarabhūṣaṇāḥ śāstrāṇy aśeṣāṇi tathā sāṃkhyayogoktayaś ca yāḥ sa vāmano jaṭī daṇḍī chattrī dhṛtakamaṇḍaluḥ sarvadevamayo bhūpa baler adhvaram abhyayāt yatra yatra padaṃ bhūpa bhūbhāge vāmano dadau dadāti bhūmir vivaraṃ tatra tatrātipīḍitā sa vāmano jaḍagatir mṛdu gacchan saparvatām sābdhidvīpavatīṃ sarvāṃ cālayām āsa medinīm tataḥ saṃśayam āpannāḥ sarve daiteyadānavāḥ saparvatavanām urvīṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃkṣubhitāṃ baliḥ papracchośanasaṃ śukraṃ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ ācārya kṣobham āyāti sābdhibhūbhṛddharā mahī kasmāc ca nāsurān bhāgān pratigṛhṇanti vahnayaḥ iti pṛṣṭo atha balinā kāvyo vedavidāṃ varaḥ uvāca daityādhipatiṃ ciraṃ dhyātvā mahāmatiḥ avatīrṇo jagadyoniḥ kaśyapasya gṛhe hariḥ vāmaneneha rūpeṇa paramātmā sanātanaḥ sa nūnaṃ yajñam āyāti tava dānavapuṅgava tatpadanyāsavikṣobhād iyaṃ pracalitā mahī kampante girayaś cāmī kṣubhitā makarālayāḥ nainaṃ bhūtapatiṃ bhūmiḥ samarthā voḍhum īśvaram sadevāsuragandharva- yakṣarākṣasapannagā anenaiva dhṛtā bhūmir āpo agniḥ pavano nabhaḥ dhārayaty akhilān deva- manuṣyādīn mahāsura iyam asya jagaddhātur māyā kṛṣṇasya gahvarī dhāryadhārakabhāvena yayā saṃpiṇḍitaṃ jagat tatsaṃnidhānād asurā na bhāgārhāḥ suradviṣaḥ bhuñjate cāsurān bhāgān amī te na tavāgnayaḥ śukrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā hṛṣṭaromābravīd baliḥ dhanyo ahaṃ kṛtapuṇyaś ca yan me yajñapatiḥ svayam yajñam abhyāgato brahman mattaḥ ko anyo adhikaḥ pumān yaṃ yoginaḥ sadodyuktāḥ paramātmānam avyayam draṣṭum icchanti devo asau madadhvaram upaiṣyati hotā bhāgaprado yasya yam udgātā ca gāyati tam adhvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ mattaḥ ko anya upaiṣyati sarveśvareśvare viṣṇau mamādhvaram upāgate yan mayā cārya kartavyaṃ tan mamādeṣṭum arhasi yajñabhāgabhujo devā vedaprāmāṇyato asura tvayā tu dānavā daityā yajñabhāgabhujaḥ kṛtāḥ ayaṃ ca devaḥ sattvasthaḥ karoti sthitipālanam nisṛṣṭeś cāyam ante ca svayam atti prajāḥ prabhuḥ tvayānubandhī bhavitā nūnaṃ viṣṇuḥ sthitau sthitaḥ viditvaitan mahābhāga kuru yat te manogatam tvayāsya daityādhipate svalpake api hi vastuni pratijñā naiva voḍhavyā vācyaṃ sāma tathāphalam kṛtakṛtyasya devasya devārthaṃ caiva kurvataḥ nālaṃ dātuṃ dhanaṃ devety evaṃ vācyaṃ tu yācataḥ kṛṣṇasya devabhūtyarthaṃ pravṛttasya mahāsura brahman katham ahaṃ brūyām anyenāpi hi yācitaḥ nāstīti kimu devena saṃsārāghaughahāriṇā vratopavāsair vividhair yaḥ pratigrāhyate hariḥ sa ced vakṣyati dehīti govindaḥ kim ato adhikam yadartham upahārāḍhyā damaśaucaguṇānvitaiḥ yajñāḥ kriyante deveśaḥ sa māṃ dehīti vakṣyati tat sādhu sukṛtaṃ karma tapaḥ sucaritaṃ ca naḥ yan mayā dattam īśeśaḥ svayam ādāsyate hariḥ nāstīty ahaṃ guro vakṣye tam apy āgatam īśvaram yadi tad vañcyate prāpte nūnam asmadvidhaḥ phalaiḥ yajñe asmin yadi yajñeśo yācate māṃ janārdanaḥ nijamūrdhānam apy adya tad dāsyāmy avicāritam nāstīti yan mayā noktam anyeṣām api yācatām vakṣyāmi katham āyāte tad anabhyastam acyute ślāghya eva hi dhīrāṇāṃ dānād āpatsamāgamaḥ nābādhākāri yad dānaṃ tad aṅgamalavat katham madrājye nāsukhī kaścin na daridro na cāturaḥ nātṛṣito na codvigno na sragādivivarjitaḥ hṛṣṭatuṣṭaḥ sugandhī ca tṛptaḥ sarvasukhānvitaḥ janaḥ sarvo mahābhāga kimutāhaṃ sadā sukhī etad viśiṣṭapātrotthaṃ dānabījaphalaṃ mama viditaṃ bhṛguśārdūla mayaitat tvatprasādataḥ etad vijānato dāna- bījaṃ patati ced guro janārdane mahāpātre kiṃ na prāptaṃ tato mayā matto dānam avāpyeśo yadi puṣṇāti devatāḥ upabhogānvayaguṇaṃ dānaṃ ślāghyataraṃ tataḥ matprasādaparo nūnaṃ yajñenārādhito hariḥ tenābhyeti na saṃdeho darśanād upakārakṛt atha kopena vābhyeti devabhāgoparodhinam māṃ nihantum ato api syād vadhaḥ ślāghyataro acyutāt yanmayaṃ sarvam evedaṃ nāprāpya yasya vidyate sa māṃ yācitum abhyeti nānugraham ṛte hariḥ yaḥ sṛjaty ātmabhūḥ sarvaṃ cetasaivāpahanti ca sa māṃ hantuṃ hṛṣīkeśaḥ kathaṃ yatnaṃ kariṣyati etad viditvā tu guro dānavighnapareṇa me naiva bhāvyaṃ jagannāthe govinde samupasthite ity evaṃ vadatas tasya prāptas tatra jagapatiḥ sarvadevamayo acintyo māyāvāmanarūpadhṛk taṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭāntaḥ- praviṣṭam asurāḥ prabhum jagmuḥ prabhāvataḥ kṣobhaṃ tejasā tasya niṣprabhāḥ jepuś ca munayas tatra ye sametā mahādhvare baliś caivākhilaṃ janma mene saphalam ātmanaḥ tataḥ saṃkṣobham āpanno na kaścit kiṃcid uktavān pratyeko devadeveśaṃ pūjayām āsa cetasā athāsurapatiṃ prahvaṃ dṛṣṭvā munivarāṃś ca tān devadevapatiḥ sākṣād viṣṇur vāmanarūpadhṛk tuṣṭāva yajñaṃ vahniṃś ca yajamānam atha rtvijaḥ yajñakarādhikārasthān sadasyān dravyasaṃpadam tataḥ prasannam akhilaṃ vāmanaṃ prati tatkṣaṇāt yajñavāṭasthitaṃ vīraṃ sādhu sādhv ity udīrayan sa cārgham ādāya baliḥ prodbhūtapulakas tadā pūjayām āsa govindaṃ prāha cedaṃ vaco asuraḥ suvarṇaratnasaṃghātaṃ gajāśvam amitaṃ tathā striyo vastrāṇy alaṃkārān gāvo grāmāṃś ca puṣkalān sarvasvaṃ sakalām urvīṃ bhavato vā yad īpsitam tad dadāmi vṛṇuṣva tvaṃ mamārthī satataṃ priyaḥ ity ukto daityapatinā prītigarvānvitaṃ vacaḥ prāha sasmitagambhīraṃ bhagavān vāmanākṛtiḥ mamāgniśaraṇārthāya dehi rājan padatrayam suvarṇagrāmaratnādi tad arthibhyaḥ pradīyatām tribhiḥ prayojanaṃ kiṃ te padaiḥ padavatāṃ vara śataṃ śatasahasraṃ vā padānāṃ mārgatāṃ bhavān etāvatā daityapate kṛtakṛtyo asmi mārgatām anyeṣām arthināṃ vittam icchayā dāsyate bhavān etac chrutvā tu gaditaṃ vāmanasya mahātmanaḥ vācayām āsa tat tasmai vāmanāya padatrayam pāṇau tu patite toye vāmano bhūtabhāvanaḥ sarvadevamayaṃ rūpaṃ darśayām āsa tatkṣaṇāt candrasūryau ca nayane dyauḥ śiraś caraṇau kṣitiḥ pādāṅgulyaḥ piśācāś ca hastāṅgulyaś ca guhyakāḥ viśvedevāś ca jānusthā jaṅghe sādhyāḥ surottamāḥ yakṣā nakheṣu saṃbhūtā rekhāsv apsarasaḥ sthitāḥ dṛṣṭir dhiṣṇāny aśeṣāṇi keśāḥ sūryāṃśavaḥ prabho tārakā romakūpāṇi romāṇi ca maharṣayaḥ bāhavo vidiśas tasya diśaḥ śrotraṃ mahātmanaḥ aśvinau śravaṇau tasya nāsā vāyur mahābalaḥ prasādaś candramā devo mano dharmaḥ samāśritaḥ satyam asyābhavad vāṇī jihvā devī sarasvatī grīvāditir devamātā vidyās tadvalayas tathā svargadvāram abhūn maitraṃ tvaṣṭā pūṣā ca vai bhruvau mukhaṃ vaiśvānaraś cāsya vṛṣaṇau tu prajāpatiḥ hṛdayaṃ ca paraṃ brahma puṃstvaṃ vai kaśyapo muniḥ pṛṣṭhe asya vasavo devā marutaḥ sarvasaṃdhiṣu sarvasūktāni daśanā jyotīṃṣi vimalaprabhāḥ vakṣaḥsthale tathā rudro dhairye cāsya mahārṇavaḥ udare cāsya gandharvā marutaś ca mahābalāḥ lakṣmīr medhā dhṛtiḥ kāntiḥ sarvavidyāś ca vai kaṭiḥ sarvajyotīṃṣi yānīha tapaś ca paramaṃ mahat tasya devātidevasya tejaḥ prodbhūtam uttamam stanau kukṣau ca vedāś ca jānū cāsya mahāmakhāḥ iṣṭayaḥ paśubandhāś ca dvijānāṃ ceṣṭitāni ca tasya devamayaṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṇor mahābalāḥ upasarpanti daiteyāḥ pataṃgā iva pāvakam pramathya sarvān asurān pādahastatalair vibhuḥ kṛtvā rūpaṃ mahākāyaṃ sa jahārāśu medinīm tasya vikramato bhumiṃ candrādityau stanāntare nabho vikramamāṇasya sakthideśe sthitāv ubhau paraṃ vikramamāṇasya jānumūle prabhākarau viṣṇor āstām mahīpāla devapālanakarmaṇi jitvā lokatrayaṃ kṛtsnaṃ hatvā cāsurapuṅgavān puraṃdarāya trailokyaṃ dadau viṣṇur urukramaḥ sutalaṃ nāma pātālam adhastād vasudhātalāt baler dattaṃ bhagavatā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā atha daityeśvaraṃ prāha viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ yat tvayā salilaṃ dattaṃ gṛhītaṃ pāṇinā mayā kalpapramāṇaṃ tasmāt te bhaviṣyaty āyur uttamam vaivasvate tathātīte bale manvantare tataḥ sāvarṇake ca saṃprāpte bhavān indro bhaviṣyati sāṃprataṃ devarājāya trailokyam akhilaṃ mayā dattaṃ caturyugānāṃ vai sādhikā hy ekasaptatiḥ niyantavyā mayā sarve ye tasya paripanthinaḥ tenāhaṃ parayā bhaktyā pūrvam ārādhito bale sutalaṃ nāma pātālaṃ tam āsādya manoramam vasāsura mamādeśaṃ yathāvat paripālayan tatra divyavanopete prāsādaśatasaṃkule protphullapadmasarasi sravacchuddhasaridvare sugandhidhūpasaṃbādhe varābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ srakcandanādidigdhāṅgo nṛtyagītamanoramaiḥ upabhuñjan mahābhogān vividhān dānaveśvara mamājñayā kālam imaṃ tiṣṭha strīśatasaṃvṛtaḥ yāvat suraiś ca vipraiś ca na virodhaṃ kariṣyasi tāvad etān mahābhogān avāpsyasy asurottama yadā ca devaviprāṇāṃ viruddhāny ācariṣyasi bandhiṣyanti tathā pāśā vāruṇās tvām asaṃśayam etad viditvā bhavatā mayājñaptam aśeṣataḥ na virodhaḥ suraiḥ kāryo viprair vā daityasattama ity evam ukto devena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā baliḥ prāha mahārāja praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ tatrāsato me pātāle bhagavan bhavadājñayā kiṃ bhaviṣyaty upādānam upabhogopapādakam āpyāyito yena deva smareyaṃ tvām ahaṃ sadā dānāny avidhidattāni śrāddhāny aśrotriyāṇi ca hutāny aśraddhayā yāni tāni dāsyanti te phalam adakṣiṇās tathā yajñāḥ kriyāś cāvidhinā kṛtāḥ phalāni tava dāsyanti adhītāny avratāni ca baler varam idaṃ dattvā śakrāya trividaṃ tathā vyāpinā tena rūpeṇa jagāmādarśanaṃ hariḥ śaśāsa ca yathā pūrvam indras trailokyam ūrjitam siṣeva ca parān kāmān baliḥ pātālam āśritaḥ ity etad devadevasya viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam vāmanasya paṭhed yas tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate baliprahrādasaṃvādaṃ mantritaṃ baliśukrayoḥ baliviṣṇvoś ca kathitaṃ yaḥ smariṣyati mānavaḥ nādhayo vyādhayo vāsya na ca mohākulaṃ manaḥ bhaviṣyati kuruśreṣṭha puṃsas tasya kadācana cyutarājyo nijaṃ rājyam iṣṭaprāptiṃ viyogavān avāpnoti mahābhāga naraḥ śrutvā kathām imām pātāle nivasan vīras tadā vairocanir baliḥ kāmopabhogasaṃprāptyā mudaṃ prāpa parāṃ vibhuḥ alaṃbuṣā miśrakeśī puṇḍarīkātha vāmanā ghṛtācī menakā rambhā nanṛtus tasya saṃnidhau prajagur devagandharvā viśvāvasupurogamāḥ tuṣṭuvuś ca mahābhāga baliṃ siddhāḥ sacāraṇāḥ tasmin saṃgītagītā tu vīṇāveṇuravākule sragādibhūṣito daityaḥ papau pānam anuttamam śarkārasavamādhvikāṃ puṣpāsavaphalāsavam divyāḥ prasannāś ca surās tadarhāṇi madhūni ca parāvadaṃśān madhurāṃl lavaṇāṃs tiktakāṇ kaṭūn kaṣāyāṃś ca mahārāja sumṛṣṭāny aparāṇi ca suhṛṭsujanasaṃbandhi- bhṛtyavargasamanvitaḥ bubhuje pātālagatas tadā vairocanir baliḥ prāsādāḥ kāñcanāḥ sarve suvarṇamaṇimaṇḍitāḥ sphāṭikāmalasopānā muktāhāraśatojjvalāḥ teṣu sarveṣu daiteyā baleḥ saṃbandhibāndhavāḥ nṛtyavādyādimuditā bubhujur viṣayān priyān baliś ca bhagavān daityo daityoragaśatair vṛtaḥ upagīyamāno bubhuje yatheṣṭaṃ viṣayān priyān patnī vindhyāvalī nāma tasya daityapater abhūt sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā śrīr ivābjaṃ vināparā na devī nāpi gandharvī nāpsarā na ca mānuṣī tasyā rūpeṇa sadṛśī babhūva manujeśvara sā tu pīnāyataśroṇī mṛdvaṅgī madhurasvarā ghanonnatakucā subhrūḥ sasmitāyatalocanā mṛdvalpapāṇipādābjā sumadhyā gajagāminī sukeśī sumukhī śyāmā sarvair yoṣidguṇair yutā tanayā merusāvarṇer dauhitrī mṛgamokinaḥ vapuṣā rūpasaṃpadā pautanā mṛgalocanā patnī sahasradvitaye pradhānā tasya sābhavat tayā tu ramatas tasya ramaṇīye rasātale śaktir āsīd anudinaṃ vivekapratilominī kadācid ramatas tasya daityarājasya pārthiva tīkṣṇāṃśur madhyamāṃ vīthīṃ yayau vaiṣuvatīṃ raviḥ yadā yadā ca viṣuvaṃ bhāskaraḥ pratipadyate tadā tadā hareś cakraṃ pātāle parivartate sravanti yoṣitāṃ garbhās tasya dhārāṃśutāpitāḥ sahasā daityapatnīnāṃ yāsu puṃsāṃ samudbhavaḥ nistejaso daityabhaṭā bhavanti ca mahīpate tad dṛṣṭvā sahasāyāntam ādityaśatatejasam jvālāmālāsuduḥprekṣyaṃ viṣṇucakraṃ sudarśanam hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvaṃ pātālam arisūdana jepur ye munayas tatra sārghapātrā mahoragāḥ babhūvuḥ praṇatāś cānye siddhagandharvacāraṇāḥ vaiklavyaṃ cāgatāḥ sarvāḥ striyaḥ parapuraṃjaya tad dṛṣṭvā vyākulībhūtaṃ pātālam asurās tataḥ ye tasthuḥ pauruṣaparās te hatāḥ śataneminā bhrāmyatā tena cakreṇa saptalokavicāriṇā samastajagadādhāra- karamuktena veginā tan niṣūditadaityaughaṃ daityastrīgarbhahānidam śrutvā cakraṃ mahācakro niścakrāma gṛhād baliḥ āḥ kim etad itīty uktvā sa tu madyamahoddhataḥ vimalaṃ khaḍgam ādāya śatacandraṃ ca bhānumat niryāntam atha vegena tam udāraparākramam vidhyāvalī nāma śubhā dadhāra dayitaṃ patim uvāca ca pariṣvajya krodhatāmrekṣaṇaṃ balim kalyāṇī guṇadoṣajñā praṇayān mṛdubhāṣiṇī daityarāja na kopasya vaśam āgantum arhasi vimṛśya tajjñaḥ sāmādīn prayuñjīta balābalam kim etat kasya vā kutra kiṃnimittam ihāgatam cakram itthaṃ vicārya tvaṃ krodhaṃ yāhi praśāmya vā etat kila jagaddhātuś cakraṃ viṣṇoḥ sudarśanam pratiṣaṇmāsam abhyeti daityagarbhavināśanam puṅgarbhān nikhilān etad dānavānāṃ mahāsura vināśayaty anantarāṃ sarvaduṣṭanibarhaṇam karoti duḥkham atulaṃ ghātanāt pratipakṣajam puruṣāṇāṃ na sarvatra saṃsthitā jagataḥ pateḥ mayi tvayi tathānyatra yathā viṣṇur vyavasthitaḥ tasyaitac cakram āyāntaṃ puruṣaḥ ko na pūjayet yasyādhikṣepajā rājaṃs tava trailokyavicyutiḥ tasya cakraṃ jaganmūrteḥ samupaiṣi ruṣā katham sadṛśe puruṣe krodhaṃ naraḥ kurvīta daityapa na tu sarveśvare viṣṇau yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam tat prasīda mahābhāga samupaihi jagatpatim śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ yaṃ praṇamya na sīdati yasmin prasanne trailokyaṃ tvattaḥ prāptaḥ śacīpatiḥ bhraṣṭaś ca yadadhikṣepāt taṃ tvaṃ śaraṇam āvraja yatra sarveśvare sarvaṃ sarvabhūte jagat sthitam tasya cakram upaihi tvaṃ vinayād asurādhipa sarvakāraṇabhūtasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ kaś cakram ativarteta martyadharmā mahāsura cakram atra jagaddhātuḥ karoti sthitipālanam vipakṣāsurasaṃbhūti- garbhavisraṃsanāt prabho prasādya cakranāmānaṃ govindaṃ jagato gurum śreyase sarvadharmajña śaraṇaṃ vraja keśavam saṃsmarasva ca daityendra prahrādaṃ svapitāmaham bhraṣṭarājyena bhavatā smartavyo aham iti prabho sa vyājahāra bhagavāṃs tavānugrahakāmyayā saṃsmaryatāṃ mahābhāga sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ viṣṇubhakto mahābāhuḥ sa te śreyo abhidhāsyati etad vacanam ākarṇya tadā vairocanir baliḥ yayau tadārgham ādāya viṣṇoś cakrasya pūjakaḥ sa dadarśa samāyāntam anantakarasaṅginam cakram akṣayacakrasya viśvasya paripālakam sasmāra ca baliḥ sarvaṃ prahrādavacanaṃ nṛpa jagāda yac ca govindaḥ prasādasumukhaḥ prabhuḥ bhaktinamras tato bhūtvā bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhoḥ tuṣṭāva vāsudevasya cakram avyaktamūrtinaḥ jvālāmālākarālāntam udyadindusamaprabham madhyāhnārkasamābhāsaṃ tejasaḥ piṇḍasaṃsthitam taṃ dṛṣṭvā tejasā rāśim upasaṃgamya cā vibhum uvāca daityaśārdūlaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ anantasyāprameyasya viśvamūrter mahātmanaḥ namāmi cakriṇaś cakraṃ karasaṅgi sudarśanam sahasram iva sūryāṇāṃ saṃghātaṃ vidyutām iva kālāgnim iva yac cakraṃ tad viṣṇoḥ praṇamāmy aham duṣṭarāhugalaccheda- śoṇitāruṇatārakam tan namāmi hareś cakraṃ śatanemi sudarśanam yasyārakeṣu śakrādyā lokapālā vyavasthitāḥ tadantar vasavo rudrās tathaiva marutāṃ gaṇāḥ dhārāyāṃ dvādaśādityāḥ samastāś ca hutāśanāḥ dhārājāle abdhayaḥ sarve nābhimadhye prajāpatiḥ samastanemiṣv akhilā yasya vidyāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ yasya rūpam anirdeśyam api yogibhir uttamaiḥ yad bhramat surasaṅghānāṃ tejasaḥ paribṛṃhaṇam daityaujasāṃ ca nāśāya tan namāmi sudarśanam bhraman matamahāvega- vibhrāntākhilakhecaram tan namāmi hareś cakram anantāraṃ sudarśanam nakṣatravadvahnikaṇa- vyāptaṃ kṛtsnaṃ nabhastalam tan namāmi hareś cakraṃ karasaṅgi sudarśanam svabhāvatejasā yuktaṃ yad arkāgnimayaṃ mahat viśeṣato harer gatvā sarvadevamayaṃ karam durvṛttadaityamathanaṃ jagataḥ paripālakam tan namāmi hareś cakraṃ daityacakraharaṃ param karotu me sadā śarma dharmatāṃ ca prayātu me prasādasumukhe kṛṣṇe tasya cakraṃ sudarśanam svabhāvatejasā yuktaṃ madhyāhnārkasamaprabham prasīda saṃyuge ariṇāṃ sudarśanasudarśanam vidyujjvālāmahākakṣaṃ dahāntar mama yat tamaḥ jahi no viṣayagrāhi mano grahaviceṣṭitam visphoṭayākhilāṃ māyāṃ kuruṣva vimalāṃ matim evaṃ saṃsthūyamānaṃ tad vahnipiṇḍopamaṃ mahat babhūva prakaṭaṃ cakraṃ daityacakrpates tadā dadarśa sa mahābāhuḥ prabhāmaṇḍaladurdṛśam agnijvālāgataṃ tāmraṃ taptacakram ivāparam bhramatas tasya cakrasya nābhimadhye mahīpate trailokyam akhilaṃ daityo dṛṣṭavān bhūrbhuvādikam mervādīn akhilāñ śailān gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathā kṣīrābdhipramukhāṃś cābdhīn dvīpāñ jambvādisaṃjñitān vaimānikān sagandharvān sūryādīṃś ca tathā grahān nakṣatratārakākāśaṃ śakrādīṃś ca divaukasaḥ rudrādityāṃś ca marutāṃ sādhyānāṃ ca mahīpate saṃnidhānaṃ nirīkṣyāsau daityānāṃ vismito abhavat tataḥ praṇamyārtiharaṃ surāṇām apārasāraṃ paramāyudhaṃ hareḥ namo namas te astv iti daityarājaḥ provāca bhūyo api namo namas te yan no aśubhaṃ cetasi vāyuvega yan no aśubhaṃ vāci hutāśanottha yac cāśubhaṃ kāyakṛtaṃ hares tad varāyudhaṃ tvaṃ praśamaṃ nayāśu prasīda satkārakṛtaṃ mamāghaṃ prayātu te nāśam anantavīrya satāṃ ca sanmārgavatāṃ manāṃsi sthirībhavantv acyutapādayugme evaṃ stute tatas tasmin viṣṇucakre sudarśane puṣpavṛṣṭir baler mūrdhni nipapātāntarikṣataḥ parihṛtya ca daityendraṃ yayau cakraṃ yathecchayā bhramad eva ca daityānāṃ yayau tadbhayam āvahat tatas tad adbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakrasyāgamanaṃ hareḥ pūrvavatsmaraṇaṃ prāpya sasmāra svapitāmaham gacchatā pūrvam āryeṇa smartavyo aham itīritam taṃ smariṣyāmi daityendraṃ sa naḥ śreyo abhidhāsyati ity etad adhisaṃsmṛtya balir ātmapitāmaham sasmāra daityādhipatiṃ prahrādaṃ bhagavatpriyam saṃsmṛtaś ca sa pātālam ājagāma mahāmatiḥ cakrodyatakaraḥ sākṣād bhagavān iva keśavaḥ tam āgatam athotthāya yathāvat sa mahāmatiḥ abhivādya balir bhaktyā nivedyārgham abhāṣata tātāṃhridarśanād adya pāvito asmy apakalmaṣaḥ divaś cyuto apy ahaṃ manye śakrād ātmānam uttamam trailokyaharaṇād ugraṃ yad duḥkhaṃ hṛdaye mama tac chāntaṃ pādasaṃparkam upetya bhavato mama iti saṃstūya dattvā ca varāsanam udāradhīḥ paryupāsata rājendro daityānāṃ svapitāmaham tam upāsīnam anaghaḥ prahrādo daityapuṅgavaḥ pratyuvāca mahātmānaṃ baliṃ vairocaniṃ nṛpa bale brūhi yadarthaṃ te smṛto aham arisūdana tavopakāraṇe viddhi dharme māṃ satatodyatam tātenāhaṃ purā jñapto bhraṣṭarājyena te bale saṃsmartavyo asmy asaṃdigdhaṃ śreyo vakṣyāmy ahaṃ tadā so ahaṃ rājyaparibhraṣṭo viṣayāsaktihṛṣitaḥ indriyair avaśas tāta yat kāryaṃ tat praśādhi mām yadi mad-vacanaṃ tāta śraddhadhāsi hitaṃ bale taṃ devadevam anaghaṃ prayāhi śaraṇaṃ harim śabdādiṣv anuraktāni tavākṣāṇy asurādhipa śabdādayaś ca govinde santy eva vyavahārataḥ gītakair gīyatāṃ viṣṇur manohāribhir ātmanaḥ anyālambanataś cittam ākṛṣyādhatsva keśave gandhān udārān bhakṣāṃś ca srajo vāsāṃsi cāsura prayaccha devadevāya taccheṣāṇy upayuñja ca yatra yatra ca te prītir viṣaye ditijeśvara tat tam acyutam uddiśya viprebhyaḥ pratipādaya sarvabhūteṣu govindo bahurūpo vyavasthitaḥ iti matvā mahābāho sarvabhūtahito bhava ātmānam acyutaṃ viddhi śatruṃ ca ripum ātmanaḥ itijñānavataḥ kopas tava kutra bhaviṣyati śabdādayo ye viṣayā viṣayī yaś ca puruṣaḥ tad aśeṣaṃ vijānīhi svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ paramātmā ca bhagavān viṣvakseno janārdanaḥ tadbhaktimān bhāgavato nālpapuṇyo hi jāyate bhagavacchāsanālambī bhagavacchāsanapriyaḥ bhagavadbhaktim āsthāya vatsa bhāgavato bhava bhagavān bhūtakṛd bhavyo bhūtānāṃ prabhavo hi yaḥ bhāvena taṃ bhajasveśaṃ bhavabhaṅgakaraṃ harim bhajasva bhāvena vibhuṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram tato bhāgavato bhūtvā bhavabandhād vimokṣyase sarvabhūte manas tasmin samādhāya mahāmate prāpsyase paramāhlāda- kāriṇīṃ paramāṃ gatim yatrānandaparaṃ jñānaṃ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitam tatra cittaṃ samāveṣṭuṃ na śaknoti bhavān yadi tadabhyāsaparas tasmin kuru yogaṃ divāniśam tatrāpy asāmarthyavataḥ kriyāyogo mahātmanā brahmaṇā yaḥ samākhyātas tanmanāḥ satataṃ bhava karoṣi yāni karmāṇi tāni deve jagatpatau samarpayasva bhadraṃ te tataḥ karma prahāsyasi kṣīṇakarmā mahābāho śubhāśubhavivarjitaḥ layam abhyeti govinde tad brahma paramaṃ mahat bhoktum icchasi daityendra karmaṇām atha cet phalam tatas tam arcayeśeśaṃ tataḥ karmaphalodayaḥ yo artham icchati daityendra sa samārādhya keśavam niḥsaṃśayam avāpnoti dhundhumāro yathā nṛpaḥ atrigehasamudbhūtaṃ dattātreyasvarūpiṇam rājyam ārādhya govindaṃ kārtavīryas tathāptavān dharmaṃ kṛṣṇaprasādena mudgalo jājaliḥ kuṇiḥ prāpur anye tathā kāmān narendrā nahuṣādayaḥ janakaḥ sudhvajo nāma janakaḥ samitidhvajaḥ dharmadhvajas tathā muktiṃ keśavārādhanād gataḥ tathānye munayo daitya rājānaś ca sahasraśaḥ prāpur muktiṃ mahābhāgāḥ kṛtvā bhaktiṃ janārdane yathā hi jvalito vahnis tamohāniṃ tadarthinām śītahāniṃ tathānyeṣāṃ svedaṃ svedābhilāṣiṇām karoti kṣudhitānāṃ ca bhojyapākaṃ tathotkaṭam tathaiva kāmān bhūteśaḥ sa dadāti yathepsitān tad etad akhilaṃ jñātvā yat taveṣṭaṃ śṛṇuṣva tat kalpadrumād iva harer yat te manasi vartate etat prahrādavacanaṃ niśāmya ditijeśvaraḥ pratyuvāca mahābhāgaṃ praṇipatya pitāmaham saṃprāptasyāmṛtasyeva tava vākyasya nāsti me tṛptir etad ahaṃ tāta śrotum icchāmi vistarāt akṣīṇakarmā puruṣo maraṇe samupasthite kīdṛśaṃ lokam āyāti yaḥ saṃsmarati keśavam yathā ca vāsudevasya smaraṇaṃ tāta mānavaiḥ mumūrṣubhiḥ prakartavyaṃ tan mamācakṣva vistarāt kiṃ japyaṃ kīdṛśaṃ rūpaṃ smartavyaṃ ca hares tadā kathaṃ dhyeyaṃ ca vidvadbhis tad ācakṣva yathātatham sādhu vatsa tvayā praśnaḥ suguhyo ayam udāhṛtaḥ tapasāṃ tāta sarveṣāṃ tapo nānaśanāt param kathyate ca mahābāho saṃvādo ayaṃ purātanaḥ bhagīrathasya rājarṣer brahmaṇaś ca prajāpateḥ atītyāmaralokaṃ ca gavāṃ lokaṃ ca mānada ṛṣilokaṃ ca yo agacchad bhagīratha iti śrutaḥ taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa vacaḥ prāha brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ kathaṃ bhagīrathāgās tvam imaṃ deśaṃ durāsadam na hi devā na gandharvā na manuṣyā bhagīratha āyānty ataptatapasaḥ kathaṃ vai tvam ihāgataḥ niḥśaṅkam annam adadaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śataṃ sahasrāṇi sadaiva dāyam brāhmaṇaṃ vrataṃ nityam āsthāya vidvan na tv evāhaṃ tasya phalād ihāgām daśaikarātrān daśa pañcarātrān ekādaśaikādaśakāṃs tathaiva jyotiṣṭomānāṃ ca śataṃ yad iṣṭaṃ phalena tenāpi na cāgato aham yac cāvasaṃ jāhnavītīranityaḥ śataṃ samās tapyamānas tapo aham pradāya tatrāśvatarīsahasraṃ phalena tasyāpi na cāgato aham daśa dhenusahasrāṇi maṇiratnavibhūṣitāḥ daśārbudāni cāśvānām ayutāni ca viṃśatiḥ puṣkareṣu dvijātibhyaḥ prādāṃ gāś ca sahasraśaḥ suvarṇacandrottamadhāriṇīnāṃ kanyottamānām adadaṃ sragviṇīnām ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrāṇi vibhūṣitānāṃ jāmbūnadair ābharaṇair na tena daśārbudāny adadaṃ gosave yās tv ekaikaśo daśa gā lokanātha samānavatsāḥ payasā samanvitāḥ suvarṇakāṃsyopaduhā na tena ahany ahani vipreṣu ekaikaṃ triṃśato adadam gṛṣṭīnāṃ kṣīradātrīṇāṃ rohiṇīnāṃ śatāni ca dogdhrīṇāṃ vai gavāṃ caiva prayutāni daśaiva tu prādāṃ daśaguṇaṃ brahman na ca tenāham āgataḥ koṭīś ca kāñcanasyāṣṭau prādāṃ brahman daśa tv aham ekaikasmin kratau tena phalenāhaṃ na cāgataḥ vājināṃ śyāmakarṇānāṃ haritānāṃ pitāmaha prādāṃ hemasrajāṃ brahman koṭīr daśa ca sapta ca īṣādantān mahākāyān kāñcanasragvibhūṣitān patnīvataḥ sahasrāṇi prāyacchaṃ daśa sapta ca alaṃkṛtānāṃ deveśa divyaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ rathānāṃ kāñcanāṅgānāṃ sahasrāṇy adadaṃ daśa sapta cānyāni yuktānāṃ vājibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ dakṣiṇāvayavāḥ kecid devair ye saṃprakīrtitāḥ vājapeyeṣu daśasu prādāṃ tenāpi nāgataḥ śakratulyaprabhāvānām ījyayā vikrameṇa ca sahasraṃ niṣkakaṇṭhānāṃ pradadan dakṣiṇām aham vijitya nṛpatīn sarvān makhair iṣṭvā pitāmaha aṣṭābhyo rājasūyebhyo na ca tenāham āgataḥ srotaś ca yāvad gaṅgāyāṃ chinnam āsīj jagatpate dakṣiṇābhiḥ pravṛttābhir mama nāgaṃ ca tatkṛte vājināṃ ca sahasre dve suvarṇamaṇibhūṣite vāraṇānāṃ śataṃ cāham ekaikasya tridhādadam varaṃ grāmaśataṃ cāham ekaikasya tridhādadam tapasvī niyatāhāraḥ śamam āsthāya vāgyataḥ dīrghakālaṃ himavati gaṅgāyāś ca durutsahām mūrdhnā dhārāṃ mahādevaḥ śirasā yām adhārayat na tenāpy aham āgacchaṃ phaleneha pitāmaha śamyākṣepair ayajaṃ devadeva tathā kratūnām ayutaiś cāpi yattaḥ trayodaśadvādaśāhaiś ca deva sapuṇḍarīkair na ca teṣāṃ phalena aṣṭau sahasrāṇi kakudminām ahaṃ śuklarṣabhāṇām adaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ patnīś caiṣām adadaṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīs teṣāṃ phaleneha na cāgato asmi hiraṇyaratnaracitān adadaṃ ratnaparvatān dhanadhānyasahasrāṃś ca grāmāñ śatasahasraśaḥ śataṃ śatānāṃ gṛṣṭīnām adadaṃ cāpy atandritaḥ iṣṭvānekair mahāyajñair brāhmaṇebhyo dhanena ca ekādaśāhair ayajaṃ sudakṣiṇair dvir dvādaśāhair aśvamedhaiś ca deva bṛhadbhir dvādaśāhaiś ca aśvamedhaiḥ pitāmaha arkāyaṇaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiś ca brahmaṃs teṣāṃ phaleneha na cāgato asmi niṣkrāmakaṃ cāpy adadaṃ yojanānāṃ dvir vistīrṇaṃ kāñcanapādapānām vanaṃ cūtānāṃ ratnavibhūṣitānām na caiva teṣām āgato ahaṃ phalena turāyaṇaṃ tu vratam apradhṛṣyam akrodhano akaravaṃ triṃśato abdān śataṃ gavām aṣṭa śatāni cāhaṃ dine dine prādadaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ payasvinīnāṃ atha rohiṇīnāṃ tathaiva cāpy anaḍuhāṃ lokanātha prādām nityaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sureśa nehāgatas tena phalena cāham triṃśataṃ vidhivad vahnīn ayajaṃ yac ca nityaśaḥ aṣṭābhiḥ sarvamedhaiś ca nṛmedhair dviguṇais tathā daśabhir viśvajidbhiś ca stobhair aṣṭādaśottaraiḥ na caiva teṣāṃ deveśa phalenāham ihāgamam saravyāṃ bāhudāyāṃ ca gayāyām atha naimiṣe gavāṃ śatānām ayutam adadaṃ na ca tena vai utkrāntikāle govindaṃ smarann anaśanasthitaḥ tyaktavān asmi yad dehaṃ tenedṛk prāptavān phalam evam etad itīty āha brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ bhagīrathaṃ mahīpālaṃ puṇyalokanivāsinam tad etad uktaṃ tapasāṃ samastānāṃ mahāmate guṇair anaśanaṃ brahmā pradhānataram abravīt tyajaty anaśanastho hi prāṇān yaḥ saṃsmaran harim sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa atītānāgatānīha kulāni puruṣarṣabha punāty anaśanaṃ kurvan sapta sapta ca sapta ca ślokāś cātra mahābāho śrūyante yān bhagīrathaḥ jagāda brahmaṇo lokam upetaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ brahma brahmamayaṃ viṣṇor yaḥ padaṃ paramātmanaḥ saṃsmaraṃs tyajati prāṇān sa viṣṇuṃ praviśaty ajam yaḥ kṣīṇakarmā bhogena tapasā vāpi saṃsmaran karoti kālaṃ kālena na paricchedyate hi saḥ akṣīṇakarmā maraṇe saṃsmaran devam acyutam yathā tvam eva devānāṃ loke bhogān upāśnute kṣutite api kule kaścij jāyeyaṃ karmaṇaḥ kṣaye manuṣyo yena sarveśaṃ cintayeyaṃ sadā harim taccintayādhunāśeṣa- puṇyapāpavivarjitaḥ maraṇe tanmanas tatra layam etya tam āpnuyāt karmabhūmau samastānāṃ karmaṇām uttamottamam yad antakāle puruṣaiḥ smaryate puruṣottamaḥ ity etān āha rājarṣiḥ ślokān ādyo bhagīrathaḥ viṣṇusaṃsmaraṇāt prāpya lokān anaśane mṛtaḥ evam atyantaśastānāṃ karmaṇām asureśvara nānyad utkṛṣṭam uddiṣṭaṃ tajjñair anaśanāt param tasyāhaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yac ca japyaṃ mumūrṣubhiḥ yādṛgrūpaś ca bhagavāṃś cintanīyo janārdanaḥ āsannam ātmanaḥ kālaṃ jñātvā prājño mahāsura nirdhūtamaladoṣaś ca snāto niyatamānasaḥ samabhyarcya hṛṣīkeśaṃ puṣpadhūpādibhis tataḥ praṇipātaiḥ stavaiḥ puṇyair dhyānayogaiś ca pūjayet dattvā dānaṃ ca viprebhyo vikalādibhya eva ca sabhāprapābrāhmaṇauka- devaukādyupayogi ca bandhuputrakalatrauka- kṣetradhānyadhanādiṣu mitravarge ca daityendra mamatvaṃ vinivartayet mitrān amitrān madhyasthān parān svāṃś ca punaḥ punaḥ abhyarthanopacāreṇa kṣāmayet kukṛtaṃ svakam tataś ca prayataḥ kuryād utsargaṃ sarvakarmaṇām śubhāśubhānāṃ daityendra vākyaṃ cedam udāharet parityajāmy ahaṃ bhogāṃs tyajāmi suhṛdo akhilān bhojanādi mayotsṛṣṭam utsṛṣṭam anulepanam sragbhūṣaṇādikaṃ geyaṃ dānam ādānam eva ca homādayaḥ padārthā ye yāś ca nityakriyā mama naimittikās tathā kāmyā varṇadharmās tathojjhitāḥ guṇadharmādayo dharmā yāś ca kāścin mama kriyāḥ padbhyāṃ karābhyāṃ viharan kurvan vā karma na tv aham kariṣye prāṇināṃ pīḍāṃ prāṇinaḥ santu nirbhayāḥ nabhasi prāṇino ye tu ye jale ye ca bhūtale kṣiter antaragā ye ca ye ca pāṣāṇasaṃpuṭe ye dhānyādiṣu vastreṣu śayaneṣv āsaneṣu ca te svapantu vibudhyantu sukhaṃ matto bhayaṃ vinā na me asti bāndhavaḥ kaścid viṣṇuṃ muktvā jagadgurum mitrapakṣe ca me viṣṇur adhaś cordhvaṃ tathāgrataḥ pārśvato mūrdhni pṛṣṭhe ca hṛdaye vāci cakṣuṣi śrotrādiṣu ca sarveṣu mama viṣṇuḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti sarvaṃ samutsṛjya dhyātvā sarvatra cācyutam vāsudevety avirataṃ nāma devasya kīrtayan dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu śayīta prācchirās tataḥ udacchirā vā daityendra cintayañ jagataḥ patim viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇuṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ keśavaṃ madhusūdanam nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam vārāhaṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam vāmanaṃ śrīdharaṃ śrīśaṃ nṛsiṃham aparājitam padmanābham ajaṃ śaurim dāmodaram adhokṣajam sarveśvareśvaraṃ śuddham anantaṃ rāmam īśvaram cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ śārṅgiṃ śaṅkhinaṃ garuḍadhvajam kirīṭakaustubhadharaṃ praṇamāmy aham avyayam aham atra jagannāthe mayi cāstu janārdanaḥ āvayor antaraṃ māstu samīranabhasor iva ayaṃ viṣṇur ayaṃ śaurir ayaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ puro mama nīlotpaladalaśyāmaḥ padmapattropamekṣaṇaḥ eṣa paśyatu mām īśaḥ paśyāmy aham adhokṣajam yato na vyatirikto ahaṃ yanmayo ahaṃ yadāśrayaḥ itthaṃ japann ekamanāḥ smaran sarveśvaraṃ harim āsīnaḥ sukhaduḥkheṣu samo mitrāhiteṣu ca oṃ namo vāsudevāyety etad vā satataṃ vadan yad vodīrayituṃ nāma samarthas tad udīrayan dhyāyeta devadevasya rūpaṃ viṣṇor manoramam praśāntanetrabhrūvaktraṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ caiva caturbāhuṃ kirīṭinam pītāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ cārukeyūradhāriṇam cintayec ca tadā rūpaṃ manaḥ kṛtvaikaniścayam yādṛśe vā manaḥ sthairyaṃ rūpe badhnāti cakriṇaḥ tad eva cintayan nāma vāsudeveti kīrtayet ittaṃ japan smaran vetthaṃ svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ ā prāṇoparamād vīras taccittas tatparāyaṇaḥ nirvikalpena manasā yaḥ smaret puruṣottamam sarvapātakayukto api puruṣaḥ puruṣarṣabha prayāti devadeveśe layam īḍyatame acyute yathāgnis tṛṇajālāni dahaty anilasaṃgataḥ tathānaśanasaṃkalpaḥ puṃsāṃ pāpam asaṃśayam viṣṇoḥ saṃsmaraṇe prāpya lokam anaśane mṛtaḥ evam atyantaśastānāṃ karmaṇām asureśvara nāsti satyāt paro dharmo nāsty adharma tathānṛtāt nāsti vidyāsamaṃ cakṣus tapo nānaśanāt param nāsti jñānasamaṃ dānaṃ na saṃtoṣasamaṃ sukham na caiverṣyāsamaṃ duḥkhaṃ tapo nānaśanāt param nāsty arogasamaṃ dhanyaṃ nāsti gaṅgāsamā sarit nāsti viṣṇusamaṃ dhyeyaṃ tapo nānaśanāt param utkrāntikāle bhūtānāṃ muhyante cittavṛttayaḥ jarāvyādhividhīnānāṃ kimu vyādhyādidoṣataḥ atyantavayasā vṛddhyā vyādhinā cātipīḍitaḥ yadi sthātuṃ na śaknoti kṣitisthe darbhasaṃstare tat kim anyo apy upāyo asti na vānaśanakarmaṇi viphalyaṃ yena nāpnoti tan me brūhi pitāmaha nātra bhūmir na ca kuśāḥ saṃstaraś ca na kāraṇam cittasyālambanībhūto viṣṇur evātra kāraṇam bhuñjann abhuñjan gacchaṃś ca svapaṃs tiṣṭhann athāpi vā utkrāntikāle govindaṃ saṃsmaraṃs tanmayo bhavet kiṃ japaiḥ kiṃ bhuvā kṛtyaṃ kiṃ kuśair daityasattama tathāpi kurvato yasya hṛdaye na janārdanaḥ tasmāt pradhānamantroktaṃ vāsudevasya kīrtanam tanmayatvena daityendra tasyopāyaś ca vistaraḥ ity etat kathitaṃ sarvaṃ pṛṣṭo ahaṃ yat tvayā bale utkrāntikāle smaraṇaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi te kriyāyogas tvayā pūrvaṃ mamokto yaḥ pitāmaha tam ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi phalaṃ cāsya yathātatham devārcāṃ devatāgāre tanmayatvena pūjayam yathāvac cetaso bhūmiṃ karoti niyato hi saḥ tapasā brahmacaryeṇa puṇyasvādhyāyasaṃstavaiḥ kriyāyogaḥ sa vidvadbhir yogināṃ samudāhṛtaḥ tatrāhaṃ śrotum icchāmi kriyāyogasthito naraḥ yat phalaṃ samavāpnoti kārayitvā harer gṛham devārcāṃ kārayitvā vā yat puṇyaṃ puruṣo aśnute saṃpūjayitvā vidhivad anulipya ca yat phalam kāni mālyāni śastāni kāni nārhanti keśave ke dhūpāḥ kṛṣṇadayitāḥ ke varjyāś ca jagatpateḥ upahāre phalaṃ kīm syāt kiṃ phalaṃ gītavādite ghṛtakṣīrādinā yac ca snāpite keśave phalam yac copalepane tāta phalam abhyukṣite ca yat vāsudevagṛhe sarvaṃ tad aśeṣaṃ vadasva me sādhu vatsa yad etat tvaṃ vāsudevasya pṛcchasi śuśrūṣaṇavidhau puṇyaṃ tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu brahmaṇā kila devānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām śuśrūṣaṇaphalaṃ viṣṇoḥ proktaṃ daityapate purā tebhyaḥ sakāśān manunā prāptaṃ svārociṣeṇa tu svārociṣaḥ svaputrāya dattavān ṛtacakṣuṣe ṛtacakṣuś ca bhargave śukras tasmād avāpa ca mamākhyātaṃ ca śukreṇa yathāvat sumahātmanā śuśrūṣave mahābhāga daityācāryeṇa dhīmatā tad etac chrūyatāṃ tāta kriyāyogāśritaṃ phalam jñānayogas tu saṃyogaś cittasyaivātmanā tu yaḥ yas tu bāhyārthasāpekṣaḥ sa kriyāyoga ucyate paramaṃ kāraṇaṃ yogo vimukter ditikeśvara kriyāyogaś ca yogasya paramaṃ tāta sādhanam yat tv etad bhavatā pṛṣṭaṃ phalam anvicchatā phalam devālayādikaraṇe tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu yas tu devālayaṃ viṣṇor dārvaṃ śailamayaṃ tathā kārayen mṛnmayaṃ vāpi śṛṇu tasya bale phalaṃ ahany ahani yajñena yajato yan mahāphalam prāpnoti tat phalaṃ viṣṇor yaḥ kārayati mandiram kulānāṃ śatam āgāmi samatītaṃ tathā śatam kārayan bhagavaddhāma nayaty acyutalokatām saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu viṣṇor ālayavinyāsa- prārambhād eva naśyati saptalokamayo viṣṇus tasya yaḥ kurute gṛham pratiṣṭhāṃ samavāpnoti sa naraḥ saptalaukikīm praśastadeśabhūbhāge yaḥ śastaṃ bhavanaṃ hareḥ kārayaty akṣayāṃl lokān sa naraḥ pratipadyate iṣṭakācayavinyāso yāvanty ṛkṣāṇi tiṣṭhati tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi tatkartur divi saṃsthitiḥ pratimāṃ lakṣaṇavatīṃ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ keśavasya sa tallokam akṣayaṃ pratipadyate ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sa modate svargaukasāṃ nivāseṣu pratyekam arisūdana pratiṣṭhāpya harer arcāṃ supraśaste niveśane puruṣaḥ kṛtakṛtyatvān nainaṃ śvomaraṇaṃ tapet ye bhaviṣyanti ye atītā ākalpāt puruṣāḥ kule tāṃs tārayati saṃsthāpya devasya pratimāṃ hareḥ anuśastāḥ kila purā yamena yamakiṃkarāḥ pāśodyatāyudhā daitya prajāsaṃyamane ratāḥ viharadhvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ niyogo me anupālyatām nājñābhaṅgaṃ kariṣyanti bhavatāṃ jantavaḥ kvacit kevalaṃ ye jagaddhātum anantaṃ samupāśritāḥ bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyās teṣāṃ nāsty atra saṃsthitiḥ ye tu bhāgavatā loke taccittās tatparāyaṇāḥ pūjayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ te vas tyājyāḥ sudūrataḥ yas tiṣṭhan prasvapan gacchaṃs tattiṣṭhan skhalite kṣute saṃkīrtayati govindaṃ te vas tyājyāḥ sudūrataḥ nityanaimittikair devaṃ ye yajanti janārdanam nāvalokya bhavadbhis te tattejo hanti vo gatim ye dhūpapuṣpavāsobhir bhūṣaṇaiś cāpi vallabhaiḥ arcayanti na te grāhyā narāḥ kṛṣṇāśrayoddhatāḥ upalepanakartāraḥ saṃmārjanaparāś ca ye kṛṣṇālaye parityājyaṃ teṣāṃ tripuruṣaṃ kulam yena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ tatkulodbhavam puṃsāṃ śataṃ nāvalokyaṃ bhavadbhir duṣṭacakṣuṣā yenārcā bhagavadbhaktyā vāsudevasya kāritā narāyutaṃ tatkulajaṃ bhavatāṃ śāsanātigam bhavatāṃ bhramatām atra viṣṇusaṃśrayamudrayā vinājñābhaṅgakṛn naiva bhaviṣyati naraḥ kvacit vatsa vaivasvatasyaitāḥ śrutvā gāthā marīcinā purukutsāya kathitāḥ pārthivendrāya dhīmate etāṃ mahāphalāṃ yo arcāṃ viṣṇoh kārayate naraḥ tavākhyātaṃ mahābāho gṛhakārayituś ca yat yajñā narāṇāṃ pāpaugha- kṣālakāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ tathaivejyo jagaddhātuḥ sarvayajñamayo hariḥ sthāpitāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ samyak saṃpūjya mānavaḥ yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ tam āpnoty asaṃśayam yaḥ snāpayati devasya ghṛtena pratimāṃ hareḥ prasthe prasthe dvijāgryāṇāṃ sa dadāti gavāṃ śatam gavāṃ śatasya viprāṇāṃ yad dattasya bhavet phalam ghṛtaprasthena tad viṣṇor labhet snānopayoginā bhūridyumnena saṃprāptā saptadvīpā vasuṃdharā ghṛtāḍhakena govinda- pratimāsnāpanāt kila pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagataḥ patim snāpayitvā samastebhyaḥ pāpebhyo vipramucyate dvādaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ ca gavyena haviṣā hareḥ snāpanaṃ daityaśārdūla mahāpātakanāśanam jñānato ajñānato vāpi yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ tat kṣālayati saṃdhyāyāṃ ghṛtena snāpayan harim sarvayajñamayo viṣṇur havyānāṃ paramaṃ ghṛtam tayor aśeṣapāpānāṃ kṣālakaḥ saṃgamo asura yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo hradāḥ pāyasakardamāḥ tāṃl lokān puruṣā yānti kṣīrasnānakarā hareḥ āhlādaṃ nirvṛtiṃ svāsthyam ārogyaṃ cārurūpatām sapta janmāny avāpnoti kṣīrasnānakaro hareḥ dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīrataḥ saṃbhavo yathā tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnāpanato hareḥ yathā ca vimalaṃ jñānaṃ yathā nirvṛtikārakam tathāsya nirmalaṃ jñānaṃ bhavaty atiphalapradam grahānukūlatāṃ puṣṭiṃ priyatvaṃ cākhile jane karoti bhagavān viṣṇuḥ kṣīrasnāpanatoṣitaḥ sarvo asya snigdhatām eti dṛṣṭamātraḥ prasīdati ghṛtakṣīreṇa deveśe snāpite madhusūdane atrāpy udāharantīmaṃ saṃvādaṃ keśavāśritam śāṇḍilyā saha kaikeyyāḥ sumanāyāḥ surālaye svarge atiśobhanāṃ dṛṣṭvā kaikeyīṃ patinā saha brāhmaṇī śāṇḍilī nāma paryapṛcchata vismitā śataśaḥ santi kaikeyi devāḥ svarganivāsinaḥ devapatnyas tathaivaitāḥ siddhāḥ siddhāṅganās tathā na teṣām īdṛśo gandho na kāntir na surūpatā na vāsasāṃ ca śobheyaṃ yathā te patinā saha naivābharaṇajātāni teṣāṃ bhrājanti vai tathā yathā tava yathā patyus tava svarganivāsinaḥ svasthatā cetasaś ceyaṃ yuvayor atiricyate śakrādyānām apīsānāṃ kṣayātiśayavarjitaḥ tapaḥprabhāvo dānaṃ vā karma vā homasaṃjñitam yuvayor yan mamācakṣva tat sarvaṃ varavarṇini yajñair yajñeśvaro viṣṇur āvābhyāṃ yat tu toṣitaḥ svargaprāptir iyaṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ phalam uttamam surūpatāṃ manaḥprīti paśyatāṃ cāruveṣatām yat pṛcchasi mahābhāge tad apy eṣā vadāmi te tīrthodakais tathā snānaiḥ snāpito ayaṃ janārdanaḥ tena kāntir atītyaitān devāṃs tribhuvaneśvarān manaḥprasādaḥ saumyatvaṃ śārīrā yā ca nirvṛtiḥ yat priyatvaṃ ca sarvasya tad ghṛtasnānajaṃ phalam yāny abhīṣṭāni vāsāṃsi yac cābhīṣṭaṃ vibhūṣaṇam ratnāni yāny abhīṣṭāni yat priyaṃ cānulepanam ye dhūpā yāni mālyāni dayitāny abhavaṃs tadā mama bhartus tathaivāsya mama rājyaṃ praśāsataḥ tāni sarvāṇi sarvajñe sarvakartari keśave dattāni tatsamuttho ayaṃ gandhabhūṣātmako guṇaḥ āhārā dayitā ye ca pavitrāś ca niveditāḥ te lokakartre kṣṛṇāya tṛptis tadguṇasaṃbhavā svargakāmena me bhartrā mayā ca śubhadarśane kṛtam etad ato nābhūd āvayor bhavasaṃkṣayaḥ ye tv akāmāṃ narāḥ samyag etat kurvanti śobhane teṣāṃ dadāti viśveśo bhagavān muktim acyutaḥ evam abhyarcya govindaṃ sarvabhūteśvareśvaram prāpnoty abhimatān kāmān daityāha sumanā yathā candanāgarukarpūra- kuṅkumośīrapadmakaiḥ anulipto harir bhaktyā varān bhogān prayacchati kāleyakaṃ tuṅgakaṃ ca padmacandanam eva ca nṝṇāṃ bhavanti rogāya dattāni puruṣottame tasmād ebhir na govindaḥ pūjanīyo mahāsura yāny ātmanaḥ sadeṣṭāni tāni śastāny upākuru tathaiva śubhagandhā ye dhūpās te jagataḥ pateḥ vāsudevasya dharmajñair nivedyā dānaveśvara na śallakījaṃ nākṣaulaṃ na śuktāsavasaṃbhṛtam dadyāt kṛṣṇāya dharmajño dhūpān ārādhanodyataḥ mālatī mallikā caiva yūthikāthātimuktakā pāṭalā karavīraś ca javā pārantir eva ca kubjakas tagaraś caiva karṇikāraḥ kuraṇṭakaḥ campako rotakaḥ kundo bāṇo varvaramālikāḥ aśokatilakā rodhrās tathā caivāṭarūṣakaḥ amī puṣpaprakārās tu śastāḥ keśavapūjane bilvapatraṃ śamīpatraṃ patraṃ bhṛṅgārakasya ca tamālapatraṃ ca bale sadaiva bhagavatpriyam tulasīkālatulasī- patraṃ bhṛṅgarajasya ca ketakīpatrapuṣpaṃ ca sadyas tuṣṭikaraṃ hareḥ padmāny ambusamutthānāṃ raktanīle tathotpale sitotpalaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya dayitāni sadāsura nārkaṃ nonmattakaṃ kāṃcit tathaiva girikarṇikām na kaṇṭakārikāpuṣpam acyutāya nivedayet kauṭajaṃ śālmalīpuṣpaṃ śairīṣaṃ ca janārdane nivedite bhayaṃ rogaṃ niḥsvatāṃ ca prayacchati yeṣāṃ na pratiṣedho asti gandhavarṇānvitāni ca tāni puṣpāṇi deyāni viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave sugandhaiś ca surāmāṃsī- karpūrāgarucandanaiḥ tathānyaiś ca śubhair dravyair arcayej jagataḥ patim dukūlapaṭukauśeya- vārkṣakarpāsikādibhiḥ vāsobhiḥ pūjayed viṣṇuṃ daiteyendrātmanaḥ priyaiḥ bhakṣyāṇi yāny abhīṣṭāni bhojyāny abhimatāni ca phalaṃ ca vallabhaṃ yat syāt tat tad deyaṃ janārdane suvarṇamaṇimuktādi yac cānyad ativallabham tat tad devātidevāya keśavāya nivedayet ātmānaṃ keśavaṃ matvā yad yat tasyaiva rocate tat tad avyaktarūpāya keśavāya nivedayet cakravartī mahāvīryo māndhātā yuvanāśvajaḥ śaśāsa sa mahābāhuḥ saptadvīpāṃ vasuṃdharām agāyanta ca yā gāthā ye purāṇavido janāḥ māndhātari mahābāho yauvanāśve samāśritāḥ yāvat sūrya udeti sma yāvac ca pratitiṣṭhati sarvaṃ tad yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate sa yauvanagataḥ saṃrāṭ saptadvīpavatīṃ mahīm śaśāsa dharmeṇa purā cakravartī mahābalaḥ nānyāyakṛn na cāśakto na daridro na kīkaṭaḥ tasyābhūt puruṣo rājye samyagdharmānuśāsinaḥ catasro gatayas tasya yauvanāśvasya dhīmataḥ babhūvur apratihatā hatārātibalasya vai tasya bhaktir atīvābhūn nisargād eva bhūpateḥ vāsudeve jagaddhāmni sarvakāraṇakāraṇe tasya rddhiṃ mahimānaṃ ca vilokya pṛthivīpateḥ na kevalaṃ janasyābhūt tasyāpy atyantavismayaḥ sa cintayām āsa nṛpaḥ samṛddhyā vismitas tayā kathaṃ syāt sampad eṣā me punar apy anyajanmani evaṃ subahuśo rājā daityendra sumahābalaḥ cintayann api tanmūlaṃ na cāsīn niścayānvitaḥ yadā na niścayaṃ rājā sa yayau yuvanāśvajaḥ tadā papraccha dharmajñān sa viprān samupāgatān vasiṣṭhapramukhān vatsa viviktāntaḥpurasthitaḥ praṇipatya mahābāhur gṛhītāsanasatkriyān yadi sānugrahā buddhir bhavatāṃ mayi sattamāḥ tad ahaṃ praṣṭum icchāmi kiṃcit tad vaktum arhatha sametyākhilavijñānaṃ samyagdhautāntarātmabhiḥ bhavadbhir yady ahaṃ na syāṃ vimalas tan mahādbhutam yad yathā tan mayā pṛṣṭā bhavanto matprasādhitāḥ vaktum arhanti vidvāṃsaḥ sarvasyaivopakāriṇaḥ yas te manasi saṃdehas taṃ pṛcchādya mahīpate gadiṣyāmo yathānyāyaṃ yat te sāṃśayikaṃ hṛdi vayaṃ hi naraśārdūla bhavatā paritoṣitāḥ samyak prajāḥ pālayatā saptadvīpe mahītale sutuṣṭo brāhmaṇo aśnīyāc chindyād vā dharmasaṃśayam hitaṃ vopadiśed dharmam ahitād vā nivartayet vivakṣum atha bhūpālaṃ bhāryā tasyaiva dhīmataḥ praṇāmapūrvam āhedaṃ vinayāt praṇayānvitam na strīṇām avanīpāla vaktum īdṛg iheśyate tathāpi bhūpate vakṣye saṃpad īdṛk sudurlabhā bhūyo api saṃśayaṃ praṣṭum alam īśa bhavān ṛṣīn na tv ahaṃ puruṣavyāghra sadāntaḥpuracāriṇī sa prasādaṃ yadi bhavān karoti mama pārthiva tan madīyam ṛṣīn praṣṭuṃ saṃśayaṃ pārthivārhasi brūhi subhru mataṃ yat te praṣṭavyā yan mayā dvijāḥ bhūyo aham ātmasaṃdehaṃ prakṣyāmy etān dvijottamān śrūyante pṛthivīpāla nṛpa ye ca purātanāḥ teṣāṃ na saṃpad bhūpāla yathā tava kilābhavat tad īdṛksaṃpadāṃ dhāma tvam aśeṣakṣitīśvaraḥ yena karmavipākena tad vadantu maharṣayaḥ ahaṃ ca bhavato bhāryā sarvasīmantinī bhuvi vidhinā kena tapasā niyuktā bhavato gṛhe atīva karmaṇā yena tadvijñāne kutūhalam tāratamyatayeśitvam anyeṣv api hi vidyate nirastātiśayatvena nūnaṃ nālpena karmaṇā tad anyajanmacaritaṃ naranātha nijaṃ bhavān munīn pṛcchatu yā cāhaṃ yan mayā ca purā kṛtam sa tathoktas tayā rājā patnyā vismitamānasaḥ munīnāṃ purato bhāryāṃ praśaṃsan vākyam abravīt sādhu devi mataṃ yan me tvayā tad idam īritam satyaṃ munivacaḥ puṃsām ardhaṃ vai gṛhiṇī yathā mamāpy etad abhipretam imān praṣṭuṃ mahāmunīn yat tvayābhihitaṃ bhadre matsvabhāvānuyātayā so aham etan mahābhāge prakṣyāmy etān mahāmunīn naiṣām aviditaṃ kiṃcit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate evam uktvā priyāṃ bhāryāṃ praṇipatya ca tān ṛṣīn yathāvad etad akhilaṃ papracchāsurasattama bhagavanto mamāśeṣaṃ prasādāhṛtacetasaḥ kathayantu yathāvṛttaṃ yan mayā sukṛtaṃ kṛtam ko aham āsaṃ purā viprāḥ kiṃ ca karma mayā kṛtam kiṃ vānayā sucārvaṅgyā mama patnyā kṛtaṃ dvijāḥ yenāvayor iyaṃ sphītir martyaloke sudurlabhā catvāraś cāpratihatā gatayo mama gacchataḥ aśeṣā bhūbhṛto vaśyāḥ kośasyānto na vidyate balaṃ caivāpratihataṃ śarīrārogyam uttamam atibhāti ca me kāntyā bhāryeyam akhilaṃ jagat mamāpi vapuṣas tejo na kaścit sahate dvijāḥ so aham icchāmi vijñātuṃ tathaiveyam aninditā nijānuṣṭhānam akhilaṃ yasyāśeṣam idaṃ phalam iti praṣṭā narendreṇa samastās te tapodhanāḥ vasiṣṭhaṃ codayām āsuḥ kathyatām iti bhūbhṛtaḥ coditaḥ so api dharmajñair maitrāvaruṇir ātmavān yogam āsthāya suciraṃ yathāvad yatamānasaḥ jñātavān nṛpates tasya pūrvadehaviceṣṭitam sa tam āha munir bhūpaṃ viditārtho mahāsura māndhātāraṃ mahābuddhiṃ sapatnīkam idaṃ vacaḥ śṛṇu bhūpāla sakalaṃ yasyedaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam tava rājyādikaṃ subhrūr yeyaṃ cāsīn mahīpate tvam āsīḥ śūdrajātīyaḥ parahiṃsāparāyaṇaḥ vākkrūro daṇḍapāruṣyo niḥsnehaḥ sarvajantuṣu tatheyaṃ bhavato bhāryā pūrvam apy āyatekṣaṇā dveṣyā babhūva taccittā tava śuśrūṣaṇe ratā pativratā mahābhāgā bhartsyamānāpy aniṣṭhurā tvadvākyād anu sarveṣu vīrakarmasu codyatā naiṣṭhuryād asahāyasya tyajyamānasya bandhubhiḥ kṣayaṃ jagāma yo artho abhūt saṃcitaḥ prapitāmahaiḥ tasmin kṣīṇe kṛṣiparas tvam āsīḥ pṛthivīpate sāpi karmavipākena kṛṣir viphalatāṃ gatā tato niḥsvaṃ parikṣīṇaṃ pareṣāṃ bhṛtyatāṃ gatam tatyāja sādhvī veyaṃ tvāṃ tyajyamānāpi pārthiva anayā ca samaṃ sādhvyā viṣṇor āvasathe tvayā kṛtaṃ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ vīra parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇām bhagnehaḥ sarvakāmebhyas tanmayas tvaṃ tadarpaṇaḥ ananyagatir ekasthas tasminn āyatane hareḥ tadvṛttilipsuḥ śuśrūṣāṃ janarañjanahetukaḥ kṛtavān yogināṃ vīra kṛṣṇasya jagataḥ pateḥ vāsudevājire nityaṃ kṛtaṃ saṃmārjanaṃ tvayā tathaivābhyukṣaṇaṃ vīra nityaṃ caivānulepanam patnyānayā ca dharmajña yaṣmaccittānuvṛttayā ahany ahani tat karma yuvayor nṛpa kurvatoḥ tatra caitanmayatvena pāpahānir ajāyata viṣṇoḥ kāryaṃ mayā kāryaṃ yogiśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathā na prabhātaṃ prabhātaṃ tu cinteyam abhavan niśi evam āyatanaṃ ramyam ity evaṃ ca sukhāvaham sthairyaṃ na caivam etat syād ity āsīt te manaḥ sadā yogināṃ sukhadaṃ tv evaṃ karmaivaṃ naivam ity api tava cittam abhūt tatra yogikarmaṇy aharniśam evaṃ tanmanasas tatra kṛtodyogasya pārthiva bhṛtyāvasāyinaḥ samyag yathoktādhikakāriṇaḥ smarataḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ kāryeṇātidṛḍhātmanaḥ niḥśeṣam upaśāntaṃ tat pāpaṃ yoginiṣevaṇāt tato adhikaṃ puras tasmād ādarād anulepanam saṃmārjanaṃ ca bahuśaḥ sapatnikena te kṛtam tatrāgataś ca sauvīraḥ purujin nāma bhūpatiḥ mahāsainyaparīvāraḥ prabhūtagajavāhanaḥ sarvasaṃpadupetaṃ taṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam vṛtaṃ bhāryāsahasreṇa dṛṣṭvā srakcandanojjvalam spṛhā kṛtā tvayā tatra cārumaulini pārthive sarvakāmapradaṃ karma devadevasya kurvatā tenaitad akhilaṃ rājyam aśeṣadvīpavat tava tejaś caivādhikaṃ yat te tathaitac chṛṇu pārthiva yogaprabhāvopalabdhaṃ kathayāmy akhilaṃ tava tatraivāvasathe dīpaḥ praśāntaḥ snehasaṃkṣayāt nijabhojanatailena punaḥ prajvālitas tvayā anayā cottarīyānta- cīravartyupavṛṃhitaḥ tava patnyā sa jajvāla kāntir asyās tato adhikā tavāpy akhilabhūpāla- manaḥkṣobhakaraṃ tataḥ tejo narendra na syāc ca kim ārādhya janārdanam evaṃ narendra śūdratvād viṣṇukarmaparāyaṇaḥ tanmayatvena saṃprāpto mahimānam anuttamam kiṃ punar yo naro bhaktyā viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇādṛtaḥ karoti satataṃ pūjāṃ niṣkāmo nānyamānasaḥ sa tvam ṛddhim imāṃ labdhvā sarvalokeśvareśvaram pūjayācyutam īśeśaṃ tam ārādhya na sīdati puṣpair dhūpais tathā gandhair dīpavastrānulepanaiḥ ārādhayācyutaṃ tadvad veśmasaṃmārjanādibhiḥ yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ kiṃcid yad yad atyantadurlabham tat tad dāttvā jagaddhātre vaikuṇṭhāya na sīdati sugandhāgarukarpūra- candanākṣodakuṃkumaiḥ vāsobhir vividhair dhūpaiḥ puṣpasragcāmarair dhvajaiḥ annopahārair vividhair ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣecanaiḥ gītavāditanṛtyādyais toṣayasvācyutaṃ nṛpa puṇyarātriṣu govindaṃ nṛtyagītaravojjvalaiḥ bhūpa jāgaraṇair bhaktyā toṣayācyutam avyayam evaṃ saṃtoṣyate bhaktyā bhagavān bhavabhaṅgakṛt bhūpa bhāgavatair bhūta- bhavyakṛt keśavo naraiḥ yeṣāṃ na vittaṃ tair bhaktyā mārjanādyupalepanaiḥ toṣito bhagavān viṣṇur dadāty abhimataṃ phalam devakarmāsamarthāṇāṃ prāṇināṃ smṛtisaṃstavaiḥ toṣito abhimatān kāmān prayacchati janārdanaḥ naiṣa vittair na ratnaughaiḥ puṣpadhūpānulepanaiḥ sadbhāvenaiva govindas toṣam āyāti saṃsmṛtaḥ tvayaikāgramanaskena gṛhasaṃmārjanādikam kṛtvālpam īdṛśaṃ prāptaṃ rājyam atyantadurlabham prāptopakaraṇo yas tvam ekāgramatir acyutam toṣayiṣyasi nendro api bhavitā tena te samaḥ tasmāt tvam anayā devyā sahātyantavinītayā keśavārādhane yatnaṃ kuru dharmabhṛtāṃ vara tataḥ prāpsyasi bhaktyaiva yat tapobhiḥ sudurlabham etan muner vasiṣṭhasya niśāmya vacanaṃ nṛpaḥ bhāryāsahāyaḥ sa tadā saṃprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ kṛtakāryam ivātmānaṃ manyamāno asurottama uvāca praṇato bhūtvā māndhātā vāruṇiṃ vacaḥ yathāmaratvaṃ saṃprāpya yathā vā brahma śāśvatam paraṃ nirvāṇam āpnoti tathāhaṃ vacasā tava kṛtakṛtyaḥ sukhī cāsmi nirvṛtiṃ paramāṃ gataḥ ajñānatamasāchanne yat pradīpas tvayaidhitaḥ aham eṣā ca tanvaṅgī vibhūtibhraṃsabhīrukau āḍhyāv āpāditau brahmann ihādya vacasā tava saṃpadāṃ kathitaṃ bījam āvayor bhavatā mune taduptāv udyatāv āvāṃ vijānīhi dvijottama na ratnair na ca vittaughair na ca puṣpānulepanaiḥ ārādhyate jagannātho bhāvaśūnyair janārdanaḥ bāhyārthanirapekṣaiś ca manasaiva manogatiḥ niḥsvair ārādhyate devo viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ sarvam etan mayā jñātaṃ yat tvam āttha mahāmune yat tvāṃ pṛcchāmi tan me tvaṃ prasādasumukho vada kāni vratāni yair devo naraiḥ strībhiś ca keśavaḥ toṣam ārādhito abhyeti kaiś ca dānair mahāmune rahasyāni ca devasya prītaye yāni cakriṇaḥ tāny aśeṣāṇi me brūhi kṛṣṇārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ śṛṇu bhūpāla yair viṣṇur narair ārādhyate vrataiḥ nārībhiś cātighore asmin patitābhir bhavārṇave samabhyarcya jagannāthaṃ vāsudevaṃ samādhinā ekam aśnāti yo bhaktaṃ dvitīyaṃ brāhmaṇātmakam karoti keśavaprītyai kārttikaṃ māsam ātmavān pūrve vayasi yat tena jñānato ajñānato api vā pāpam ācaritaṃ tasmān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ anenaiva vidhānena mārgaśīrṣe api mādhavam samabhyarcyaikabhaktaṃ vai varṇibhyo yaḥ prayacchati bhagavatprīṇanārthāya phalaṃ tasya śṛṇuṣva me madhye vayasi yat pāpaṃ yoṣitā puruṣeṇa vā kṛtaṃ tasmāc ca tenokto vimokṣaḥ paramātmanā tathā caivaikabhaktaṃ vai varṇāgrebhyaḥ prayacchati puṇḍarīkākṣam abhyarcya pauṣamāse mahīpate tatprīṇanāya yat pāpaṃ vārddhike tena vai kṛtam sa tasmān mucyate rājan pumān yoṣid athāpi vā traimāsikavratam idaṃ yaḥ karoti nareśvara sa viṣṇuprīṇanāt pāpair laghubhir vipramucyate dvitīye vatsare rājan mucyate copapātakaiḥ tadvat tṛtīye api kṛtaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam vratam etan naraiḥ strībhis tribhir māsair anuṣṭhitam tribhiḥ saṃvatsarair eva pradadāti phalaṃ nṛṇām tribhir māsais trir avasthās trividhāt pātakān nṛpa trīṇi nāmāni devasya mocayanti trivārṣikaiḥ yatas tato vratam idaṃ trikramaṃ samudāhṛtam sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ keśavārādhanaṃ param śṛṇuṣva ca mahīpāla vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ yaj jagāda purā hariḥ prācetasāya dakṣāya dakṣaś cāha vivasvate vivasvān alasidhrāya alasidhro asitāya ca asitena samākhyātam alpāyāsaṃ mahāphalam tad idaṃ śrūyatāṃ samyag vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ pūrvaṃ viṣṇum ārādhya pṛṣṭavān bahuśas tu
