vipannāyāṃ sṛṣṭāv arinisūdana bhagavan sarvakaṛtvaṃ mamādiṣṭaṃ svayaṃbhuvā brahmaṇā devadeveśa tavādeśena keśava vipannā ca jagannātha mama sṛṣṭiḥ kṛtā kṛtā pūrvakarmavipākena vyākulaś cāsmi cetasā yathā ca deva mucyeya asmāt saṃsārasaṃkaṭāt viṣayāsaṅgaviṣamāt tan mamājñāpayācyuta ity evam ukto dakṣeṇa devadevo janārdanaḥ ācaṣṭa duḥkhakṣayadaṃ vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam sarvārambhaviniṣpatti- kārakaṃ pāpanāśanam saṃsārocchedakaṃ dhīrair ācīrṇaṃ sthirabuddhibhiḥ tad ahaṃ tava rājendra vratānām uttamottamam kathayāmi samācaṣṭa yathā pūrvaṃ mamāsitaḥ āṣāḍhe māsi pūrvāsu tathāṣāḍhāsu pārthiva samabhyarcya jagannātham acyutaṃ niyataḥ śuciḥ puṣpair hṛdyais tathā dhūpair gandhaiḥ sāgarucandanaiḥ yathāvibhavataś cānyair annair vāsobhir eva ca kṣīrasnehasthitaṃ tadvat paiṣṭaṃ viṣṇupadadvayam samabhyarcya yathānyāyaṃ keśavasyāgrato nyaset yavāṃś ca dadyād viprāya bhūgatiḥ prīyatām iti naktaṃ bhuñjīta rājendra haviṣyānnaṃ susaṃskṛtam tathottarāsv āṣāḍhāsu śrāvaṇe māsi mānavaḥ tathaivābhyarcya govindaṃ tadvad viṣṇupadadvayam viprāya ca yavān dadyāt prīṇayitvā ca bhūgatim naktaṃ bhūñjīta rājendra naro yoṣid athāpi vā prāpte bhādrapade māsi pūrvabhadrapadāsu ca tathaivābhyarcya govindaṃ tadvad viṣṇupadadvayam viprāya ca yavān dattvā prīṇayitvā bhuvogatim bhuñjīta gorasaprāyaṃ naro yoṣid athāpi vā tadvad āśvayuje dānaṃ tadvad govindapūjanam padadvayasya pūjāṃ ca prīṇanaṃ ca bhuvogateḥ tathaiva naktaṃ bhuñjīta gorasaṃ maunam āsthitaḥ strī vā rājendra pūrvāsu tathā bhadrapadāsu vai phālgune phalgunī pūrvā bhavatī ha yadā nṛpa trivikramaṃ tadā devaṃ pūrvoktavidhinārcayet padadvayaṃ ca devasya samyag abhyarcya pārthiva hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā svargatiḥ prīyatām iti naktaṃ bhuñjīta rājendra vahnipākavivarjitam eṣa evottarāyoge caitre māse vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ etaj jagāda govindaḥ purā dakṣāya pṛcchate sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ vrataṃ viṣṇupadatrayam yathoktam etad yo bhakto karoti nṛpasattama sarvakāmān avāpnoti keśavasya vaco yathā aputro labhate putram apatir labhate patim samāgamaṃ proṣitaiś ca tathā prāpnoti bāndhavaiḥ dravyam aiśvaryam ārogyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ cārurūpatām prāpnuvanty akhilān etān pūjayitvā padatrayam yān yān kāmān naraḥ strī vā hṛdayenābhivāñchanti tāṃs tāṃś cāpnoti niṣkāmo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati pūrvaṃ kṛtvāpi pāpāni naraḥ strī vā narādhipa padatrayavrataṃ cīrtvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ viṣṇor ārādhanārthāya yāni dānāni sattama deyāni tāny aśeṣāṇi mamācakṣva dvijottama yena caiva vidhānena dānaṃ puṃsaḥ sukhāvaham prīṇanāya ca kṛṣṇasya tan mamākhyāhi vistarāt kṛtopavāsaḥ saṃprāśya pañcagavyaṃ nareśvara ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣekaṃ ca kṛtvā viṣṇoḥ samāhitaḥ samabhyarcya ca govindaṃ puṣpādibhir ariṃdama udaṅmukhīm arcayitvā tathā gṛṣṭiṃ payasvinīm saputrāṃ vastrasaṃvītāṃ sitayajñopavītinīm svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ śubhākārāṃ hiraṇyoparisaṃsthitām hiraṇyaṃ vācayitvāgre brāhmaṇāyopapādayet imāṃ tvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva govindaḥ prīyatām iti samyag uccārya taṃ vipraṃ govindaṃ nṛpa kalpayet anuvrajec ca gacchantaṃ padāny aṣṭau narādhipa anena vidhinā dhenuṃ yo viprāya prayacchati govindaprīṇanād rājan viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati saptāvarāṃs tathā pūrvān saptātmānaṃ ca mānavaḥ saptajanmakṛtāt pāpān mocayaty avanīpate pade pade ca yajñasya gosavasya sa mānavaḥ phalam āpnoti rājendra dakṣāyaivaṃ jagau hariḥ sarvakāmasamṛddhasya sarvakāleṣu pārthiva bhavaty aghaughāpaharā yāvad indrāś caturdaśa sarveṣām eva pāpānāṃ kṛtānām avijānatā prāyaścittam idaṃ śastam anutāpopavṛṃhitam ikṣvākunaiṣā rājendra pūrvaṃ dattā mahātmanā tataḥ sa lokān amalān prāptavān avanīpatiḥ tathaivānyair mahīpālair dvijavaiśyādibhis tathā lokāḥ kāmadughāḥ prāptā dattvedṛgvidhinā nṛpa tiladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi keśavaprīṇanāya yā dattā bhavati yaś cāsyā narendra vidhir uttamaḥ phalam āpnoti rājendra tadvad vā vidhivat tadā yāṃ dattvā brahmahā goghnaḥ pitṛghno gurutalpagaḥ āgāradāhī garadaḥ sarvapāparato api vā mahāpātakayukto yo yukto yaś copapātakaiḥ sa mucyate akhilaiḥ pāpair viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati svanulipte mahīpṛṣṭe vastrājinasamāvṛte dhenuṃ tilamayīṃ kṛtvā sarvaratnaiḥ samanvitām suvarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ gandhaghrāṇavatīṃ śubhām mṛṣṭānnajihvāṃ kurvīta guḍāsyāṃ sūtrakambalām ikṣupādāṃ tāmrapṛṣṭhāṃ kuryān muktāphalekṣaṇām praśastapatraśravaṇāṃ phaladantavatīṃ śubhām sragdāmapucchāṃ kurvīta navanītastanānvitām phalair manoharair bhakṣair maṇimuktāphalānvitām tiladroṇena kurvīta āḍhakena tu vatsakam śubhavastrayugacchannāṃ cārucchattrasamanvitām īdṛksaṃsthānasaṃpannāṃ kṛtvā śrāddhasamanvitaḥ kāṃsyopadohanāṃ dadyāt keśavaḥ prīyatām iti samyag uccārya vidhinā dattvaitena narādhipa sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ pitaraṃ sapitāmaham prapitāmahaṃ tathā pūrvaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ catuṣṭayam ātmānaṃ tanayaṃ pautraṃ tadadhas tu catuṣṭayam tārayaty avanīpāla tiladhenuprado naraḥ yaś ca gṛhṇāti vidhivat tasyāpy evaṃvidhān kulān caturdaśa tathā caiva dadataś cānumodakāḥ dīyamānāṃ prapaśyanti tiladhenuṃ ca ye narāḥ te apy aśeṣāghanirmuktāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim praśāntāya suśīlāya tathāmatsariṇe budhaḥ tiladhenuṃ naro dadyād vedasnātāya dharmiṇe trirātraṃ yas tilāhāras tiladhenuṃ prayacchati dattvaikarātraṃ ca punas tilān atti nareśvara dātur viśuddhapāpasya tasya puṇyavato nṛpa cāndrāyaṇād abhyadhikaṃ śastaṃ tat tilabhakṣaṇam tilābhāve tathā dadyād ghṛtadhenuṃ yatavrataḥ kalpayitvā yathānyāyaṃ tiladhenvā yatavrataḥ yena bhūpa vidhānena tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu vāsudevaṃ jagannāthaṃ puruṣeśam ajaṃ vidhum sarvapāpanihantāraṃ ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣecanāt saṃpūjya pūrvavat puṣpa- gandhadhūpādibhir naraḥ ahorātroṣito bhūtvā tatparaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ parameśam atho nāmnā abhiṣṭūya ghṛtārciṣā gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ kumbhaṃ puṣpamālyādibhūṣitam kāṃsyopadhānasaṃyuktaṃ sitavastrayugena ca hiraṇyagarbhasahitaṃ maṇividrumamuktikaiḥ ikṣuyaṣṭimayān pādān khurān raupyamayāṃs tathā sauvarṇe cākṣiṇī kuryāc śṛṅge cāgarukāṣṭhaje saptadhānyamaye pārśve pattrorṇāni ca kambalam kuryāt turuṣkakarpūrau ghrāṇaṃ phalamayān stanān maṇiratnasuvarṇānāṃ samyakkalpanayā kṛtām tadvac charkarayā jihvāṃ guḍakṣīramayaṃ mukham kṣaumasūtreṇa lāṅgūlaṃ romāṇi sitasarṣapaiḥ tāmrapātramayaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ īdṛksvarūpāṃ saṃkalpya ghṛtadhenuṃ narādhipa tadvatkalpanayā dhenvā ghṛtavatsaṃ prakalpayet taṃ ca vipraṃ mahābhāga manasaiva ghṛtārciṣam kalpayitvā tatas tasmai prayataḥ pratipādayet etāṃ mamopakārāya ghṛhṇīṣva tvaṃ dvijottama prīyatāṃ mama deveśo ghṛtāṛciḥ puruṣottamaḥ ity udāhṛtya viprāya dadyād dhenuṃ narottama maṇimuktāsuvarṇānāṃ samyakkalpanayā kṛtām dattvaikarātraṃ sthitvā ca ghṛtāhāro narādhipa mucyate sarvapāpebhyas tathā dānaphalaṃ śṛṇu ghṛtakṣīravahā nadyo yatra pāyasakardamāḥ teṣu lokeṣu lokeśa sa puṇyeṣūpajāyate pitur ūrdhvena ye sapta puruṣāḥ sapta ye apy adhaḥ tāṃs teṣu nṛpa lokeṣu sa nayaty astakalmaṣaḥ sakāmānām iyaṃ vyuṣṭiḥ kathitā nṛpasattama viṣṇulokaṃ narā yānti niṣkāmā ghṛtadhenudāḥ ghṛtam agnir ghṛtaṃ somas tanmayāḥ sarvadevatāḥ ghṛtaṃ prayacchatā dattā bhavanty akhiladevatāḥ jaladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi prīyate dattayā yayā devadevo hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ jalakumbhaṃ naravyāghra suvarṇarajatānvitam ratnagarbham aśeṣais tu grāmyair dhānyaiḥ samanvitam sitavastrayugacchannaṃ dūrvāpallavaśobhitam kuṣṭhaṃ māṃsīm uśīraṃ ca vālakāmalakair yutam priyaṅgupātrasahitaṃ sitayajñopavītinam sacchattraṃ saupānatkaṃ darbhavistarasaṃsthitam caturbhiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ bhūpa tilapātraiś caturdiśam sthagitaṃ dadhipātreṇa ghṛtakṣaudravatā mukhe upoṣitaḥ samabhyarcya vāsudevaṃ janeśvaram puṣpadhūpopahārais tu yathāvibhavam ādṛtaḥ saṃkalpya jaladhenuṃ ca kumbhaṃ samabhipūjya ca pūjayed vatsakaṃ tadvat kṛtaṃ jalamayaṃ budhaḥ evaṃ saṃpūjya govindaṃ jaladhenuṃ savatsakām sitavastradharaḥ śānto vītarāgo vimatsaraḥ dadyād viprāya rājendra prītyarthaṃ jalaśāyinaḥ jalaśāyī jagadyoniḥ prīyatāṃ mama keśavaḥ iti coccārya bhūnātha viprāya pratipādyatām apakvānnāśinā stheyam ahorātram ataḥparam anena vidhinā dattvā jaladhenuṃ janādhipa sarvāhlādān avāpnoti ye divyā ye ca mānuṣāḥ śarīrārogyam ābādhā- praśamaḥ sārvakāmikaḥ nṛṇāṃ bhavati dattāyāṃ jaladhenvāṃ na saṃśayaḥ atrāpi śrūyate bhūpa pudgalena mahātmanā jātismareṇa yad gītam ihābhyetya purā kila sa pudgalaḥ purā vipro yamalokagato muniḥ dadarśa yātanā ghorāḥ pāpakarmakṛtāṃ kila dīptāgnitīkṣṇaśastrotthāḥ kvāthatailagatās tathā uṣṇakṣāranadīpātā bhairavāḥ puruṣarṣabha vraṇāḥ kṣāranipātogrāḥ kumbhīpākamahābhayāḥ tā dṛṣṭvā yātanā vipraś cakāra paramāṃ kṛpām āhlādaṃ te tadā jagmuḥ pāpās tadanukampitāḥ taṃ dṛṣṭvā nārakāḥ kecit kecit tadavalokinaḥ tadā svasthaṃ vilokyaiva munir nārakamaṇḍalam dharmarājaṃ sa papraccha teṣāṃ praśamakāraṇam tasmai cācaṣṭa rājendra tadā vaivasvato yamaḥ āhlādahetuṃ viprāya pṛcchate pṛthivīpate tavānubhāvād eteṣāṃ nārakāṇāṃ dvijottam saṃpravṛtto ayam āhlādaḥ kāraṇaṃ yac chṛṇuṣva tat tvayābhyarcya jagannāthaṃ sarveśaṃ jalaśāyinam jaladhenuḥ purā dattā vidhivan munipuṅgava asmāt tu janmano atīte tṛtīye dvija janmani tasya dānasya te vyuṣṭir iyam āhlādadāyinī yena tvaṃ tapasā yukto mānavānām agocaram saṃprāpto asi mahāprajña sarvaśāstraviśārada ye tvāṃ paśyanti śṛṇvanti ye ca dhyāyanti pāpinaḥ śṛṇoṣi yāṃs tvaṃ viprendra yāṃś ca dhyāyasi paśyasi nirvṛtiḥ paramā teṣāṃ sarvāhlādapradāyinī sadyo bhavati mātra tvaṃ dvijendra kuru vismayam āhlādahetujananaṃ nāsti viprendra tādṛśam jaladhenur yathā nṝṇāṃ janmāny ekonasaptatiḥ na dāgho na klamo nārtir na moho vipra jāyate api janmasahasreṣu jaladhenupradāyinām ekajanmakṛtaṃ vāñchā trijanmotthaṃ samāhṛtā saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ hanti dattāmbugaur nṛṇām sa tvaṃ gaccha gṛhītvārgham asmatto dvijasattama yeṣāṃ samāśrayaḥ kṛṣṇo na niyamyā hi te mayā kṛṣṇaḥ saṃpūjito yais tu ye kṛṣṇārtham upoṣitāḥ yaiś ca nityaṃ smṛtaḥ kṛṣṇo na te madviṣayopagāḥ namaḥ kṛṣṇācyutānanta vāsudevety udīritam yair bhāvabhāvitair vipra na te madviṣayopagāḥ dānaṃ dadadbhir yair uktam acyutaḥ prīyatām iti śraddhāpuraḥsarair vipra na te madviṣayopagāḥ uttiṣṭhadbhiḥ svapadbhiś ca vrajadbhiś ca janārdanaḥ yaiḥ saṃsmṛto dvijaśreṣṭha na te madviṣayopagāḥ kṣutaskhalitabhītyādāv asahadbhiś ca vedanām kṛṣṇety udīritaṃ yaiś ca na te madviṣayopagāḥ sarvābādhāsu ye kṛṣṇaṃ smaranty uccārayanti ca tadbhāvabhāvitā vipra na te madviṣayopagāḥ sa eva dhātā sarvasya tanniyogakarā vayam janasaṃyamanodyuktāḥ so asmatsaṃyamano hariḥ itthaṃ niśāmya vacanaṃ yamasya vadato munim ūcus te nārakāḥ sarve vahniśastrāstrabhīravaḥ namaḥ kṛṣṇāya haraye viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ hṛṣīkeśāya devāya jagaddhātre acyutāya ca namaḥ paṅkajanetrāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye janārdanāya śrīśāya śrīpate pītavāsase govindāya namo nityaṃ namaś codadhiśāyine namaḥ karālavaktrāya nṛsiṃhāyātinādine śārṅgiṇe sitakhaḍgāya śaṅkhacakragadādhṛte namo vāmanarūpāya krāntalokatrayāya ca varāharūpāya tathā namo yajñāṅgadhāriṇe vyāptāśeṣadigantāya śāntāya paramātmane vāsudeva namas tubhyaṃ namaḥ kaiṭabhasūdana keśavāya namo vyāpin namas te astu mahīdhara namo astu vāsudevāyety evam uccārite tataḥ śastrāṇi kuṇṭhatāṃ jagmur analaś cāpy aśīśamat abhajyanta ca yantrāṇi samutpetur ayomukhāḥ saṃśuṣkāḥ kṣārasaritaḥ patitaḥ kūṭaśālmaliḥ prakāśatāmasītattvaṃ narakaś cāgatas tu saḥ vivān babhañja pavano apy asipatravanaṃ tataḥ nirutsāhā jaḍadhiyo babhūvur yamakiṃkarāḥ āsan gandhāmbuvāhinyaḥ pūyaśoṇitanimnagāḥ vavau sugandhī pavano manaḥprītikaras tataḥ veṇuvīṇāsvanayutān gītaśabdāṃś ca śuśruvuḥ taṃ tādṛśam athālakṣya nṛpa vaivasvato yamaḥ narakasya viparyāsaṃ saṃkṣuddhahṛdayas tataḥ dadarśa nārakān sadyo divyasraganulepanān jājvalyamānāṃs tejobhir amalāmbaravāsasaḥ namo namo astu kṛṣṇāya govindāyāvyayātmane vāsudevāya devāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave ity evaṃ vādinas tatra prajāsaṃyamano yamaḥ kṣīṇapāpacayāṃs tāṃs tu pādyārghyādibhir arcayan pūjayitvā ca tān āha sa kṛṣṇāya kṛtāñjaliḥ samāhitamanā bhūtvā dharmarājo nareśvara viṣṇor devātidevasya jagaddhātuḥ prajāpateḥ praṇāmaṃ ye api kurvanti teṣām api namo namaḥ sarvasya sarvasaṃsthasya sarvādhārasya yoginaḥ ye viṣṇoḥ praṇatās tebhyo namaḥ sadyaḥ punaḥ punaḥ tasya yajñavarāhasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ praṇāmaṃ ye api kurvanti teṣām api namo namaḥ evaṃ te saṃstutās tena dharmarājena nārakāḥ vimānāni samārūḍhā nṛttagāndharvavanti vai pudgalo api mahābuddhir dṛṣṭvaitad akhilaṃ nṛpa jātismaro abhavad bhūpa kaṇvagotre mahāmuniḥ saṃsmṛtya yamavākyāni viṣṇor māhātmyam eva ca jaladhenvāś ca māhātmyaṃ saṃsmṛtyaitad agāyata aho duruttarā viṣṇor māyeyam atigahvarī yayā mohitacittas taṃ na vetti parameśvaram jīvo vāñchati kīṭatvaṃ yūkāmatkuṇayonitaḥ tasmāc ca śalabhādīnāṃ yoniṃ tasmāc ca pakṣiṇām tataś ca paśutāṃ prāpya naratvam abhivāñchati vimuktihetukī dhanyā narayoniḥ kṛtātmanām na prāpnuvanti saṃsāre vibhrāntamanaso gatim jīvā mānuṣyatām anye janmanām ayutair api viṣṇumāyāparītās te prāpyāpi na taranti ye tad īdṛgdurlabhaṃ prāpya muktidvāram acetasaḥ patanti bhūyaḥ saṃsāre viṣṇumāyāvimohitāḥ dustarāpi tu sādhyāsau māyā kṛṣṇasya mohanī chidyate yāmanonyaste mudhaiva hi janārdane asaṃtyajya ca gārhasthyam ataptvaiva tathā tapaḥ chindanti vaiṣṇavīṃ māyāṃ keśavārpitamānasāḥ avirodhena viṣayām bhuñjan viṣṇuvyapāśrayaḥ kṛtvā manas taraty etāṃ viṣṇor māyāṃ sudustarām īdṛgbahuphalāṃ bhaktiṃ sarvadhātari keśave māyayā tasya devasya na kurvanti vimohitāḥ mudhaivoktaṃ mudhāyātaṃ mudhā tad vidhiceṣṭitam mudhaiva janma tan naṣṭaṃ yatra nārādhito hariḥ ārādhito hi yaḥ puṃsām aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam dadāti bhagavān devaḥ kas taṃ na pratipūjayet saṃvatsarās tathā māsā viphalā divasāś ca te narāṇāṃ viṣayāndhānāṃ yeṣu nārādhito hariḥ yo na vittarddhivibhavair na vasobhir na bhūṣaṇaiḥ tuṣyate hṛdayenaiva kas tam īśaṃ na pūjayet jaladhenvāś ca māhātmyaṃ niśāmyāpīdṛśaṃ narāḥ tāṃ na yacchanti ye teṣāṃ vivekaḥ kutra tiṣṭhati karmabhūmau hi mānuṣyaṃ janmanām ayutair api svargāpavargaphaladaṃ kadācit prāpyate naraiḥ saṃprāpya tan na yair viṣṇus toṣito nāmbudhenukā dattā ca samyak te muṣṭā janmani subahūni bhoḥ ūrdhvabāhur viraumy eṣa dṛṣṭalokadvayo asmi bhoḥ ārādhayata govindaṃ jaladhenuṃ prayacchata duḥsaho nārako vahnir aviṣahyāś ca yātanāḥ jñānaṃ mamaitad ālambya kṛṣṇe bhavata susthirāḥ adeśike deśiko aham atra mārge mayoditam vimṛṣya satyam ity etan manaḥ kṛṣṇe niveśyatām prātaḥ kṛṣṇeti deveti govindeti ca jalpatām madhyāhne cāparāhne ca yo avasādaḥ sa ucyatām anekaviṣayālambi yac cittaṃ taj janārdane kurudhvam ālambanavat saṃsmṛtaḥ puṇyado hi saḥ mudhaiva jihvā kṛṣṇeti keśaveti ca vakṣyati mudhā ca cittaṃ tadgāmi yadi syāt kim ato adhikam mayoktam etad bahuśo vinaṣṭe tu śarīrake manuṣyatvaṃ vinā viṣṇur durlabho vo bhaviṣyati etāḥ pudgalagāthās te yamavākyaṃ tavoditam jaladhenvāś ca māhātmyaṃ viṣṇusaṃpūjanasya ca vratāni sopavāsāni sarvakāmapradāni te vratam anyan mahābhāga sarvakāmapradaṃ śṛṇu bhaviṣyaṃ cāparaṃ bhūpa mamaitac chrotum arhasi yat prakṣyati mahīpālaḥ parikṣit svapurohitam parīkṣitaḥ purodhās tu dvijo gauramukho nṛpa bhaviṣyati śamīkasya śiṣyaḥ paramasaṃmataḥ sa ca rājā jagaddhātur devadevasya śārṅginaḥ sadaivārādhane yatnaṃ bhaktiyuktaḥ kariṣyati purodhasaṃ gauramukhaṃ praṇipatya sa pārthivaḥ prakṣyaty ārādhanārthāya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ bhagavan bhavabhīto aham abhavāya tato bhavān ārādhayitum icchāmi sarvecchāpūrakaṃ hariṃ saṃkuruṣva mahābhāga prasādaṃ mama suvrata kṛṣṇārādhanakāmasya manaso deśiko bhava ārādhanena yeneśo jagatām īśvareśvaraḥ viṣṇur ārādhyate puṃbhiḥ saṃsārābdhiparikṣataiḥ tan mamopadiśa brahman prasādapravaṇaṃ manaḥ kṛtvā sadaivārtimatāṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ guruḥ evaṃ sa tena bhūpāla bhūpālena rṣipuṅgavaḥ keśavārādhanārthāya samyak pṛṣṭaḥ pravakṣyati namaskṛtya jagaddhātre devadevāya śārṅgine parameśasureśāya hṛṣīkeśāya vedhase varārthinām amoghāya parasmai harimedhase sarvakalyāṇabhūtāya śaṅkhacakragadādhṛte varāsicarmāvitate krūraśāntātmamūrtaye yadyadbhūtopakārāya tattadrūpavikāriṇe paramāṇvantaparyanta- sahasrāṃśāṇumūrtaye jaṭharāntāyutāśānta- sthitabrahmāṇḍadhāriṇe śvetādidīrghahrasvādi- kaṭhinādivikalpanā yogicintye jagaddhāmni yatra nāsty akhilātmani tam ajaṃ śāśvataṃ nityaṃ pariṇāmavivarjitam yogibhiś cintyate mūrtir yatra tatrākhilātmani tatra tatrātmano nityaṃ pariṇāmavivarjitam praṇamya jagatām īśam anantaṃ parataḥ param paraṃ parāṇāṃ sraṣṭāraṃ purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ prabhum varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ sthūlasūkṣmasvarūpiṇam aśeṣajagatāṃ mūlam anādinidhanasthitim parāparasvarūpastham avikārasvarūpiṇam yasyopacārataḥ svargaṃ svarūpaṃ vyatiricyate jñānajñeyasya munibhir jñānavidbhir mahātmabhiḥ tasmai pārthivamukhyāya raghuvaryamahātmane śrūyatāṃ sa muniśreṣṭho yad vakṣyati parīkṣite devakī nāma rājendra devakasyābhavat sutā anapatyā tapas tepe putrārthaṃ kila bhāminī bhāryā sā vasudevasya satyadharmaparāyaṇā na cātuṣyata govindas tatas tām āha bhārgavaḥ kimarthaṃ tapyate bhadre tapaḥ paramaduścaram ko arthas tavābhilaṣito gantuṃ kutra tavepsitam aputrāhaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha patyur me nāsti saṃtatiḥ sāham ārādhya govindaṃ putram icchāmi śobhanam tapas tāvat kariṣyāmi parameṇa samādhinā yāvad ārādhito viṣṇur dāsyaty abhimataṃ mama govindārādhane yatno yadi te kulanandini tad idaṃ vratam āsthāya toṣayāśu janārdanam prathame kārttikasyāhni saṃprāpte devakātmaje pañcagavyajalasnātaḥ pañcagavyakṛtāśanaḥ bāṇapuṣpaiḥ samabhyarcya vāsudevam ajaṃ vibhum dattvā ca candanaṃ dhūpaṃ paramānnaṃ nivedayet ghṛtena vācayed vipraṃ gṛhṇīyāc ca tato vratam adyaprabhṛty ahaṃ māsaṃ virataḥ prāṇināṃ vadhāt asatyavacanāt stainyān madhumāṃsādibhakṣaṇāt svapan vibudhyan gacchaṃś ca smariṣyāmy aham acyutam parāpavādapaiśūnyaṃ parapīḍākaraṃ tathā sacchāstradevatāyajvi- nindām anyasya vā bhuvi na vakṣyāmi jagaty asmin paśyan sarvagata harim ity anyac cāpi śaknoti yan nirvoḍhuṃ yaśasvini kurvīta niyamaṃ tasya tyāgo dharmāya yasya ca kṛtvaivaṃ purato viṣṇor nivṛttiṃ pāpataḥ śubhe naivedyaṃ svayam aśnīyān maunī nityam udaṅmukhaḥ mārgaśīrṣe tathā māsi jātipuṣpair janārdanam samabhyarcya śubhe dhūpaṃ candanaṃ saṃnivedya ca paramānnaṃ ca devāya viprāya ca punar ghṛtam dattvā tathaiva gṛhṇīyān niyamaṃ cāsya rocate tathaiva naktaṃ bhuñjīta naivedyaṃ kulanandini sarveṣv eva tu māseṣu pañcagavyādikaṃ samam puṣpadhūpopahāreṣu viśeṣo dakṣiṇāsu ca snānaprāśanayoḥ sāmyaṃ tathā vai naktabhojane arcayet pratimāsaṃ ca yaiḥ puṣpais tāni me śṛṇu ye ca dhūpāḥ pradātavyā naivedyānnaṃ ca yad yadā bāṇasya jātikusumais tathaiva ca kuruṇṭhakaiḥ kundātimuktakai rakta- karavīraiś ca devaki śvetais tato mālikayā tathā mallikayā tataḥ dadhipiṇḍyātha ketakyā padmaraktotpalena ca krameṇābhyarcito viṣṇur dadāti manasepsitam kārttike mārgaśīrṣe ca dhūpaḥ pauṣe ca candanam māghaphālgunacaitreṣu dadyād viṣṇos tathāgarum vaiśākhādiṣu māseṣu triṣu devaki bhaktitaḥ karpūraṃ devadevāya guggulaṃ śrāvaṇādiṣu kārttikādiṣu māseṣu paramānnaṃ śubhe triṣu kāsāraṃ māghapūrveṣu yavānnaṃ ca tatas triṣu ghṛtaṃ tilāñ jalaghaṭān hiraṇyam athavājinam pratimāsaṃ tathā dadyād brāhmaṇāya śubhavrate yathoktaṃ niyamānāṃ ca grahaṇaṃ pratimāsikam kurvañ jagatpatir viṣṇuḥ prīyatām iti mānavaḥ yoṣid apy amalaprajñe vratam etad yathāvidhi karoti yā sā sakalān avāpnoti manorathān vratenārādhito viṣṇur anena jagataḥ patiḥ dadāty abhimatān kāmān alpakālena bhāmini dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ saubhāgyārogyadaṃ tathā vratam etat priyatamaṃ vratebhyo avyaktajanmanaḥ vratenānena śuddhānām abdenaikena keśavaḥ sukhadṛśyo na saṃdeho dīpenaivāgrataḥ sthitaḥ kāyavāṅmanaso śuddhiṃ karoty etan mahāvratam śuddhānāṃ cāmalo devo dṛśya eva janārdanaḥ tasminn ekāgracittānāṃ prāṇināṃ varavarṇini viprā eva prayatnena muktibhājo vibhūtayaḥ yathā kalpataruṃ prāpya yad yad icchati cetasā tat tat phalam avāpnoti tathā saṃprāpya taṃ vibhum śuddhivratam idaṃ tasmān mahāpātakanāśanam ārādhanāya kṛṣṇasya kuru devaki pāvanam tasmiṃś cīrṇe hṛṣīkeśas tubhyaṃ dāsyati darśanam dṛṣṭe cābhimataṃ yat te tad aśeṣaṃ bhaviṣyati devakī bhārgavasyaitac śrutvā vākyaṃ narādhipa śuddhikāmā cacārātha sarvakāmapradaṃ vratam vratenārādhitas tena tadā devyā janārdanaḥ dadau darśanam īśeśaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ dṛṣṭe tasminn aśeṣeśe jagaddhātari keśave kṛtvā praṇāmam āhedaṃ bhaktinamrātha devakī jagatām īśvareśeśa jñāna jñeya bhavāvyaya samastadevatādeva vāsudeva namo astu te pradhānapuṃsor ajayor yaḥ kāraṇam akāraṇam aviśeṣyam ajaṃ rūpaṃ tava tasmai namo astu te tvaṃ pradhānaṃ pumāṃś caiva kāraṇākāraṇātmakaḥ sad asac cākhilaṃ deva kenoktena tava stavaḥ prasīda deva devānām ariśātana vāmana lobhābhibhūtā yad ahaṃ varayāmi prayaccha tat aditis tvaṃ mahābhāge bhuvaṃ prāptā surāraṇi bhartā ca te kaśyapo ayaṃ deyas tava varo mayā aputrāsmi na me bhartur asti keśava saṃtatiḥ prasīda dehi me putram aridurdhārapauruṣam bhaviṣyaty acirād devi madaṃśena sutas tava hantavyā dānavās tena saddharmaparipanthinaḥ tvām ahaṃ jagaddhātāram udāroruparākramam dhārayiṣyāmi garbheṇa katham acyuta śaṃsa me tavodare avatāraṃ vai purāpi balibandhane kurvatā vidhṛtāḥ sapta lokās tvaṃ cātmamāyayā tathā sāṃpratam apy etāṃl lokān sasthāṇujaṅgamān dhārayiṣyāmy athātmānaṃ tvāṃ ca devaki līlayā ity evam uktvā tāṃ devīṃ devakīṃ bhagavān prabhuḥ tirobabhūva govindo bhūrbhuvaḥprabhavo vibhuḥ avāpa ca tato garbhaṃ devakī vasudevataḥ ajāyata ca viśveśaḥ svenāṅgena janārdanaḥ nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ tāmrāyatavilocanam caturbāhum udārāṅgaṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam taṃ jātaṃ devakī devaṃ nidhānaṃ sarvatejasām praṇipatyābhituṣṭāva saṃprastutapayodharā abālo bālarūpeṇa yeneśa tvam ihāsthitaḥ tvadrūpaṃ praṇipatyāhaṃ yad bravīmi nibodha tat namas te sarvabhūteśa namas te madhusūdana namas te puṇḍarīkākṣa namas te astu janārdana namas te śārṅgacakrāsi- gadāparighapāṇaye upendrāyāprameyāya hṛṣīkeśāya vai namaḥ namo astu te aṇurūpāya bṛhadrūpāya vai namaḥ aśeṣabhūtarūpāya tathārūpāya te namaḥ anirdeśyaviśeṣāya tubhyaṃ sarvātmane namaḥ sarveśvarāya sarvāya sarvabhūtāya te namaḥ namo astu te vāsudeva namo astu kamalekṣaṇa aśeṣabhūtarūpāya tathābhūtāya te namaḥ namo astu te aśvarūpāya tathārūpāya te namaḥ anirdeśyaviśeṣāya tubhyaṃ sarvātmane namaḥ namo astu te vāsudeva namas te puṣkarekṣaṇa namo astu te sadācintya yogicintya jagatpate viṣṇo namo astu te kṛṣṇa namas te puruṣottama namo nārāyaṇa hare namas te astu sadācyuta namo namas te govinda namas te garuḍadhvaja śrīśa śrīvatsa yogīśa śrīkānteśa namo astu te nīlotpaladalaśyāma daṃṣṭroddhṛtavasuṃdhara hiraṇyākṣaripo deva namas te yajñasūkara nṛsiṃha jaya viśvātman daityoraḥsthaladāraka namo namas te astu sadā vikṣepadhvastatāraka māyāvāmanarūpāya tubhyaṃ deva namo namaḥ trivikrama namas tubhyaṃ trailokyakrānti durjaya ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūtāya vedāharaṇakarmaṇe praṇavodgītavacase mahāśvaśirase namaḥ niḥkṣatriyorvīkaraṇa vikarālaparākrama jāmadagnya namas tubhyaṃ kārtavīryāsutaskara paulastyakulanāśāya sādhumārgavicāriṇe nalasetukṛte tubhyaṃ namo rāghavarūpiṇe sāṃprataṃ matprasannāya saṃbhūtāya mamodare svamāyābālarūpāya namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vai hare yāvanti tava rūpāṇi yāvatyaś ca vibhūtayaḥ namāmi kṛṣṇa sarvebhyas tebhyas tābhyaś ca sarvadā svarūpaceṣṭitaṃ yat te yad devatve viceṣṭitam yac ca tiryaṅmanuṣyatve ceṣṭitaṃ tan namāmy aham parameśa pareśeśa tiryagīśa nareśvara sarveśvareśvareśeśa namas te puruṣottama evaṃ stutas tayā devyā devakyā madhusūdanaḥ bālarūpī jagādaivaṃ vasudevasya śṛṇvataḥ samyag ārādhitenoktaṃ yat prasannena vai śubhe tat kṛtaṃ sakalaṃ bhūyo yad vṛṇoṣi dadāmi tat avatāre tathaivāsmin varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam sthāsyāmi naratāṃ prāpto duṣṭadaityanibarhaṇaḥ tat tvaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te varaṃ yan manasecchasi dāsyāmy aham asaṃdigdhaṃ yady api syāt sudurlabham yadi deva prasannas tvaṃ pradadāsi mamepsitam vṛṇomi tad ahaṃ nityaṃ tava keśava darśanam tavedṛgrūpam ālokya hārdaprasrutalocanā nālaṃ viyogaṃ saṃsoḍhuṃ tavāhaṃ madhusūdana dākṣāyaṇī tvam aditiḥ saṃbhūtā vasudhātale nityam eva jagaddhātri prasādaṃ te karomy aham ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā pakṣe dine asminn eva bhāmini tvaṃ māṃ drakṣyasy asaṃdigdhaṃ prasādas te kṛto mayā anenaiva mahābhāge bālarūpeṇa saṃvṛtaḥ tava darśanam eṣyāmi yatra te snehavan manaḥ tasmin kāle ca lokās tvāṃ pūjayiṣyanti devaki māṃ ca puṣpādibhir devi tavotsaṅgavyavasthitam saṃpūjito ahaṃ lokānāṃ tasmin kāle sutoṣitaḥ pradāsyāmi jagaddhātri yathābhilaṣitaṃ varam aputrāṇāṃ varān putrān adhanānāṃ tathā dhanam śubhān dārān adārāṇāṃ sarogāṇām arogatām sugatiṃ gatikāmānāṃ vidyāṃ vidyārthinām api pradāsyasi mahābhāge matprasādopavṛṃhitā prasāditā hi martyānāṃ yat tvaṃ dāsyasi śobhane tat teṣāṃ matprasādena bhaviṣyati na durlabham tvām abhyarcyopacāreṇa snāpayitvā ghṛtena mām sarvakāmān avāpsyanti kāle ṣaṭpakṣasaṃjñite tvadaṅkasthaṃ ca māṃ bālaṃ saṃsmariṣyanti bhaktitaḥ pratimāsaṃ ca te pūjām aṣṭamyāṃ yaḥ kariṣyati mama caivākhilān kāmān saṃprāpnoty apakalmaṣaḥ evaṃ pūrvaṃ hṛṣīkeśo devakyāḥ pradadau varam tasmāt kṛṣṇāṣṭamī puṃsām aśeṣāghaughahāriṇī tasyāṃ hi pūjitaḥ kṛṣṇo devakī ca samādhinā pāpāpanodaṃ kurute dadāti ca manorathān tad eṣa puṣṭikāmānāṃ nṝṇāṃ puṇyārthinām api upavāso mahīpāla śastaḥ keśavatoṣadaḥ śrāvaṇe śuklapakṣe tu dvādaśyāṃ prīyate nṛpa gopradānena govindo yat pūrvaṃ kathitaṃ tava pauṣaśukle tu tadvac ca dvādaśyāṃ ghṛtadhenukām ghṛtārciḥ prīṇanāyālaṃ pradadyāt phaladāyinīm tathaiva māghadvādaśyāṃ pradattā tilagaur nṛpa keśavaṃ prīṇayaty āśu sarvakāmān prayacchati jyaiṣṭhe māsi site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ jaladhenukā dattā yathāvad vidhinā prīṇayaty ambuśāyinam lavaṇaṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu kṛṣṇam abhyarcya yo naraḥ prayacchati dvijāgryāya sa sarvarasadāyakaḥ sarvabhogamahābhogān bhrājiṣmanto manoramān lokān avāpnoti nṛpa prasanne garuḍadhvaje pauṣamāse tu yo dadyād ghṛtaṃ viprāya pārthiva samabhyarcyācyutaṃ so api sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt māghamāse tu saṃpūjya mādhavaṃ brāhmaṇāya yaḥ prayacchati tilāṃl lokān saṃprāpnoty abhivāñchitān phālgune puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ yaḥ samabhyarcya yacchati saptadhānyaṃ naraśreṣṭha sa sarvasyeśvaro bhavet caitre citrāṇi vastrāṇi yaḥ prayacchati keśavam pūjayitvā sa vai bhogān vicitrāṃl labhate naraḥ vaiśākhe viṣṇum abhyarcya yavagodhūmado naraḥ lokān aindrān samāsādya modate vigatajvaraḥ durnivartyam ahaṃ manye cañcalaṃ hi mano yataḥ jyaiṣṭhe abhyarcya hṛṣīkeśam udakumbhaprado hi yaḥ sa parāṃ nirvṛtiṃ yāti sapta janmāntarāṇi vai āṣāḍhamāse ca hariṃ yaḥ samabhyarcya yacchati viprāya candanaṃ so api paramāhlādabhājanam yo nṛsiṃhaṃ samabhyarcya brāhmaṇāya prayacchati śrāvaṇe navanītaṃ tu sa svargaṃ sukṛtī vrajet chattraṃ ca yo bhādrapade vāsudevābhipūjakaḥ prayacchati dvijāgryāya sa cchattrādhipatir bhavet guḍaśarkarayā yuktaṃ modakaṃ ca prayacchati tathaivāśvayuje abhyarcya yo anantaṃ so amaro bhavet nārāyaṇaṃ samabhyarcya yaḥ prayacchati kārttike dīpakaṃ viprageheṣu vimānaṃ so adhirohati kāmyāny etāny aśeṣāṇi yaḥ saṃpūjya jagatpatim dānāni yacchati naraḥ sa saṃpūrṇamanorathaḥ sarvaśreṣṭhaḥ samastānāṃ bandhūnām āśrayo bhavet evaṃ sarvāṇi dānāni prīṇanāyācyutasya yaḥ prayacchati sa sarveṣāṃ phalānāṃ bhuvi bhājanam tasmān narendra viprebhyaḥ prīṇanāya jagadguroḥ prayacchaitāni dānāni yac cānyad dayitaṃ tava yadīcchasi punaḥ prāptuṃ bhūtim abhraṃśanīṃ nṛpa tadārādhaya govindaṃ nānyathā syur vibhūtayaḥ evaṃ vasiṣṭhena tadā māndhātā nṛpa bodhitaḥ saha patnyā mahīpālaḥ paritoṣaṃ paraṃ yayau jagāda ca mudā yuktaḥ praṇipatya purohitam saha patnyā naraśreṣṭhaḥ samutthāya varāsanāt dhig dhig vṛthaiva yātāni mamaitāni dināny aho anāsajya manaḥ kṛṣṇe viṣayāsaktacetasaḥ tā niśās te ca divasās te rtavas te ca vatsarāḥ narāṇāṃ saphalā yeṣu cintito bhagavān hariḥ cintyamānaḥ samastānāṃ pāpānāṃ hāṇido hi saḥ samutsṛjyākhilaṃ cintyaṃ so acyutaḥ kiṃ na cintyate kaṣṭaṃ muṣṭo asmi śiṣṭeṣu vidyamāneṣu mantriṣu parāṅmukhānāṃ govinde yat prāptaṃ paramaṃ vayaḥ evaṃ vinindya so atmānāṃ māndhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ cakārārādhane yatnaṃ devadevasya śārṅgitiṇaḥ tam ārādhya ca viśveśam upendram asureśvara prāpa siddhiṃ parāṃ pūrvaṃ dakṣaḥ prācetaso yathā tathā tvam api rājendra sarvabhāvena keśavam samārādhaya govindaṃ tam ārādhya na sīdati evaṃ sa daityarājendraḥ prahrādenāvabodhitaḥ balir ārādhane yatnaṃ cakre cakrabhṛtas tadā puṣpopahārair dhūpaiś ca tathā caivānulepanaiḥ vāsobhir bhūṣaṇaiḥ samyag brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥ japair homair vrataiś caiva yathoktaṃ puruṣarṣabha saha patnyā tathaiva tvaṃ samārādhaya keśavam bhagavaṃś cañcalaṃ cittaṃ manuṣyāṇām aharniśam viṣayāsaṅgadurduṣṭaṃ pāpāyaiva pravartate maunena vācikaṃ pāpaṃ puṃbhir brahman nivartyate śārīram apy akaraṇāt sunivartyaṃ mataṃ mama yat tv etan mānasaṃ pāpaṃ manuṣyais tan mahāmate durnivartyam ahaṃ manye cañcalaṃ hi mano yataḥ tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi manuṣyair durvicintitaiḥ yat smartavyaṃ ca japyaṃ ca mānasāghapraśāntaye tvadyukto ayam anupraśnaḥ sādhv etad bhavatoditam cañcalatvād dhi cittānāṃ mānasaṃ bahu pātakam bhūmau tṛṇam asaṃkhyātaṃ yathā ca divi tārakāḥ tathā pāpam asaṃkhyeyaṃ cetasā kriyate tu yat paradāraparadravya- parahiṃsāsu mānasam aharniśaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ sātatyena pravartate yady asyopaśamo rājan bhuvi na kriyate nṛbhiḥ tan nāsti narakottāro varṣakoṭīśatair api tad asya praśamāyālaṃ prāyaścittaṃ narādhipa śṛṇuṣva yena cittotthaṃ sadyaḥ pāpaṃ vyapohati oṃ namo vāsudevāya puruṣāya mahātmane hiraṇyaretase acintya- svarūpāyātivedhase viṣṇave jiṣṇave nityaṃ śāntāyānagharūpiṇe sarvasthityantakaraṇa- vratine pītavāsase nārāyaṇāya viśvāya viśveśāyeśvarāya ca namaḥ kamalakiñjalka- suvarṇamukuṭāya ca keśavāyātisūkṣmāya brahmamūrtimate namaḥ namaḥ paramakalyāṇa- kalyāṇāyātmayonaye janārdanāya devāya śrīdharāya sumedhase mahātmane vareṇyāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye smṛtamātrāghaghātāya kṛṣṇāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe namo natāya namreśair aśeṣair vāsavādibhiḥ namo māyāvine tubhyaṃ haraye harimedhase hiraṇyagarbhagarbhāya jagataḥ kāraṇātmane govindāyādibhūtāya śrādīnāṃ mahātmane namo bhūtātmabhūtāya ātmane paramātmane acyutāya namo nityam anantāya namo namaḥ dāmodarāya śucaye yajñeśāya namo namaḥ namo māyāpaṭacchanna- jagaddhāmne mahātmane hṛṣīkeśāya ceśāya sarvabhūtātmarūpiṇe dayālave namo nityaṃ kapilāya sumedhase saṃsārasāgarottāra- jñānapotapradāyine akuṇṭhamataye dhātre sargasthityantakarmaṇi karālasaumyarūpāya vaikuṇṭhāya namo namaḥ yathā hi vāsudeveti prokte naśyati pātakam tathā vilayam abhyetu mamaitad durvicintitam yathā na viṣṇubhakteṣu pāpam āpnoti saṃsthitim tathā vināśam abhyetu mamaitad durvicintitam smṛtamātro yathā viṣṇuḥ sarvaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohati tathā praṇāśam abhyetu mamaitad durvicintitam yathā sarvatrago viṣṇus tatra sarvaṃ ca saṃsthitam upayātu tathā nāśaṃ mamāghaṃ cittasaṃbhavam pāpaṃ praṇāśaṃ mama saṃprayātu yan mānasaṃ yac ca karomi vācā śārīram apy ācaritaṃ ca yan me smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve prayāntu doṣā mama nāśam āśu rāgādayaḥ kāraṇakāraṇeśe vijñānadīpāmalamārgadṛśye smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve bhavantu bhadrāṇi samastadoṣāḥ prayāntu nāśaṃ jagato akhilasya mayādya bhaktyā parameśvareśe smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve ye bhūtale ye divi ye antarikṣe rasātale prāṇigaṇāś ca kecit bhavantu te siddhiyujo mayādya smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve puṣyantu maitrīṃ viramantu rāgād ujjhantu lobhaṃ kṣamiṇo bhavantu ābrahmavṛkṣāntaragā mayādya smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve ye prāṇinaḥ kutracid atra santi brahmāṇḍamadhye parataś ca kecit te yāntu siddhiṃ paramāṃ mayādya smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve ajñānino jñānavido bhavantu praśāntibhājaḥ satatogracittāḥ kurvantu bhaktiṃ paramām anante matstotratuṣṭasya hareḥ prasādāt śṛṇvanti ye me paṭhatas tathānye paśyanti ye mām idam īrayantam devāsurādyā manujās tiraśco bhavantu te apy acyutayogabhājaḥ ye cāpi mūkā vikalendriyatvāc śṛṇvanti no naiva vilokayanti paśvādayaḥ kīṭapipīlikāś ca bhavantu te apy acyutayogabhājaḥ nāmasv anantasya ca kīrtiteṣu yad atra puṇyaṃ jagataḥ prasūteḥ tenāvivekopahatātmabodhā bhavantu puṃsāṃ matayaḥ suśīlāḥ ye duḥkhitās te sukhino bhavantu dveṣānvitā maitraguṇopapannāḥ satyārjavādyās tv anṛtā vimāyā matsaṃstavārādhitakṛṣṇadṛṣṭāḥ naśyantu duḥkhāni jagaty apaitu lobhādiko doṣaguṇaḥ prajābhyaḥ yathātmani bhrātari cātmaje ca tathā janasyāstu jane api hārdam saṃsāravaidye akhiladoṣahāni- vicakṣaṇe nirvṛtihetubhūte saṃsārabandhāḥ śithilībhavantu hṛdi sthite sarvajanasya viṣṇau etat paṭhan pārthiva sarvapāpair vimucyate viṣṇuparaḥ sadaiva prāpnoti siddhiṃ vipulaṃ maharddhim na cāpy anartheṣu matiṃ karoti uddiśya sattvāni ca yāni yāni stotraṃ paṭhante kṛpayā manuṣyāḥ sarvāṇi tāny apratighā bhavanti prayānti siddhiṃ bhagavatprasādāt tasmāt tvayaitat satataṃ niśāsu dineṣu caiveśvara mādhavasya saṃkīrtanaṃ kāryam aśeṣapāpa- vimokṣahetor abhavāya caiva iti sakalajanopakārakārī haricaraṇābjaviniṣṭaśuddhabuddhiḥ paṭhati khalu mahīpa yo manuṣyaḥ sa layam upaiti harau hṛtākhilāghaḥ idaṃ ca śṛṇu bhūpāla naśyate durvicintitam yenopāyena vai puṃsāṃ yoṣitāṃ vāpy asaṃśayam paradāraparadravya- jīvahiṃsādike sadā pravartate nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ tad etad abhisaṃsmaret viṣṇave viṣṇave nityaṃ viṣṇave viṣṇave namaḥ jiṣṇave jiṣṇave sarvaṃ jiṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ namāmi viṣṇuṃ buddhistham ahaṃkāra-gataṃ harim cittastham īśam avyaktam anantam aparājitam viṣṇum īḍyam aśeṣeśam anādinidhanaṃ vibhum viṣṇuś cittagato yan me viṣṇur buddhigataś ca yat yac cāhaṃkārago viṣṇur yad viṣṇur mayi saṃsthitaḥ karoti kartṛbhūto asau sthāvarasya carasya ca tat pāpaṃ nāśam āyātu tasminn eva vicintite dhyāto harati yaḥ pāpaṃ svapne dṛṣṭaḥ śubhāvahaḥ tam upendram ahaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato artiharaṃ harim jagaty asmin nirādhāre majjamāne tamasy adhaḥ hastāvalambadaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇato asmi parātparam sarveśvareśvara vibho paramātmann adhokṣaja hṛṣīkeśa hṛṣīkeśa hṛṣīkeśa namo astu te nṛsiṃhānanta govinda bhūtabhāvana keśava duruktaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ dhyātaṃ praśamāgrya namo astu te yan mayā cintitaṃ duṣṭaṃ svacittavaśavartinā narakāvaham atyugraṃ tac chamaṃ naya keśava brahmaṇyadeva govinda paramārtha parāyaṇa jagannātha jagaddhātaḥ pāpaṃ praśamayācyuta yac cāparāhne pūrvāhne madhyāhne ca tathā niśi kāyena manasā vācā kṛtaṃ pāpam ajānatā jānatā vā hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mādhava nāmatrayoccāraṇatas tat prayātu mama kṣayam śārīraṃ me hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mānasam pāpaṃ praśamayādya tvaṃ vākkṛtaṃ mama mādhava yad vrajan yat svapan bhuñjan yad uttiṣṭhan yad āsthitaḥ kṛtavāṃś cāpi yac cāhaṃ kāyena manasā girā mahat svalpam atisthūlaṃ kuyoninarakāvaham tad yātu praśamaṃ sarvaṃ vāsudevasya kīrtanāt paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma pavitraṃ paramaṃ ca yat tasmin saṃkīrtite viṣṇoḥ pade pāpaṃ praṇaśyatu sūrayo yat pravekṣyanti hy apunarbhavakāṅkṣiṇaḥ mamākhilaṃ daha tvaṃ hi tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam yat prāpya na ninvartante gandhasparśādivarjitam pāpaṃ praṇāśayatv adya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam sadasad yat tathā vyaktā- vyaktarūpam ajājaram praṇamāmi jagaddhāma tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam śārīre mānase caiva pāpe vāgje ca pārthiva kṛte samyaṅ naro bhaktyā paṭhec chraddhāsamanvitaḥ mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ kṛṣṇanāmaprakīrtanāt uccāryamāne caitasmin devadevasya saṃstave vilayaṃ pāpam āyāti bhāṇḍam āmam ivāmbhasi tasmāt saṃcintite pāpe samanantaram eva te japtavyam etat pāpasya praśamāya mahīpate saṃsārārṇavamagnena puruṣeṇa mahāmune viṣayāsaktacittena yat kāryaṃ tad vadasva me bhrāmyatāṃ saṃkaṭe durge saṃsāre viṣayaiṣiṇām svakarmabhir manuṣyāṇām upakārakam ucyatām kṣīpte manasy anāyatte vṛddhe lobhādike gaṇe śaraṇaṃ yan manuṣyāṇāṃ tad ācakṣva mahāmune saṃsārāṇavapotāya haraye harimedhase namaskṛtya pravakṣyāmi narāṇām upakārakam samyag ārādhito bhaktyā vedabhāraguror guruḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prāha yac chiṣyāya sumantave purā kila durācāro durbuddhir ajitendriyaḥ kṣatrabandhur abhūt pāpaḥ paramarmāvaghaṭṭakaḥ mātāpitror aśuśrūṣur drogdhā bandhujanasya ca gurudevadvijātīnāṃ nindāsu satatodyataḥ moṣṭā viśvasatāṃ nityam aprītiḥ prītim icchatām ṛjūnām anṛjuḥ kṣudraḥ parahiṃsāparāyaṇaḥ sa bāndhavaiḥ parityaktas tathānyaiḥ sādhuvṛttibhiḥ avṛttimān aviśvāsyo mṛgayājīvano abhavat ahany ahani cakrāṅgān eṇakādīṃs tathā mṛgān hatvātmapoṣaṇaṃ cakre vyādhavṛttirato adhamaḥ etayā tasya duṣṭasya kuvṛttyā pāpacetasaḥ jagāma sumahān kālaḥ kurvato dārapoṣaṇam ekadā tu munis tena nidāghe vijane vane mṛgayām aṭatā dṛṣṭo vartmanaḥ pracyutaḥ pathi kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhaḥ suśrāntaḥ śuṣkajihvāsyatālukaḥ tṛṭparīto ativibhrāntaḥ kāṃdigbhūto alpacetanaḥ śvāsāyāsaślathair aṅgaiḥ kṛcchrād ātmānam udvahan sūryāṃśutāpāt pragalat- svedārdracaraṇo nṛpa tasmin dṛṣṭe tatas tasya kṣatrabandhor ajāyata kāruṇyaṃ dāruṇasyāpi vyādhavṛttiparigrahāt tam upetya ca bhūpāla kṣatrabandhuḥ sa tāpasam uvāca viprapravaraṃ vimārge vartate bhavān naiṣa panthā dvijaśreṣṭha vipino ayaṃ mahāṭaviḥ mām anvehi tvarāyukto mā vipattiṃ sameṣyasi niśāmya tad vacaḥ śrāntaḥ kṣatrabandhor mahānuniḥ anuvavrāja rājendra jalāśājanitodyamaḥ kiṃcid bhūbhāgam āsādya dadarśa ca mahāmuniḥ haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaṃ protphullanalinaṃ saraḥ sārasābhirutaṃ ramyaṃ sūpatīrtham akardamam padmotpalayutaṃ cāru pūrṇaṃ svacchena vāriṇā suśītavanaṣaṇḍaiś ca samantāt pariveṣṭitam tatkṣaṇāt tṛṭparītānāṃ cakṣuṣo hlādakāriṇam dṛṣṭvaiva sa munis tatra tadāmalajalaṃ saraḥ sūryāṃśutapto gharmārto nipapāta tadambhasi tatrāśvāsya kṛtāhlādaḥ papau vāri narādhipa ujjīvayan munivaro jihvātālu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ so api kṣatriyadāyādo munitrāṇaparāyaṇaḥ vihāya saśaraṃ cāpam ujjahāra bisāny atha dadau ca tasmai rājendra kṣudhitāya tapasvine yayau ca tṛptiṃ vipro api bisanālāmbubhakṣaṇāt tam āśvastaṃ kṛtāhāram upaviṣṭaṃ suśītale nyagrodhaśākhāsaṃchanne niṣpaṅke sarasas taṭe saṃvāhayām āsa ca taṃ kṣatrabandhuḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ pādajaṅghorupṛṣṭeṣu tena saṃvāhito muniḥ jahau śramam amitraghna vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha kas tvaṃ bhadramukhādyeha mama prāṇaparikṣaye hastāvalambado dhātrā janito vipine vane vibhraṣṭamārgo mūḍho ahaṃ kṣutpipāsāśramāturaḥ trātas tvayā mahābhāga kas tvam atra vane ajane kṣutpipāsāśramārtasya yas trāṇaṃ vipine vane karoti puruṣavyāghra tasya lokā madhuścyutaḥ sa tvaṃ brūhi mahābhāga mamābhyuddhārakārakaḥ yeṣāṃ prakhyātayaśasāṃ samutpannaḥ kule bhavān haryaśvasya kule jātaḥ putraś citrarathasya ca vimatir nāma nāmnāhaṃ hantum abhyāgato mṛgān pitrarthaṃ mṛgayeyaṃ te lakṣyārthaṃ vā mahāmate āhārārtham utāho atra mṛgayā vyasanaṃ tu te vṛttir eṣā mama brahman parityaktasya bāndhavaiḥ bhṛtyair anyaiś ca naṣṭe arthe nirdhanasyāmiṣāśinaḥ kimarthaṃ tvaṃ parityakto bhṛtyasvajanabandhubhiḥ pātakī kīkaṭaḥ kṣudrair upajaptaḥ pareṇa vā ity uktaḥ so abhavan maunī paśyan doṣaṃ nṛpātmani aduṣṭāṃś cātmano bhṛtyān vicintyātīva durmanāḥ avekṣya taṃ sādhvasinaṃ kṣatrabandhuṃ mahāmuniḥ dhyātvā ciram athāpaśyat kṣatrabandhuṃ svadoṣiṇam saṃtyaktabandhuloke ca tasmin durvṛttacetasi kṛpāṃ cakāra sa muniḥ kṣatrabandhau dayāparaḥ uvāca ca munir bhūyaḥ kṣatrabandhuṃ kṛpālukaḥ upakāriṇam ugreṇa karmaṇā taṃ vidūṣitam api śaknoṣi saṃyantum akāryaprasṛtaṃ manaḥ prāṇi pīḍānivṛttiṃ ca kartuṃ krodhādisaṃyamam api maitrīṃ jane kartuṃ śaknoṣi tvaṃ mudhaiva yā aihikāmuṣmikī vīra kriyamāṇā mahāphalā na śaknomi kṣamāṃ kartuṃ na maitrīṃ mama cetasi prāṇinām avadhād brahman nāsti dārādipoṣaṇam anāyattaṃ ca me cittaṃ viṣayān eva dhāvati tadaprāptau ca sarveṣāṃ krodhādīnāṃ samudbhavaḥ so ahaṃ na maitrīṃ na kṣāntiṃ na hiṃsādivivarjanam kartuṃ śaknomi yat kāryaṃ tadanyad upadiśyatām tenaivam ukto vipro asau tam upekṣyam amanyata tathāpy atikṛpālutvāt kṣatrabandhum abhāṣata yady etad akhilaṃ kartuṃ na śaknoṣi bravīhi me svalpam anyan mayoktaṃ hi kariṣyati bhavān yadi aśakyam uktaṃ bhavatā cañcalatvād dhi cetasaḥ vākśarīraviniṣpādyaṃ yac chakyaṃ tad udīraya uttiṣṭhatā prasvapatā prasthitena gamiṣyatā govindeti sadā vācyaṃ kṣutapraskhalitādiṣu kāryaṃ vartmani mūḍhānāṃ kṣemamārge avatāraṇam hitaṃ ca vācyaṃ pṛṣṭena śatrūṇām api jānatā etat tavopakārāya bhaviṣyaty anupālitam yady anyad upasaṃhartuṃ na śaknoṣi mahīpate ity uktvā prayayau vipras tena vartmani darśite so api tac chāsanaṃ sarvaṃ kṣatrabandhuś cakāra ha govindeti kṣute gacchan prasthānaskhalitādiṣu udīrayann avāpāgryāṃ ratiṃ tatra śanaiḥ śanaiḥ tataḥ kālena mahatā kṣatrabandhur mamāra vai ajāyata ca viprasya kule jātismaro nṛpa tasya saṃsmarato jātīḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ nirvedaḥ sumahāñ jajñe saṃsāre atrātiduḥkhade sa cintayām āsa jagat sarvam etad acetanam aham eko atra saṃjñāvān govindodīritaṃ hi yat yac cādhvani vimūḍhānāṃ kṛtaṃ vartmāvatāraṇam hitam uktaṃ ca pṛṣṭena tasya jātismṛtiḥ phalam so ahaṃ jātismaro bhūyaḥ kariṣyāmy atisaṃkaṭe tadā saṃsāracakre asmin yena prāpsyāmi nirvṛtim yasyoccāraṇamātreṇa jātā jātismṛtir mama tam evārādhayiṣyāmi jagatām īśvaraṃ harim yanmayaṃ paramaṃ brahma tad avyaktaṃ ca yanmayam yanmayaṃ vyaktam apy etad bhaviṣyāmi hi tanmayaḥ yady anārādhite viṣṇau mamaitaj janma yāsyati dhruvaṃ bandhavato muktir naiva jātūpapadyate aho duḥkham aho duḥkham aho duḥkham atīva hi svarūpam atighorasya saṃsārasyātidurlabham viṇmūtrapūyakalile garbhavāse atipīḍanāt aśucāv atibībhatse duḥkham atyantaduḥsaham duḥkhaṃ ca jāyamānānāṃ gātrabhaṅgādipīḍanāt vātena preryamāṇānāṃ mūrchākāry atibhītidam bālatve nirvivekānāṃ bhūtadevātmasaṃbhavam yauvane vārddhake caiva maraṇe cātidāruṇam śītoṣṇatṛṣṇākṣudroga- jvarādiparivāritaḥ sarvadaiva pumān āste yāvaj janmāntasaṃsthitiḥ duḥkhātiśayabhūtaṃ hi yad ante vāsukhaṃ nṛṇām tasyānumānaṃ naivāsti kāryeṇaivānumīyate kṛṣyamāṇasya puruṣair yad yamasyātiduḥsaham duḥkhaṃ tatsaṃsmṛtiprāptaṃ karoti mama vepathum kumbhīpāke taptakumbhe mahārauravaraurave kālasūtre mahāyantre śūkare kūṭaśālmalau asipatravane duḥkham apratiṣṭhe ca yan mahat viḍālavaktre ca tathā tamasy ugre ca duḥsaham śastrāgniyantravegeṣu śītoṣṇādiṣu dāruṇam tataś ca muktasya punar yonisaṃkramaṇeṣu yat garbhasthasya ca yad duḥkham atiduḥsaham ulvaṇam punaś ca jāyamānasya janma yauvanajaṃ ca yat duḥkhāny etāny asahyāni saṃsārāntarvivartibhiḥ puruṣair anubhūyante sukhabhrāntivimohitaiḥ na vai sukhakalā kācit tatrāsty atyantaduḥkhade saṃsārasaṃkaṭe tīvre upetānāṃ kadācana viṣayāsaktacittānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ kadā matiḥ saṃsārottāraṇe vāñchāṃ kariṣyati hi cañcalā govindanāmnā satataṃ samuccāraṇasaṃbhavam jātismaratvam etan naḥ kiṃ vṛthaiva prayāsyati so ahaṃ muktipradānārtham anantam ajam avyayam taccittas tanmayo bhūtvā toṣayiṣyāmi keśavam ātmānam ātmanaivaṃ sa proktvā jātismaro dvijaḥ tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ praṇataḥ puruṣottamam praṇipatyākṣaraṃ viśvaṃ viśvahetuṃ nirañjanam yat prārthayāmy avikalaṃ sakalaṃ tat prayacchatu kartāram akṛtaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam aṇor aṇīyāṃsam ajaṃ sarvavyāpinam īśvaram parāt parataraṃ yasmān nāsti sarveśvarāt param taṃ praṇamyācyutaṃ devaṃ prārthayāmi yad astu tat sarveśvarācyutānanta paramātmañ janārdana saṃsārābdhimahāpota samuddhara mahārṇavāt vyomānilāgnyambudharāsvarūpa tanmātrasarvendriyabuddhirūpa antaḥsthitātman paramātmarūpa prasīda sarveśvara viśvarūpa tam ādir anto jagato asya madhyam ādes tvam ādiḥ pralayasya cāntaḥ tvatto bhavaty etad aśeṣam īśa tvayy eva cānte layam abhyupaiti pradīpavartyantagato agnir alpo yathātikakṣe vitataṃ prayāti tadvad visṛṣṭer amarādibhinnair vikāśam āyāsi vibhūtibhedaiḥ yathā nadīnāṃ bahavo ambuvegāḥ samantato abdhiṃ bhagavan viśanti tvayy antakāle jagad acyutedaṃ tathā layaṃ gacchati sarvabhūte tvaṃ sarvam etad bahudhaika eva jagatpate kāryam ivābhyupetam yad asti yan nāsti ca tat tvam eva hare tvadanyad bhagavan kim asti kiṃtv īśa māyā bhavato nijeyam āviṣkṛtāviṣkṛtalokasṛṣṭe yayāham eṣo anyatamo mameti madīyam asyābhivadanti mūḍhāḥ tayā vimūḍhena mayābhanābha na yat kṛtaṃ tat kvacid asti kiṃcit bhūmyambarāgnisalileṣu deva jāgratsuṣuptādiṣu duḥkhitena na santi tāvanti jalāny apīḍya sarveṣu nāthābdhiṣu sarvakālam stanyāni yāvanti mayātighore pītāni saṃsāramahāsamudre saṃpac chilānāṃ himavanmahendra- kailāsamervādiṣu naiva tādṛk dehāny anekāny anugṛhṇato me prāptāsthisaṃpan mahati yatheśa tvayy arpitaṃ nātha punaḥ punar me manaḥ samākṣipya sudurdharo api rāgo hi vaśyaṃ kurute tato anu lobhādayaḥ kiṃ bhagavan karomi ekāgratāmūlyabalena labhyaṃ bhavauṣadhaṃ tvaṃ bhagavan kilaikaḥ manaḥ parāyattam idaṃ bhave asmin saṃsāraduḥkhāt kim ahaṃ karomi na santi te deva bhuvi pradeśā na yeṣu jāto asmi tathā vinaṣṭaḥ attā mayā yeṣu na jantavaś ca saṃbhakṣito yaiś ca na jantusaṃghaiḥ siṃhena bhūtvā bahavo mayāttā vyāghreṇa bhūtvā bahavo mayāttāḥ tathānyarūpair bahavo mayāttāḥ saṃbhakṣito ahaṃ bahubhis tataś ca utkrāntiduḥkhāny atiduḥsahāni sahasraśo yāny anusaṃsmarāmi taiḥ saṃsmṛtais tat kṣaṇam eva deva taḍid yathā me hṛdayaṃ prayāti tataś ca duḥkhāny anivāraṇāni yantrāgniśastraughasamudbhavāni bhavanti yāny acyuta nārakānāṃ tāny eva teṣām upamānamātram duḥkhāny asahyāni ca garbhavāse viṇmūtramadhye atinipīḍitasya bhavanti yāni cyavataś ca garbhāt teṣāṃ svarūpaṃ gadituṃ na śakyam duḥkhāni bāleṣu mahanti nātha kaumārake yauvaninaś ca puṃsaḥ jvarātisārākṣirugādikāni samastaduḥkhālaya eva vṛddhaḥ karoti karmācyuta tatkṣaṇena pāpaṃ naraḥ kāyamanovacobhiḥ yasyābdalakṣair api nāntam eti śastrādiyantrāgninipīḍaneṣu duḥkhāni yānīṣṭaviyogajāni bhavanti saṃsāravihārabhājām pratyekaśas teṣu narā vināśam icchanty asūnāṃ mamatābhibhūtāḥ śokābhibhūtasya mamāśru deva yāvatpramāṇaṃ na jalaṃ payodā tāvatpramāṇaṃ na jalaṃ payodā muñcanty anekair api varṣalakṣaiḥ manye dharitrī paramāṇusaṃkhyām upaiti pitror gaṇanāmaśeṣam mitrāṇy amitrāṇy anujīvibandhūn saṃkhyātam īśo asmi na devadeva so ahaṃ bhṛśārtaḥ karuṇāṃ kuru tvaṃ saṃsāragātre patitasya viṣṇo mahātmanāṃ saṃśrayam abhyupeto naivāvasīdaty atidurgato api parāyaṇaṃ rogavatāṃ hi vaidyo mahābdhimagnasya ca naur narasya bālasya mātāpitarau sughora- saṃsārakhinnasya hare tvam ekaḥ prasīda sarveśvara sarvabhūta sarvasya heto paramārthasāra mām uddharāsmād uruduḥkhapaṅkāt saṃsāragartāt svaparigraheṇa dharmātmanām avikalāṃ tvayi nātha bhaktiṃ śraddhāvatāṃ satatam udvahatāṃ vareṇya kāryaṃ kiyan mama vimūḍhadhiyo adhamasya bhūtvā kṛpālur amalām aja dehi buddhim jñātvā yayākhilam asāram asāram eva bhūtendriyādikam apāram amuktimūlam māyāntareyam acalāṃ tava viśvarūpa saṃmohitaṃ sakalam eva jagad yayaitat brahmendrarudramarudaśvidivākarādyā jñātuṃ na yaṃ paramaguhyatamaṃ samarthāḥ na tvām alaṃ stutipatheṣv aham īśitāraṃ stoṣyāmi mohakaluṣālpamatir manuṣyaḥ yasmād idaṃ bhavati yatra jagat tathedaṃ yasmiṃl layaṃ vrajati yaś ca jagatsvarūpaḥ taṃ sargasaṃsthitivināśanimittabhūtaṃ stotuṃ bhavantam alam īśa na kaścid asti mūḍho ayam alpamatir alpasuceṣṭito ayaṃ kliṣṭaṃ mano asya viṣayair na mayi prasaṅgi itthaṃ kṛpāṃ kuru mayi praṇate kileśa tvāṃ stotum ambujabhavo api hi deva neśaḥ yasyodare sakala eva mahīdhracandra- devendrarudramarudaśvidivākarāgni- bhūmyambuvāyugaganaṃ jagatāṃ samuhāṃ stoṣyāmi taṃ stutipadaiḥ katamair bhavantam yasyāgnirudrakamalodbhavavāsavādyaiḥ svāṃśāvatārakaraṇeṣu sadāṅghriyugmam abhyarcyate vada hare sa kathaṃ mayādya saṃpūjitaḥ param upaiṣyasi toṣam īśa na stotum acyuta bhavantam ahaṃ samartho naivārcanair alam ahaṃ tava deva yogyaḥ cittaṃ ca na tvayi samāhitam īśa doṣair ākṣipyate kathaya kiṃ nu karomi pāpaḥ tat tvaṃ prasīda bhagavan kuru mayy anāthe viṣṇo kṛpāṃ paramakāruṇikaḥ kila tvam saṃsārasāgaranimagnam ananta dīnam uddhartum arhasi hare puruṣottamo asi itthaṃ tena naravyāghra stuto bhaktimatā tataḥ saṃsārabandhabhītena kṛṣṇaḥ pratyakṣatāṃ yayau sa taṃ pratyakṣam īśānam anantam aparājitam devadevam uvācedam anādinidhanaṃ harim śirasā dharaṇīṃ gatvā yatavākkāyamānasaḥ parāpareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇum ādyam anopamam divyākṣarapadānanta prasanno bhagavān yadi tad deva dehi dīnāya mahyam ekam imaṃ varam varaṃ varaya mattas tvaṃ yat te manasi vartate varārthināṃ dvijaśreṣṭha nāphalaṃ mama darśanam janmasaṃpaccitā deva pāpasaṃpan mamākhilā prayātu nāśam īśeśa tvatprasādād adhokṣaja bhaktibhāvapareṇādya manmayena dvijottama yaḥ stuto asmi kṣayaṃ pāpaṃ tenaivākhilam āgatam asmatto varayehādya dvijavaryāparaṃ varam mayi bhaktimatām atra loke kiṃcin na durlabham dhanyo asmi sarvanāthena yatkṛto mayy anugrahaḥ tad ekam eva tvatto ahaṃ varam icchāmi keśava nirdhūtasarvapāpebhyo nātha puṇyakṣayān mama tvatparasyāstu govinda mā punar dehasaṃbhavaḥ yad akṣaraṃ yad acalaṃ vyāpi sūkṣmaṃ ca yat param viśeṣāir aviśeṣaṃ ca gaccheyaṃ tat padaṃ tava evaṃ bhaviṣyatīty uktvā prasādasumukhas tataḥ bhūpāla taṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ gato antardhānam īśvaraḥ tatprasādād dvijaḥ so api tanmayas tadvyapāśrayaḥ prakṣīṇakarmabandhas tu prayātaḥ paramaṃ padam evam akṣīṇapāpo api jagatām īśvareśvaram vyapāśrito hariṃ yāti pāpamuktaḥ paraṃ padam etat tvayā nāvratine na cāśuśrūṣave param ākhyeyaṃ rājaśārdūla yaś ca nārcayate harim viṣṇubhaktāya dāntāya vratine puṇyaśīline kathanīyam idaṃ bhūpa rahasyaṃ paramaṃ hareḥ bahuśo bhavatā proktaṃ sāṃprataṃ ca yad īritam śrotum icchāmi viprendra tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam yatsvarūpaṃ yadādhāraṃ yatpramāṇaṃ yadātmakam sarvadhātuḥ padaṃ tan me śrotum icchā pravartate sādhv etad bhavatā pṛṣṭaṃ pṛṣṭam ātmajñānasamāśritam tat kathyamānam ekāgraḥ śṛṇu viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam yat tad brahma yataḥ sarvaṃ yad sarvaṃ sarvasaṃsthitiḥ agrāhyakam anirdeśyaṃ tad eva bhagavatpadam tatsvarūpaṃ ca rājendra śṛṇuṣveha samāhitaḥ viṣṇoḥ padasyāvyayasya brahmaṇo gadato mama pradhānādiviśeṣāntaṃ yad etat paṭhyate jagat carācarasya tasyādyaṃ paraṃ brahma vilakṣaṇam janmasvapnādirūpādi- duḥkhādirahitaṃ ca yat nopacaryam anirdeśyaṃ svapratiṣṭhaṃ ca tat param kṣīṇakleśās tu saṃsāra- vimuktipatham āśritāḥ yoginas tat prapaśyanti samarthā naiva coditum tat sarvaṃ sarvabhāvasthaṃ viśeṣeṇa vivarjitam paśyatām apy anirdeśyaṃ yato vāgviṣaye na tat kurvanty ālambanatvena yatprāptyarthaṃ ca devatāḥ brahma prakāśate teṣāṃ tad vareṇaiva sarvagam pradhānādiviśeṣāntaṃ yatraitad akhilaṃ jagat tasyānantasya kaḥ śaktaḥ pramāṇaṃ gadituṃ naraḥ sūkṣmāṇāṃ tat paraṃ sūkṣmaṃ sthūlānāṃ tan mahattaram sarvavyāpy api rājendra dūrasthaṃ cāntike ca tat parāṅmukhānāṃ govinde viṣayākrāntacetasām teṣāṃ tat paramaṃ brahma dūrād dūratare sthitam na prāpnuvanti gacchanto yato janmāyutair api saṃsārādhvani rājendra tato dūratare hi tat tanmayatvena govinde ya narā nyastacetasaḥ viṣayatyāginas teṣāṃ vijñeyaṃ ca tadantike sarvataḥ pāṇipādāntaṃ sarvato akṣiśiromukham sarvataḥ śrutimal loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati sarvendriyagunābhāsaṃ sarvendriyavivarjitam asaktaṃ sarvabhṛc cainan nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ ca avibhaktaṃ ca bhūteṣu vibhaktam iva ca sthitam bhūtabhartṛ ca taj jñeyaṃ grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca jyotiṣām api taj jyotis tamasaḥ param ucyate jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānagamyaṃ hṛdi sarvasy adhiṣṭhitam tac cādyo jagatām īśaḥ pareśaḥ parameśvaraḥ parāparasvarūpeṇa viṣṇuḥ sarvahṛdi sthitaḥ yajñeśaṃ yajñapuruṣaṃ kecid icchanti tatparam kecid viṣṇuṃ hariṃ kecit kecit keśavasaṃjñitam kecid govindanāmānaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam kecij janārdanaṃ tv anye vadanti puruṣottamam kecid viriñciṃ brāhmaṇam abjayoniṃ tathāpare śarvam īśam ajaṃ rudraṃ śūlinaṃ cāpare nṛpa varuṇaṃ kecid ādityam indram agnim athāpare yamaṃ dhaneśam apare somam anye prajāpatim hiraṇyagarbhaṃ kapilaṃ kṣetrajñaṃ kālam īśvaram svabhāvam antarātmānam ātmānaṃ buddhirūpiṇam vadanti nāmabhiś cānyair anāmānam arūpiṇam śrūyatāṃ tu naravyāghra vedavedāntaniścayaḥ yajñeśo yajñapuruṣo puṇḍarīkākṣasaṃjñitaḥ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ brahma yato nāvartate punaḥ sa eva rudraś candro agniḥ sūryo vaiśravaṇo yamaḥ brahmā prajāpatiḥ kālaḥ svabhāvo buddhir eva ca kṣetrajñākhyas tathaivānyāḥ saṃjñābhiḥ procyate budhaiḥ saṃjñā tu tasya naivāsti na rūpaṃ nāpi kalpanā sa sarvabhūtānugataḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ ākhyātaṃ bhavatā brahmann etad brahma sanātanam yasmād utpadyate kṛtsnaṃ jagad etac carācaram kiṃtu kautukam atrāsti mama bhārgavanandana tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi tvattaḥ saṃdeham uttamam yad etad bhavatākhyātaṃ brahma brahmavidāṃ vara pariṇāmo na tasyāsti nirguṇaṃ sarvagaṃ yataḥ sanātanāt sarvagatāt pariṇāmavivarjitāt kathaṃ saṃjāyate kṛtsnaṃ tasmād apaguṇād api dvividhaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhūpa nibodha gadato mama nimittakāraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ dvitīyaṃ pariṇāmi ca yathā kumbhasya karaṇe kulālaḥ prathamaṃ nṛpa kāraṇaṃ pariṇāmākhyaṃ mṛddravyam aparaṃ smṛtam dharmādharmādayas tadvaj jagatsṛṣṭer mahīpate kāraṇaṃ pariṇāmākhyaṃ nimittākhyaṃ tu tat param kāraṇaṃ kālagagane yathā saṃnidhimātrataḥ avikāritayā brahma tathā sṛṣṭer nareśvara ajñānapaṭalācchanair ekadeśātmavṛttibhiḥ anātmavedibhir jīvair nijakarmanibandhanaiḥ kurvadbhir nṛpate karma kartṛtvam upacārataḥ kriyate sarvabhūtasya sarvagasyāvyayātmanaḥ yataḥ saṃbandhavān ebhir aśeṣaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ prabhuḥ kartṛtvam upacāreṇa tatas tasyāpi bhūpate bhedābhedasvarūpeṇa tatra brahma vyavasthitam tayoḥ svarūpaṃ nṛpate śrūyatām ubhayor api anādisaṃbandhavatyā kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetravidyayā vyāptaḥ paśyaty abhedena brahma tad dhy ātmani sthitam paśyatv ātmānam anyatra yāvad vai paramātmanaḥ tāvat saṃbhrāmyate jantur mohito nijakarmaṇā saṃkṣīnāśeṣakarmā tu paraṃ brahma prapaśyati abhedenātmanaḥ śuddhaṃ śuddhatvād akṣayo akṣayam bhedaś ca karmajanitaḥ kṣetrajñaparamātmanoḥ saṃkṣīṇakarmabandhasya na bhedo brahmaṇā saha upāsyopāsyakatayā bhedo yair api kathyate tau hi śuddhyartham icchanti malānāṃ tad upāsanam paro asāv apareṇātmā saṃtyaktamamatena tu upāsyate tadā so api tadbhāvaṃ pratipadyate karmiṇāṃ karmabhedena bhedād evādayo yataḥ karmakṣayād aśeṣāṇāṃ bhedānāṃ saṃkṣayas tataḥ avidyā tu kriyā sarvā vidyā jñānaṃ pracakṣate karmaṇā jāyate jantur vidyayā tu vimucyate advaitaṃ paramārtho hi dvaitaṃ tadbheda ucyate ubhayaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ dvaitādvaitavibhedataḥ tayoḥ svarūpaṃ vadato nibodha mama pārthiva devatiryaṅmanuṣyākhyas tathaiva nṛpa tārakaḥ caturvidho hi bhedo yo mithyājñānanibandhanaḥ aham anyo aparaś cāyam amī cātra tathāpare vijñānam etat tad dvaitaṃ yad anyac chrūyatāṃ param mametyahamitiprajñā- viyuktam avikalpavat avikāram anākhyeyam advaitam api bhūpate abhedena tavākhyātaṃ yad etad brahma śāśvatam jñānajñeyaikyasadbhāvaṃ tad evādvaitasaṃjñitam yaś ca dvaite prapañcaḥ syān nivartyobhayacetasaḥ manovṛttimayaṃ dvaitam advaitaṃ paramārthataḥ manaso vṛttayas tasmād dharmādharmanimittajāḥ nirodhavyās tannirodhād dvaitaṃ naivopapadyate manodṛśyam idaṃ dvaitaṃ yat kiṃcit sacarācaram manaso hy amatībhāve dvaitābhāvāt tad āpnuyāt mano hi viṣayaṃ yadvad ādatte tadvad eva tat bhavaty apāstaviṣayaṃ grāhidharme ca jāyate agrāhi tac ca vidhṛtaṃ yogināṃ viṣayaṃ prati nirodhe yogasāmarthyād brahmagrāhy eva jāyate grāhyaṃ ca paramaṃ brahma yogicittasya pārthiva samujjhitagrāhyavṛttir amalasya malaṃ mahat kṣīṇakleśās tu saṃsāra- vimuktipatham āśritāḥ ye api karmāṇi kurvanti bhagavantam apāśritāḥ kriyāyogaparā rājan kāmākāṅkṣāvivarjitāḥ brahmaniṣṭhā dhyānaparā brahmaṇy eva vyavasthitāḥ te api tadbhāvam āyānti vimuktipatham āśritāḥ yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti samarthā naiva coditum karmaṇo bhāvanā yeyaṃ sā brahmaparipanthinī karmabhāvanayā tulyaṃ vijñānam upapadyate tādṛg bhavato vijñaptir yādṛśī karmabhāvanā kṣaye tasyāḥ paraṃ brahma svayam eva prakāśate evam etan mayā bhūpa yathāvat kathitaṃ tava dvaitādvaitasvarūpeṇa yathā brahma vyavasthitam yathāvat karmaniṣṭhānāṃ tatprāptiḥ kathitaṃ tathā svarūpaṃ brahmaṇaś coktam ubhayatrāpi te pṛthak vāsudevamayasyānyat kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi te ākhyātaṃ bhagavan samyak paraṃ brahma tvayā mama viṣṇur eva jagaddhātā yogināṃ vartate yataḥ upāyas tasya yaḥ prāpto viṣṇor īśasya bhārgava advaitadvaitarūpasya tan me vistarato vada yena janmajarāmṛtyu- mahāgrāhabhavārṇavam tvadvākyanāvam āruhya muktitīram avāpnuyām tan mama brūhi tattvena prāpnuyāṃ yena tat padam bandhaḥ karmamayo hy atra yathāmuktivighātakṛt tasyāpagamane yatnaḥ kāryaḥ saṃsārabhīruṇā suvarṇādimahādāna- puṇyatīrthāvagāhanaiḥ śārīraiś ca tathā kleśaiḥ śāstroktais tacchamo bhavet devatāstutisacchāstra- śravaṇaiḥ puṇyadarśanaiḥ guruśuśrūṣaṇāc caiva pāpabandhaḥ praṇaśyati prapākūpataḍāgāni devatāyatanāni ca kārayan puruṣavyāghra pāpabandhāt pramucyate yoginām atha śuśrūṣāṃ tathaivāvasathān nṛpa kurvan pūrtāśritaṃ cānyat pāpabandhāt pramucyate viṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇo vāsudevo govindaḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ ityādi vyāharan nityaṃ pāpabandhāt pramucyate viśvo viśveśvaro viśva- vidhātā dhāma śāśvatam viṣṇur ityādi ca japan pāpabandhāt pramucyate padmanābho hṛṣīkeśaḥ keśavo madhusūdanaḥ ityādi vyāharan nityaṃ pāpabandhāt pramucyate nārāyaṇaś cakradharo viśvarūpas trivikramaḥ ityādi vyāharan nityaṃ pāpabandhāt pramucyate viṣṇau pratiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ viṣṇur viśve pratiṣṭhitaḥ viṣṇur viśveśvaro viśvam iti bhāvāt pramucyate evaṃ saṃśāntapāpasya puṇyavṛddhimato nṛpa icchā pravartate pūṃso muktidāyiṣu karmasu muktidāyīni karmāṇi niṣkāmena kṛtāni tu bhavanti doṣakṣayakāḥ puṇyabandhāt pramucyate nityanaimittikānīha karmāṇy uktāni yāni vai teṣāṃ niṣkāmakāraṇāt puṇyabandhaḥ praśāmyati anekajanmasaṃsāra- citasyāpi dṛḍhātmanaḥ karmabandhasya śaithilya- kāraṇaṃ cāparaṃ śṛṇu ahiṃsā nātimānitvam adambhitvam amatsaram titikṣā samadarśitvaṃ maitryādau daṇḍasaṃyamaḥ ṛjutvam indriyajayaḥ śaucam ācāryapūjanam puṇyastavādipaṭhanam apaiśunyam akatthanam viṣayān prati vairāgyam anahaṃkāram eva ca akāmitvaṃ manaḥsthairyam adrohaḥ sarvajantuṣu avivādas tathā mūḍhair amūḍhaiḥ praśnasatkathā viviktadeśe abhiratir mahājanavivarjanam sadbhiḥ sahāsya satataṃ yogābhyāso mitoktitā strībhartsotsavasaṃlāpa- vivarjanam avekṣaṇam parayoṣidvilāsānāṃ kāvyālāpavivarjanam gītavāditanṛtteṣu mṛdaṅgeṣv apareṣu ca asaktir manaso maunam ātmatattvāvalokanam tapaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ satyeṣu sthitir lobhavivarjanam tathā parigraho rājan māyāvyājavivarjanam asṛṅmāṃsādibhūtatvān nijadehajugupsanam sarvāṇy etāni bhūtāni viṣṇur ity acalā matiḥ tatraivāśeṣabhūteśe bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī ete guṇā mayākhyātā manonirvṛtikārakāḥ śaithilyahetavaś caite karmabandhasya pūrthiva ebhiḥ śāntiṃ gate citte dhyānākṛṣṭaḥ sthito hariḥ śamaṃ nayati karmāṇi sitamiśrāsitāni vai bhūyaś ca śṛṇu śāstrārthaṃ saṃkṣepād vadato mama yathā saṃprāpyate muktir manujendra mumukṣubhiḥ nityanaimittikānāṃ tu niṣkāmasya hi yā kriyā nisiddhānāṃ sakāmānāṃ tathaivākaraṇaṃ nṛpa sarveśvare ca govinde bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī prayacchati nṛṇāṃ muktiṃ mā te bhūd atra saṃśayaḥ ākhyātam etad akhilaṃ yat pṛṣṭo asi mayā dvija jāyate śamakāmānāṃ praśamaḥ karmaṇāṃ yathā kiṃtv atra bhavatā proktā praśāntiḥ sarvakarmaṇām nātyantanāśaḥ śāntānām udbhavo bhavitā punaḥ nijakāraṇam āsādya stokasyāgner yathā tṛṇam tad ācakṣva mahābhāga prasādasumukho mama saṃkṣayo yena bhavati mūlodvartena karmaṇām na karmaṇāṃ kṣayo bhūpa janmanām ayutair api karmakṣayam ṛte yogād yogāgniḥ kṣapayet param taṃ yogaṃ mama viprarṣe praṇatasyābhiyācataḥ tvam ācakṣva kṣayo yena jāyate akhilakarmaṇām hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān anādir munibhiḥ purā pṛṣṭaḥ provāca yaṃ yogaṃ taṃ samāsena me śṛṇu anādikālaprasṛtā yathā vidyā mahīpate tathā tatkṣayahetutvād yogo vidyāmayo avyayaḥ taṃ paraṃparayā śrutvā munayo atra dayālavaḥ prakāśayanti bhūtānām upakāracikīrṣavaḥ devā maharṣayo rājaṃs tathā rājarṣayo akhilāḥ śreyo'rthinaḥ purā jagmuḥ śaraṇaṃ kapilaṃ kila te tam ūcur bhavān nityaṃ dayāluḥ sarvajantuṣu so asmān uddhara saṃmagnān itaḥ saṃsārakardamāt yac chreyaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ strīṇām apy upakārakam yasmāt parataraṃ nānyac śreyas tad brūhi naḥ prabho ādāv ante ca madhye ca nṝṇāṃ yad upakārakam api kīṭapataṃgānāṃ tan naḥ śreyaḥ paraṃ vada ity uktaḥ kapilaḥ sarvair devair devarṣibhis tathā nāsti yogāt paraṃ śreyaḥ kiṃcid ity uktavān purā yathā janmāyutaiḥ kleśāḥ sthairyaṃ cetasy upāgatāḥ tacchāntaye tathā yogo bahujanmārjito bhavet sa evābhyasatāṃ nṝṇāṃ tīvrasaṃvegicetasām āsannatāṃ prayāty āśu viṣṇuḥ saṃnyastakarmaṇām brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ strīśūdrasya ca pāvanam śāntaye karmaṇāṃ nānyad yogād asti hi muktaye abhyastaṃ janmabhir naikaiḥ śubhajātibhaveṣu yat yogasvarūpaṃ tat teṣāṃ strīśūdratve vyavasthitam yogābhyāso nṛṇāṃ yeṣāṃ nāsti janmāntarāhṛtaḥ yogasya prāptaye teṣāṃ śūdravaiśyādikaḥ kramaḥ strītvāc chūdratvam abhyeti tato vaiśyatvam āpnuyāt tataś ca kṣatriyo vipraḥ kriyāhīnas tato bhavet anūcānas tathā yajvī karmanyāsī tataḥ param tato jñānitvam abhyetya yogī muktiṃ kramāl labhet yeṣāṃ tu jātimātreṇa yogābhyāsas tirohitaḥ āste tatraiva mucyante jātihetau kṣayaṃgate asatkarma kṛtaṃ pūrvam asajjātipradāyi yat tasmin yogāgninā dagdhe tasya jāter balaṃ kutaḥ yathā vāteritaḥ kakṣaṃ dahaty ūrdhvaśikho analaḥ sarvakarmāṇi yogāgnir bhasmasāt kurute tathā yathā dagdhatuṣaṃ bījam abījatvān na jāyate yogadagdhais tathā kleśair nātmā saṃjāyate punaḥ adṛṣṭā dṛṣṭatattvānāṃ yogināṃ yogavicyutiḥ yeṣāṃ bhavati yogitvaṃ prāpnuvantīha te punaḥ sajjātiprāpakaṃ karma kṛtaṃ tena tadātmanā jātiṃ prayānti viprādyā yogakarmānurañjitāḥ tatrāpy anekajanmottha- yogābhyāsānurañjitāḥ tenaivābhyāsayogena hriyante tattvavidyayā jaigīṣavyo yathā vipro yathā caivāsitādayaḥ hiraṇyanābho rājanyas tathā vai janakādayaḥ pūrvābhyastena yogena tulādhārādayo viśaḥ saṃprāptāḥ paramāṃ siddhiṃ śūdrāḥ pailavakādayaḥ maitreyī sulabhā gārgī śāṇḍilī ca tapasvinī strītve prāptāḥ parāṃ siddhim anyajanmasamādhitaḥ dharmavyādhādayo apy anye pūrvābhyāsāj jugupsite varṇāvaratve saṃprāptāḥ saṃsiddhiṃ śravaṇī tathā pūrvābhyastaṃ ca tat teṣāṃ yogajñānaṃ mahātmanām suptotthitapratyayavad upadeśādinā vinā tasmād yogaḥ paraṃ śreyo vimuktiphalado hi yaḥ vimuktau sukham atyantaṃ saṃmohas tv itarat sukham etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ mayā manujakuñjara śreyaḥ parataraṃ yogāt kiṃcid anyan na vidyate kathitaṃ yogamāhātmyaṃ bhavatā munisattama svarūpaṃ tu na me proktaṃ śrotum icchāmi tad dhy aham dvaividhyaṃ nṛpa yogasya paraṃ cāparam eva ca tac chṛṇuṣva vadāmy eṣa vācyaṃ śuśrūṣatāṃ satām yo dadyād bhagavajjñānaṃ kuryād vā dharmadeśanām kṛtsnāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ dadyān na tattulyaṃ kathaṃcana kṣayiṣṇūny aparāṇīha dānāni manujādhipa ekam evākṣayaṃ śastaṃ jñānadānam anuttamam dānāny ekaphalānīha trailokye dadatā satām jñānaṃ prayacchatā samyak kiṃ na dattaṃ bhaven nṛpa jñānāny anyāny asārāṇi śilpinīva nareśvara ekam eva paraṃ jñānaṃ yad yogaprāptikārakam ahaṃ vaktā bhavāñ śrotā vācyo yogo vimuktidaḥ prāṇinām upakārāya saṃpad eṣā guṇādhikā pareṇa brahmaṇā sārdham ekatvaṃ yan nṛpātmanaḥ sa eva yogo vikhyātaḥ kim anyad yogalakṣaṇam aparaṃ ca paraṃ caiva dvau yogau pṛthivīpate tayoḥ svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu sattāmātraṃ paraṃ brahma viṣṇvākhyam aviśeṣaṇam durvicintyaṃ yataḥ pūrvaṃ tatprāptyartham athocyate vātālīcañcalaṃ cittam anālambanam asthiti sūkṣmatvād brahmaṇo rājann agrāhy agrāhyadharmiṇaḥ samyag abhyasyato ajasram upavṛṃhitaśaktimat janmāntaraśatair vāpi brahmagrāhy abhijāyate yady antarāya doṣeṇa nāpakarṣo narādhipa yogino yogarūḍhasya tālāgrāt patanaṃ yathā jñānaṃ prayacchatāṃ samyak kiṃ vadatu bhaven nṛpa tad āpnoti paraṃ brahma kleśena mahatā nṛpa janmābhyāsāntarotthena vijñānena samedhitaḥ viṣṇvākhyaṃ brahma duṣprāpaṃ viṣayākṛṣṭacetasā manuṣyeṇeti tatprāptāv upāyam aparaṃ śṛṇu surūpāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ prasannavadanekṣaṇām kṛtvātmanaḥ prītikarīṃ suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ tasyāś ca lakṣaṇaṃ bhūpa śṛṇuṣva gadato mama yaddravyā yatsvarūpā ca kartavyā dhyānakarmaṇi suvarṇarūpyatāmrais tu ārakūṭamayīṃ tathā śailadārumṛdā vāpi lekhyajāṃ vāpi kārayet kāryas tu viṣṇur bhagavān saumyarūpaś caturbhujaḥ salilādhmātameghābhaḥ śrīmāñ śrīvatsabhūṣitaḥ ābaddhamakuṭaḥ sragvī hārabhārārpitodaraḥ svakṣeṇa cārucipukaḥ sulalāṭena subhruṇā svoṣṭhena sukapolena vadanena virājatā kaṇṭhena śubhalekhena varābharaṇadhāriṇā nānāratnānatārtābhyāṃ śravaṇābhyām alaṃkṛtaḥ puṣṭaśliṣṭāyatabhujas tanutāmranakhāṅguliḥ madhyena trivalībhaṅga- bhūṣitena ca cāruṇā supādaḥ sūruyugalaḥ sukaṭīgulphajānukaḥ vāmapārśve gadādevī cakraṃ devasya dakṣiṇe śaṅkho vāmakare deyo dakṣiṇe padma suprabham ūrdhvadṛṣṭim adhodṛṣṭiṃ tiryagdṛṣṭiṃ na kārayet nimīlitākṣo bhagavān na praśasto janārdanaḥ saumyā tu dṛṣṭiḥ kartavyā kiṃcit prahasiteva ca kāryaś caraṇavinyāsaḥ sarvataḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ caraṇāntarasaṃsthā ca bibhratī rūpam uttamam kāryā vasuṃdharā devī tatpādataladhāriṇī yādṛgvidhā vā manasaḥ sthairyalambhopapādikā nṛsiṃhavāmanādīnāṃ tādṛśīṃ kārayed budhaḥ brahma tasyāṃ samāropya manasā tanmayo bhavet tām ārcayet tāṃ praṇamet tāṃ smaret tāṃ vicintayet tām arcayaṃs tāṃ praṇamaṃs tāṃ smaraṃs tāṃ ca cintayan viśaty apāstadoṣas tu tām eva brahmarūpiṇīm saṃkalpanakriyārūḍhaḥ svarūpeṇa nṛpātmanaḥ kurvīta bhāvanāṃ tatra tadbhāvotpattikāraṇāt nānyatra manasāneyā buddhir īṣad api kvacit yamaiś ca niyamaiś caiva pūtātmā pṛthivīśvara mūrtiṃ bhagavataḥ saṃyak pūjayet tanmayaḥ sadā yamāṃś ca niyamāṃś caiva śrotum icchāmi bhārgava yair dhūtakalmaṣo yogī muktibhāg upajāyate ahiṃsā satyam asteyaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahau yamās tavaite kathitā niyamān api me śṛṇu saṃtoṣaśaucasvādhyāyās tapaś ceśvarabhāvanā niyamāḥ kauravaśreṣṭha yogasaṃsiddhihetavaḥ ebhir mūlaguṇaiḥ sadbhir viṣṇor bhaktimatas tathā śraddadhānasya cānyāni yogāṅgāni nibodha me madhyamaprāṇam acalaṃ sukhadāyi śubhaṃ śuci yogasaṃsiddhaye bhūpa yoginām āsanaṃ smṛtam prāṇāyāmas tridhā vāyoḥ prāṇasya hṛdi dhāraṇam kumbharecakapūrākhyās tasya bhedās trayo nṛpa ete nibodha mātrās tu nālambanaguṇānvitāḥ sālambanaś caturtho anyo bāhyāntarviṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ indriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayād buddhiḥ pratyekaśas tu yat karoty āharaṇaṃ jñeyaḥ pratyāhāraḥ sa paṇḍitaiḥ śubhe hy ekatra viṣaye cetaso yac ca dhāraṇam niścalatvāt tu sā sadbhir dhāraṇety abhidhīyate paunaḥpunyena tatraiva viṣaye saiva dhāraṇā dhyānākhyā labhate rājan samādhim api me śṛṇu arthamātraṃ ca yad grāhye cittam ādāya pārthiva arthasvarūpavad bhāti samādhiḥ so abhidhīyate kathitāni tavaitāni yogāṅgāni kṛtais tu yaiḥ utkarṣo jāyate vyastaiḥ samastair heyasaṃkṣayaḥ yogāṅgāny aṅgabhūtāni dhyānasyaitāny aśeṣataḥ dhyānam apy avanīpāla yogasyāṅgatvam archati dhyānam ekavratānāṃ tu kuśalākuśaleṣu tat artheṣv āśaktim abhyeti sarvadaiva nareśvara śubhāvyāvartitaṃ dhyānam avivekasya jāyate saṃsāraduḥkhadaṃ rājann aśubhālambi tad yataḥ tad evākṛṣya duṣṭebhyo viṣayebhyaḥ śubhāśubham sarvasaṃsārakāntāra- pāram abhyeti mānavaḥ duḥkhadāghapraśamane yā cintāharniśaṃ nṛṇām taddhyānam aviśuddhārthaṃ sukhadānām apālane kathaṃ saṃsārabandho ayam asmān muktiḥ kathaṃ tv iti manovṛttir manuṣyāṇāṃ dhyānam etac chubhaṃ dvidhā śuddham apy etad akhilaṃ lobhakāryatayānayā sukhābhilāṣo yanmuktau bandhuduḥkhādipīḍanāt avāñchitaphalaṃ lobham alobhāṃśavivarjitam śubhāśubhaphalaṃ dhyānam araktaṃ dviṣṭam iṣyate dṛṣṭānumānāgamikaṃ dhyānasyālambanaṃ tridhā na hi nirviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ mūḍhavṛttir iveṣyate prāk sthūleṣu padārtheṣu tataḥ sūkṣmeṣu paṇḍitaḥ dhyānaṃ kurvīta tatpaścāt paramāṇau mahīpate dhyānābhyāsaparasyaivaṃ heyālambanabādhane tacchāntaye tadvipakṣa- bhāvanām eva bhāvayet taccittas tanmayo jñānī bhavaty asmān na doṣavat kurvītālambanaṃ kāle kasmiṃścid api pārthiva ābrahmastambaparyanta- jagadantarvyavasthitāḥ prāṇinaḥ karmajanita- saṃskāravaśavartinaḥ yatas tato na te dhyāne dhyāninām upakārakāḥ avidyāntargatāḥ sarve te hi saṃsāragocarāḥ paścād udbhūtabodhāś ca dhyātā naivopakārakāḥ naisargiko na vai bodhas teṣām apy anyato yataḥ tasmāt tad amalaṃ brahma nisargād eva bodhavat dhyeyaṃ dhyānavidāṃ samyag yad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam na tad yajñair na dānena na tapobhir na tad vrataiḥ paśyanty ekāgramanaso dhyānenaiva sanātanam tac ca viṣṇoḥ paraṃ rūpam anirdeśyam ajaṃ sthiram yataḥ pravartate sarvaṃ layam abhyeti yatra ca anidram ajam asvapnam arūpānāma śāśvatam yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti jñānadṛśyaṃ sanātanam nirdhūtapuṇyapāpā ye te viśanty evam īśvaram tac ca sarvagataṃ brahma viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ paramātmā paraḥ proktaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam anantaśaktim īśeśaṃ svapratiṣṭham anopamam yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam yatra sarvaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ yaḥ sarvaṃ sarvataś ca yaḥ yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam sargādikāraṇaṃ yasya svabhāvād eva śaktayaḥ yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam nirdhūtapuṇyapāpā yaṃ viśanty avyayam īśvaram yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam tatra yogavataḥ samyak puruṣasya nareśvara yad uktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tan me gadataḥ śrotum arhasi brahmaṇy eva sthitaṃ cittaṃ sarvataḥ saṃnivartitam nānyālambanasāpekṣaṃ yoginaḥ siddhikārakam saṃsthānam avikāreṇa cetaso brahmasaṃsthitau nivāta iva dīpasya yoginaḥ siddhilakṣaṇam evam ekāgracittasya puṇyāpuṇyam aśeṣataḥ prayāti saṃkṣayam ṛte dehārambhakare nṛpa dehārambhakarasyāpi karmaṇaḥ saṃkṣayāvahaḥ yo yogaḥ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu tasyāpi lakṣaṇam yat tad brahma paraṃ proktaṃ viṣṇvākhyam ajam avyayam cetasaḥ pralayas tatra yoga ity abhidhīyate yogasevānirodhena pralīne tatra cetasi puruṣaḥ kāranābhāvād bhedaṃ naivānupaśyati parātmanor manuṣyendra vibhāgo jñānakalpitaḥ kṣaye tasyātmaparayor vibhāgābhāga eva hi paramātmātmanor yo ayam avibhāgaḥ paraṃtapa sa eva paramo yogaḥ samāsāt kathitas tava yathā kamaṇḍalau bhinne tattoyaṃ salile gatam vrajaty aikyaṃ tathaivaitad ubhayaṃ kāraṇakṣayāt yathāgnir agnau saṃkṣiptaḥ samānatvam anuvrajet tadākhyas tanmayo bhūtvā gṛhyate na viśeṣataḥ evaṃ brahmātmanor yogād akatvam upapannayoḥ na bhedaḥ kalaśākāśa- nabhasor iva jāyate prakṣīṇāśeṣakarmā tu yadā brahmamayaḥ pumān tadā svarūpam asyokter gocare nopapadyate ghaṭadhvaṃse ghaṭākāśaṃ na bhinnaṃ nabhaso yathā brahmaṇā heyavidhvaṃse viṣṇvākhyena pumāṃs tathā bhinne dṛtau yathā vāyur naivānyaḥ saha vāyunā kṣīṇapuṇyāghabandhas tu tathātmā brahmaṇā saha tataḥ samastakalyāṇa- samastasukhasaṃpadām āhlādam anyam atulaṃ kam apy āpnoti śāśvatam brahmasvarūpasya tadā hy ātmano nityadaiva saḥ vyuttānakāle rājendra āste heyatirohitaḥ ādarśasya malābhāvād vaimalyaṃ kāśate yathā jñānāgnidagdhaheyasya so ahlādo hy ātmanas tathā yathā na kriyate jyotsnā malaprakṣālanādinā doṣaprahāṇaṃ na jñānam ātmanaḥ kriyate tathā yathodupānakaraṇāt kriyate na jalāmbaram sadaiva nīyate vyaktim asataḥ saṃbhavaḥ kutaḥ yathā heyagaṇadhvaṃsād avabodhādayo guṇāḥ prakāśyante na janyante nityā evātmano hite jñānavairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ dharmaś ca manujeśvara ātmano brahmabhūtasya nityam eva catuṣṭayam etad advaitam ākhyātam eṣa yogas tavoditaḥ ayaṃ viṣṇur idaṃ brahma tathaitat satyam uttamam punaś ca śrūyatām eṣa saṃkṣepād gadato mama nānādvaikatvavijñāna- svarūpam avanīpate ātmā kṣetrajñasaṃjño ayaṃ saṃyuktaḥ prākṛtair guṇaiḥ tair eva vigataiḥ śuddhaḥ paramātmā nigadyate dhyeyaṃ brahma pumān dhyātā upāyo dhyānasaṃjñitaḥ yas tv etat karaṇeṣv āste tadvarge kā vibhāgatā saṃkṣepād api bhūpāla saṃkṣepan aparaṃ śṛṇu putrāya yat pitā brūyāt svaśiṣyāyāthavā guruḥ na vāsudevāt param asti kiṃcin na vāsudevād gaditaṃ paraṃ ca satyaṃ paraṃ vāsudevo amitātmā namo namo vāsudevāya nityam tasmāt tam ārādhaya cintayeśam abhyarcayānantam atandritātmā saṃsārapāraṃ param īpsamānair ārādhanīyo harir eka eva ārādhito arthān dhanakāṅkṣakānāṃ dharmārthināṃ dharmam aśeṣadharmī dadāti kāmāṃś ca manoniviṣṭān mokṣārthināṃ muktida eva viṣṇuḥ mamaitat kathitaṃ samyag ātmavidyāśritaṃ mune yat tv anyac chrotum icchāmi tat prasanno vadasva me yeyaṃ muktir bhagavatā proktā varṇakramān mama tatrecchāmi mune śrotuṃ varṇād varṇottarocchrayam śūdro vaiśyatvam abhyeti kathaṃ vaiśyaś ca bhārgava kṣatriyatvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha brāhmaṇatvaṃ kathaṃ tataḥ vipratvān muktiyogyatvaṃ yathā yāti mahāmune tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi tvatto bhārgavanandana tvadyukto ayam anupraśnaḥ kuruvarya śṛṇuṣva tam mayocyamānam akhilaṃ varṇānām upakārakam śūdradharmān aśeṣeṇa kurvañ śūdro yathāvidhi vaiśyatvam eti vaiśyaś ca kṣatriyatvaṃ svakarmakṛt vipratvaṃ kṣatriyaḥ samyag dvijadharmaparo nṛpa vipraś ca muktilābhena yujyate satkriyāparaḥ sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ svadharmam anuvartatām sadocchritir nyūnakṛto hāniś cotkṛṣṭakarmaṇaḥ teṣāṃ ca brāhmaṇādīnāṃ varṇadharmān anukramāt samucchritipradān rājan gadato me niśāmaya anasūyā dayā kṣāntiḥ śaucaṃ maṅgalam aspṛhā akārpaṇyam anāyāsas tathānyaḥ sārvavarṇikaḥ aṣṭāv ete guṇāḥ puṃsāṃ paratreha ca bhūtaye bhavanti kuruśārdūla pṛthagdharmāṃś ca me śṛṇu yajñādhyayanadānāni brahmakṣatraviśāṃ nṛpa sādhāraṇāni teṣāṃ tu jīvikākarma kathyate yājanādhyāpanair vipras tathā śastapratigrahaiḥ bhṛtyādibharaṇaṃ kuryād yajñāṃś ca vibhave sati bhṛtyādibharaṇe nālaṃ svavṛttyā hi yadā dvijaḥ tadā jīvet samālambya vṛttiṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ saṃtyajeta samastāṃs tān na kuryād vṛttisaṃkaram āpatkāle api viprasya śūdrakarma na śasyate prajānāṃ pālanaṃ samyag vidhiḥ prathamakalpitaḥ rājanyasya mahīpāla śastrājīvena vā bhṛtiḥ tadutpannair dhanaiḥ kuryāt samastāḥ kṣatriyakriyāḥ tasyāpy āpadi vaiśyasya yā vṛttiḥ sā vidhīyate vāṇijyaṃ vaiśyajātasya paśūnāṃ pālanaṃ kṛṣiḥ dadyād yajec ca vidhivat tadutpannadhanena saḥ dvijātijanaśuśrūṣāṃ krayavikrayajair dhanaiḥ śūdro yajet pākayajñair dadyād iṣṭāni cārthinām tasmai śuśrūṣave deyaṃ jīrṇavastram upānahau chattrādikaṃ tathā kuryāt samyagdharmopapādanam caturṇām api varṇānāṃ dharmas te kathito mayā śṛṇuṣva ca mahīpāla dharmam āśramiṇām ataḥ kṛtopanayanaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmacārī guror gṛhe guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ kuryād bhaikṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ nivedya gurave bhaikṣam attavyaṃ tadanujñayā guror bhuktavataḥ paścān nātisvādumudāvatā vahniśuśrūṣaṇaṃ kruyād vedāharaṇam eva ca guror arthe sadā toyaṃ samidāharaṇaṃ tathā puṣpādīnāṃ ca kurvīta supte tasmiñ śayīta ca śayane ca samuttiṣṭhet taṃ vrajantam anuvrajet āhūtaś ca paṭhet tena tanmanā nānyatomukhaḥ vratāni caratā saṃyag grāhyo vedo yatātmanā daṇḍavatplavanaṃ snāne śastaṃ nāsyāṅgaśodhanam adhītya vedān vedau vā vedaṃ vāpi yathākramam aviplutabrahmacaryo gṛhasthāśramam āvaset yatheṣṭāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā gurave kurunandana tato anujñāṃ samāsādya gṛhasthāśramam āvaset tenaivāntaṃ vrajet prājñas tacchuśrūṣaṇatatparaḥ vānaprasthāśramaṃ tasmāc caturthaṃ vāpi saṃśrayet yathākramaṃ vā kurvīta vidhivad dārasaṃgraham tatas tv arogikulajāṃ tulyāṃ patnīṃ samudvahet gṛhasthāśramavṛttyartham avyaṅgāṃ vidhinā nṛpa ākhyātavarṇadharmeṇa dhanaṃ labdhvā mahīpate kurvīta śraddhayā yukto nityanaimittikīḥ kriyāḥ abhyāgatātithīn bandhūn bhṛtyādīn āturāṃs tathā toṣayec chaktito annena vayāṃsy antyapaśūn api ṛtāv upagamaś caiva gṛhasthasyāpi śabditaḥ dharmo dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha yajñocchiṣṭaṃ ca bhojanam havyena prīṇayed devān pitṛn kavyena śaktitaḥ manuṣyān annapānena svādhyāyena rṣitarpaṇam kuryāc ca prīṇanaṃ nityaṃ bhūtānāṃ balikarmaṇā prajāpatiṃ sutotpattyā hārdena sakalaṃ janam śubhena karmaṇātmānam upadeśena cātmajān anujīvijanaṃ vṛtyā gṛhasthas toṣayet sadā tathaivāparamānebhyaḥ pradeyaṃ gṛhamedhinā annaṃ bhikṣārthino ye ca parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇaḥ evaṃ gṛhāśrame devāḥ pitaro munayas tathā sarvakāmān prayacchanti manuṣyāś ca supūjitāḥ gṛhasthas tu yadā paśyed valīpalitam ātmanaḥ apatyasya tathāpatyaṃ tadāraṇyaṃ samāśrayet pitṛdevātithīnāṃ tu smṛtaṃ tatrāpi pūjanam tathaivāraṇyabhogaś ca tapobhiś cātmakarṣaṇam brahmacaryaṃ mahīśayyā homas triṣavaṇāplutiḥ maunādikaraṇaṃ śastaṃ jaṭāvalkaladhāraṇam grīṣme pañcatapobhiś ca varṣāsv abhrāvakāśikaiḥ jalaśayyā ca hemante bhāvyaṃ vananiketanaiḥ iṅgudairaṇḍatailena gātrābhyaṅgāni ceṣyate śyāmākanīvāramayaṃ phalamūlaiś ca bhojanam apraveśas tathā grāme vānaprasthavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ vānaprasthasya te proktaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam āditaḥ āśramaṇaṃ tv aparaṃ bhikṣoḥ śṛṇuṣva gadato mama grāmaikarātrir vasatir nagare pañcarātrikā sarvasaṅgaparityāgaḥ kṣāntir indriyasaṃyamaḥ vikālabhaikṣacaraṇam anārambhas tathā nṛpa ātmajñānāvabodhecchā brahmacaryaṃ samādhinā ātmāvalokanaṃ caiva bhikṣoḥ śastāni pārthiva caturthaś caiṣa kathitas tava bhikṣor mayāśramaḥ kramād vimuktikāmānāṃ puruṣāṇām ayaṃ vidhiḥ evaṃ tu varṇadharmeṇa tathā cāśramakarmanā nijena saṃpūjya hariṃ siddhim āpnoti mānavaḥ brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca bhikṣur vaikhānasas tathā kurvanto nijakarmāṇi viṣṇum eva yajanti te yato hi devatāḥ sarvā brahmādyāḥ kurunandana aṃśabhūtā jagaddhātur viṣṇor avyaktajanmanaḥ viśve devā yato viṣṇur viṣṇuḥ pitṛgaṇo yataḥ devā yajñabhujaś ceśo yataḥ pāpaharo hariḥ viśve bhūtāni bhūtāni yato viṣṇus tatharṣayaḥ tataḥ sarvāśramāṇāṃ hi pūjya eko janārdanaḥ sarveśvaraṃ sarvamayaṃ samasta- saṃsārahetukṣayakāraṇeśam varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ variṣṭhaṃ viṣṇuṃ kriyāvān yajate manuṣyaḥ yasyodare jagad idaṃ paramāṇubhūtaṃ candrendrarudramarudaśvivasuprajeśaiḥ sarvaiḥ sametam amitātmatanos tam ekam abhyarcya viṣṇum abhivāñchitam asty alabhyam ārādhya yaṃ bhuvanabhāvanam acyutākhyam aiśvaryam īpsitam avāpa patiḥ surāṇām trailokyasāram amarārcitapādapadmam ekaṃ tam eva harim arcayatārcanīyam yasyāṅghripadmagalitāmbhasi deva daitya- yakṣādibhiḥ sakalapāpam apohya siddhiḥ saṃprāpyate maraṇajanmajarāpahantrī viṣṇor ajāt kathaya ko abhyadhikas tato asti kamalajaharasūryacandraśakraiḥ satatam abhiṣṭutam ādyam īśitāram sakalabhuvanakāryakāraneśaṃ puruṣatanuṃ praṇato asmi vāsudevam śrutaṃ bhagavato rūpam advaite yat tvayoditam viṣṇor bhṛgukulaśreṣṭha yac ca dvaite mahātmanaḥ avidyābhinnadṛgbuddhiḥ puruṣo munipuṅgava dvaitabhūte jagaty asminn advaitaṃ bhāvayet katham krodhalobhādayo doṣā ye mukteḥ paripanthinaḥ vinivṛttirūpā yena teṣāṃ yena vader ha tam sarveśvareśvareśasya yac ca rūpaṃ hareḥ param tac cāhaṃ śrotum icchāmi tvatto bhṛgukulodvaha samyak pṛṣṭam idaṃ bhūpa bhavatā guhyam uttamam dvaitādvaitakathālāpa- saṃbandhād upakārakam purā dharmagṛhe jajñe caturmūrtir nareśvara devadevo jagaddhātā paramātmā janārdanaḥ jagataḥ pālanārthāya durvṛttanidhanāya ca svecchayā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ saṃbhavaty eva bhūtale svarge vāpi bhūloke vā bhuvarloke athavā vibhuḥ yatra vā rocate tatra cikīrṣur jagato hitam turīyāṃśena dharmasya bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ yadāvatāraṃ kṛtavāṃs tadā taccaritaṃ śṛṇu naro nārāyaṇaś caiva hariḥ kṛṣṇas tathaiva ca viṣṇor aṃśāṃśakā hy ete catvāro dharmasūnavaḥ teṣāṃ nārāyaṇanarau gandhamādanaparvate ātmany ātmānam ādhāya tepate paramaṃ tapaḥ dhyāyamānāv anaupamyaṃ svakāraṇam akāraṇam vāsudevam anirdeśyam apratarkyam ajaṃ param yogayuktau mahāmaunam āsthitau gurutejasau tayos tapaḥprabhāveṇa na tatāpa divākaraḥ vavau cāśaṅkito vāyuḥ sukhasparśo hy asarkaraḥ śiśiro abhavad atyarthaṃ jvalann api vibhāvasuḥ siṃhavyāghrādayaḥ saumyāś ceruḥ saha mṛgair girau tayor gauravabhārārtā pṛthivī pṛthivīpate cacāla bhūdharāś celuś cukṣubhuś ca mahābdhayaḥ devāś ca sveṣu dhiṣṇyeṣu niṣprabheṣu hataprabhāḥ babhūvur avanīpāla paramaṃ kṣobham āgatāḥ devarājas tataḥ śakraḥ saṃtrastas tapasas tayoḥ yuyojāpsarasaḥ śubhrās tayor vighnacikīrṣayā rambhe tilottame kuṇṭhe ghṛtāci lalitāvati umloce subhrupramloce saurabhe api madoddhate alambuṣe miśrakeśi puṇḍarīke varūthini vilobhanīyaṃ bibhrāṇā vapur manmathabodhanam gandhamādanam āsādya kurudhvaṃ vacanaṃ mama naranārāyaṇau tatra tapodīkṣānvitau dvijau tapyete dharmatanayau tapaḥ paramaduścaram tāv asmākaṃ varārohāḥ kurvāṇau paramaṃ tapaḥ karmātiśayaduḥkhārti- pradāvayatināśakau tad gacchata na bhīḥ kāryā bhavatībhir idaṃ vacaḥ smaraḥ sahāyo bhavitā vasantaś ca varāṅganāḥ rūpaṃ ca vaḥ samālokya madanoddīpanaṃ param kandarpavaśam abhyeti vivaśaḥ ko na mānavaḥ ity uktā devarājena madanena samaṃ tadā jagmur apsarasaḥ sarvā vasantaś ca mahīpate gandhamādanam āsādya puṃskokilakulākulam cakāra mādhavo ramyaṃ protphullavanapādapam pravavau dakṣiṇaḥ sadyo malayānugato anilaḥ bhṛṅgamālārutaravair ramaṇīyam abhūd vanam gandhaś ca surabhiḥ sadyo vanarājisamudbhavaḥ kiṃnaroragayakṣāṇāṃ babhūva ghrāṇatarpaṇaḥ varāṅganāś ca tāḥ sarvā naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī vilobhayitum ārabdhā varāṅgalalitaiḥ smitaiḥ jagur manoharaṃ kāścin nanṛtuś cātra cāparāḥ avādayaṃs tathaivānyā manoharataraṃ nṛpa hāvair bhāvaiḥ smitais trāsais tathānyā valgubhāṣitaiḥ tayoḥ kṣobhāya tanvaṅgyaś cakrur udyamam aṅganāḥ tathāpi na tayoḥ kaścin manasaḥ pṛthivīpate vikāro abhavad adhyātma- pārasaṃprāptacetasoḥ nivātasthau yathā dīpāv akampau nṛpa tiṣṭhataḥ vāsudevārpaṇe svacche tathaiva manasī tayoḥ pūryamāṇo api cāmbhobhir bhuvam anyāṃ mahodadhiḥ yathā na yāti na yayau tathā tanmānasaṃ kvacit sarvabhūtahitau brahma vāsudevamayaṃ param manyamānau na rāgasya dveṣasya ca vaśaṃgatau smaro api na śaśākātha praveṣṭuṃ hṛdayaṃ tayoḥ vidyāmayaṃ dīpayutam andhakāram ivālayam puṣpojjvalāṃs taruvarān vasantaṃ dakṣiṇānilam tāś caivāpsarasaḥ sarvāḥ kandarpaṃ ca mahāmunī yac cārabdhaṃ tapas tābhyām ātmānaṃ gandhamādanam dadṛśāte akhilaṃ rūpaṃ brahmaṇaḥ puruṣarṣabha dāhāya nānalo vahner nāpaḥkledāya cāmbhasaḥ taddravyam eva taddravya- vikārāya na vai yataḥ tato vijñānavijñāta- parabrahmasvarūpayoḥ madhukandarpayoṣitsu vikāro nābhavat tayoḥ tato gurutaraṃ yatnaṃ vasantamadanau nṛpa cakrāte tāś ca tanvaṅgyas tatkṣobhāya punaḥ punaḥ atha nārāyaṇo dhairya- gāmbhīryodāryamānasaḥ ūror utpādayām āsa tāṃ varorubalāṃ tadā trailokyasundarīratnam aśeṣam avanīpate guṇalāghavam abhyeti yasyāḥ saṃdarśanād anu tāṃ vilokya mahīpāla cakampe mādhavānilam vasanto vismayaṃ yātaḥ saṃyātaḥ saṃsmaraṃ smaraḥ rambhātilottamādyāś ca vilakṣā devayoṣitaḥ na rejur avanīpāla tallakṣahṛdayekṣaṇāḥ tataḥ kāmo vasantaś ca pārthivāpsarasaś ca tāḥ praṇamya bhagavantau tau tuṣṭuvur munisattamau prasīdatu jagaddhātā yasya devasya māyayā mohitāḥ sma vijānīmo nāntaraṃ vandyanindyayoḥ prasīdatu sa no devo yasya rūpam idaṃ dvidhā dhāma bhūtasya lokānām anāder atra tiṣṭhati naranārāyaṇau devau śārṅgacakrāyudhāv ubhau āstāṃ prasādasumukhāv asmākam aparādhinām nidhānaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ sarvapāpendhanānalaḥ nārāyaṇo no bhagavān sarvapāpaṃ vyapohatu śārṅgacakrāyudhaḥ śrīmān ātmajñānamayo anaghaḥ naraḥ samastapāpāni hatvātmā sarvadehinām jaṭākalāpabandho ayam anayor akṣayātmanoḥ saumyā ca dṛṣṭiḥ pāpāni hantu sarvāṇi naḥ śubhā prasīdatu naro asmākaṃ tathā nārāyaṇo avyayaḥ aparādhaḥ kṛto asmābhir yayor avyaktajanmanoḥ kva mūrtir aiśvaryaguṇair yuktā divyair mahātmanoḥ kva naḥ śarīrakāṇīdṛg miśrakarmacitāni vai tathāpy avidyāduṣṭena manasā yaḥ kṛto hi vām asmābhir aparādho ayaṃ kṣamyatāṃ sumahādyutī śaraṇaṃ ca prapannānāṃ tavāsmīti ca vādinām prasādaṃ pitṛhantṝṇām api kurvanti sādhavaḥ eṣa eva varo asmākam avivekāhṛto mahān trailokyavandyau yannāthau vilobhayitum āgatāḥ prasīda deva vijñāna- ghanamūḍhadṛśām api bhavanti santaḥ satataṃ saddharmanyavatārakāḥ dṛṣṭvaitan naḥ samutpannaṃ yathā strīratnam īdṛśam tvayi nārāyaṇotpannā śreṣṭhā pāravatī matiḥ tena satyena satyātman paramātman sanātanam nārāyaṇa prasīdeti sarvalokaparāyaṇa prasannabuddhe śāntātman prasannavadanekṣaṇa prasīda yoginām īśa nara sarvagatācyuta namasyāmo naraṃ devaṃ tathā nārāyaṇaṃ harim namo narāya namyāya namo nārāyaṇāya ca prasannānām anāthānām aparādhavatāṃ prabhuḥ śaṃ karotu naro asmākaṃ śaṃ nārāyaṇa dehi naḥ evam abhyarthitaḥ stutyā rāgadveṣādivarjitaḥ prāheśaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sādhyo nārāyaṇo nṛpa svāgataṃ madhave kāma
