bhavato apsarasām api yat kāryam āgatānāṃ va ihāsmābhis tad ucyatām yūyaṃ saṃsiddhaye nūnam asmākaṃ valaśatruṇā saṃpreṣitās tato asmākaṃ nṛttageyādidarśitam na vayaṃ nṛttagītena nāṅgaceṣṭādibhāṣitaiḥ lubhyāmo viṣato manye viṣayā dāruṇātmakāḥ śabdādisaṅgaduṣṭāni yadā nākṣāṇi naḥ śubhāḥ tadā nṛttādayo bhāvāḥ kathaṃ lobhapradāyinaḥ te siddhāḥ sma na vai sādhyā bhavatīnāṃ smarasya ca mādhavasya ca śakro api svāsthyaṃ yātv aviśaṅkitaḥ yo asau parasmāt paramaḥ puruṣāt parameśvaraḥ paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sthāvarasya carasya ca utpattihetur ante ca yasmin sarvaṃ pralīyate sa sarvavāsidevatvād vāsudevety udāhṛtaḥ vayam aṃśāṃśakās tasya caturvyūhasya māyinaḥ tadādeśitavartmano jagadbodhāya dehinaḥ taṃ sarvabhūtaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvatra samadarśinaḥ paśyantaḥ kutra rāgādīn kariṣyāmo vibhedakān vasante mayi cendre ca bhavatīṣu tathā smare yadā sa eva viśvātmā tadā dveṣādayaḥ katham tanmayāny avibhaktāni yadā sarveṣu jantuṣu pṛthivy āpas tathā tejo vāyur ākāśam eva ca tathendriyāṇy ahaṃkāro buddhiś ca na pṛthag yataḥ samadṛṣṭir yataḥ kutra rāgadveṣau pravartataḥ ātmā cāyam abhedena yataḥ sarveṣu jantuṣu sarveśvareśvaro viṣṇuḥ kutra rāgādayas tataḥ brahmāṇam indram īśānam ādityān maruto akhilān viśvedevān ṛṣīn sādhyān vasūn pitṛgaṇāṃs tathā yakṣarākṣasabhūtādīn nāgasarpasarīsṛpān manuṣyapakṣigorūpa- gajasiṃhajalecarān makṣikāmaśakādaṃśāñ śalabhān alasān kṛmīn gulmavṛkṣalatāvalli- tvaksāratṛṇajātijān yac ca kiṃcid adṛśyaṃ vā dṛśyaṃ vā tridaśāṅganāḥ manyadhvaṃ rūpam ekasya tat sarvaṃ paramātmanaḥ jānamānaḥ kathaṃ viṣṇum ātmānaṃ paramaṃ ca yat rāgadveṣau tathā lobhaṃ kaḥ kuryād amarāṅganāḥ sarvabhūtasthite viṣṇau sarvage sarvadhātari nipātyatāṃ pṛthagbhūte kutra rāgādiko gaṇaḥ evam asmāsu yuṣmāsu sarvabhūteṣu cābalāḥ tanmayatvaikabhūteṣu rāgādyavasaraḥ kutaḥ samyagdṛṣṭir iyaṃ proktā samastaikyāvalokinī pṛthagvijñānam atraiva lokasaṃvyavahāravat bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇa- pradhānapuruṣātmakam jagad yad etad akhilaṃ tadā bhedaḥ kimātmakaḥ bhavanti layam āyānti samudre salilormayaḥ na vāribhedato bhinnās tathaivaikyād idaṃ jagat yathāgner arciṣaḥ pītāḥ piṅgalāruṇadhūsarāḥ bhavanti nāgnibhedena tathaitad brahmaṇo jagat bhavatībhiś ca yat kṣobham asmākaṃ sa puraṃdaraḥ kārayaty asad etac ca vivekādhāracetasām bhavatyaḥ sa ca devendro lokāś ca sasurāsurāḥ samudrādrivanopetā maddehāntaragocarāḥ yatheyaṃ cārusarvāṅgī bhavatīnāṃ mayorutaḥ darśitā darśayiṣyāmi tathātraivākhilaṃ jagat prayātu śakro mā garvam indratvaṃ kasya susthiram yūyaṃ ca mā smayaṃ yāta santi rūpānvitāḥ striyaḥ kiṃ surūpaṃ kurūpaṃ vā yadā bhedo na dṛśyate tāratamyaṃ surūpatve satataṃ bhinnadarśinām bhavatīnāṃ smayaṃ matvā rūpaudāryaguṇodbhavam mayeyaṃ darśitā tanvī tatas tacchamam icchatā yasmān madūror udbhūtā iyam indīvarekṣaṇā urvaśī nāma kalyāṇī bhaviṣyati tato apsarāḥ tad iyaṃ devarājāya nīyatāṃ varavarṇinī bhavatyas tena cāsmākaṃ preṣitāḥ prītim icchatā vaktavyaś ca sahasrākṣo nāsmākaṃ bhogakāraṇāt tapaścaryā na cāprāpya- phalaṃ prāptum abhīpsitam sanmārgam asya jagato darśayiṣyan karomy aham tapo nareṇa sahito jagataḥ pālanodyataḥ yadi kaścit tavābādhāṃ karoti tridaśeśvara tam ahaṃ vārayiṣyāmi nirvṛto bhava vāsava kartāsi cet tvam ābādhām aduṣṭasyeha kasyacit tavāpi śāstaitad ahaṃ pravartiṣyāmy asaṃśayam etaj jñātvā na saṃtāpas tvayā kāryo hi māṃ prati upakārāya jagatām avatīrṇo asmi vāsava yā ceyam urvaśī mattaḥ samudbhūtā puraṃdara tretāgnihetubhūteyam ailaṃ prāpya bhaviṣyati ity ukte apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ praṇipatyātivismitāḥ ūcur nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ taddarśanakutūhalāḥ ukto bhagavatā yo ayam upadeśo hitārthinām proktaḥ sa sarvo vijñāto māhātmyaṃ viditaṃ ca te yat tv etad bhavatā proktaṃ prasannenāvyayātmanā darśiteyaṃ viśālākṣī darśayiṣyāmi vo jagat tannātha sarvabhāvena prapannānāṃ jagatpate darśayātmānam akhilaṃ darśiteyaṃ yathorvaśī yadi devāparāddheṣu nāsmāsu kupitaṃ tava manas taj jagatam īśa darśayātmānam ātmanā paśyatehākhilāṃl lokān mama dehe surāṅganāḥ madhuṃ madanam ātmānaṃ yac cānyad draṣṭum icchatha ity uktvā bhagavān devas tadā nārāyaṇo nṛpa uccair jahāsa svanavat tatrābhūd akhilaṃ jagat brahmā prajāpatiḥ śakraḥ saha rudraiḥ pinākadhṛk ādityā vasavaḥ sādhyā viśvedevā maharṣayaḥ nāsatyadasrāv anilāḥ sarve sarve tathāgnayaḥ yakṣagandharvasiddhāś ca piśācāḥ kiṃnaroragāḥ samastāpsaraso vidyāḥ sāṅgā vedās taduktayaḥ manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ kīṭāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ pādapās tathā sarīsṛpāś ca ye sūkṣmā yac cānyaj jīvasaṃjñitam samudrāḥ sakalāḥ śailāḥ saritaḥ kānanāni ca dvīpāny aśeṣāṇi tathā nadāḥ sarvasarāṃsi ca nagaragrāmapūrṇā ca medinī medinīpate devāṅganābhir devasya dehe dṛṣṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ nakṣatragrahatārābhiḥ samavetaṃ nabhastalam dadṛśus tāḥ sucārvaṅgyas tasyāntar viśvarūpiṇaḥ nordhvaṃ na tiryaṅ nādhaś ca yadāntas tasya dṛśyate tam anantam anādiṃ ca tatas tās tuṣṭuvuḥ prabhum madanena samaṃ sarvā madhunā ca surāṅganāḥ sasādhvasā bhaktimatyaḥ paraṃ vismayam āgatāḥ paśyāma nādiṃ tava deva nāntam na madhyam avyākṛtarūpapāram parāyaṇaṃ tvā jagatām anantam natāḥ sma nārāyaṇam ātmabhūtam mahī divaṃ vāyujalāgnayas tvaṃ śabdādirūpaś ca parāparātman tvatto bhavaty acyuta sarvam etad abhedarūpo asi vibho tvam ebhiḥ draṣṭāsi rūpasya rasasya vettā śrotā ca śabdasya hare tvam ekaḥ spraṣṭā bhavān spraśavato akhilasya ghrātāsi gandhasya pṛthakśarīrī sureṣu sarveṣu na so asti kaścin manuṣyaloke ca na so asti kaścit paśvādivarge ca na so asti kaścid yo nāṃśabhūtas tava devadeva brahmādyupendrapramukhāni saumyeṣv indrāgnirūpāṇi ca vīryavatsu rudrāntakādīni ca raudravatsu rūpeṣu rūpāṇi tavottamāni samudrarūpaṃ tava dhairyavatsu tejasvirūpeṣu ravis tathāgniḥ kṣamādhaneṣu kṣitirūpam agryaṃ rūpaṃ tavāgryaṃ balavatsu vāyuḥ manuṣyarūpaṃ tava rājaseṣu mūḍheṣu sarveśvara pādapo asi darpānviteṣv acyuta dānavas tvaṃ sanatsujātaś ca vivekavatsu rasasvarūpeṇa jale sthito asi gandhasvarūpo bhavato dharitryam dṛśyasvarūpaś ca hutāśane tvaṃ sparśasvarūpo bhagavān samīre śabdātmakaṃ te nabhasi svarūpaṃ mantavyarūpo manasi prabho tvam bodhavyarūpaś ca vibho tvam ekaḥ sarvatra sarveśvara sarvabhūtaḥ paśyāma te nābhisarojamadhye brahmāṇam etaṃ ca haraṃ bhrukūṭyam tatrāśvinau karṇagatau samastāṇ avasthitān bāhuṣu lokapālān ghrāṇe anilaṃ netragatau ravīndū jihvā ca te nātha sarasvatīyam pādau dharitrīṃ jaṭharaṃ samastāṃl lokān hṛṣīkeśa vilokayāmaḥ jaṅghe viyat pādakarāṅgulīṣu piśācarakṣoragasiddhasaṅghān puṃstve prajānāṃ patir oṣṭhayugme pratiṣṭhitās te kratavaḥ samastāḥ sarveṣṭayas te daśaneṣu deva daṃṣṭṛāsu vidyā bhavataś catasraḥ romasv aśeṣās tava devasaṅghā vidyādharā nātha karāṅghrirekhāḥ sāṅghāḥ samastās tava deva vedāḥ samāsthitā bahuṣu saṃdhibhūtāḥ varāharūpaṃ dharaṇīdhṛtas te nṛsiṃharūpaṃ ca saṭākarālam paśyāma te vājiśiras tathoccais trivikrame yaś ca tavāprameyaḥ amī samudrās tava deva dehe mervādayaḥ śailavarās tavāmī imāś ca gaṅgāpramukhāḥ sravatyo dvīpāny aśeṣāṇi vanāni caiva stuvanti caite munayas taveśa dehe sthitās tvanmahimānam agryam tvām īśitāraṃ jagatām anantam yajñeśam arcanti ca yajvino amī tvatto na saumyaṃ jagatīha kiṃcit tvatto na raudraṃ ca samastamūrte tvatto na śītaṃ na ca keśavoṣṇaṃ sarvasvarūpātiśayī tvam ekaḥ prasīda sarveśvara sarvabhūta sanātanātman parameśvareśa tvanmāyayā mohitamānasābhir yat te aparāddhaṃ tad idaṃ kṣamasva kiṃ vāparāddhaṃ tava deva mūḍhair yan māyayā no hṛdayaṃ tathāpi pāpāvaśaṃ kiṃ praṇatārtihārin mano hi no viṅkalatām upaiti na te aparāddhaṃ yadi vāparāddham asmābhir unmārgavivartanībhiḥ tat kṣamyatāṃ sṛṣṭikaras tavaiva devāparādhaṃ sṛjato vivekān namo namas te govinda nārāyaṇa janārdana tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu tato ananta namas tubhyaṃ viśvātman viśvabhāvana tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu namo namas te vaikuṇṭha śrīvatsāṅkābjalocana vareṇya yajñapuruṣa prajāpālaka vāmana namo astu te abjanābhāya prajāpatikṛte hare tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu saṃsārārṇavapotāya namas tubhyam adhokṣaja tvannāmasmaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣaṃ naḥ praṇaśyatu namaḥ parasmai śrīśāya vāsudevāya vedhase svecchayā guṇabhoktṛtve sargāntasthitikāriṇe upasaṃhāra viśvātman rūpam etat samantataḥ vardhamānaṃ na no draṣṭuṃ samarthaṃ cakṣur īśvara pralayāgnisahasrasya samā dīptis tavācyuta pramāṇena diśo bhūmir gaganaṃ ca samāvṛtam na vidmaḥ kva nu vartāmo bhavān naivopalakṣyate sarvaṃ jagad ihaikasthaṃ piṇḍitaṃ lakṣayāmahe kiṃ varṇayāmo rūpaṃ te kiṃ pramāṇam idaṃ hare māhātmyaṃ kiṃtu te deva jihvāyā yan na gocaram vaktrāṇām ayutenāpi buddhīnām ayutāyutaiḥ guṇānāṃ varṇanaṃ nātha tava vaktuṃ na śakyate tad etad darśitaṃ rūpaṃ prasādaḥ paramaḥ kṛtaḥ chandato jagatām īśa tad etad upasaṃhara ity evaṃ saṃstutas tābhir apsarobhir janārdanaḥ divyajñānopapannānāṃ tāsāṃ pratyakṣam īśvaraḥ viveśa sarvabhūtāni svair aṃśair bhūtabhāvanaḥ taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvabhūteṣu līyamānam adhokṣajam vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ samastā devayoṣitaḥ sa ca sarveśvaraḥ śailān pādapān sāgarān bhuvam jalam agniṃ tathā vāyum ākāśaṃ ca viveśa ha kāle dikṣv atha sarvātmā manuṣyātmany athāpi ca ātmarūpaḥ sthitaḥ svena mahimnā bhāvayañ jagat devadānavarakṣāṃsi yakṣavidyādharoragān manuṣyapaśukīṭādīn mṛgapakṣyantarikṣagān ye antarikṣe tathā bhūmau divi ye ye jalāśrayāḥ tān praviśya sa viśvātmā punas tad rūpam āsthitaḥ nareṇa sārchaṃ yat tābhir dṛṣṭapūrvam ariṃdama tāḥ paraṃ vismayaṃ gatvā sarvās tridaśayoṣitaḥ praṇemuḥ sādhyasāḥ pāṇḍu- vadanā nṛpasattama nārāyaṇo api bhagavān āha tās tridaśāṅganāḥ nīyatām urvaśī bhadrā yatrāste tridaśeśvaraḥ bhavatīnāṃ hitārthāya sarvabhūteṣv asāv iti jñānam utpāditaṃ bhūyo layaṃ bhūteṣu kurvatā tad gacchata samasto ayaṃ bhūtagrāmo madaṃśakaḥ aham apy ātmabhūtasya vāsudevasya yoginaḥ yasmāt parataraṃ nāsti yo anantaḥ paripaṭhyate tam ajaṃ sarvabhūteśaṃ jānīta paramaṃ padam ahaṃ bhavatyo devāś ca manuṣyāḥ paśavaś ca ye etat sarvam anantasya devadevasya vistṛtiḥ etaj jñātvā samaṃ sargaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam sapaśvādigaṇaṃ caiva draṣṭavyaṃ tridaśāṅganāḥ ity uktas tena devena samastās tāḥ surastriyaḥ praṇamya tau samadanāḥ savasantāś ca pārthiva ādāya corvaśīṃ bhūyo devarājam upāgatāḥ ācakhyuś ca yathāvṛttaṃ devarājāya tat tathā tathā tvam api rājendra sarvabhūteṣu keśavam cintayan samatāṃ gaccha samataiva hi muktaye jānann evam aśeṣeṣu bhūteṣu parameśvaram vāsudevaṃ kathaṃ doṣāṃl lobhādīn na prahāsyasi sarvabhūtāni govindād yadā nānyāni bhūpate tadā vairādayo bhāvāḥ kriyatāṃ kutra pārthiva iha paśyañ jagat sarvaṃ vāsudevātmakaṃ nṛpa etad eva hi kṛṣṇena rūpam āviṣkṛtaṃ tadā paramasmād api mahad rūpaṃ yat kathitaṃ tava janmādibhāvarahitaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam saṃkṣepeṇa ca bhūpāla śrūyatāṃ yad vadāmi te yan matau puruṣaḥ kṛtvā paraṃ nirvāṇam ṛcchati sarvaṃ viṣṇuḥ samastau hi bhāvābhāvau ca tanmayau sadasat sarvam īśeśo vāsudevaḥ paraṃ padam bhavajaladhigatānāṃ dvandvavātāhatānāṃ sutaduhitṛkalatratrāṇabhārārditānām viṣamaviṣayatoye majjatām aplavānāṃ bhavati śaraṇam eko viṣṇupoto narāṇām ity uktaṃ tava dharmajña viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam svarūpaṃ ca jagaddhātur ārādhanaviniścayaḥ ārādhitāt phalaṃ yac ca keśavāt prāpyate naraiḥ kathitaś ca mahābhāga dānānāṃ vistarād vidhiḥ yogadvaidhaṃ ca kathitam advaitaṃ dvaitam eva ca advaitabhāvanopāyo vistarāc ca tavoditaḥ saṃkṣepavistarābhyāṃ ca sarvam etat tavoditam devadevasya māhātmyaṃ sarvagasyāvyayātmanaḥ sa eṣa sarvapravaraḥ sarvabhūtaś ca mādhavaḥ sarvam atra ca sarvasminn eṣa eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ triyugaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam apavargamahāhradam samutpatya parāhlādam anantaṃ pratipadyate śrutam etan mayā pūrvaṃ vistareṇa tvayoditam yat tv etat triyugety uktaṃ tasya nirvacanaṃ vada caturyugena kālasya parisaṃkhyā yadā dvija triyugena tadā viṣṇoḥ kriyate kiṃ viśeṣaṇam kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliś ceti caturyugam yadā jagati vikhyātaṃ tadā triyugatā kutaḥ sādhu pṛṣṭo asmi bhūpāla bhavatā triyugāśritam viśeṣaṇam anantasya gadatas tan niśāmaya kāṣṭhā pārthiva vijñeyā nimeṣā daśa pañca ca kāṣṭhātriṃśat kalā jñeyā muhūrtaṃ tāvatīḥ kalāḥ triṃśanmuhūrtā bhūpāla tathāhorātram ucyate tatsaṃkhyātair ahorātrair māsaḥ pārthivasattama ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ māsāḥ ṣaṇ māsāś ca tathottaram ayanadvitayākhyaś ca kālaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇaṃ tv ayanaṃ rātrir devānām uttaraṃ dinam saṃvatsareṇa devānām ahorātram ihocyate śatatrayeṇa varṣāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭyā ca pṛthivīpate manuṣyasaṃkhyayā varṣaṃ devānām api gaṇyate iti divyena mānena caturyugavikalpanām kathyamānāṃ mayā rājan yathāvac chrotum arhasi catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ kṛtam ucyate tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ tretā trīṇi sahasrāṇi divyābdānāṃ nararṣabha tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ dvāparaṃ dve sahasre tu varṣāṇām abhidhīyate tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ kaliḥ sahasram ekaṃ tu divyābdānāṃ nararṣabha tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ kṛtaṃ nāmayugaṃ pūrvaṃ yatra dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ kṛtam eva ca kartavyaṃ tasmin kāle nṛpepsitam na tatra dharmāḥ sīdanti na ca kṣīyanti vai prajāḥ tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ nāma guṇataḥ procyate yugam devadānavagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ nāsan kṛtayuge rājan na tadā krayavikrayaḥ na sāmayajurṛgvarṇāḥ kriyā nāsīc ca mānavī nābhisaṃdhāya ca phalaṃ kaścid dharme pravartate na tasmin yugasaṃsarge vyādhayo nendriyakṣayaḥ nāsūyā nāpi ruditaṃ na darpo nāpi paiśunam na vigrahaḥ kutas tandrī na dveṣo nāpi dambhanam na bhayaṃ nāpi saṃtāpo na cerṣyā nāpi matsaraḥ tataḥ paramakaṃ brahma yā gatir yogināṃ parā ātmā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ śuklo nārāyaṇas tadā tasminn ātmani lokānāṃ sarvalokamaye acyute svecchayā śauklyam āpanne sarvaṃ bhavati nirmalam brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ kṛte yuge bhavantīha svakarmaniratāḥ prajāḥ svam āśramaṃ svam ācāraṃ samyagjñānasamanvitam jagad bhavati rājendra satyaprāyaṃ taporatam ekavedasamāyuktā ekamantravidhikriyāḥ pṛthagdharmās tv ekavedā dharmam ekam anuvratāḥ caturāśramayuktena karmaṇā kālayoginā akāmaphalasaṃyogāt prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim ātmayogasamāyukto dharmo ayaṃ kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ kṛte yuge catuṣpādaś caturvarṇyasya śāśvataḥ etat kṛtayugaṃ nāma traiguṇyaparivarjitam tretām api nibodha tvaṃ yādṛgrūpaṃ pravartate pādena hrasate dharmo raktatāṃ yāti cācyutaḥ satyapravṛttāś ca narāḥ kriyādharmaparāyaṇāḥ tato yajñāḥ pravartante dharmāś ca vividhāḥ kriyāḥ tretāyāṃ bhāvasaṃkalpāḥ kriyādānaphalodayāḥ pracaranti tato varṇās tapodānaparāyaṇāḥ svakarmasthāḥ kriyāvantaḥ samatvād rajasānvitāḥ dvāpare api yuge dharmo dvibhāgonaḥ pravartate viṣṇuḥ pītatvam abhyeti caturdhā veda eva ca tato anye ca caturvedās trivedāś ca tathāpare dvivedāś caikavedāś ca anṛcaś ca tathāpare evaṃ śāstreṣu bhinneṣu bahudhā nīyate kriyā tapodānapravṛttā ca rājasī bhavati prajā alpāyuṣo narā vedaḥ sumahāṃś ceti dustaraḥ karoti bahudhā vedān vyāsarūpī tadā hariḥ sattvasya cāpy avijñānāt sattve kaścid vyavasthitaḥ sattvāt pracyavamānānāṃ vyādhayo bahavo abhavan kāmāś copadravāś caiva tadā daivatakāritāḥ yair ardyamānāḥ subhṛśaṃ tapas tapyanti mānavāḥ dhanakāmāḥ svargakāmā yajñāṃs tanvanti cāpare evaṃ dvāparam āsādya prajāḥ kṣīyanty adharmataḥ pādenaikena rājendra dharmaḥ kaliyuge api hi tāmasaṃ yugam āsādya kṛṣṇo bhavati keśavaḥ vratācārāḥ praśāmyanti dharmayajñakriyās tathā ītayo vyādhayas tandrī doṣāḥ krodhādayas tathā upadravāś ca vardhante manastāpāś ca saṃgatāḥ yugeṣv āvartamāneṣu loko vyāvartate punaḥ loke kṣīṇe kṣayaṃ yānti bhāvā lokapravartakāḥ yugadvayakṛtān dharmān prārthanā na ca kurvate etat kaliyugaṃ bhūpa yatra jāto asi pārthiva nātrāvatāraṃ kurute kṛṣṇāṃśena svarūpiṇā kṛtādiṣu jagat pāti daityebhyo rūpadhṛd dhariḥ kalau tv anyaṃ samāviśya pūrvotpannaṃ bibharti tam pratyagrarūpadhṛg devo dṛśyate na kalau hariḥ kṛtādiṣv eva tenaiṣa triyugaḥ paripaṭhyate kaler ante ca saṃprāpte kalkinaṃ brahmavādinam anupraviśya kurute vāsudevo jagatsthitim pūrvotpanneṣu bhūteṣu teṣu teṣu kalau prabhuḥ kṛtvā praveśaṃ kurute yad abhipretam acyutaḥ svecchāśukle jagac chuklaṃ rakte raktaṃ ca jāyate pīte ca pītatām asmin kṛṣṇe cātrāsitaṃ nṛpa eṣa eva jagaddevo jagatsraṣṭā jagadguruḥ yadrūpa eva devo ayaṃ tadrūpaṃ jāyate jagat caturyugaṃ naḥ kathitaṃ saṃkṣepād bhavatākhilam kaliṃ vistarato brūhi yatra jāto asmi bhārgava bhagavaty amale viṣṇau krīḍayā kṛṣṇatāṃ gate kimāhārāḥ kimācārā bhaviṣyanti prajās tadā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca dvija kīdṛśāḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpte tan mamācakṣva vistarāt tapaḥ paraṃ kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ yajña eva hi pradhānaṃ dvāpare dānaṃ satyam eva kalau yuge kṛte yuge manaḥśuddhir asty evāyatnatas tapaḥ tapo niṣpādyate bhūpa yogasaṃsādhanaṃ param rāgādidoṣaduṣṭena manasā yat tapo nṛpa kriyate kleśanāśāya tat tapo na vimuktaye tretāyāṃ tu kriyāyajñān manoyajñāṃs tato narāḥ vitanvate sthūlataraḥ panthā dharmasya sa prabho dvāpare nātividvattā yathā tretāyuge abhavat tataḥ sthūlataraḥ panthā dānātmā kriyate naraiḥ na vidvattā na śuddhārtho na śuddhir manasaḥ kalau yato ataḥ satyam evaikam ekāntenopakārakam yathā satyaṃ tathā kṣāntir ahiṃsā ca kalau yuge paropatāpād viratir narāṇām upakārikā tasmin ghore yuge prāpte kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate yādṛgrūpaṃ jagad idaṃ bhavatīha śṛṇuṣva tat rājāno brāhmaṇā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca manujeśvara vyājadharmaparāś caiva dharmavaitaṃsikā janāḥ satyaṃ saṃkṣipyate loke naraiḥ paṇḍitamānibhiḥ satyahānyā tatas teṣāṃ svalpam āyur bhaviṣyati āyuṣaḥ prakṣayād vidyāṃ na śakṣyanty upaśikṣitum vidyāhīnān abuddhīṃs tāṃl lobho apy abhibhaviṣyati lobhakrodhaparā mūḍhāḥ kāmavaśyāś ca mānavāḥ baddhavairā bhaviṣyanti parasparavadhepsavaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ saṃkīryantaḥ parasparam śūdratulyā bhaviṣyanti tapaḥsatyavinākṛtāḥ antyā madhyā bhaviṣyanti madhyāś cāntāvasāyinaḥ īdṛśo bhavitā lokaḥ kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate vastrāṇāṃ pravarā śāṇī dhānyānāṃ koradūṣakaḥ bhāryāmitrāś ca puruṣā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge matsyāmiṣeṇa jīvanto duhantaś cāpy ajāvikāḥ goṣu naṣṭāsu puruṣā bhaviṣyanti tadā nṛpa sarittīreṣu kuddālair vāpayiṣyanti cauṣadhīḥ tāś cāpy alpaphalās teṣāṃ bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye aniṣkrāntās tu saṃbandhāḥ svagotrāt puruṣarṣabha aniṣkrāntāni śrāddhāni bhaviṣyanti ca gehataḥ na vratāni cariṣyanti brāhmaṇā vedanindakāḥ na yakṣyanti na hoṣyanti hetuvādavikūlinaḥ prāyaśaḥ kṛpaṇānāṃ ca tathā bandhimatām api vidhavānāṃ ca vittāni hariṣyanti balānvitāḥ anyāyopāttavitteṣu kariṣyanti narāḥ spṛhām veśyālāvaṇyabhāveṣu spṛhāṃ yoṣit kariṣyati kanyāṃ na yācitā kaścin na ca kanyāprado naraḥ kanyā varaś ca cchandena gṛhīṣyanti parasparam bhāryā na patiśuśrūṣāṃ tadā kācit kariṣyati narā devadvijāṃs tyaktvā bhaviṣyanty anyatomukhāḥ yajñabhāgabhujo devā ye vedapaṭhitā dvijāḥ brahmādyās tān parityajya narāḥ kālabalātkṛtāḥ hetuvādaparā devān kariṣyanty aparāṃs tadā ye yavānnā janapadā godhūmānnās tathaiva ca tān deśān saṃśrayiṣyanti narāḥ kaliyuge nṛpa na śrāddhaiś ca pitṝṃś cāpi tarpayiṣyanti mānavāḥ bahu maṃsyanti te snānaṃ nāpi śaucaparā narāḥ na viṣṇubhaktipravaṇaṃ narāṇāṃ nṛpa mānasam bhavitā tu yuge prāpte kṛṣṇe kārṣṇyopalakṣite vinindāṃ prathame pāde kariṣyanti harer narāḥ yugānte tu harer nāma naiva kaścid gṛhīṣyati dhanyās te puruṣavyāghra pāpāmbhodhāv apāpinaḥ ye nāmāpi kalau viṣṇor gṛhīṣyanty akṣayātmanaḥ dhyāyan hariṃ kṛtayuge tretādvāparayor yajan yad āpnoti kalau nāmnā tad eva parikīrtayan harir harati pāpāni nāma bhaktyā yadīritam vāsudeveti na janas tad evoccārayiṣyati bahupāṣaṇḍasaṃkīrṇe jagaty asmin kalau yuge kṛṣṇāyeti namo astv atra sukṛtī yadi vakṣyati hetuvādabalair mohaṃ kuhakaiś ca jane tadā pāṣaṇḍinaḥ kariṣyanti cāturāśramyadūṣakāḥ pāṣaṇḍabhūtam atyarthaṃ jagad etad asatkṛtam bhaviṣyati tadā bhūpa vṛthāpravrajitotkaṭam na tu dvijātiśuśrūṣāṃ na svadharmānupālanam kariṣyanti tadā śūdrāḥ pravrajyāliṅgino vṛthā utkocāḥ saugatāś caiva mahāyānaratās tathā bhaviṣyanty atha pāṣaṇḍāḥ kāpilā bhikṣavas tathā vṛddhāḥ śrāvakanirgranthāḥ siddhaputrās tathāpare bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ kaliyuge nṛpa niḥśaucā vakramatayaḥ parapākānnabhojanāḥ bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ pravrajitās tadā ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ puruṣarṣabha brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā bhaviṣyanti tathā pare rājaśulkaharāḥ kṣudrā gṛhasthaparimoṣakāḥ muniveṣākṛticchannā vāṇijyam upajīvikāḥ na dvijān na kalau devān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ mlecchabhāṣānibandhais tu hetuvādair vikūlitāḥ evaṃ teṣv atiduṣṭeṣu vimārgapathivartinaḥ bhaviṣyanty apare duṣṭās teṣāṃ mārgānuyāyinaḥ asaṃskṛtoktivaktāro vedaśāstravinindakāḥ jagadunmārgakartāro bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ tacchīlavartibhir bhūpa manuṣyaiḥ paripūrite jagaty atra tadā nṝṇāṃ svalpam āyur bhaviṣyati paramāyuś ca bhavitā tadā varṣāṇi ṣoḍaśa tataḥ prāṇān prahāsyanti kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate pañcame vātha ṣaṣṭhe vā varṣe kanyā prasūyate saptavarṣāṣṭavarṣā vā prajāsyanti narās tadā alpadravyā vṛthāliṅgā hiṃsāratiparāyaṇāḥ hartāro na tu dātāro bhaviṣyanti kalau narāḥ śuklādānaparāḥ kṣudrāḥ parapākāśino dvijāḥ vaiśyās tathā tu rājāno na tu kṣatriyavaṃśajāḥ śūdrā bhikṣavatā viprāḥ śuśrūṣāvipaṇāśritāḥ bhaviṣyanti nṛpaśreṣṭha kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇatvam āgate na śiṣyo na guruḥ kaścin na putro na pitā tathā na bhāryā na patir bhūpa bhavitā tatra saṃkule etat kālasvarūpaṃ te śatānīka mayoditam viṣṇubhaktān naraśreṣṭha na narān bādhate kaliḥ ye aharniśaṃ jagaddhātur vāsudevasya kīrtanam kurvanti tān naravyāghra na kalir bādhate narān ye tanmanaskās tiṣṭhanti prayāntaḥ saṃsthitās tathā svapantaś ca naravyāghra tān kalir na prabādhate sarvatra bhagavān viṣṇur govindaḥ keśavo hariḥ yasya bhāvo na taṃ bhūpa kadācid bādhate kaliḥ na kalau kaliceṣṭo asau mūḍheṣu na sa muhyate bhagavaty acyute nityaṃ yena bhāvaḥ samarpitaḥ kaliprabhāvo duṣṭoktiḥ pāṣaṇḍānāṃ tathoktayaḥ na krāmante manas tasya yasya cetasi keśavaḥ kalau kṛtayugaṃ tasya kalis tasya kṛte yuge yasya cetasi govindo hṛdaye yasya nācyutaḥ aniṣṭvāpi mahāyajñair akṛtvāpi pitṛsvadhām kṛṣṇam abhyarcya yad bhaktyā nainaṃ śvomaraṇaṃ tapet yasyāgratas tathā pṛṣṭhe gacchatas tiṣṭhato api vā govinde niyataṃ cetaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ sadaiva saḥ etad viditvā bhūpāla sarve sarveśvare harau tanmanā bhava taccittas tanmanā nāvasīdati paramārtham aśeṣasya jagataḥ prabhavāvyayam śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchan govindaṃ nāvasīdati kalikalmaṣakakṣāgniṃ nirvāṇaṃ padam avyayam sarvakāraṇam avyaktaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati yatra sarvamaye dhyāte dhyeyam anyan na vidyate yatrārcite arcanīyaś ca jāyate taṃ namāmy aham jagatsraṣṭāram iśeśam anādiṃ parataḥ param sarvāspadaṃ sarvabhūtaṃ gacchan sarvātmanā harim haraty agham aśeṣaṃ yo harir ity abhisaṃstutaḥ aśeṣāghaharaṃ viṣṇuṃ harivarṇaṃ hariṃ namaḥ yatkīrtanād aghaḥ śuddhaḥ smṛte yatrāśuciḥ suciḥ tam ātmani sthitaṃ bhūpa puṇḍarīkekṣaṇaṃ namaḥ apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthagato api vā yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ yady apy upahataḥ pāpair yadi vātyantaduṣkṛtaiḥ tathāpi saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ kalāv atrātidoṣāḍhye viṣayāsaktamānasaḥ kṛtvāpi pāpaṃ govindaṃ dhyāyan pāpair vimucyate tad dhyānaṃ yatra govindaḥ sā kathā yatra keśavaḥ tat karma yat tadarthīyaṃ kim anyair bahubhāṣitaiḥ naitat pitā tanūjāya na śiṣyāya gurur nṛpa paramārthapadaṃ brūyād yad etat te mayoditam saṃsāre bhramatā labhyaṃ putradāradhanaṃ vasu suhṛdaś ca tathivānye nopadeśo nṛpedṛśaḥ kiṃ putradārair vittair vā na mitre kṣetrabāndhavaiḥ upadeṣṭā paro bandhur īdṛśo yo vimuktaye yo naikāgramanā viṣṇāv iti jñātvāpi pārthiva sa nūnam acyutasyaiva nānugrāhyo atra pāpakṛt dvividho bhūtasargo ayaṃ daiva āsura eva ca viṣṇubhaktiparo daivo viparītas tathāsuraḥ upadeśapradānena saṃbhūtitraya āsuraḥ naiva viṣṇuparo bhūpa bhavaty akṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ upadeśeṣu so atyantaṃ saṃrambhī yuktiyojitam hetuvādāśrito mūḍho dadāty uttaram akṣayam snātasya devakāryeṣu tathāpatsu kathāsu ca āsurasyāpi tanmātrā jāyate nṛpate matiḥ iti matvātisadbhāvaṃ rahasyaṃ param īritam tvayācyutān matir bhūpa nāpaneyā kathaṃcana aprāpya vāñchati ratiṃ sarvadaiva nṛṇāṃ manaḥ ihaivācyutasaṃsargi yadi tat kiṃ prahīyate tad alaṃ tava rājyena balakośādibhis tathā cintitair acyutaś cintyo yadbhāvi na tadanyathā etat pavitram ārogyaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam sukhaprītikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ patatāṃ nirvṛtipradam yeṣāṃ gṛheṣu likhitam etat sthāsyati nityadā na tadgṛhāṇi daivotthā bādhiṣyante hy upadravāḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ pradānair vā kiṃ yajñaiḥ kim upoṣitaiḥ ahany ahany etad eva tanmayatvena śṛṇvataḥ yao dadāti tilaprasthaṃ suvarṇasya ca māsakam śṛṇoti ślokam ekaṃ ca dharmasyāsya samaṃ hi tat adhyāyapāraṇaṃ cāsya gopradānāh viśiṣyate śṛṇvaṃś cāsya daśādhyāyān sadyaḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate rātryā yad enaḥ kurute divasena ca mānavaḥ śrotuṃ vāñchā samastaṃ tat pārthivasya vyapohati kapilānāṃ śate datte yad bhavej jyeṣṭhapuṣkare narendra viṣṇudharmāṇāṃ tadāvāpnoti pāraṇe pravṛttau ca nivṛttau ca dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara nāsty anyad viṣṇudhamāṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ śāstram uttamam maitrīṃ karoti bhūteṣu bhaktim atyantam acyute śrutvā dharmān imān vetti abhedenātmano jagat paṭhann anudinaṃ dharmān etāñ śṛṇvaṃs tathāpi vā bhaktyā matimatāṃ śreṣṭha sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate nopasargo na cānartho na caurāgnibhayaṃ gṛhe tasmin bhavati bhūpāla yatraitat pustakaṃ sthitam na garbhahāriṇī bhītir na ca bālagrahā gṛhe yatraitad bhūpate tatra na piśācādikād bhayam śṛṇvan vipro vedavit syāt kṣatriyaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ṛddhiṃ prayāti vaiśyaś ca śūdraś cārogyam ṛcchati yaś caitān niyatān dharmān paṭhec chraddhāsamanvitaḥ viṣṇau manaḥ samāveśya sarvatra samadarśanaḥ tasya pāpaṃ tathā rogān duḥsvapnādyābhicārukān yac cānyad duritaṃ kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ hanti keśavaḥ hemante ya imān dharmāñ śṛṇoti vasudhādhipa śraddhāsamanvitaḥ samyak so agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet śiśire ca naravyāghra yaḥ śṛṇoti yathāvidhi puṇḍarīkasya yajñasya sa prāpnoti phalaṃ naraḥ madhumādhavasaṃjñe tu yaḥ śṛṇoti naras tv imān so aśvamedhakrator bhūpa prāpnoty avikalaṃ phalam śṛṇvann etān nidāghe ca dharmān dharmabhṛtāṃ vara vājapeyasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam varṣāsu cemān yo dharmān saṃśṛṇvan vasudhādhipa rājasūyakratoḥ puṇyam akhilaṃ samavāpnuyāt śaratkāle ca saṃśṛṇvan dharmān etān nararṣabha prāpnoti gosavaphalaṃ samyak śraddhāsamanvitaḥ ṛtuṣv eteṣv etad eva paṭhatām api pārthiva phalaṃ bhavati duṣṭeṣu graheṣv ete śubhapradāḥ kapilānāṃ śatasyoktaṃ yat phalaṃ jyeṣṭhapuṣkare bhūyo bhūyas tad āpnoti pāraṇe pāraṇe gate bhaktyā paṭhati yaś caitān devasya purato hareḥ so arcayaty avanīpāla jñānayajñena keśavam sarvābādhās tathā pāpam akhilaṃ manujeśvara viṣṇudharmā vyapohanti saṃsmṛtāḥ paṭhitāḥ śrutāḥ etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ hareḥ nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcic śrāvyaṃ śrutisukhāvaham atroktavidhiyuktasya puruṣasya vipaścitaḥ na durlabhaṃ naravyāghra paramaṃ brahma śāśvatam
